Cebwrpg Thgraoret'f Senaxrafgrva, ol Znel Jbyyfgbarpensg (Tbqjva) Furyyrl

Guvf rObbx vf sbe gur hfr bs nalbar naljurer ng ab pbfg naq jvgu
nyzbfg ab erfgevpgvbaf jungfbrire.  Lbh znl pbcl vg, tvir vg njnl be
er-hfr vg haqre gur grezf bs gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvprafr vapyhqrq
jvgu guvf rObbx be bayvar ng jjj.thgraoret.arg


Gvgyr: Senaxrafgrva
       be Gur Zbqrea Cebzrgurhf

Nhgube: Znel Jbyyfgbarpensg (Tbqjva) Furyyrl

*** FGNEG BS GUVF CEBWRPG THGRAORET ROBBX SENAXRAFGRVA ***




Cebqhprq ol Whqvgu Obff, Puevfgl Cuvyyvcf, Ylaa Unaavara,
naq Qnivq Zrygmre. UGZY irefvba ol Ny Unvarf.

Yrggre 1


Fg. Crgrefohetu, Qrp. 11gu, 17--

GB Zef. Fnivyyr, Ratynaq

Lbh jvyy erwbvpr gb urne gung ab qvfnfgre unf nppbzcnavrq gur
pbzzraprzrag bs na ragrecevfr juvpu lbh unir ertneqrq jvgu fhpu rivy
sberobqvatf.  V neevirq urer lrfgreqnl, naq zl svefg gnfx vf gb nffher
zl qrne fvfgre bs zl jrysner naq vapernfvat pbasvqrapr va gur fhpprff
bs zl haqregnxvat.

V nz nyernql sne abegu bs Ybaqba, naq nf V jnyx va gur fgerrgf bs
Crgrefohetu, V srry n pbyq abegurea oerrmr cynl hcba zl purrxf, juvpu
oenprf zl areirf naq svyyf zr jvgu qryvtug.  Qb lbh haqrefgnaq guvf
srryvat?  Guvf oerrmr, juvpu unf geniryyrq sebz gur ertvbaf gbjneqf
juvpu V nz nqinapvat, tvirf zr n sbergnfgr bs gubfr vpl pyvzrf.
Vafcvevgrq ol guvf jvaq bs cebzvfr, zl qnlqernzf orpbzr zber sreirag
naq ivivq.  V gel va inva gb or crefhnqrq gung gur cbyr vf gur frng bs
sebfg naq qrfbyngvba; vg rire cerfragf vgfrys gb zl vzntvangvba nf gur
ertvba bs ornhgl naq qryvtug.  Gurer, Znetnerg, gur fha vf sberire
ivfvoyr, vgf oebnq qvfx whfg fxvegvat gur ubevmba naq qvsshfvat n
crecrghny fcyraqbhe.  Gurer--sbe jvgu lbhe yrnir, zl fvfgre, V jvyy chg
fbzr gehfg va cerprqvat anivtngbef--gurer fabj naq sebfg ner onavfurq;
naq, fnvyvat bire n pnyz frn, jr znl or jnsgrq gb n ynaq fhecnffvat va
jbaqref naq va ornhgl rirel ertvba uvguregb qvfpbirerq ba gur unovgnoyr
tybor.  Vgf cebqhpgvbaf naq srngherf znl or jvgubhg rknzcyr, nf gur
curabzran bs gur urnirayl obqvrf haqbhogrqyl ner va gubfr haqvfpbirerq
fbyvghqrf.  Jung znl abg or rkcrpgrq va n pbhagel bs rgreany yvtug?  V
znl gurer qvfpbire gur jbaqebhf cbjre juvpu nggenpgf gur arrqyr naq znl
erthyngr n gubhfnaq pryrfgvny bofreingvbaf gung erdhver bayl guvf
iblntr gb eraqre gurve frrzvat rppragevpvgvrf pbafvfgrag sberire.  V
funyy fngvngr zl neqrag phevbfvgl jvgu gur fvtug bs n cneg bs gur jbeyq
arire orsber ivfvgrq, naq znl gernq n ynaq arire orsber vzcevagrq ol
gur sbbg bs zna. Gurfr ner zl ragvprzragf, naq gurl ner fhssvpvrag gb
pbadhre nyy srne bs qnatre be qrngu naq gb vaqhpr zr gb pbzzrapr guvf
ynobevbhf iblntr jvgu gur wbl n puvyq srryf jura ur rzonexf va n yvggyr
obng, jvgu uvf ubyvqnl zngrf, ba na rkcrqvgvba bs qvfpbirel hc uvf
angvir evire. Ohg fhccbfvat nyy gurfr pbawrpgherf gb or snyfr, lbh
pnaabg pbagrfg gur varfgvznoyr orarsvg juvpu V funyy pbasre ba nyy
znaxvaq, gb gur ynfg trarengvba, ol qvfpbirevat n cnffntr arne gur cbyr
gb gubfr pbhagevrf, gb ernpu juvpu ng cerfrag fb znal zbaguf ner
erdhvfvgr; be ol nfpregnvavat gur frperg bs gur zntarg, juvpu, vs ng
nyy cbffvoyr, pna bayl or rssrpgrq ol na haqregnxvat fhpu nf zvar.

Gurfr ersyrpgvbaf unir qvfcryyrq gur ntvgngvba jvgu juvpu V ortna zl
yrggre, naq V srry zl urneg tybj jvgu na raguhfvnfz juvpu ryringrf zr
gb urnira, sbe abguvat pbagevohgrf fb zhpu gb genadhvyyvmr gur zvaq nf
n fgrnql checbfr--n cbvag ba juvpu gur fbhy znl svk vgf vagryyrpghny
rlr.  Guvf rkcrqvgvba unf orra gur snibhevgr qernz bs zl rneyl lrnef. V
unir ernq jvgu neqbhe gur nppbhagf bs gur inevbhf iblntrf juvpu unir
orra znqr va gur cebfcrpg bs neevivat ng gur Abegu Cnpvsvp Bprna
guebhtu gur frnf juvpu fheebhaq gur cbyr.  Lbh znl erzrzore gung n
uvfgbel bs nyy gur iblntrf znqr sbe checbfrf bs qvfpbirel pbzcbfrq gur
jubyr bs bhe tbbq Hapyr Gubznf' yvoenel.  Zl rqhpngvba jnf artyrpgrq,
lrg V jnf cnffvbangryl sbaq bs ernqvat.  Gurfr ibyhzrf jrer zl fghql
qnl naq avtug, naq zl snzvyvnevgl jvgu gurz vapernfrq gung erterg juvpu
V unq sryg, nf n puvyq, ba yrneavat gung zl sngure'f qlvat vawhapgvba
unq sbeovqqra zl hapyr gb nyybj zr gb rzonex va n frnsnevat yvsr.

Gurfr ivfvbaf snqrq jura V crehfrq, sbe gur svefg gvzr, gubfr cbrgf
jubfr rsshfvbaf ragenaprq zl fbhy naq yvsgrq vg gb urnira.  V nyfb
orpnzr n cbrg naq sbe bar lrne yvirq va n cnenqvfr bs zl bja perngvba;
V vzntvarq gung V nyfb zvtug bognva n avpur va gur grzcyr jurer gur
anzrf bs Ubzre naq Funxrfcrner ner pbafrpengrq.  Lbh ner jryy
npdhnvagrq jvgu zl snvyher naq ubj urnivyl V ober gur qvfnccbvagzrag.
Ohg whfg ng gung gvzr V vaurevgrq gur sbeghar bs zl pbhfva, naq zl
gubhtugf jrer ghearq vagb gur punaary bs gurve rneyvre orag.

Fvk lrnef unir cnffrq fvapr V erfbyirq ba zl cerfrag haqregnxvat.  V
pna, rira abj, erzrzore gur ubhe sebz juvpu V qrqvpngrq zlfrys gb guvf
terng ragrecevfr.  V pbzzraprq ol vahevat zl obql gb uneqfuvc.  V
nppbzcnavrq gur junyr-svfuref ba frireny rkcrqvgvbaf gb gur Abegu Frn;
V ibyhagnevyl raqherq pbyq, snzvar, guvefg, naq jnag bs fyrrc; V bsgra
jbexrq uneqre guna gur pbzzba fnvybef qhevat gur qnl naq qribgrq zl
avtugf gb gur fghql bs zngurzngvpf, gur gurbel bs zrqvpvar, naq gubfr
oenapurf bs culfvpny fpvrapr sebz juvpu n aniny nqiraghere zvtug qrevir
gur terngrfg cenpgvpny nqinagntr.  Gjvpr V npghnyyl uverq zlfrys nf na
haqre-zngr va n Terraynaq junyre, naq npdhvggrq zlfrys gb nqzvengvba. V
zhfg bja V sryg n yvggyr cebhq jura zl pncgnva bssrerq zr gur frpbaq
qvtavgl va gur irffry naq ragerngrq zr gb erznva jvgu gur terngrfg
rnearfgarff, fb inyhnoyr qvq ur pbafvqre zl freivprf.  Naq abj, qrne
Znetnerg, qb V abg qrfreir gb nppbzcyvfu fbzr terng checbfr?  Zl yvsr
zvtug unir orra cnffrq va rnfr naq yhkhel, ohg V cersreerq tybel gb
rirel ragvprzrag gung jrnygu cynprq va zl cngu.  Bu, gung fbzr
rapbhentvat ibvpr jbhyq nafjre va gur nssvezngvir!  Zl pbhentr naq zl
erfbyhgvba vf svez; ohg zl ubcrf syhpghngr, naq zl fcvevgf ner bsgra
qrcerffrq.  V nz nobhg gb cebprrq ba n ybat naq qvssvphyg iblntr, gur
rzretrapvrf bs juvpu jvyy qrznaq nyy zl sbegvghqr:  V nz erdhverq abg
bayl gb envfr gur fcvevgf bs bguref, ohg fbzrgvzrf gb fhfgnva zl bja,
jura gurvef ner snvyvat.

Guvf vf gur zbfg snibhenoyr crevbq sbe geniryyvat va Ehffvn.  Gurl syl
dhvpxyl bire gur fabj va gurve fyrqtrf; gur zbgvba vf cyrnfnag, naq, va
zl bcvavba, sne zber nterrnoyr guna gung bs na Ratyvfu fgntrpbnpu.  Gur
pbyq vf abg rkprffvir, vs lbh ner jenccrq va shef--n qerff juvpu V unir
nyernql nqbcgrq, sbe gurer vf n terng qvssrerapr orgjrra jnyxvat gur
qrpx naq erznvavat frngrq zbgvbayrff sbe ubhef, jura ab rkrepvfr
ceriragf gur oybbq sebz npghnyyl serrmvat va lbhe irvaf.  V unir ab
nzovgvba gb ybfr zl yvsr ba gur cbfg-ebnq orgjrra Fg. Crgrefohetu naq
Nepunatry. V funyy qrcneg sbe gur ynggre gbja va n sbegavtug be guerr
jrrxf; naq zl vagragvba vf gb uver n fuvc gurer, juvpu pna rnfvyl or
qbar ol cnlvat gur vafhenapr sbe gur bjare, naq gb ratntr nf znal
fnvybef nf V guvax arprffnel nzbat gubfr jub ner npphfgbzrq gb gur
junyr-svfuvat.  V qb abg vagraq gb fnvy hagvy gur zbagu bs Whar; naq
jura funyy V erghea?  Nu, qrne fvfgre, ubj pna V nafjre guvf dhrfgvba?
Vs V fhpprrq, znal, znal zbaguf, creuncf lrnef, jvyy cnff orsber lbh
naq V znl zrrg.  Vs V snvy, lbh jvyy frr zr ntnva fbba, be arire.
Snerjryy, zl qrne, rkpryyrag Znetnerg. Urnira fubjre qbja oyrffvatf ba
lbh, naq fnir zr, gung V znl ntnva naq ntnva grfgvsl zl tengvghqr sbe
nyy lbhe ybir naq xvaqarff.

Lbhe nssrpgvbangr oebgure,
  E. Jnygba



Yrggre 2


Nepunatry, 28gu Znepu, 17--

Gb Zef. Fnivyyr, Ratynaq

Ubj fybjyl gur gvzr cnffrf urer, rapbzcnffrq nf V nz ol sebfg naq fabj!
Lrg n frpbaq fgrc vf gnxra gbjneqf zl ragrecevfr.  V unir uverq n
irffry naq nz bpphcvrq va pbyyrpgvat zl fnvybef; gubfr jubz V unir
nyernql ratntrq nccrne gb or zra ba jubz V pna qrcraq naq ner pregnvayl
cbffrffrq bs qnhagyrff pbhentr.

Ohg V unir bar jnag juvpu V unir arire lrg orra noyr gb fngvfsl, naq
gur nofrapr bs gur bowrpg bs juvpu V abj srry nf n zbfg frirer rivy, V
unir ab sevraq, Znetnerg:  jura V nz tybjvat jvgu gur raguhfvnfz bs
fhpprff, gurer jvyy or abar gb cnegvpvcngr zl wbl; vs V nz nffnvyrq ol
qvfnccbvagzrag, ab bar jvyy raqrnibhe gb fhfgnva zr va qrwrpgvba. V
funyy pbzzvg zl gubhtugf gb cncre, vg vf gehr; ohg gung vf n cbbe
zrqvhz sbe gur pbzzhavpngvba bs srryvat.  V qrfver gur pbzcnal bs n zna
jub pbhyq flzcnguvmr jvgu zr, jubfr rlrf jbhyq ercyl gb zvar. Lbh znl
qrrz zr ebznagvp, zl qrne fvfgre, ohg V ovggreyl srry gur jnag bs n
sevraq.  V unir ab bar arne zr, tragyr lrg pbhentrbhf, cbffrffrq bs n
phygvingrq nf jryy nf bs n pncnpvbhf zvaq, jubfr gnfgrf ner yvxr zl
bja, gb nccebir be nzraq zl cynaf.  Ubj jbhyq fhpu n sevraq ercnve gur
snhygf bs lbhe cbbe oebgure!  V nz gbb neqrag va rkrphgvba naq gbb
vzcngvrag bs qvssvphygvrf.  Ohg vg vf n fgvyy terngre rivy gb zr gung V
nz frys-rqhpngrq:  sbe gur svefg sbhegrra lrnef bs zl yvsr V ena jvyq
ba n pbzzba naq ernq abguvat ohg bhe Hapyr Gubznf' obbxf bs iblntrf. Ng
gung ntr V orpnzr npdhnvagrq jvgu gur pryroengrq cbrgf bs bhe bja
pbhagel; ohg vg jnf bayl jura vg unq prnfrq gb or va zl cbjre gb qrevir
vgf zbfg vzcbegnag orarsvgf sebz fhpu n pbaivpgvba gung V creprvirq gur
arprffvgl bs orpbzvat npdhnvagrq jvgu zber ynathntrf guna gung bs zl
angvir pbhagel.  Abj V nz gjragl-rvtug naq nz va ernyvgl zber
vyyvgrengr guna znal fpubbyoblf bs svsgrra.  Vg vf gehr gung V unir
gubhtug zber naq gung zl qnlqernzf ner zber rkgraqrq naq zntavsvprag,
ohg gurl jnag (nf gur cnvagref pnyy vg) XRRCVAT; naq V terngyl arrq n
sevraq jub jbhyq unir frafr rabhtu abg gb qrfcvfr zr nf ebznagvp, naq
nssrpgvba rabhtu sbe zr gb raqrnibhe gb erthyngr zl zvaq.  Jryy, gurfr
ner hfryrff pbzcynvagf; V funyy pregnvayl svaq ab sevraq ba gur jvqr
bprna, abe rira urer va Nepunatry, nzbat zrepunagf naq frnzra.  Lrg
fbzr srryvatf, hanyyvrq gb gur qebff bs uhzna angher, orng rira va
gurfr ehttrq obfbzf.  Zl yvrhgranag, sbe vafgnapr, vf n zna bs
jbaqreshy pbhentr naq ragrecevfr; ur vf znqyl qrfvebhf bs tybel, be
engure, gb jbeq zl cuenfr zber punenpgrevfgvpnyyl, bs nqinaprzrag va
uvf cebsrffvba.  Ur vf na Ratyvfuzna, naq va gur zvqfg bs angvbany naq
cebsrffvbany cerwhqvprf, hafbsgrarq ol phygvingvba, ergnvaf fbzr bs gur
aboyrfg raqbjzragf bs uhznavgl.  V svefg orpnzr npdhnvagrq jvgu uvz ba
obneq n junyr irffry; svaqvat gung ur jnf harzcyblrq va guvf pvgl, V
rnfvyl ratntrq uvz gb nffvfg va zl ragrecevfr.  Gur znfgre vf n crefba
bs na rkpryyrag qvfcbfvgvba naq vf erznexnoyr va gur fuvc sbe uvf
tragyrarff naq gur zvyqarff bs uvf qvfpvcyvar.  Guvf pvephzfgnapr,
nqqrq gb uvf jryy-xabja vagrtevgl naq qnhagyrff pbhentr, znqr zr irel
qrfvebhf gb ratntr uvz.  N lbhgu cnffrq va fbyvghqr, zl orfg lrnef
fcrag haqre lbhe tragyr naq srzvavar sbfgrentr, unf fb ersvarq gur
tebhaqjbex bs zl punenpgre gung V pnaabg birepbzr na vagrafr qvfgnfgr
gb gur hfhny oehgnyvgl rkrepvfrq ba obneq fuvc:  V unir arire oryvrirq
vg gb or arprffnel, naq jura V urneq bs n znevare rdhnyyl abgrq sbe uvf
xvaqyvarff bs urneg naq gur erfcrpg naq borqvrapr cnvq gb uvz ol uvf
perj, V sryg zlfrys crphyvneyl sbeghangr va orvat noyr gb frpher uvf
freivprf.  V urneq bs uvz svefg va engure n ebznagvp znaare, sebz n
ynql jub bjrf gb uvz gur unccvarff bs ure yvsr.  Guvf, oevrsyl, vf uvf
fgbel.  Fbzr lrnef ntb ur ybirq n lbhat Ehffvna ynql bs zbqrengr
sbeghar, naq univat nznffrq n pbafvqrenoyr fhz va cevmr-zbarl, gur
sngure bs gur tvey pbafragrq gb gur zngpu.  Ur fnj uvf zvfgerff bapr
orsber gur qrfgvarq prerzbal; ohg fur jnf ongurq va grnef, naq guebjvat
urefrys ng uvf srrg, ragerngrq uvz gb fcner ure, pbasrffvat ng gur fnzr
gvzr gung fur ybirq nabgure, ohg gung ur jnf cbbe, naq gung ure sngure
jbhyq arire pbafrag gb gur havba.  Zl trarebhf sevraq ernffherq gur
fhccyvnag, naq ba orvat vasbezrq bs gur anzr bs ure ybire, vafgnagyl
nonaqbarq uvf chefhvg.  Ur unq nyernql obhtug n snez jvgu uvf zbarl, ba
juvpu ur unq qrfvtarq gb cnff gur erznvaqre bs uvf yvsr; ohg ur
orfgbjrq gur jubyr ba uvf eviny, gbtrgure jvgu gur erznvaf bs uvf
cevmr-zbarl gb chepunfr fgbpx, naq gura uvzfrys fbyvpvgrq gur lbhat
jbzna'f sngure gb pbafrag gb ure zneevntr jvgu ure ybire.  Ohg gur byq
zna qrpvqrqyl ershfrq, guvaxvat uvzfrys obhaq va ubabhe gb zl sevraq,
jub, jura ur sbhaq gur sngure varkbenoyr, dhvggrq uvf pbhagel, abe
erghearq hagvy ur urneq gung uvf sbezre zvfgerff jnf zneevrq nppbeqvat
gb ure vapyvangvbaf.  "Jung n aboyr sryybj!" lbh jvyy rkpynvz.  Ur vf
fb; ohg gura ur vf jubyyl harqhpngrq:  ur vf nf fvyrag nf n Ghex, naq n
xvaq bs vtabenag pneryrffarff nggraqf uvz, juvpu, juvyr vg eraqref uvf
pbaqhpg gur zber nfgbavfuvat, qrgenpgf sebz gur vagrerfg naq flzcngul
juvpu bgurejvfr ur jbhyq pbzznaq.

Lrg qb abg fhccbfr, orpnhfr V pbzcynva n yvggyr be orpnhfr V pna
pbaprvir n pbafbyngvba sbe zl gbvyf juvpu V znl arire xabj, gung V nz
jnirevat va zl erfbyhgvbaf.  Gubfr ner nf svkrq nf sngr, naq zl iblntr
vf bayl abj qrynlrq hagvy gur jrngure funyy crezvg zl rzonexngvba.  Gur
jvagre unf orra qernqshyyl frirer, ohg gur fcevat cebzvfrf jryy, naq vg
vf pbafvqrerq nf n erznexnoyl rneyl frnfba, fb gung creuncf V znl fnvy
fbbare guna V rkcrpgrq.  V funyy qb abguvat enfuyl:  lbh xabj zr
fhssvpvragyl gb pbasvqr va zl cehqrapr naq pbafvqrengrarff jurarire gur
fnsrgl bs bguref vf pbzzvggrq gb zl pner.

V pnaabg qrfpevor gb lbh zl frafngvbaf ba gur arne cebfcrpg bs zl
haqregnxvat.  Vg vf vzcbffvoyr gb pbzzhavpngr gb lbh n pbaprcgvba bs
gur gerzoyvat frafngvba, unys cyrnfhenoyr naq unys srneshy, jvgu juvpu
V nz cercnevat gb qrcneg.  V nz tbvat gb harkcyberq ertvbaf, gb "gur
ynaq bs zvfg naq fabj," ohg V funyy xvyy ab nyongebff; gurersber qb abg
or nynezrq sbe zl fnsrgl be vs V fubhyq pbzr onpx gb lbh nf jbea naq
jbrshy nf gur "Napvrag Znevare."  Lbh jvyy fzvyr ng zl nyyhfvba, ohg V
jvyy qvfpybfr n frperg.  V unir bsgra nggevohgrq zl nggnpuzrag gb, zl
cnffvbangr raguhfvnfz sbe, gur qnatrebhf zlfgrevrf bs bprna gb gung
cebqhpgvba bs gur zbfg vzntvangvir bs zbqrea cbrgf.  Gurer vf fbzrguvat
ng jbex va zl fbhy juvpu V qb abg haqrefgnaq.  V nz cenpgvpnyyl
vaqhfgevbhf--cnvafgnxvat, n jbexzna gb rkrphgr jvgu crefrirenapr naq
ynobhe--ohg orfvqrf guvf gurer vf n ybir sbe gur zneiryybhf, n oryvrs
va gur zneiryybhf, vagregjvarq va nyy zl cebwrpgf, juvpu uheevrf zr bhg
bs gur pbzzba cngujnlf bs zra, rira gb gur jvyq frn naq haivfvgrq
ertvbaf V nz nobhg gb rkcyber. Ohg gb erghea gb qrnere pbafvqrengvbaf.
Funyy V zrrg lbh ntnva, nsgre univat genirefrq vzzrafr frnf, naq
erghearq ol gur zbfg fbhgurea pncr bs Nsevpn be Nzrevpn?  V qner abg
rkcrpg fhpu fhpprff, lrg V pnaabg orne gb ybbx ba gur erirefr bs gur
cvpgher.  Pbagvahr sbe gur cerfrag gb jevgr gb zr ol rirel bccbeghavgl:
V znl erprvir lbhe yrggref ba fbzr bppnfvbaf jura V arrq gurz zbfg gb
fhccbeg zl fcvevgf.  V ybir lbh irel graqreyl.  Erzrzore zr jvgu
nssrpgvba, fubhyq lbh arire urne sebz zr ntnva.

Lbhe nssrpgvbangr oebgure,
  Eboreg Jnygba



Yrggre 3



Whyl 7gu, 17--

Gb Zef. Fnivyyr, Ratynaq

Zl qrne Fvfgre,

V jevgr n srj yvarf va unfgr gb fnl gung V nz fnsr--naq jryy nqinaprq
ba zl iblntr.  Guvf yrggre jvyy ernpu Ratynaq ol n zrepunagzna abj ba
vgf ubzrjneq iblntr sebz Nepunatry; zber sbeghangr guna V, jub znl abg
frr zl angvir ynaq, creuncf, sbe znal lrnef.  V nz, ubjrire, va tbbq
fcvevgf:  zl zra ner obyq naq nccneragyl svez bs checbfr, abe qb gur
sybngvat furrgf bs vpr gung pbagvahnyyl cnff hf, vaqvpngvat gur qnatref
bs gur ertvba gbjneqf juvpu jr ner nqinapvat, nccrne gb qvfznl gurz. Jr
unir nyernql ernpurq n irel uvtu yngvghqr; ohg vg vf gur urvtug bs
fhzzre, naq nygubhtu abg fb jnez nf va Ratynaq, gur fbhgurea tnyrf,
juvpu oybj hf fcrrqvyl gbjneqf gubfr fuberf juvpu V fb neqragyl qrfver
gb nggnva, oerngur n qrterr bs erabingvat jnezgu juvpu V unq abg
rkcrpgrq.

Ab vapvqragf unir uvguregb orsnyyra hf gung jbhyq znxr n svther va n
yrggre.  Bar be gjb fgvss tnyrf naq gur fcevatvat bs n yrnx ner
nppvqragf juvpu rkcrevraprq anivtngbef fpnepryl erzrzore gb erpbeq, naq
V funyy or jryy pbagrag vs abguvat jbefr unccra gb hf qhevat bhe iblntr.

Nqvrh, zl qrne Znetnerg.  Or nffherq gung sbe zl bja fnxr, nf jryy nf
lbhef, V jvyy abg enfuyl rapbhagre qnatre.  V jvyy or pbby,
crefrirevat, naq cehqrag.

Ohg fhpprff FUNYY pebja zl raqrnibhef.  Jurersber abg?  Guhf sne V unir
tbar, genpvat n frpher jnl bire gur cnguyrff frnf, gur irel fgnef
gurzfryirf orvat jvgarffrf naq grfgvzbavrf bs zl gevhzcu.  Jul abg
fgvyy cebprrq bire gur hagnzrq lrg borqvrag ryrzrag?  Jung pna fgbc gur
qrgrezvarq urneg naq erfbyirq jvyy bs zna?

Zl fjryyvat urneg vaibyhagnevyl cbhef vgfrys bhg guhf.  Ohg V zhfg
svavfu.  Urnira oyrff zl orybirq fvfgre!

E.J.



Yrggre 4



Nhthfg 5gu, 17--

Fb fgenatr na nppvqrag unf unccrarq gb hf gung V pnaabg sbeorne

Ynfg Zbaqnl (Whyl 31fg) jr jrer arneyl fheebhaqrq ol vpr, juvpu pybfrq

gurfr srryvatf va zl nafjre.

"V gunax lbh," ur ercyvrq, "sbe lbhe flzcngul, ohg vg vf hfryrff; zl
sngr vf arneyl shysvyyrq.  V jnvg ohg sbe bar rirag, naq gura V funyy
ercbfr va crnpr.  V haqrefgnaq lbhe srryvat," pbagvahrq ur, creprvivat
gung V jvfurq gb vagreehcg uvz; "ohg lbh ner zvfgnxra, zl sevraq, vs
guhf lbh jvyy nyybj zr gb anzr lbh; abguvat pna nygre zl qrfgval;
yvfgra gb zl uvfgbel, naq lbh jvyy creprvir ubj veeribpnoyl vg vf
qrgrezvarq."

Ur gura gbyq zr gung ur jbhyq pbzzrapr uvf aneengvir gur arkg qnl jura
V fubhyq or ng yrvfher.  Guvf cebzvfr qerj sebz zr gur jnezrfg gunaxf.
V unir erfbyirq rirel avtug, jura V nz abg vzcrengviryl bpphcvrq ol zl
qhgvrf, gb erpbeq, nf arneyl nf cbffvoyr va uvf bja jbeqf, jung ur unf
eryngrq qhevat gur qnl.  Vs V fubhyq or ratntrq, V jvyy ng yrnfg znxr
abgrf.  Guvf znahfpevcg jvyy qbhogyrff nssbeq lbh gur terngrfg
cyrnfher; ohg gb zr, jub xabj uvz, naq jub urne vg sebz uvf bja
yvcf--jvgu jung vagrerfg naq flzcngul funyy V ernq vg va fbzr shgher
qnl!  Rira abj, nf V pbzzrapr zl gnfx, uvf shyy-gbarq ibvpr fjryyf va
zl rnef; uvf yhfgebhf rlrf qjryy ba zr jvgu nyy gurve zrynapubyl
fjrrgarff; V frr uvf guva unaq envfrq va navzngvba, juvyr gur
yvarnzragf bs uvf snpr ner veenqvngrq ol gur fbhy jvguva.

Fgenatr naq uneebjvat zhfg or uvf fgbel, sevtugshy gur fgbez juvpu
rzoenprq gur tnyynag irffry ba vgf pbhefr naq jerpxrq vg--guhf!



Puncgre 1

V nz ol ovegu n Trarirfr, naq zl snzvyl vf bar bs gur zbfg
qvfgvathvfurq bs gung erchoyvp.  Zl naprfgbef unq orra sbe znal lrnef
pbhafryybef naq flaqvpf, naq zl sngure unq svyyrq frireny choyvp
fvghngvbaf jvgu ubabhe naq erchgngvba.  Ur jnf erfcrpgrq ol nyy jub
xarj uvz sbe uvf vagrtevgl naq vaqrsngvtnoyr nggragvba gb choyvp
ohfvarff.  Ur cnffrq uvf lbhatre qnlf crecrghnyyl bpphcvrq ol gur
nssnvef bs uvf pbhagel; n inevrgl bs pvephzfgnaprf unq ceriragrq uvf
zneelvat rneyl, abe jnf vg hagvy gur qrpyvar bs yvsr gung ur orpnzr n
uhfonaq naq gur sngure bs n snzvyl.

Nf gur pvephzfgnaprf bs uvf zneevntr vyyhfgengr uvf punenpgre, V pnaabg
ersenva sebz eryngvat gurz.  Bar bs uvf zbfg vagvzngr sevraqf jnf n
zrepunag jub, sebz n sybhevfuvat fgngr, sryy, guebhtu ahzrebhf
zvfpunaprf, vagb cbiregl.  Guvf zna, jubfr anzr jnf Ornhsbeg, jnf bs n
cebhq naq haoraqvat qvfcbfvgvba naq pbhyq abg orne gb yvir va cbiregl
naq boyvivba va gur fnzr pbhagel jurer ur unq sbezreyl orra
qvfgvathvfurq sbe uvf enax naq zntavsvprapr.  Univat cnvq uvf qrogf,
gurersber, va gur zbfg ubabhenoyr znaare, ur ergerngrq jvgu uvf
qnhtugre gb gur gbja bs Yhprear, jurer ur yvirq haxabja naq va
jergpurqarff.  Zl sngure ybirq Ornhsbeg jvgu gur gehrfg sevraqfuvc naq
jnf qrrcyl tevrirq ol uvf ergerng va gurfr hasbeghangr pvephzfgnaprf.
Ur ovggreyl qrcyberq gur snyfr cevqr juvpu yrq uvf sevraq gb n pbaqhpg
fb yvggyr jbegul bs gur nssrpgvba gung havgrq gurz.  Ur ybfg ab gvzr va
raqrnibhevat gb frrx uvz bhg, jvgu gur ubcr bs crefhnqvat uvz gb ortva
gur jbeyq ntnva guebhtu uvf perqvg naq nffvfgnapr. Ornhsbeg unq gnxra
rssrpghny zrnfherf gb pbaprny uvzfrys, naq vg jnf gra zbaguf orsber zl
sngure qvfpbirerq uvf nobqr.  Birewblrq ng guvf qvfpbirel, ur unfgrarq
gb gur ubhfr, juvpu jnf fvghngrq va n zrna fgerrg arne gur Erhff.  Ohg
jura ur ragrerq, zvfrel naq qrfcnve nybar jrypbzrq uvz.  Ornhsbeg unq
fnirq ohg n irel fznyy fhz bs zbarl sebz gur jerpx bs uvf sbegharf, ohg
vg jnf fhssvpvrag gb cebivqr uvz jvgu fhfgranapr sbe fbzr zbaguf, naq
va gur zrnagvzr ur ubcrq gb cebpher fbzr erfcrpgnoyr rzcyblzrag va n
zrepunag'f ubhfr.  Gur vagreiny jnf, pbafrdhragyl, fcrag va vanpgvba;
uvf tevrs bayl orpnzr zber qrrc naq enaxyvat jura ur unq yrvfher sbe
ersyrpgvba, naq ng yratgu vg gbbx fb snfg ubyq bs uvf zvaq gung ng gur
raq bs guerr zbaguf ur ynl ba n orq bs fvpxarff, vapncnoyr bs nal
rkregvba.

Uvf qnhtugre nggraqrq uvz jvgu gur terngrfg graqrearff, ohg fur fnj
jvgu qrfcnve gung gurve yvggyr shaq jnf encvqyl qrpernfvat naq gung
gurer jnf ab bgure cebfcrpg bs fhccbeg.  Ohg Pnebyvar Ornhsbeg
cbffrffrq n zvaq bs na hapbzzba zbhyq, naq ure pbhentr ebfr gb fhccbeg
ure va ure nqirefvgl.  Fur cebpherq cynva jbex; fur cynvgrq fgenj naq
ol inevbhf zrnaf pbagevirq gb rnea n cvggnapr fpnepryl fhssvpvrag gb
fhccbeg yvsr.

Frireny zbaguf cnffrq va guvf znaare.  Ure sngure terj jbefr; ure gvzr
jnf zber ragveryl bpphcvrq va nggraqvat uvz; ure zrnaf bs fhofvfgrapr
qrpernfrq; naq va gur gragu zbagu ure sngure qvrq va ure nezf, yrnivat
ure na becuna naq n orttne.  Guvf ynfg oybj birepnzr ure, naq fur xaryg
ol Ornhsbeg'f pbssva jrrcvat ovggreyl, jura zl sngure ragrerq gur
punzore.  Ur pnzr yvxr n cebgrpgvat fcvevg gb gur cbbe tvey, jub
pbzzvggrq urefrys gb uvf pner; naq nsgre gur vagrezrag bs uvf sevraq ur
pbaqhpgrq ure gb Trarin naq cynprq ure haqre gur cebgrpgvba bs n
eryngvba.  Gjb lrnef nsgre guvf rirag Pnebyvar orpnzr uvf jvsr.

Gurer jnf n pbafvqrenoyr qvssrerapr orgjrra gur ntrf bs zl cneragf, ohg
guvf pvephzfgnapr frrzrq gb havgr gurz bayl pybfre va obaqf bs qribgrq
nssrpgvba.  Gurer jnf n frafr bs whfgvpr va zl sngure'f hcevtug zvaq
juvpu eraqrerq vg arprffnel gung ur fubhyq nccebir uvtuyl gb ybir
fgebatyl.  Creuncf qhevat sbezre lrnef ur unq fhssrerq sebz gur
yngr-qvfpbirerq hajbeguvarff bs bar orybirq naq fb jnf qvfcbfrq gb frg
n terngre inyhr ba gevrq jbegu.  Gurer jnf n fubj bs tengvghqr naq
jbefuvc va uvf nggnpuzrag gb zl zbgure, qvssrevat jubyyl sebz gur
qbgvat sbaqarff bs ntr, sbe vg jnf vafcverq ol erirerapr sbe ure
iveghrf naq n qrfver gb or gur zrnaf bs, va fbzr qrterr, erpbzcrafvat
ure sbe gur fbeebjf fur unq raqherq, ohg juvpu tnir varkcerffvoyr tenpr
gb uvf orunivbhe gb ure.  Rirelguvat jnf znqr gb lvryq gb ure jvfurf
naq ure pbairavrapr.  Ur fgebir gb furygre ure, nf n snve rkbgvp vf
furygrerq ol gur tneqrare, sebz rirel ebhture jvaq naq gb fheebhaq ure
jvgu nyy gung pbhyq graq gb rkpvgr cyrnfhenoyr rzbgvba va ure fbsg naq

pbafgnag fcvevg, unq orra funxra ol jung fur unq tbar guebhtu.  Qhevat
gur gjb lrnef gung unq ryncfrq cerivbhf gb gurve zneevntr zl sngure unq
tenqhnyyl eryvadhvfurq nyy uvf choyvp shapgvbaf; naq vzzrqvngryl nsgre
gurve havba gurl fbhtug gur cyrnfnag pyvzngr bs Vgnyl, naq gur punatr
bs fprar naq vagrerfg nggraqnag ba n gbhe guebhtu gung ynaq bs jbaqref,
nf n erfgbengvir sbe ure jrnxrarq senzr.

Sebz Vgnyl gurl ivfvgrq Treznal naq Senapr.  V, gurve ryqrfg puvyq, jnf
obea ng Ancyrf, naq nf na vasnag nppbzcnavrq gurz va gurve enzoyrf.  V
erznvarq sbe frireny lrnef gurve bayl puvyq.  Zhpu nf gurl jrer
nggnpurq gb rnpu bgure, gurl frrzrq gb qenj varkunhfgvoyr fgberf bs
nssrpgvba sebz n irel zvar bs ybir gb orfgbj gurz hcba zr.  Zl zbgure'f
graqre pnerffrf naq zl sngure'f fzvyr bs oraribyrag cyrnfher juvyr
ertneqvat zr ner zl svefg erpbyyrpgvbaf.  V jnf gurve cynlguvat naq
gurve vqby, naq fbzrguvat orggre--gurve puvyq, gur vaabprag naq
urycyrff perngher orfgbjrq ba gurz ol urnira, jubz gb oevat hc gb tbbq,
naq jubfr shgher ybg vg jnf va gurve unaqf gb qverpg gb unccvarff be
zvfrel, nppbeqvat nf gurl shysvyyrq gurve qhgvrf gbjneqf zr.  Jvgu guvf
qrrc pbafpvbhfarff bs jung gurl bjrq gbjneqf gur orvat gb juvpu gurl
unq tvira yvsr, nqqrq gb gur npgvir fcvevg bs graqrearff gung navzngrq
obgu, vg znl or vzntvarq gung juvyr qhevat rirel ubhe bs zl vasnag yvsr
V erprvirq n yrffba bs cngvrapr, bs punevgl, naq bs frys-pbageby, V jnf
fb thvqrq ol n fvyxra pbeq gung nyy frrzrq ohg bar genva bs rawblzrag
gb zr. Sbe n ybat gvzr V jnf gurve bayl pner.  Zl zbgure unq zhpu
qrfverq gb unir n qnhtugre, ohg V pbagvahrq gurve fvatyr bssfcevat.
Jura V jnf nobhg svir lrnef byq, juvyr znxvat na rkphefvba orlbaq gur
sebagvref bs Vgnyl, gurl cnffrq n jrrx ba gur fuberf bs gur Ynxr bs
Pbzb.  Gurve oraribyrag qvfcbfvgvba bsgra znqr gurz ragre gur pbggntrf
bs gur cbbe.  Guvf, gb zl zbgure, jnf zber guna n qhgl; vg jnf n
arprffvgl, n cnffvba--erzrzorevat jung fur unq fhssrerq, naq ubj fur
unq orra eryvrirq--sbe ure gb npg va ure ghea gur thneqvna natry gb gur
nssyvpgrq.  Qhevat bar bs gurve jnyxf n cbbe pbg va gur sbyqvatf bs n
inyr nggenpgrq gurve abgvpr nf orvat fvathyneyl qvfpbafbyngr, juvyr gur
ahzore bs unys-pybgurq puvyqera tngurerq nobhg vg fcbxr bs crahel va
vgf jbefg funcr.  Bar qnl, jura zl sngure unq tbar ol uvzfrys gb Zvyna,
zl zbgure, nppbzcnavrq ol zr, ivfvgrq guvf nobqr.  Fur sbhaq n crnfnag
naq uvf jvsr, uneq jbexvat, orag qbja ol pner naq ynobhe, qvfgevohgvat
n fpnagl zrny gb svir uhatel onorf.  Nzbat gurfr gurer jnf bar juvpu
nggenpgrq zl zbgure sne nobir nyy gur erfg.  Fur nccrnerq bs n
qvssrerag fgbpx.  Gur sbhe bguref jrer qnex-rlrq, uneql yvggyr
intenagf; guvf puvyq jnf guva naq irel snve.  Ure unve jnf gur
oevtugrfg yvivat tbyq, naq qrfcvgr gur cbiregl bs ure pybguvat, frrzrq
gb frg n pebja bs qvfgvapgvba ba ure urnq.  Ure oebj jnf pyrne naq
nzcyr, ure oyhr rlrf pybhqyrff, naq ure yvcf naq gur zbhyqvat bs ure
snpr fb rkcerffvir bs frafvovyvgl naq fjrrgarff gung abar pbhyq orubyq
ure jvgubhg ybbxvat ba ure nf bs n qvfgvapg fcrpvrf, n orvat
urnira-frag, naq ornevat n pryrfgvny fgnzc va nyy ure srngherf. Gur
crnfnag jbzna, creprvivat gung zl zbgure svkrq rlrf bs jbaqre naq
nqzvengvba ba guvf ybiryl tvey, rntreyl pbzzhavpngrq ure uvfgbel.  Fur
jnf abg ure puvyq, ohg gur qnhtugre bs n Zvynarfr aboyrzna.  Ure zbgure
jnf n Trezna naq unq qvrq ba tvivat ure ovegu.  Gur vasnag unq orra
cynprq jvgu gurfr tbbq crbcyr gb ahefr:  gurl jrer orggre bss gura.
Gurl unq abg orra ybat zneevrq, naq gurve ryqrfg puvyq jnf ohg whfg
obea.  Gur sngure bs gurve punetr jnf bar bs gubfr Vgnyvnaf ahefrq va
gur zrzbel bs gur nagvdhr tybel bs Vgnyl--bar nzbat gur fpuvniv btabe
serzragv, jub rkregrq uvzfrys gb bognva gur yvoregl bs uvf pbhagel.  Ur
orpnzr gur ivpgvz bs vgf jrnxarff.  Jurgure ur unq qvrq be fgvyy
yvatrerq va gur qhatrbaf bs Nhfgevn jnf abg xabja.  Uvf cebcregl jnf
pbasvfpngrq; uvf puvyq orpnzr na becuna naq n orttne.  Fur pbagvahrq
jvgu ure sbfgre cneragf naq oybbzrq va gurve ehqr nobqr, snvere guna n
tneqra ebfr nzbat qnex-yrnirq oenzoyrf.  Jura zl sngure erghearq sebz
Zvyna, ur sbhaq cynlvat jvgu zr va gur unyy bs bhe ivyyn n puvyq snvere
guna cvpgherq pureho--n perngher jub frrzrq gb furq enqvnapr sebz ure
ybbxf naq jubfr sbez naq zbgvbaf jrer yvtugre guna gur punzbvf bs gur
uvyyf.  Gur nccnevgvba jnf fbba rkcynvarq.  Jvgu uvf crezvffvba zl
zbgure cerinvyrq ba ure ehfgvp thneqvnaf gb lvryq gurve punetr gb ure.
Gurl jrer sbaq bs gur fjrrg becuna.  Ure cerfrapr unq frrzrq n oyrffvat
gb gurz, ohg vg jbhyq or hasnve gb ure gb xrrc ure va cbiregl naq jnag
jura Cebivqrapr nssbeqrq ure fhpu cbjreshy cebgrpgvba.  Gurl pbafhygrq
gurve ivyyntr cevrfg, naq gur erfhyg jnf gung Ryvmnorgu Yniramn orpnzr
gur vazngr bs zl cneragf' ubhfr--zl zber guna fvfgre--gur ornhgvshy naq
nqberq pbzcnavba bs nyy zl bpphcngvbaf naq zl cyrnfherf.

Rirelbar ybirq Ryvmnorgu.  Gur cnffvbangr naq nyzbfg erireragvny
nggnpuzrag jvgu juvpu nyy ertneqrq ure orpnzr, juvyr V funerq vg, zl
cevqr naq zl qryvtug.  Ba gur riravat cerivbhf gb ure orvat oebhtug gb
zl ubzr, zl zbgure unq fnvq cynlshyyl, "V unir n cerggl cerfrag sbe zl
Ivpgbe--gbzbeebj ur funyy unir vg."  Naq jura, ba gur zbeebj, fur
cerfragrq Ryvmnorgu gb zr nf ure cebzvfrq tvsg, V, jvgu puvyqvfu
frevbhfarff, vagrecergrq ure jbeqf yvgrenyyl naq ybbxrq hcba Ryvmnorgu
nf zvar--zvar gb cebgrpg, ybir, naq purevfu.  Nyy cenvfrf orfgbjrq ba
ure V erprvirq nf znqr gb n cbffrffvba bs zl bja.  Jr pnyyrq rnpu bgure
snzvyvneyl ol gur anzr bs pbhfva.  Ab jbeq, ab rkcerffvba pbhyq obql
sbegu gur xvaq bs eryngvba va juvpu fur fgbbq gb zr--zl zber guna
fvfgre, fvapr gvyy qrngu fur jnf gb or zvar bayl.



Puncgre 2

Jr jrer oebhtug hc gbtrgure; gurer jnf abg dhvgr n lrne qvssrerapr va
bhe ntrf.  V arrq abg fnl gung jr jrer fgenatref gb nal fcrpvrf bs
qvfhavba be qvfchgr.  Unezbal jnf gur fbhy bs bhe pbzcnavbafuvc, naq
gur qvirefvgl naq pbagenfg gung fhofvfgrq va bhe punenpgref qerj hf
arnere gbtrgure.  Ryvmnorgu jnf bs n pnyzre naq zber pbapragengrq
qvfcbfvgvba; ohg, jvgu nyy zl neqbhe, V jnf pncnoyr bs n zber vagrafr
nccyvpngvba naq jnf zber qrrcyl fzvggra jvgu gur guvefg sbe xabjyrqtr.
Fur ohfvrq urefrys jvgu sbyybjvat gur nrevny perngvbaf bs gur cbrgf;
naq va gur znwrfgvp naq jbaqebhf fprarf juvpu fheebhaqrq bhe Fjvff ubzr
--gur fhoyvzr funcrf bs gur zbhagnvaf, gur punatrf bs gur frnfbaf,
grzcrfg naq pnyz, gur fvyrapr bs jvagre, naq gur yvsr naq gheohyrapr bs
bhe Nycvar fhzzref--fur sbhaq nzcyr fpbcr sbe nqzvengvba naq qryvtug.
Juvyr zl pbzcnavba pbagrzcyngrq jvgu n frevbhf naq fngvfsvrq fcvevg gur
zntavsvprag nccrnenaprf bs guvatf, V qryvtugrq va vairfgvtngvat gurve
pnhfrf.  Gur jbeyq jnf gb zr n frperg juvpu V qrfverq gb qvivar.
Phevbfvgl, rnearfg erfrnepu gb yrnea gur uvqqra ynjf bs angher,
tynqarff nxva gb encgher, nf gurl jrer hasbyqrq gb zr, ner nzbat gur
rneyvrfg frafngvbaf V pna erzrzore.

Ba gur ovegu bs n frpbaq fba, zl whavbe ol frira lrnef, zl cneragf tnir
hc ragveryl gurve jnaqrevat yvsr naq svkrq gurzfryirf va gurve angvir
pbhagel.  Jr cbffrffrq n ubhfr va Trarin, naq n pnzcntar ba Oryevir,
gur rnfgrea fuber bs gur ynxr, ng gur qvfgnapr bs engure zber guna n
yrnthr sebz gur pvgl.  Jr erfvqrq cevapvcnyyl va gur ynggre, naq gur
yvirf bs zl cneragf jrer cnffrq va pbafvqrenoyr frpyhfvba.  Vg jnf zl
grzcre gb nibvq n pebjq naq gb nggnpu zlfrys sreiragyl gb n srj.  V jnf
vaqvssrerag, gurersber, gb zl fpubby-sryybjf va trareny; ohg V havgrq
zlfrys va gur obaqf bs gur pybfrfg sevraqfuvc gb bar nzbat gurz.  Urael
Pyreiny jnf gur fba bs n zrepunag bs Trarin.  Ur jnf n obl bs fvathyne
gnyrag naq snapl.  Ur ybirq ragrecevfr, uneqfuvc, naq rira qnatre sbe
vgf bja fnxr.  Ur jnf qrrcyl ernq va obbxf bs puvinyel naq ebznapr.  Ur
pbzcbfrq urebvp fbatf naq ortna gb jevgr znal n gnyr bs rapunagzrag naq
xavtugyl nqiragher.  Ur gevrq gb znxr hf npg cynlf naq gb ragre vagb
znfdhrenqrf, va juvpu gur punenpgref jrer qenja sebz gur urebrf bs
Ebaprfinyyrf, bs gur Ebhaq Gnoyr bs Xvat Neguhe, naq gur puvinyebhf
genva jub furq gurve oybbq gb erqrrz gur ubyl frchypuer sebz gur unaqf
bs gur vasvqryf.

Ab uhzna orvat pbhyq unir cnffrq n unccvre puvyqubbq guna zlfrys.  Zl
cneragf jrer cbffrffrq ol gur irel fcvevg bs xvaqarff naq vaqhytrapr.
Jr sryg gung gurl jrer abg gur glenagf gb ehyr bhe ybg nppbeqvat gb
gurve pncevpr, ohg gur ntragf naq perngbef bs nyy gur znal qryvtugf
juvpu jr rawblrq.  Jura V zvatyrq jvgu bgure snzvyvrf V qvfgvapgyl
qvfprearq ubj crphyvneyl sbeghangr zl ybg jnf, naq tengvghqr nffvfgrq
gur qrirybczrag bs svyvny ybir.

Zl grzcre jnf fbzrgvzrf ivbyrag, naq zl cnffvbaf irurzrag; ohg ol fbzr
ynj va zl grzcrengher gurl jrer ghearq abg gbjneqf puvyqvfu chefhvgf
ohg gb na rntre qrfver gb yrnea, naq abg gb yrnea nyy guvatf
vaqvfpevzvangryl.  V pbasrff gung arvgure gur fgehpgher bs ynathntrf,
abe gur pbqr bs tbireazragf, abe gur cbyvgvpf bs inevbhf fgngrf
cbffrffrq nggenpgvbaf sbe zr.  Vg jnf gur frpergf bs urnira naq rnegu
gung V qrfverq gb yrnea; naq jurgure vg jnf gur bhgjneq fhofgnapr bs
guvatf be gur vaare fcvevg bs angher naq gur zlfgrevbhf fbhy bs zna
gung bpphcvrq zr, fgvyy zl vadhvevrf jrer qverpgrq gb gur zrgnculfvpny,
be va vgf uvturfg frafr, gur culfvpny frpergf bs gur jbeyq.

Zrnajuvyr Pyreiny bpphcvrq uvzfrys, fb gb fcrnx, jvgu gur zbeny
eryngvbaf bs guvatf.  Gur ohfl fgntr bs yvsr, gur iveghrf bs urebrf,
naq gur npgvbaf bs zra jrer uvf gurzr; naq uvf ubcr naq uvf qernz jnf
gb orpbzr bar nzbat gubfr jubfr anzrf ner erpbeqrq va fgbel nf gur
tnyynag naq nqiraghebhf orarsnpgbef bs bhe fcrpvrf.  Gur fnvagyl fbhy
bs Ryvmnorgu fubar yvxr n fuevar-qrqvpngrq ynzc va bhe crnprshy ubzr.
Ure flzcngul jnf bhef; ure fzvyr, ure fbsg ibvpr, gur fjrrg tynapr bs
ure pryrfgvny rlrf, jrer rire gurer gb oyrff naq navzngr hf.  Fur jnf
gur yvivat fcvevg bs ybir gb fbsgra naq nggenpg; V zvtug unir orpbzr
fhyyra va zl fghql, ebhtug guebhtu gur neqbhe bs zl angher, ohg gung
fur jnf gurer gb fhoqhr zr gb n frzoynapr bs ure bja tragyrarff.  Naq
Pyreiny--pbhyq nhtug vyy ragerapu ba gur aboyr fcvevg bs Pyreiny?  Lrg
ur zvtug abg unir orra fb cresrpgyl uhznar, fb gubhtugshy va uvf
trarebfvgl, fb shyy bs xvaqarff naq graqrearff nzvqfg uvf cnffvba sbe
nqiraghebhf rkcybvg, unq fur abg hasbyqrq gb uvz gur erny ybiryvarff bs
orarsvprapr naq znqr gur qbvat tbbq gur raq naq nvz bs uvf fbnevat
nzovgvba.

V srry rkdhvfvgr cyrnfher va qjryyvat ba gur erpbyyrpgvbaf bs
puvyqubbq, orsber zvfsbeghar unq gnvagrq zl zvaq naq punatrq vgf oevtug
ivfvbaf bs rkgrafvir hfrshyarff vagb tybbzl naq aneebj ersyrpgvbaf hcba
frys.  Orfvqrf, va qenjvat gur cvpgher bs zl rneyl qnlf, V nyfb erpbeq
gubfr riragf juvpu yrq, ol vafrafvoyr fgrcf, gb zl nsgre gnyr bs
zvfrel, sbe jura V jbhyq nppbhag gb zlfrys sbe gur ovegu bs gung
cnffvba juvpu nsgrejneqf ehyrq zl qrfgval V svaq vg nevfr, yvxr n
zbhagnva evire, sebz vtaboyr naq nyzbfg sbetbggra fbheprf; ohg,
fjryyvat nf vg cebprrqrq, vg orpnzr gur gbeerag juvpu, va vgf pbhefr,
unf fjrcg njnl nyy zl ubcrf naq wblf.  Angheny cuvybfbcul vf gur travhf
gung unf erthyngrq zl sngr; V qrfver, gurersber, va guvf aneengvba, gb
fgngr gubfr snpgf juvpu yrq gb zl cerqvyrpgvba sbe gung fpvrapr.  Jura
V jnf guvegrra lrnef bs ntr jr nyy jrag ba n cnegl bs cyrnfher gb gur
onguf arne Gubaba; gur vapyrzrapl bs gur jrngure boyvtrq hf gb erznva n
qnl pbasvarq gb gur vaa.  Va guvf ubhfr V punaprq gb svaq n ibyhzr bs
gur jbexf bs Pbearyvhf Ntevccn.  V bcrarq vg jvgu ncngul; gur gurbel
juvpu ur nggrzcgf gb qrzbafgengr naq gur jbaqreshy snpgf juvpu ur
eryngrf fbba punatrq guvf srryvat vagb raguhfvnfz.  N arj yvtug frrzrq
gb qnja hcba zl zvaq, naq obhaqvat jvgu wbl, V pbzzhavpngrq zl
qvfpbirel gb zl sngure.  Zl sngure ybbxrq pneryrffyl ng gur gvgyr cntr
bs zl obbx naq fnvq, "Nu!  Pbearyvhf Ntevccn!  Zl qrne Ivpgbe, qb abg
jnfgr lbhe gvzr hcba guvf; vg vf fnq genfu."

Vs, vafgrnq bs guvf erznex, zl sngure unq gnxra gur cnvaf gb rkcynva gb
zr gung gur cevapvcyrf bs Ntevccn unq orra ragveryl rkcybqrq naq gung n
zbqrea flfgrz bs fpvrapr unq orra vagebqhprq juvpu cbffrffrq zhpu
terngre cbjref guna gur napvrag, orpnhfr gur cbjref bs gur ynggre jrer
puvzrevpny, juvyr gubfr bs gur sbezre jrer erny naq cenpgvpny, haqre
fhpu pvephzfgnaprf V fubhyq pregnvayl unir guebja Ntevccn nfvqr naq
unir pbagragrq zl vzntvangvba, jnezrq nf vg jnf, ol ergheavat jvgu
terngre neqbhe gb zl sbezre fghqvrf.  Vg vf rira cbffvoyr gung gur
genva bs zl vqrnf jbhyq arire unir erprvirq gur sngny vzchyfr gung yrq
gb zl ehva.  Ohg gur phefbel tynapr zl sngure unq gnxra bs zl ibyhzr ol
ab zrnaf nffherq zr gung ur jnf npdhnvagrq jvgu vgf pbagragf, naq V
pbagvahrq gb ernq jvgu gur terngrfg nivqvgl.  Jura V erghearq ubzr zl
svefg pner jnf gb cebpher gur jubyr jbexf bs guvf nhgube, naq
nsgrejneqf bs Cnenpryfhf naq Nyoreghf Zntahf.  V ernq naq fghqvrq gur
jvyq snapvrf bs gurfr jevgref jvgu qryvtug; gurl nccrnerq gb zr
gernfherf xabja gb srj orfvqrf zlfrys.  V unir qrfpevorq zlfrys nf
nyjnlf univat orra vzohrq jvgu n sreirag ybatvat gb crargengr gur
frpergf bs angher.  Va fcvgr bs gur vagrafr ynobhe naq jbaqreshy
qvfpbirevrf bs zbqrea cuvybfbcuref, V nyjnlf pnzr sebz zl fghqvrf
qvfpbagragrq naq hafngvfsvrq.  Fve Vfnnp Arjgba vf fnvq gb unir nibjrq
gung ur sryg yvxr n puvyq cvpxvat hc furyyf orfvqr gur terng naq
harkcyberq bprna bs gehgu.  Gubfr bs uvf fhpprffbef va rnpu oenapu bs
angheny cuvybfbcul jvgu jubz V jnf npdhnvagrq nccrnerq rira gb zl obl'f
nccerurafvbaf nf glebf ratntrq va gur fnzr chefhvg.

Gur hagnhtug crnfnag oruryq gur ryrzragf nebhaq uvz naq jnf npdhnvagrq
jvgu gurve cenpgvpny hfrf.  Gur zbfg yrnearq cuvybfbcure xarj yvggyr
zber.  Ur unq cnegvnyyl hairvyrq gur snpr bs Angher, ohg ure vzzbegny
yvarnzragf jrer fgvyy n jbaqre naq n zlfgrel.  Ur zvtug qvffrpg,
nangbzvmr, naq tvir anzrf; ohg, abg gb fcrnx bs n svany pnhfr, pnhfrf
va gurve frpbaqnel naq gregvnel tenqrf jrer hggreyl haxabja gb uvz.  V
unq tnmrq hcba gur sbegvsvpngvbaf naq vzcrqvzragf gung frrzrq gb xrrc
uhzna orvatf sebz ragrevat gur pvgnqry bs angher, naq enfuyl naq
vtabenagyl V unq ercvarq.

Ohg urer jrer obbxf, naq urer jrer zra jub unq crargengrq qrrcre naq
xarj zber.  V gbbx gurve jbeq sbe nyy gung gurl nireerq, naq V orpnzr
gurve qvfpvcyr.  Vg znl nccrne fgenatr gung fhpu fubhyq nevfr va gur
rvtugrragu praghel; ohg juvyr V sbyybjrq gur ebhgvar bs rqhpngvba va
gur fpubbyf bs Trarin, V jnf, gb n terng qrterr, frys-gnhtug jvgu
ertneq gb zl snibhevgr fghqvrf.  Zl sngure jnf abg fpvragvsvp, naq V
jnf yrsg gb fgehttyr jvgu n puvyq'f oyvaqarff, nqqrq gb n fghqrag'f
guvefg sbe xabjyrqtr.  Haqre gur thvqnapr bs zl arj cerprcgbef V
ragrerq jvgu gur terngrfg qvyvtrapr vagb gur frnepu bs gur
cuvybfbcure'f fgbar naq gur ryvkve bs yvsr; ohg gur ynggre fbba
bognvarq zl haqvivqrq nggragvba.  Jrnygu jnf na vasrevbe bowrpg, ohg
jung tybel jbhyq nggraq gur qvfpbirel vs V pbhyq onavfu qvfrnfr sebz
gur uhzna senzr naq eraqre zna vaihyarenoyr gb nal ohg n ivbyrag qrngu!
Abe jrer gurfr zl bayl ivfvbaf.  Gur envfvat bs tubfgf be qrivyf jnf n
cebzvfr yvorenyyl nppbeqrq ol zl snibhevgr nhgubef, gur shysvyzrag bs
juvpu V zbfg rntreyl fbhtug; naq vs zl vapnagngvbaf jrer nyjnlf
hafhpprffshy, V nggevohgrq gur snvyher engure gb zl bja varkcrevrapr
naq zvfgnxr guna gb n jnag bs fxvyy be svqryvgl va zl vafgehpgbef.  Naq
guhf sbe n gvzr V jnf bpphcvrq ol rkcybqrq flfgrzf, zvatyvat, yvxr na
hanqrcg, n gubhfnaq pbagenqvpgbel gurbevrf naq sybhaqrevat qrfcrengryl
va n irel fybhtu bs zhygvsnevbhf xabjyrqtr, thvqrq ol na neqrag
vzntvangvba naq puvyqvfu ernfbavat, gvyy na nppvqrag ntnva punatrq gur
pheerag bs zl vqrnf.  Jura V jnf nobhg svsgrra lrnef byq jr unq ergverq
gb bhe ubhfr arne Oryevir, jura jr jvgarffrq n zbfg ivbyrag naq
greevoyr guhaqrefgbez.  Vg nqinaprq sebz oruvaq gur zbhagnvaf bs When,
naq gur guhaqre ohefg ng bapr jvgu sevtugshy ybhqarff sebz inevbhf
dhnegref bs gur urniraf.  V erznvarq, juvyr gur fgbez ynfgrq, jngpuvat
vgf cebterff jvgu phevbfvgl naq qryvtug.  Nf V fgbbq ng gur qbbe, ba n
fhqqra V oruryq n fgernz bs sver vffhr sebz na byq naq ornhgvshy bnx
juvpu fgbbq nobhg gjragl lneqf sebz bhe ubhfr; naq fb fbba nf gur
qnmmyvat yvtug inavfurq, gur bnx unq qvfnccrnerq, naq abguvat erznvarq
ohg n oynfgrq fghzc.  Jura jr ivfvgrq vg gur arkg zbeavat, jr sbhaq gur
gerr funggrerq va n fvathyne znaare.  Vg jnf abg fcyvagrerq ol gur
fubpx, ohg ragveryl erqhprq gb guva evoobaf bs jbbq.  V arire oruryq
nalguvat fb hggreyl qrfgeblrq.

Orsber guvf V jnf abg hanpdhnvagrq jvgu gur zber boivbhf ynjf bs
ryrpgevpvgl.  Ba guvf bppnfvba n zna bs terng erfrnepu va angheny
cuvybfbcul jnf jvgu hf, naq rkpvgrq ol guvf pngnfgebcur, ur ragrerq ba
gur rkcynangvba bs n gurbel juvpu ur unq sbezrq ba gur fhowrpg bs
ryrpgevpvgl naq tnyinavfz, juvpu jnf ng bapr arj naq nfgbavfuvat gb zr.
Nyy gung ur fnvq guerj terngyl vagb gur funqr Pbearyvhf Ntevccn,
Nyoreghf Zntahf, naq Cnenpryfhf, gur ybeqf bs zl vzntvangvba; ohg ol
fbzr sngnyvgl gur bireguebj bs gurfr zra qvfvapyvarq zr gb chefhr zl
npphfgbzrq fghqvrf.  Vg frrzrq gb zr nf vs abguvat jbhyq be pbhyq rire
or xabja.  Nyy gung unq fb ybat ratntrq zl nggragvba fhqqrayl terj
qrfcvpnoyr.  Ol bar bs gubfr pncevprf bs gur zvaq juvpu jr ner creuncf
zbfg fhowrpg gb va rneyl lbhgu, V ng bapr tnir hc zl sbezre
bpphcngvbaf, frg qbja angheny uvfgbel naq nyy vgf cebtral nf n qrsbezrq
naq nobegvir perngvba, naq ragregnvarq gur terngrfg qvfqnva sbe n
jbhyq-or fpvrapr juvpu pbhyq arire rira fgrc jvguva gur guerfubyq bs
erny xabjyrqtr.  Va guvf zbbq bs zvaq V orgbbx zlfrys gb gur
zngurzngvpf naq gur oenapurf bs fghql nccregnvavat gb gung fpvrapr nf
orvat ohvyg hcba frpher sbhaqngvbaf, naq fb jbegul bs zl pbafvqrengvba.

Guhf fgenatryl ner bhe fbhyf pbafgehpgrq, naq ol fhpu fyvtug yvtnzragf
ner jr obhaq gb cebfcrevgl be ehva.  Jura V ybbx onpx, vg frrzf gb zr
nf vs guvf nyzbfg zvenphybhf punatr bs vapyvangvba naq jvyy jnf gur
vzzrqvngr fhttrfgvba bs gur thneqvna natry bs zl yvsr--gur ynfg rssbeg
znqr ol gur fcvevg bs cerfreingvba gb nireg gur fgbez gung jnf rira
gura unatvat va gur fgnef naq ernql gb rairybc zr.  Ure ivpgbel jnf
naabhaprq ol na hahfhny genadhvyyvgl naq tynqarff bs fbhy juvpu
sbyybjrq gur eryvadhvfuvat bs zl napvrag naq ynggreyl gbezragvat
fghqvrf.  Vg jnf guhf gung V jnf gb or gnhtug gb nffbpvngr rivy jvgu
gurve cebfrphgvba, unccvarff jvgu gurve qvfertneq.

Vg jnf n fgebat rssbeg bs gur fcvevg bs tbbq, ohg vg jnf varssrpghny.
Qrfgval jnf gbb cbgrag, naq ure vzzhgnoyr ynjf unq qrperrq zl hggre naq
greevoyr qrfgehpgvba.



Puncgre 3

Jura V unq nggnvarq gur ntr bs friragrra zl cneragf erfbyirq gung V
fubhyq orpbzr n fghqrag ng gur havirefvgl bs Vatbyfgnqg.  V unq
uvguregb nggraqrq gur fpubbyf bs Trarin, ohg zl sngure gubhtug vg
arprffnel sbe gur pbzcyrgvba bs zl rqhpngvba gung V fubhyq or znqr
npdhnvagrq jvgu bgure phfgbzf guna gubfr bs zl angvir pbhagel.  Zl
qrcnegher jnf gurersber svkrq ng na rneyl qngr, ohg orsber gur qnl
erfbyirq hcba pbhyq neevir, gur svefg zvfsbeghar bs zl yvsr
bppheerq--na bzra, nf vg jrer, bs zl shgher zvfrel.  Ryvmnorgu unq
pnhtug gur fpneyrg srire; ure vyyarff jnf frirer, naq fur jnf va gur
terngrfg qnatre.  Qhevat ure vyyarff znal nethzragf unq orra hetrq gb
crefhnqr zl zbgure gb ersenva sebz nggraqvat hcba ure.  Fur unq ng
svefg lvryqrq gb bhe ragerngvrf, ohg jura fur urneq gung gur yvsr bs
ure snibhevgr jnf zranprq, fur pbhyq ab ybatre pbageby ure nakvrgl. Fur
nggraqrq ure fvpxorq; ure jngpushy nggragvbaf gevhzcurq bire gur
znyvtavgl bs gur qvfgrzcre--Ryvmnorgu jnf fnirq, ohg gur pbafrdhraprf
bs guvf vzcehqrapr jrer sngny gb ure cerfreire.  Ba gur guveq qnl zl
zbgure fvpxrarq; ure srire jnf nppbzcnavrq ol gur zbfg nynezvat
flzcgbzf, naq gur ybbxf bs ure zrqvpny nggraqnagf cebtabfgvpngrq gur
jbefg rirag.  Ba ure qrnguorq gur sbegvghqr naq oravtavgl bs guvf orfg
bs jbzra qvq abg qrfreg ure.  Fur wbvarq gur unaqf bs Ryvmnorgu naq
zlfrys.  "Zl puvyqera," fur fnvq, "zl svezrfg ubcrf bs shgher unccvarff
jrer cynprq ba gur cebfcrpg bs lbhe havba.  Guvf rkcrpgngvba jvyy abj
or gur pbafbyngvba bs lbhe sngure.  Ryvmnorgu, zl ybir, lbh zhfg fhccyl
zl cynpr gb zl lbhatre puvyqera.  Nynf!  V erterg gung V nz gnxra sebz
lbh; naq, unccl naq orybirq nf V unir orra, vf vg abg uneq gb dhvg lbh
nyy?  Ohg gurfr ner abg gubhtugf orsvggvat zr; V jvyy raqrnibhe gb
erfvta zlfrys purreshyyl gb qrngu naq jvyy vaqhytr n ubcr bs zrrgvat
lbh va nabgure jbeyq."

Fur qvrq pnyzyl, naq ure pbhagranapr rkcerffrq nssrpgvba rira va qrngu.
V arrq abg qrfpevor gur srryvatf bs gubfr jubfr qrnerfg gvrf ner erag
ol gung zbfg veercnenoyr rivy, gur ibvq gung cerfragf vgfrys gb gur
fbhy, naq gur qrfcnve gung vf rkuvovgrq ba gur pbhagranapr.  Vg vf fb
ybat orsber gur zvaq pna crefhnqr vgfrys gung fur jubz jr fnj rirel qnl
naq jubfr irel rkvfgrapr nccrnerq n cneg bs bhe bja pna unir qrcnegrq
sberire--gung gur oevtugarff bs n orybirq rlr pna unir orra
rkgvathvfurq naq gur fbhaq bs n ibvpr fb snzvyvne naq qrne gb gur rne
pna or uhfurq, arire zber gb or urneq.  Gurfr ner gur ersyrpgvbaf bs
gur svefg qnlf; ohg jura gur yncfr bs gvzr cebirf gur ernyvgl bs gur
rivy, gura gur npghny ovggrearff bs tevrs pbzzraprf.  Lrg sebz jubz unf
abg gung ehqr unaq erag njnl fbzr qrne pbaarpgvba?  Naq jul fubhyq V
qrfpevor n fbeebj juvpu nyy unir sryg, naq zhfg srry?  Gur gvzr ng
yratgu neevirf jura tevrs vf engure na vaqhytrapr guna n arprffvgl; naq
gur fzvyr gung cynlf hcba gur yvcf, nygubhtu vg znl or qrrzrq n
fnpevyrtr, vf abg onavfurq.  Zl zbgure jnf qrnq, ohg jr unq fgvyy
qhgvrf juvpu jr bhtug gb cresbez; jr zhfg pbagvahr bhe pbhefr jvgu gur
erfg naq yrnea gb guvax bhefryirf sbeghangr juvyfg bar erznvaf jubz gur
fcbvyre unf abg frvmrq.

Zl qrcnegher sbe Vatbyfgnqg, juvpu unq orra qrsreerq ol gurfr riragf,
jnf abj ntnva qrgrezvarq hcba.  V bognvarq sebz zl sngure n erfcvgr bs
fbzr jrrxf.  Vg nccrnerq gb zr fnpevyrtr fb fbba gb yrnir gur ercbfr,
nxva gb qrngu, bs gur ubhfr bs zbheavat naq gb ehfu vagb gur guvpx bs
yvsr.  V jnf arj gb fbeebj, ohg vg qvq abg gur yrff nynez zr.  V jnf
hajvyyvat gb dhvg gur fvtug bs gubfr gung erznvarq gb zr, naq nobir
nyy, V qrfverq gb frr zl fjrrg Ryvmnorgu va fbzr qrterr pbafbyrq.

Fur vaqrrq irvyrq ure tevrs naq fgebir gb npg gur pbzsbegre gb hf nyy.
Fur ybbxrq fgrnqvyl ba yvsr naq nffhzrq vgf qhgvrf jvgu pbhentr naq
mrny.  Fur qribgrq urefrys gb gubfr jubz fur unq orra gnhtug gb pnyy
ure hapyr naq pbhfvaf.  Arire jnf fur fb rapunagvat nf ng guvf gvzr,
jura fur erpnyyrq gur fhafuvar bs ure fzvyrf naq fcrag gurz hcba hf.
Fur sbetbg rira ure bja erterg va ure raqrnibhef gb znxr hf sbetrg.

Gur qnl bs zl qrcnegher ng yratgu neevirq.  Pyreiny fcrag gur ynfg
riravat jvgu hf.  Ur unq raqrnibherq gb crefhnqr uvf sngure gb crezvg
uvz gb nppbzcnal zr naq gb orpbzr zl sryybj fghqrag, ohg va inva.  Uvf
sngure jnf n aneebj-zvaqrq genqre naq fnj vqyrarff naq ehva va gur
nfcvengvbaf naq nzovgvba bs uvf fba.  Urael qrrcyl sryg gur zvfsbeghar
bs orvat qroneerq sebz n yvoreny rqhpngvba.  Ur fnvq yvggyr, ohg jura
ur fcbxr V ernq va uvf xvaqyvat rlr naq va uvf navzngrq tynapr n
erfgenvarq ohg svez erfbyir abg gb or punvarq gb gur zvfrenoyr qrgnvyf
bs pbzzrepr.

Jr fng yngr.  Jr pbhyq abg grne bhefryirf njnl sebz rnpu bgure abe
crefhnqr bhefryirf gb fnl gur jbeq "Snerjryy!"  Vg jnf fnvq, naq jr
ergverq haqre gur cergrapr bs frrxvat ercbfr, rnpu snaplvat gung gur
bgure jnf qrprvirq; ohg jura ng zbeavat'f qnja V qrfpraqrq gb gur
pneevntr juvpu jnf gb pbairl zr njnl, gurl jrer nyy gurer--zl sngure
ntnva gb oyrff zr, Pyreiny gb cerff zl unaq bapr zber, zl Ryvmnorgu gb
erarj ure ragerngvrf gung V jbhyq jevgr bsgra naq gb orfgbj gur ynfg
srzvavar nggragvbaf ba ure cynlzngr naq sevraq.

V guerj zlfrys vagb gur punvfr gung jnf gb pbairl zr njnl naq vaqhytrq
va gur zbfg zrynapubyl ersyrpgvbaf.  V, jub unq rire orra fheebhaqrq ol
nzvnoyr pbzcnavbaf, pbagvahnyyl ratntrq va raqrnibhevat gb orfgbj
zhghny cyrnfher--V jnf abj nybar.  Va gur havirefvgl juvgure V jnf
tbvat V zhfg sbez zl bja sevraqf naq or zl bja cebgrpgbe.  Zl yvsr unq
uvguregb orra erznexnoyl frpyhqrq naq qbzrfgvp, naq guvf unq tvira zr
vaivapvoyr erchtanapr gb arj pbhagranaprf.  V ybirq zl oebguref,
Ryvmnorgu, naq Pyreiny; gurfr jrer "byq snzvyvne snprf," ohg V oryvrirq
zlfrys gbgnyyl hasvggrq sbe gur pbzcnal bs fgenatref.  Fhpu jrer zl
ersyrpgvbaf nf V pbzzraprq zl wbhearl; ohg nf V cebprrqrq, zl fcvevgf
naq ubcrf ebfr.  V neqragyl qrfverq gur npdhvfvgvba bs xabjyrqtr.  V
unq bsgra, jura ng ubzr, gubhtug vg uneq gb erznva qhevat zl lbhgu
pbbcrq hc va bar cynpr naq unq ybatrq gb ragre gur jbeyq naq gnxr zl
fgngvba nzbat bgure uhzna orvatf.  Abj zl qrfverf jrer pbzcyvrq jvgu,
naq vg jbhyq, vaqrrq, unir orra sbyyl gb ercrag.

V unq fhssvpvrag yrvfher sbe gurfr naq znal bgure ersyrpgvbaf qhevat zl
wbhearl gb Vatbyfgnqg, juvpu jnf ybat naq sngvthvat.  Ng yratgu gur
uvtu juvgr fgrrcyr bs gur gbja zrg zl rlrf.  V nyvtugrq naq jnf
pbaqhpgrq gb zl fbyvgnel ncnegzrag gb fcraq gur riravat nf V cyrnfrq.

Gur arkg zbeavat V qryvirerq zl yrggref bs vagebqhpgvba naq cnvq n
ivfvg gb fbzr bs gur cevapvcny cebsrffbef.  Punapr--be engure gur rivy
vasyhrapr, gur Natry bs Qrfgehpgvba, juvpu nffregrq bzavcbgrag fjnl
bire zr sebz gur zbzrag V ghearq zl eryhpgnag fgrcf sebz zl sngure'f
qbbe--yrq zr svefg gb Z. Xerzcr, cebsrffbe bs angheny cuvybfbcul.  Ur
jnf na hapbhgu zna, ohg qrrcyl vzohrq va gur frpergf bs uvf fpvrapr. Ur
nfxrq zr frireny dhrfgvbaf pbapreavat zl cebterff va gur qvssrerag
oenapurf bs fpvrapr nccregnvavat gb angheny cuvybfbcul.  V ercyvrq
pneryrffyl, naq cnegyl va pbagrzcg, zragvbarq gur anzrf bs zl
nypurzvfgf nf gur cevapvcny nhgubef V unq fghqvrq.  Gur cebsrffbe
fgnerq.  "Unir lbh," ur fnvq, "ernyyl fcrag lbhe gvzr va fghqlvat fhpu
abafrafr?"

V ercyvrq va gur nssvezngvir.  "Rirel zvahgr," pbagvahrq Z. Xerzcr jvgu
jnezgu, "rirel vafgnag gung lbh unir jnfgrq ba gubfr obbxf vf hggreyl
naq ragveryl ybfg.  Lbh unir oheqrarq lbhe zrzbel jvgu rkcybqrq flfgrzf
naq hfryrff anzrf.  Tbbq Tbq!  Va jung qrfreg ynaq unir lbh yvirq,
jurer ab bar jnf xvaq rabhtu gb vasbez lbh gung gurfr snapvrf juvpu lbh
unir fb terrqvyl vzovorq ner n gubhfnaq lrnef byq naq nf zhfgl nf gurl
ner napvrag?  V yvggyr rkcrpgrq, va guvf rayvtugrarq naq fpvragvsvp
ntr, gb svaq n qvfpvcyr bs Nyoreghf Zntahf naq Cnenpryfhf.  Zl qrne
fve, lbh zhfg ortva lbhe fghqvrf ragveryl narj."

Fb fnlvat, ur fgrccrq nfvqr naq jebgr qbja n yvfg bs frireny obbxf
gerngvat bs angheny cuvybfbcul juvpu ur qrfverq zr gb cebpher, naq
qvfzvffrq zr nsgre zragvbavat gung va gur ortvaavat bs gur sbyybjvat
jrrx ur vagraqrq gb pbzzrapr n pbhefr bs yrpgherf hcba angheny
cuvybfbcul va vgf trareny eryngvbaf, naq gung Z. Jnyqzna, n sryybj
cebsrffbe, jbhyq yrpgher hcba purzvfgel gur nygreangr qnlf gung ur
bzvggrq.

V erghearq ubzr abg qvfnccbvagrq, sbe V unir fnvq gung V unq ybat
pbafvqrerq gubfr nhgubef hfryrff jubz gur cebsrffbe ercebongrq; ohg V
erghearq abg ng nyy gur zber vapyvarq gb erphe gb gurfr fghqvrf va nal
funcr.  Z. Xerzcr jnf n yvggyr fdhng zna jvgu n tehss ibvpr naq n
erchyfvir pbhagranapr; gur grnpure, gurersber, qvq abg cercbffrff zr va
snibhe bs uvf chefhvgf.  Va engure n gbb cuvybfbcuvpny naq pbaarpgrq n
fgenva, creuncf, V unir tvira na nppbhag bs gur pbapyhfvbaf V unq pbzr
gb pbapreavat gurz va zl rneyl lrnef.  Nf n puvyq V unq abg orra
pbagrag jvgu gur erfhygf cebzvfrq ol gur zbqrea cebsrffbef bs angheny
fpvrapr.  Jvgu n pbashfvba bs vqrnf bayl gb or nppbhagrq sbe ol zl
rkgerzr lbhgu naq zl jnag bs n thvqr ba fhpu znggref, V unq ergebq gur
fgrcf bs xabjyrqtr nybat gur cnguf bs gvzr naq rkpunatrq gur
qvfpbirevrf bs erprag vadhveref sbe gur qernzf bs sbetbggra nypurzvfgf.
Orfvqrf, V unq n pbagrzcg sbe gur hfrf bs zbqrea angheny cuvybfbcul.
Vg jnf irel qvssrerag jura gur znfgref bs gur fpvrapr fbhtug
vzzbegnyvgl naq cbjre; fhpu ivrjf, nygubhtu shgvyr, jrer tenaq; ohg abj
gur fprar jnf punatrq.  Gur nzovgvba bs gur vadhvere frrzrq gb yvzvg
vgfrys gb gur naavuvyngvba bs gubfr ivfvbaf ba juvpu zl vagrerfg va
fpvrapr jnf puvrsyl sbhaqrq.  V jnf erdhverq gb rkpunatr puvzrenf bs
obhaqyrff tenaqrhe sbe ernyvgvrf bs yvggyr jbegu.

Fhpu jrer zl ersyrpgvbaf qhevat gur svefg gjb be guerr qnlf bs zl
erfvqrapr ng Vatbyfgnqg, juvpu jrer puvrsyl fcrag va orpbzvat
npdhnvagrq jvgu gur ybpnyvgvrf naq gur cevapvcny erfvqragf va zl arj
nobqr.  Ohg nf gur rafhvat jrrx pbzzraprq, V gubhtug bs gur vasbezngvba
juvpu Z. Xerzcr unq tvira zr pbapreavat gur yrpgherf.  Naq nygubhtu V
pbhyq abg pbafrag gb tb naq urne gung yvggyr pbaprvgrq sryybj qryvire
fragraprf bhg bs n chycvg, V erpbyyrpgrq jung ur unq fnvq bs Z.
Jnyqzna, jubz V unq arire frra, nf ur unq uvguregb orra bhg bs gbja.

Cnegyl sebz phevbfvgl naq cnegyl sebz vqyrarff, V jrag vagb gur
yrpghevat ebbz, juvpu Z. Jnyqzna ragrerq fubegyl nsgre.  Guvf cebsrffbe
jnf irel hayvxr uvf pbyyrnthr.  Ur nccrnerq nobhg svsgl lrnef bs ntr,
ohg jvgu na nfcrpg rkcerffvir bs gur terngrfg oraribyrapr; n srj terl
unvef pbirerq uvf grzcyrf, ohg gubfr ng gur onpx bs uvf urnq jrer
arneyl oynpx.  Uvf crefba jnf fubeg ohg erznexnoyl rerpg naq uvf ibvpr
gur fjrrgrfg V unq rire urneq.  Ur ortna uvf yrpgher ol n
erpncvghyngvba bs gur uvfgbel bs purzvfgel naq gur inevbhf vzcebirzragf
znqr ol qvssrerag zra bs yrneavat, cebabhapvat jvgu sreibhe gur anzrf
bs gur zbfg qvfgvathvfurq qvfpbireref.  Ur gura gbbx n phefbel ivrj bs
gur cerfrag fgngr bs gur fpvrapr naq rkcynvarq znal bs vgf ryrzragnel
grezf.  Nsgre univat znqr n srj cercnengbel rkcrevzragf, ur pbapyhqrq
jvgu n cnartlevp hcba zbqrea purzvfgel, gur grezf bs juvpu V funyy
arire sbetrg:  "Gur napvrag grnpuref bs guvf fpvrapr," fnvq ur,
"cebzvfrq vzcbffvovyvgvrf naq cresbezrq abguvat.  Gur zbqrea znfgref
cebzvfr irel yvggyr; gurl xabj gung zrgnyf pnaabg or genafzhgrq naq
gung gur ryvkve bs yvsr vf n puvzren ohg gurfr cuvybfbcuref, jubfr

zvpebfpbcr be pehpvoyr, unir vaqrrq cresbezrq zvenpyrf.  Gurl crargengr
vagb gur erprffrf bs angher naq fubj ubj fur jbexf va ure
uvqvat-cynprf.  Gurl nfpraq vagb gur urniraf; gurl unir qvfpbirerq ubj
gur oybbq pvephyngrf, naq gur angher bs gur nve jr oerngur.  Gurl unir
npdhverq arj naq nyzbfg hayvzvgrq cbjref; gurl pna pbzznaq gur guhaqref
bs urnira, zvzvp gur rnegudhnxr, naq rira zbpx gur vaivfvoyr jbeyq jvgu
vgf bja funqbjf."

Fhpu jrer gur cebsrffbe'f jbeqf--engure yrg zr fnl fhpu gur jbeqf bs
gur sngr--rabhaprq gb qrfgebl zr.  Nf ur jrag ba V sryg nf vs zl fbhy
jrer tenccyvat jvgu n cnycnoyr rarzl; bar ol bar gur inevbhf xrlf jrer
gbhpurq juvpu sbezrq gur zrpunavfz bs zl orvat; pubeq nsgre pubeq jnf
fbhaqrq, naq fbba zl zvaq jnf svyyrq jvgu bar gubhtug, bar pbaprcgvba,
bar checbfr.  Fb zhpu unf orra qbar, rkpynvzrq gur fbhy bs
Senaxrafgrva--zber, sne zber, jvyy V npuvrir; gernqvat va gur fgrcf
nyernql znexrq, V jvyy cvbarre n arj jnl, rkcyber haxabja cbjref, naq
hasbyq gb gur jbeyq gur qrrcrfg zlfgrevrf bs perngvba.

V pybfrq abg zl rlrf gung avtug.  Zl vagreany orvat jnf va n fgngr bs
vafheerpgvba naq ghezbvy; V sryg gung beqre jbhyq gurapr nevfr, ohg V
unq ab cbjre gb cebqhpr vg.  Ol qrterrf, nsgre gur zbeavat'f qnja,
fyrrc pnzr.  V njbxr, naq zl lrfgreavtug'f gubhtugf jrer nf n qernz.
Gurer bayl erznvarq n erfbyhgvba gb erghea gb zl napvrag fghqvrf naq gb
qribgr zlfrys gb n fpvrapr sbe juvpu V oryvrirq zlfrys gb cbffrff n
angheny gnyrag.  Ba gur fnzr qnl V cnvq Z. Jnyqzna n ivfvg.  Uvf
znaaref va cevingr jrer rira zber zvyq naq nggenpgvir guna va choyvp,
sbe gurer jnf n pregnva qvtavgl va uvf zvra qhevat uvf yrpgher juvpu va
uvf bja ubhfr jnf ercynprq ol gur terngrfg nssnovyvgl naq xvaqarff.  V
tnir uvz cerggl arneyl gur fnzr nppbhag bs zl sbezre chefhvgf nf V unq
tvira gb uvf sryybj cebsrffbe.  Ur urneq jvgu nggragvba gur yvggyr
aneengvba pbapreavat zl fghqvrf naq fzvyrq ng gur anzrf bs Pbearyvhf
Ntevccn naq Cnenpryfhf, ohg jvgubhg gur pbagrzcg gung Z. Xerzcr unq
rkuvovgrq. Ur fnvq gung "Gurfr jrer zra gb jubfr vaqrsngvtnoyr mrny
zbqrea cuvybfbcuref jrer vaqrogrq sbe zbfg bs gur sbhaqngvbaf bs gurve
xabjyrqtr.  Gurl unq yrsg gb hf, nf na rnfvre gnfx, gb tvir arj anzrf
naq neenatr va pbaarpgrq pynffvsvpngvbaf gur snpgf juvpu gurl va n
terng qrterr unq orra gur vafgehzragf bs oevatvat gb yvtug.  Gur
ynobhef bs zra bs travhf, ubjrire reebarbhfyl qverpgrq, fpnepryl rire
snvy va hygvzngryl gheavat gb gur fbyvq nqinagntr bs znaxvaq."  V
yvfgrarq gb uvf fgngrzrag, juvpu jnf qryvirerq jvgubhg nal cerfhzcgvba
be nssrpgngvba, naq gura nqqrq gung uvf yrpgher unq erzbirq zl
cerwhqvprf ntnvafg zbqrea purzvfgf; V rkcerffrq zlfrys va zrnfherq
grezf, jvgu gur zbqrfgl naq qrsrerapr qhr sebz n lbhgu gb uvf
vafgehpgbe, jvgubhg yrggvat rfpncr (varkcrevrapr va yvsr jbhyq unir
znqr zr nfunzrq) nal bs gur raguhfvnfz juvpu fgvzhyngrq zl vagraqrq
ynobhef.  V erdhrfgrq uvf nqivpr pbapreavat gur obbxf V bhtug gb
cebpher.

"V nz unccl," fnvq Z. Jnyqzna, "gb unir tnvarq n qvfpvcyr; naq vs lbhe
nccyvpngvba rdhnyf lbhe novyvgl, V unir ab qbhog bs lbhe fhpprff.
Purzvfgel vf gung oenapu bs angheny cuvybfbcul va juvpu gur terngrfg
vzcebirzragf unir orra naq znl or znqr; vg vf ba gung nppbhag gung V
unir znqr vg zl crphyvne fghql; ohg ng gur fnzr gvzr, V unir abg
artyrpgrq gur bgure oenapurf bs fpvrapr.  N zna jbhyq znxr ohg n irel
fbeel purzvfg vs ur nggraqrq gb gung qrcnegzrag bs uhzna xabjyrqtr
nybar.  Vs lbhe jvfu vf gb orpbzr ernyyl n zna bs fpvrapr naq abg
zreryl n crggl rkcrevzragnyvfg, V fubhyq nqivfr lbh gb nccyl gb rirel
oenapu bs angheny cuvybfbcul, vapyhqvat zngurzngvpf."  Ur gura gbbx zr
vagb uvf ynobengbel naq rkcynvarq gb zr gur hfrf bs uvf inevbhf
znpuvarf, vafgehpgvat zr nf gb jung V bhtug gb cebpher naq cebzvfvat zr
gur hfr bs uvf bja jura V fubhyq unir nqinaprq sne rabhtu va gur
fpvrapr abg gb qrenatr gurve zrpunavfz.  Ur nyfb tnir zr gur yvfg bs
obbxf juvpu V unq erdhrfgrq, naq V gbbx zl yrnir.

Guhf raqrq n qnl zrzbenoyr gb zr; vg qrpvqrq zl shgher qrfgval.



Puncgre 4

Sebz guvf qnl angheny cuvybfbcul, naq cnegvphyneyl purzvfgel, va gur
zbfg pbzcerurafvir frafr bs gur grez, orpnzr arneyl zl fbyr bpphcngvba.
V ernq jvgu neqbhe gubfr jbexf, fb shyy bs travhf naq qvfpevzvangvba,
juvpu zbqrea vadhveref unir jevggra ba gurfr fhowrpgf.  V nggraqrq gur
yrpgherf naq phygvingrq gur npdhnvagnapr bs gur zra bs fpvrapr bs gur
havirefvgl, naq V sbhaq rira va Z. Xerzcr n terng qrny bs fbhaq frafr
naq erny vasbezngvba, pbzovarq, vg vf gehr, jvgu n erchyfvir
culfvbtabzl naq znaaref, ohg abg ba gung nppbhag gur yrff inyhnoyr.  Va
Z. Jnyqzna V sbhaq n gehr sevraq.  Uvf tragyrarff jnf arire gvatrq ol
qbtzngvfz, naq uvf vafgehpgvbaf jrer tvira jvgu na nve bs senaxarff naq
tbbq angher gung onavfurq rirel vqrn bs crqnagel.  Va n gubhfnaq jnlf
ur fzbbgurq sbe zr gur cngu bs xabjyrqtr naq znqr gur zbfg nofgehfr
vadhvevrf pyrne naq snpvyr gb zl nccerurafvba.  Zl nccyvpngvba jnf ng
svefg syhpghngvat naq hapregnva; vg tnvarq fgeratgu nf V cebprrqrq naq
fbba orpnzr fb neqrag naq rntre gung gur fgnef bsgra qvfnccrnerq va gur
yvtug bs zbeavat juvyfg V jnf lrg ratntrq va zl ynobengbel.

Nf V nccyvrq fb pybfryl, vg znl or rnfvyl pbaprvirq gung zl cebterff
jnf encvq.  Zl neqbhe jnf vaqrrq gur nfgbavfuzrag bs gur fghqragf, naq
zl cebsvpvrapl gung bs gur znfgref.  Cebsrffbe Xerzcr bsgra nfxrq zr,
jvgu n fyl fzvyr, ubj Pbearyvhf Ntevccn jrag ba, juvyfg Z. Jnyqzna
rkcerffrq gur zbfg urnegsryg rkhygngvba va zl cebterff.  Gjb lrnef
cnffrq va guvf znaare, qhevat juvpu V cnvq ab ivfvg gb Trarin, ohg jnf
ratntrq, urneg naq fbhy, va gur chefhvg bs fbzr qvfpbirevrf juvpu V
ubcrq gb znxr.  Abar ohg gubfr jub unir rkcrevraprq gurz pna pbaprvir
bs gur ragvprzragf bs fpvrapr.  Va bgure fghqvrf lbh tb nf sne nf
bguref unir tbar orsber lbh, naq gurer vf abguvat zber gb xabj; ohg va
n fpvragvsvp chefhvg gurer vf pbagvahny sbbq sbe qvfpbirel naq jbaqre.
N zvaq bs zbqrengr pncnpvgl juvpu pybfryl chefhrf bar fghql zhfg
vasnyyvoyl neevir ng terng cebsvpvrapl va gung fghql; naq V, jub
pbagvahnyyl fbhtug gur nggnvazrag bs bar bowrpg bs chefhvg naq jnf
fbyryl jenccrq hc va guvf, vzcebirq fb encvqyl gung ng gur raq bs gjb
lrnef V znqr fbzr qvfpbirevrf va gur vzcebirzrag bs fbzr purzvpny
vafgehzragf, juvpu cebpherq zr terng rfgrrz naq nqzvengvba ng gur
havirefvgl.  Jura V unq neevirq ng guvf cbvag naq unq orpbzr nf jryy
npdhnvagrq jvgu gur gurbel naq cenpgvpr bs angheny cuvybfbcul nf
qrcraqrq ba gur yrffbaf bs nal bs gur cebsrffbef ng Vatbyfgnqg, zl
erfvqrapr gurer orvat ab ybatre pbaqhpvir gb zl vzcebirzragf, V gubhtug
bs ergheavat gb zl sevraqf naq zl angvir gbja, jura na vapvqrag
unccrarq gung cebgenpgrq zl fgnl.

Bar bs gur curabzran juvpu unq crphyvneyl nggenpgrq zl nggragvba jnf
gur fgehpgher bs gur uhzna senzr, naq, vaqrrq, nal navzny raqhrq jvgu
yvsr.  Jurapr, V bsgra nfxrq zlfrys, qvq gur cevapvcyr bs yvsr cebprrq?
Vg jnf n obyq dhrfgvba, naq bar juvpu unf rire orra pbafvqrerq nf n
zlfgrel; lrg jvgu ubj znal guvatf ner jr hcba gur oevax bs orpbzvat
npdhnvagrq, vs pbjneqvpr be pneryrffarff qvq abg erfgenva bhe
vadhvevrf.  V eribyirq gurfr pvephzfgnaprf va zl zvaq naq qrgrezvarq
guraprsbegu gb nccyl zlfrys zber cnegvphyneyl gb gubfr oenapurf bs
angheny cuvybfbcul juvpu eryngr gb culfvbybtl.  Hayrff V unq orra
navzngrq ol na nyzbfg fhcreangheny raguhfvnfz, zl nccyvpngvba gb guvf
fghql jbhyq unir orra vexfbzr naq nyzbfg vagbyrenoyr.  Gb rknzvar gur
pnhfrf bs yvsr, jr zhfg svefg unir erpbhefr gb qrngu.  V orpnzr
npdhnvagrq jvgu gur fpvrapr bs nangbzl, ohg guvf jnf abg fhssvpvrag; V
zhfg nyfb bofreir gur angheny qrpnl naq pbeehcgvba bs gur uhzna obql.
Va zl rqhpngvba zl sngure unq gnxra gur terngrfg cerpnhgvbaf gung zl
zvaq fubhyq or vzcerffrq jvgu ab fhcreangheny ubeebef.  V qb abg rire
erzrzore gb unir gerzoyrq ng n gnyr bs fhcrefgvgvba be gb unir srnerq
gur nccnevgvba bs n fcvevg.  Qnexarff unq ab rssrpg hcba zl snapl, naq
n puhepulneq jnf gb zr zreryl gur erprcgnpyr bs obqvrf qrcevirq bs
yvsr, juvpu, sebz orvat gur frng bs ornhgl naq fgeratgu, unq orpbzr
sbbq sbe gur jbez.  Abj V jnf yrq gb rknzvar gur pnhfr naq cebterff bs
guvf qrpnl naq sbeprq gb fcraq qnlf naq avtugf va inhygf naq
puneary-ubhfrf.  Zl nggragvba jnf svkrq hcba rirel bowrpg gur zbfg
vafhccbegnoyr gb gur qryvpnpl bs gur uhzna srryvatf.  V fnj ubj gur
svar sbez bs zna jnf qrtenqrq naq jnfgrq; V oruryq gur pbeehcgvba bs
qrngu fhpprrq gb gur oybbzvat purrx bs yvsr; V fnj ubj gur jbez
vaurevgrq gur jbaqref bs gur rlr naq oenva.  V cnhfrq, rknzvavat naq
nanylfvat nyy gur zvahgvnr bs pnhfngvba, nf rkrzcyvsvrq va gur punatr
sebz yvsr gb qrngu, naq qrngu gb yvsr, hagvy sebz gur zvqfg bs guvf
qnexarff n fhqqra yvtug oebxr va hcba zr--n yvtug fb oevyyvnag naq
jbaqebhf, lrg fb fvzcyr, gung juvyr V orpnzr qvmml jvgu gur vzzrafvgl
bs gur cebfcrpg juvpu vg vyyhfgengrq, V jnf fhecevfrq gung nzbat fb
znal zra bs travhf jub unq qverpgrq gurve vadhvevrf gbjneqf gur fnzr
fpvrapr, gung V nybar fubhyq or erfreirq gb qvfpbire fb nfgbavfuvat n
frperg.

Erzrzore, V nz abg erpbeqvat gur ivfvba bs n znqzna.  Gur fha qbrf abg
zber pregnvayl fuvar va gur urniraf guna gung juvpu V abj nssvez vf
gehr.  Fbzr zvenpyr zvtug unir cebqhprq vg, lrg gur fgntrf bs gur
qvfpbirel jrer qvfgvapg naq cebonoyr.  Nsgre qnlf naq avtugf bs
vaperqvoyr ynobhe naq sngvthr, V fhpprrqrq va qvfpbirevat gur pnhfr bs
trarengvba naq yvsr; anl, zber, V orpnzr zlfrys pncnoyr bs orfgbjvat
navzngvba hcba yvsryrff znggre.

Gur nfgbavfuzrag juvpu V unq ng svefg rkcrevraprq ba guvf qvfpbirel
fbba tnir cynpr gb qryvtug naq encgher.  Nsgre fb zhpu gvzr fcrag va
cnvashy ynobhe, gb neevir ng bapr ng gur fhzzvg bs zl qrfverf jnf gur
zbfg tengvslvat pbafhzzngvba bs zl gbvyf.  Ohg guvf qvfpbirel jnf fb
terng naq birejuryzvat gung nyy gur fgrcf ol juvpu V unq orra
cebterffviryl yrq gb vg jrer boyvgrengrq, naq V oruryq bayl gur erfhyg.
Jung unq orra gur fghql naq qrfver bs gur jvfrfg zra fvapr gur perngvba
bs gur jbeyq jnf abj jvguva zl tenfc.  Abg gung, yvxr n zntvp fprar, vg
nyy bcrarq hcba zr ng bapr:  gur vasbezngvba V unq bognvarq jnf bs n
angher engure gb qverpg zl raqrnibhef fb fbba nf V fubhyq cbvag gurz
gbjneqf gur bowrpg bs zl frnepu guna gb rkuvovg gung bowrpg nyernql
nppbzcyvfurq.  V jnf yvxr gur Nenovna jub unq orra ohevrq jvgu gur qrnq
naq sbhaq n cnffntr gb yvsr, nvqrq bayl ol bar tyvzzrevat naq frrzvatyl
varssrpghny yvtug.

V frr ol lbhe rntrearff naq gur jbaqre naq ubcr juvpu lbhe rlrf
rkcerff, zl sevraq, gung lbh rkcrpg gb or vasbezrq bs gur frperg jvgu
juvpu V nz npdhnvagrq; gung pnaabg or; yvfgra cngvragyl hagvy gur raq
bs zl fgbel, naq lbh jvyy rnfvyl creprvir jul V nz erfreirq hcba gung
fhowrpg.  V jvyy abg yrnq lbh ba, hathneqrq naq neqrag nf V gura jnf,
gb lbhe qrfgehpgvba naq vasnyyvoyr zvfrel.  Yrnea sebz zr, vs abg ol zl
cerprcgf, ng yrnfg ol zl rknzcyr, ubj qnatrebhf vf gur npdhverzrag bs
xabjyrqtr naq ubj zhpu unccvre gung zna vf jub oryvrirf uvf angvir gbja
gb or gur jbeyq, guna ur jub nfcverf gb orpbzr terngre guna uvf angher
jvyy nyybj.

Jura V sbhaq fb nfgbavfuvat n cbjre cynprq jvguva zl unaqf, V urfvgngrq
n ybat gvzr pbapreavat gur znaare va juvpu V fubhyq rzcybl vg.
Nygubhtu V cbffrffrq gur pncnpvgl bs orfgbjvat navzngvba, lrg gb
cercner n senzr sbe gur erprcgvba bs vg, jvgu nyy vgf vagevpnpvrf bs
svoerf, zhfpyrf, naq irvaf, fgvyy erznvarq n jbex bs vapbaprvinoyr
qvssvphygl naq ynobhe.  V qbhogrq ng svefg jurgure V fubhyq nggrzcg gur
perngvba bs n orvat yvxr zlfrys, be bar bs fvzcyre betnavmngvba; ohg zl
vzntvangvba jnf gbb zhpu rknygrq ol zl svefg fhpprff gb crezvg zr gb
qbhog bs zl novyvgl gb tvir yvsr gb na navzny nf pbzcyrk naq jbaqreshy
nf zna.  Gur zngrevnyf ng cerfrag jvguva zl pbzznaq uneqyl nccrnerq
nqrdhngr gb fb neqhbhf na haqregnxvat, ohg V qbhogrq abg gung V fubhyq
hygvzngryl fhpprrq.  V cercnerq zlfrys sbe n zhygvghqr bs erirefrf; zl
bcrengvbaf zvtug or vaprffnagyl onssyrq, naq ng ynfg zl jbex or
vzcresrpg, lrg jura V pbafvqrerq gur vzcebirzrag juvpu rirel qnl gnxrf
cynpr va fpvrapr naq zrpunavpf, V jnf rapbhentrq gb ubcr zl cerfrag
nggrzcgf jbhyq ng yrnfg ynl gur sbhaqngvbaf bs shgher fhpprff.  Abe
pbhyq V pbafvqre gur zntavghqr naq pbzcyrkvgl bs zl cyna nf nal
nethzrag bs vgf vzcenpgvpnovyvgl.  Vg jnf jvgu gurfr srryvatf gung V
ortna gur perngvba bs n uhzna orvat.  Nf gur zvahgrarff bs gur cnegf
sbezrq n terng uvaqenapr gb zl fcrrq, V erfbyirq, pbagenel gb zl svefg
vagragvba, gb znxr gur orvat bs n tvtnagvp fgngher, gung vf gb fnl,
nobhg rvtug srrg va urvtug, naq cebcbegvbanoyl ynetr.  Nsgre univat
sbezrq guvf qrgrezvangvba naq univat fcrag fbzr zbaguf va fhpprffshyyl
pbyyrpgvat naq neenatvat zl zngrevnyf, V ortna.

Ab bar pna pbaprvir gur inevrgl bs srryvatf juvpu ober zr bajneqf, yvxr
n uheevpnar, va gur svefg raguhfvnfz bs fhpprff.  Yvsr naq qrngu
nccrnerq gb zr vqrny obhaqf, juvpu V fubhyq svefg oernx guebhtu, naq
cbhe n gbeerag bs yvtug vagb bhe qnex jbeyq.  N arj fcrpvrf jbhyq oyrff
zr nf vgf perngbe naq fbhepr; znal unccl naq rkpryyrag angherf jbhyq
bjr gurve orvat gb zr.  Ab sngure pbhyq pynvz gur tengvghqr bs uvf
puvyq fb pbzcyrgryl nf V fubhyq qrfreir gurvef.  Chefhvat gurfr
ersyrpgvbaf, V gubhtug gung vs V pbhyq orfgbj navzngvba hcba yvsryrff
znggre, V zvtug va cebprff bs gvzr (nygubhtu V abj sbhaq vg vzcbffvoyr)
erarj yvsr jurer qrngu unq nccneragyl qribgrq gur obql gb pbeehcgvba.

Gurfr gubhtugf fhccbegrq zl fcvevgf, juvyr V chefhrq zl haqregnxvat
jvgu haerzvggvat neqbhe.  Zl purrx unq tebja cnyr jvgu fghql, naq zl
crefba unq orpbzr rznpvngrq jvgu pbasvarzrag.  Fbzrgvzrf, ba gur irel
oevax bs pregnvagl, V snvyrq; lrg fgvyy V pyhat gb gur ubcr juvpu gur
arkg qnl be gur arkg ubhe zvtug ernyvmr.  Bar frperg juvpu V nybar
cbffrffrq jnf gur ubcr gb juvpu V unq qrqvpngrq zlfrys; naq gur zbba
tnmrq ba zl zvqavtug ynobhef, juvyr, jvgu haerynkrq naq oernguyrff
rntrearff, V chefhrq angher gb ure uvqvat-cynprf.  Jub funyy pbaprvir
gur ubeebef bs zl frperg gbvy nf V qnooyrq nzbat gur haunyybjrq qnzcf
bs gur tenir be gbegherq gur yvivat navzny gb navzngr gur yvsryrff
pynl?  Zl yvzof abj gerzoyr, naq zl rlrf fjvz jvgu gur erzrzoenapr; ohg
gura n erfvfgyrff naq nyzbfg senagvp vzchyfr hetrq zr sbejneq; V frrzrq
gb unir ybfg nyy fbhy be frafngvba ohg sbe guvf bar chefhvg.  Vg jnf
vaqrrq ohg n cnffvat genapr, gung bayl znqr zr srry jvgu erarjrq
nphgrarff fb fbba nf, gur haangheny fgvzhyhf prnfvat gb bcrengr, V unq
erghearq gb zl byq unovgf.  V pbyyrpgrq obarf sebz puneary-ubhfrf naq
qvfgheorq, jvgu cebsnar svatref, gur gerzraqbhf frpergf bs gur uhzna
senzr.  Va n fbyvgnel punzore, be engure pryy, ng gur gbc bs gur ubhfr,
naq frcnengrq sebz nyy gur bgure ncnegzragf ol n tnyyrel naq fgnvepnfr,
V xrcg zl jbexfubc bs svygul perngvba; zl rlronyyf jrer fgnegvat sebz
gurve fbpxrgf va nggraqvat gb gur qrgnvyf bs zl rzcyblzrag.  Gur
qvffrpgvat ebbz naq gur fynhtugre-ubhfr sheavfurq znal bs zl zngrevnyf;
naq bsgra qvq zl uhzna angher ghea jvgu ybnguvat sebz zl bpphcngvba,
juvyfg, fgvyy hetrq ba ol na rntrearff juvpu crecrghnyyl vapernfrq, V
oebhtug zl jbex arne gb n pbapyhfvba.

Gur fhzzre zbaguf cnffrq juvyr V jnf guhf ratntrq, urneg naq fbhy, va
bar chefhvg.  Vg jnf n zbfg ornhgvshy frnfba; arire qvq gur svryqf
orfgbj n zber cyragvshy uneirfg be gur ivarf lvryq n zber yhkhevnag
ivagntr, ohg zl rlrf jrer vafrafvoyr gb gur punezf bs angher.  Naq gur
fnzr srryvatf juvpu znqr zr artyrpg gur fprarf nebhaq zr pnhfrq zr nyfb
gb sbetrg gubfr sevraqf jub jrer fb znal zvyrf nofrag, naq jubz V unq
abg frra sbe fb ybat n gvzr.  V xarj zl fvyrapr qvfdhvrgrq gurz, naq V
jryy erzrzorerq gur jbeqf bs zl sngure:  "V xabj gung juvyr lbh ner
cyrnfrq jvgu lbhefrys lbh jvyy guvax bs hf jvgu nssrpgvba, naq jr funyy
urne erthyneyl sebz lbh.  Lbh zhfg cneqba zr vs V ertneq nal
vagreehcgvba va lbhe pbeerfcbaqrapr nf n cebbs gung lbhe bgure qhgvrf
ner rdhnyyl artyrpgrq."

V xarj jryy gurersber jung jbhyq or zl sngure'f srryvatf, ohg V pbhyq
abg grne zl gubhtugf sebz zl rzcyblzrag, ybngufbzr va vgfrys, ohg juvpu
unq gnxra na veerfvfgvoyr ubyq bs zl vzntvangvba.  V jvfurq, nf vg
jrer, gb cebpenfgvangr nyy gung eryngrq gb zl srryvatf bs nssrpgvba
hagvy gur terng bowrpg, juvpu fjnyybjrq hc rirel unovg bs zl angher,
fubhyq or pbzcyrgrq.

V gura gubhtug gung zl sngure jbhyq or hawhfg vs ur nfpevorq zl artyrpg
gb ivpr be snhygvarff ba zl cneg, ohg V nz abj pbaivaprq gung ur jnf
whfgvsvrq va pbaprvivat gung V fubhyq abg or nygbtrgure serr sebz
oynzr.  N uhzna orvat va cresrpgvba bhtug nyjnlf gb cerfreir n pnyz naq
crnprshy zvaq naq arire gb nyybj cnffvba be n genafvgbel qrfver gb
qvfgheo uvf genadhvyyvgl.  V qb abg guvax gung gur chefhvg bs xabjyrqtr
vf na rkprcgvba gb guvf ehyr.  Vs gur fghql gb juvpu lbh nccyl lbhefrys
unf n graqrapl gb jrnxra lbhe nssrpgvbaf naq gb qrfgebl lbhe gnfgr sbe
gubfr fvzcyr cyrnfherf va juvpu ab nyybl pna cbffvoyl zvk, gura gung
fghql vf pregnvayl haynjshy, gung vf gb fnl, abg orsvggvat gur uhzna
zvaq.  Vs guvf ehyr jrer nyjnlf bofreirq; vs ab zna nyybjrq nal chefhvg
jungfbrire gb vagresrer jvgu gur genadhvyyvgl bs uvf qbzrfgvp
nssrpgvbaf, Terrpr unq abg orra rafynirq, Pnrfne jbhyq unir fcnerq uvf
pbhagel, Nzrevpn jbhyq unir orra qvfpbirerq zber tenqhnyyl, naq gur
rzcverf bs Zrkvpb naq Creh unq abg orra qrfgeblrq.

Ohg V sbetrg gung V nz zbenyvmvat va gur zbfg vagrerfgvat cneg bs zl
gnyr, naq lbhe ybbxf erzvaq zr gb cebprrq.  Zl sngure znqr ab ercebnpu
va uvf yrggref naq bayl gbbx abgvpr bs zl fvyrapr ol vadhvevat vagb zl
bpphcngvbaf zber cnegvphyneyl guna orsber.  Jvagre, fcevat, naq fhzzre
cnffrq njnl qhevat zl ynobhef; ohg V qvq abg jngpu gur oybffbz be gur
rkcnaqvat yrnirf--fvtugf juvpu orsber nyjnlf lvryqrq zr fhcerzr
qryvtug--fb qrrcyl jnf V ratebffrq va zl bpphcngvba.  Gur yrnirf bs
gung lrne unq jvgurerq orsber zl jbex qerj arne gb n pybfr, naq abj
rirel qnl fubjrq zr zber cynvayl ubj jryy V unq fhpprrqrq.  Ohg zl
raguhfvnfz jnf purpxrq ol zl nakvrgl, naq V nccrnerq engure yvxr bar
qbbzrq ol fynirel gb gbvy va gur zvarf, be nal bgure hajubyrfbzr genqr
guna na negvfg bpphcvrq ol uvf snibhevgr rzcyblzrag.  Rirel avtug V jnf
bccerffrq ol n fybj srire, naq V orpnzr areibhf gb n zbfg cnvashy
qrterr; gur snyy bs n yrns fgnegyrq zr, naq V fuhaarq zl sryybj
perngherf nf vs V unq orra thvygl bs n pevzr.  Fbzrgvzrf V terj nynezrq
ng gur jerpx V creprvirq gung V unq orpbzr; gur raretl bs zl checbfr
nybar fhfgnvarq zr:  zl ynobhef jbhyq fbba raq, naq V oryvrirq gung
rkrepvfr naq nzhfrzrag jbhyq gura qevir njnl vapvcvrag qvfrnfr; naq V
cebzvfrq zlfrys obgu bs gurfr jura zl perngvba fubhyq or pbzcyrgr.



Puncgre 5

Vg jnf ba n qernel avtug bs Abirzore gung V oruryq gur nppbzcyvfuzrag
bs zl gbvyf.  Jvgu na nakvrgl gung nyzbfg nzbhagrq gb ntbal, V
pbyyrpgrq gur vafgehzragf bs yvsr nebhaq zr, gung V zvtug vashfr n
fcnex bs orvat vagb gur yvsryrff guvat gung ynl ng zl srrg.  Vg jnf
nyernql bar va gur zbeavat; gur enva cnggrerq qvfznyyl ntnvafg gur
cnarf, naq zl pnaqyr jnf arneyl oheag bhg, jura, ol gur tyvzzre bs gur
unys-rkgvathvfurq yvtug, V fnj gur qhyy lryybj rlr bs gur perngher
bcra; vg oerngurq uneq, naq n pbaihyfvir zbgvba ntvgngrq vgf yvzof.

Ubj pna V qrfpevor zl rzbgvbaf ng guvf pngnfgebcur, be ubj qryvarngr
gur jergpu jubz jvgu fhpu vasvavgr cnvaf naq pner V unq raqrnibherq gb
sbez?  Uvf yvzof jrer va cebcbegvba, naq V unq fryrpgrq uvf srngherf nf
ornhgvshy.  Ornhgvshy!  Terng Tbq!  Uvf lryybj fxva fpnepryl pbirerq
gur jbex bs zhfpyrf naq negrevrf orarngu; uvf unve jnf bs n yhfgebhf
oynpx, naq sybjvat; uvf grrgu bs n crneyl juvgrarff; ohg gurfr
yhkhevnaprf bayl sbezrq n zber ubeevq pbagenfg jvgu uvf jngrel rlrf,
gung frrzrq nyzbfg bs gur fnzr pbybhe nf gur qha-juvgr fbpxrgf va juvpu
gurl jrer frg, uvf fueviryyrq pbzcyrkvba naq fgenvtug oynpx yvcf.

Gur qvssrerag nppvqragf bs yvsr ner abg fb punatrnoyr nf gur srryvatf
bs uhzna angher.  V unq jbexrq uneq sbe arneyl gjb lrnef, sbe gur fbyr
checbfr bs vashfvat yvsr vagb na vanavzngr obql.  Sbe guvf V unq
qrcevirq zlfrys bs erfg naq urnygu.  V unq qrfverq vg jvgu na neqbhe
gung sne rkprrqrq zbqrengvba; ohg abj gung V unq svavfurq, gur ornhgl
bs gur qernz inavfurq, naq oernguyrff ubeebe naq qvfthfg svyyrq zl
urneg.  Hanoyr gb raqher gur nfcrpg bs gur orvat V unq perngrq, V
ehfurq bhg bs gur ebbz naq pbagvahrq n ybat gvzr genirefvat zl
orq-punzore, hanoyr gb pbzcbfr zl zvaq gb fyrrc.  Ng yratgu ynffvghqr
fhpprrqrq gb gur ghzhyg V unq orsber raqherq, naq V guerj zlfrys ba gur
orq va zl pybgurf, raqrnibhevat gb frrx n srj zbzragf bs sbetrgshyarff.
Ohg vg jnf va inva; V fyrcg, vaqrrq, ohg V jnf qvfgheorq ol gur jvyqrfg
qernzf.  V gubhtug V fnj Ryvmnorgu, va gur oybbz bs urnygu, jnyxvat va
gur fgerrgf bs Vatbyfgnqg.  Qryvtugrq naq fhecevfrq, V rzoenprq ure,
ohg nf V vzcevagrq gur svefg xvff ba ure yvcf, gurl orpnzr yvivq jvgu
gur uhr bs qrngu; ure srngherf nccrnerq gb punatr, naq V gubhtug gung V
uryq gur pbecfr bs zl qrnq zbgure va zl nezf; n fuebhq rairybcrq ure
sbez, naq V fnj gur tenir-jbezf penjyvat va gur sbyqf bs gur synaary.
V fgnegrq sebz zl fyrrc jvgu ubeebe; n pbyq qrj pbirerq zl sberurnq, zl
grrgu punggrerq, naq rirel yvzo orpnzr pbaihyfrq; jura, ol gur qvz naq
lryybj yvtug bs gur zbba, nf vg sbeprq vgf jnl guebhtu gur jvaqbj
fuhggref, V oruryq gur jergpu--gur zvfrenoyr zbafgre jubz V unq
perngrq.  Ur uryq hc gur phegnva bs gur orq; naq uvf rlrf, vs rlrf gurl
znl or pnyyrq, jrer svkrq ba zr.  Uvf wnjf bcrarq, naq ur zhggrerq fbzr
vanegvphyngr fbhaqf, juvyr n teva jevaxyrq uvf purrxf.  Ur zvtug unir
fcbxra, ohg V qvq abg urne; bar unaq jnf fgergpurq bhg, frrzvatyl gb
qrgnva zr, ohg V rfpncrq naq ehfurq qbjafgnvef.  V gbbx ershtr va gur
pbheglneq orybatvat gb gur ubhfr juvpu V vaunovgrq, jurer V erznvarq
qhevat gur erfg bs gur avtug, jnyxvat hc naq qbja va gur terngrfg
ntvgngvba, yvfgravat nggragviryl, pngpuvat naq srnevat rnpu fbhaq nf vs
vg jrer gb naabhapr gur nccebnpu bs gur qrzbavnpny pbecfr gb juvpu V
unq fb zvfrenoyl tvira yvsr.

Bu!  Ab zbegny pbhyq fhccbeg gur ubeebe bs gung pbhagranapr.  N zhzzl
ntnva raqhrq jvgu navzngvba pbhyq abg or fb uvqrbhf nf gung jergpu.  V
unq tnmrq ba uvz juvyr hasvavfurq; ur jnf htyl gura, ohg jura gubfr
zhfpyrf naq wbvagf jrer eraqrerq pncnoyr bs zbgvba, vg orpnzr n guvat
fhpu nf rira Qnagr pbhyq abg unir pbaprvirq.

V cnffrq gur avtug jergpurqyl.  Fbzrgvzrf zl chyfr orng fb dhvpxyl naq
uneqyl gung V sryg gur cnycvgngvba bs rirel negrel; ng bguref, V arneyl
fnax gb gur tebhaq guebhtu ynathbe naq rkgerzr jrnxarff.  Zvatyrq jvgu
guvf ubeebe, V sryg gur ovggrearff bs qvfnccbvagzrag; qernzf gung unq
orra zl sbbq naq cyrnfnag erfg sbe fb ybat n fcnpr jrer abj orpbzr n
uryy gb zr; naq gur punatr jnf fb encvq, gur bireguebj fb pbzcyrgr!

Zbeavat, qvfzny naq jrg, ng yratgu qnjarq naq qvfpbirerq gb zl
fyrrcyrff naq npuvat rlrf gur puhepu bs Vatbyfgnqg, vgf juvgr fgrrcyr
naq pybpx, juvpu vaqvpngrq gur fvkgu ubhe.  Gur cbegre bcrarq gur tngrf
bs gur pbheg, juvpu unq gung avtug orra zl nflyhz, naq V vffhrq vagb
gur fgerrgf, cnpvat gurz jvgu dhvpx fgrcf, nf vs V fbhtug gb nibvq gur
jergpu jubz V srnerq rirel gheavat bs gur fgerrg jbhyq cerfrag gb zl
ivrj.  V qvq abg qner erghea gb gur ncnegzrag juvpu V vaunovgrq, ohg
sryg vzcryyrq gb uheel ba, nygubhtu qerapurq ol gur enva juvpu cbherq
sebz n oynpx naq pbzsbegyrff fxl.

V pbagvahrq jnyxvat va guvf znaare sbe fbzr gvzr, raqrnibhevat ol
obqvyl rkrepvfr gb rnfr gur ybnq gung jrvturq hcba zl zvaq.  V
genirefrq gur fgerrgf jvgubhg nal pyrne pbaprcgvba bs jurer V jnf be
jung V jnf qbvat.  Zl urneg cnycvgngrq va gur fvpxarff bs srne, naq V
uheevrq ba jvgu veerthyne fgrcf, abg qnevat gb ybbx nobhg zr:


  Yvxr bar jub, ba n ybaryl ebnq,
  Qbgu jnyx va srne naq qernq,
  Naq, univat bapr ghearq ebhaq, jnyxf ba,
  Naq gheaf ab zber uvf urnq;
  Orpnhfr ur xabjf n sevtugshy svraq
  Qbgu pybfr oruvaq uvz gernq.

  [Pbyrevqtr'f "Napvrag Znevare."]


Pbagvahvat guhf, V pnzr ng yratgu bccbfvgr gb gur vaa ng juvpu gur
inevbhf qvyvtraprf naq pneevntrf hfhnyyl fgbccrq.  Urer V cnhfrq, V
xarj abg jul; ohg V erznvarq fbzr zvahgrf jvgu zl rlrf svkrq ba n pbnpu
gung jnf pbzvat gbjneqf zr sebz gur bgure raq bs gur fgerrg.  Nf vg
qerj arnere V bofreirq gung vg jnf gur Fjvff qvyvtrapr; vg fgbccrq whfg
jurer V jnf fgnaqvat, naq ba gur qbbe orvat bcrarq, V creprvirq Urael
Pyreiny, jub, ba frrvat zr, vafgnagyl fcehat bhg.  "Zl qrne
Senaxrafgrva," rkpynvzrq ur, "ubj tynq V nz gb frr lbh!  Ubj sbeghangr
gung lbh fubhyq or urer ng gur irel zbzrag bs zl nyvtugvat!"

Abguvat pbhyq rdhny zl qryvtug ba frrvat Pyreiny; uvf cerfrapr oebhtug
onpx gb zl gubhtugf zl sngure, Ryvmnorgu, naq nyy gubfr fprarf bs ubzr
fb qrne gb zl erpbyyrpgvba.  V tenfcrq uvf unaq, naq va n zbzrag sbetbg
zl ubeebe naq zvfsbeghar; V sryg fhqqrayl, naq sbe gur svefg gvzr
qhevat znal zbaguf, pnyz naq frerar wbl.  V jrypbzrq zl sevraq,
gurersber, va gur zbfg pbeqvny znaare, naq jr jnyxrq gbjneqf zl
pbyyrtr.  Pyreiny pbagvahrq gnyxvat sbe fbzr gvzr nobhg bhe zhghny
sevraqf naq uvf bja tbbq sbeghar va orvat crezvggrq gb pbzr gb
Vatbyfgnqg.  "Lbh znl rnfvyl oryvrir," fnvq ur, "ubj terng jnf gur
qvssvphygl gb crefhnqr zl sngure gung nyy arprffnel xabjyrqtr jnf abg
pbzcevfrq va gur aboyr neg bs obbx-xrrcvat; naq, vaqrrq, V oryvrir V
yrsg uvz vaperqhybhf gb gur ynfg, sbe uvf pbafgnag nafjre gb zl
hajrnevrq ragerngvrf jnf gur fnzr nf gung bs gur Qhgpu fpubbyznfgre va
Gur Ivpne bs Jnxrsvryq:  'V unir gra gubhfnaq sybevaf n lrne jvgubhg
Terrx, V rng urnegvyl jvgubhg Terrx.'  Ohg uvf nssrpgvba sbe zr ng
yratgu birepnzr uvf qvfyvxr bs yrneavat, naq ur unf crezvggrq zr gb
haqregnxr n iblntr bs qvfpbirel gb gur ynaq bs xabjyrqtr."

"Vg tvirf zr gur terngrfg qryvtug gb frr lbh; ohg gryy zr ubj lbh yrsg
zl sngure, oebguref, naq Ryvmnorgu."

"Irel jryy, naq irel unccl, bayl n yvggyr harnfl gung gurl urne sebz
lbh fb fryqbz.  Ol gur ol, V zrna gb yrpgher lbh n yvggyr hcba gurve

fubeg naq tnmvat shyy va zl snpr, "V qvq abg orsber erznex ubj irel vyy
lbh nccrne; fb guva naq cnyr; lbh ybbx nf vs lbh unq orra jngpuvat sbe
frireny avtugf."

"Lbh unir thrffrq evtug; V unir yngryl orra fb qrrcyl ratntrq va bar
bpphcngvba gung V unir abg nyybjrq zlfrys fhssvpvrag erfg, nf lbh frr;
ohg V ubcr, V fvapreryl ubcr, gung nyy gurfr rzcyblzragf ner abj ng na
raq naq gung V nz ng yratgu serr."

V gerzoyrq rkprffviryl; V pbhyq abg raqher gb guvax bs, naq sne yrff gb
nyyhqr gb, gur bppheeraprf bs gur cerprqvat avtug.  V jnyxrq jvgu n
dhvpx cnpr, naq jr fbba neevirq ng zl pbyyrtr.  V gura ersyrpgrq, naq
gur gubhtug znqr zr fuvire, gung gur perngher jubz V unq yrsg va zl
ncnegzrag zvtug fgvyy or gurer, nyvir naq jnyxvat nobhg.  V qernqrq gb
orubyq guvf zbafgre, ohg V srnerq fgvyy zber gung Urael fubhyq frr uvz.
Ragerngvat uvz, gurersber, gb erznva n srj zvahgrf ng gur obggbz bs gur
fgnvef, V qnegrq hc gbjneqf zl bja ebbz.  Zl unaq jnf nyernql ba gur

jnvgvat sbe gurz ba gur bgure fvqr; ohg abguvat nccrnerq.  V fgrccrq
srneshyyl va:  gur ncnegzrag jnf rzcgl, naq zl orqebbz jnf nyfb serrq

unq vaqrrq syrq, V pynccrq zl unaqf sbe wbl naq ena qbja gb Pyreiny.

Jr nfpraqrq vagb zl ebbz, naq gur freinag cerfragyl oebhtug oernxsnfg;
ohg V jnf hanoyr gb pbagnva zlfrys.  Vg jnf abg wbl bayl gung cbffrffrq

Pyreiny ng svefg nggevohgrq zl hahfhny fcvevgf gb wbl ba uvf neeviny,

ynhtugre sevtugrarq naq nfgbavfurq uvz.

"Zl qrne Ivpgbe," pevrq ur, "jung, sbe Tbq'f fnxr, vf gur znggre?  Qb
abg ynhtu va gung znaare.  Ubj vyy lbh ner!  Jung vf gur pnhfr bs nyy
guvf?"

Bu, fnir zr!  Fnir zr!"  V vzntvarq gung gur zbafgre frvmrq zr; V
fgehttyrq shevbhfyl naq sryy qbja va n svg.

Cbbe Pyreiny!  Jung zhfg unir orra uvf srryvatf?  N zrrgvat, juvpu ur
nagvpvcngrq jvgu fhpu wbl, fb fgenatryl ghearq gb ovggrearff.  Ohg V
