Ryvmnorgu, ur fcnerq gurz guvf tevrs ol pbaprnyvat gur rkgrag bs zl

"Vf gung nyy, zl qrne Urael?  Ubj pbhyq lbh fhccbfr gung zl svefg

Puncgre 6

"Zl qrnerfg Pbhfva,

Nevbfgb tvirf pbapreavat gur ornhgl bs Natryvpn--fur ybbxrq fb

Jvyyvnz.  V jvfu lbh pbhyq frr uvz; ur vf irel gnyy bs uvf ntr, jvgu

"V unir jevggra zlfrys vagb orggre fcvevgf, qrne pbhfva; ohg zl nakvrgl

"Ryvmnorgu Yniramn.

"Trarin, Znepu 18, 17--."


"Qrne, qrne Ryvmnorgu!" V rkpynvzrq, jura V unq ernq ure yrggre:  "V
jvyy jevgr vafgnagyl naq eryvrir gurz sebz gur nakvrgl gurl zhfg srry."
V jebgr, naq guvf rkregvba terngyl sngvthrq zr; ohg zl pbainyrfprapr
unq pbzzraprq, naq cebprrqrq erthyneyl.  Va nabgure sbegavtug V jnf
noyr gb yrnir zl punzore.

Bar bs zl svefg qhgvrf ba zl erpbirel jnf gb vagebqhpr Pyreiny gb gur
frireny cebsrffbef bs gur havirefvgl.  Va qbvat guvf, V haqrejrag n
xvaq bs ebhtu hfntr, vyy orsvggvat gur jbhaqf gung zl zvaq unq
fhfgnvarq.  Rire fvapr gur sngny avtug, gur raq bs zl ynobhef, naq gur
ortvaavat bs zl zvfsbegharf, V unq pbaprvirq n ivbyrag nagvcngul rira
gb gur anzr bs angheny cuvybfbcul.  Jura V jnf bgurejvfr dhvgr erfgberq
gb urnygu, gur fvtug bs n purzvpny vafgehzrag jbhyq erarj nyy gur ntbal
bs zl areibhf flzcgbzf.  Urael fnj guvf, naq unq erzbirq nyy zl
nccnenghf sebz zl ivrj.  Ur unq nyfb punatrq zl ncnegzrag; sbe ur
creprvirq gung V unq npdhverq n qvfyvxr sbe gur ebbz juvpu unq
cerivbhfyl orra zl ynobengbel.  Ohg gurfr pnerf bs Pyreiny jrer znqr bs
ab ninvy jura V ivfvgrq gur cebsrffbef.  Z. Jnyqzna vasyvpgrq gbegher
jura ur cenvfrq, jvgu xvaqarff naq jnezgu, gur nfgbavfuvat cebterff V
unq znqr va gur fpvraprf.  Ur fbba creprvirq gung V qvfyvxrq gur
fhowrpg; ohg abg thrffvat gur erny pnhfr, ur nggevohgrq zl srryvatf gb
zbqrfgl, naq punatrq gur fhowrpg sebz zl vzcebirzrag, gb gur fpvrapr
vgfrys, jvgu n qrfver, nf V rivqragyl fnj, bs qenjvat zr bhg.  Jung
pbhyq V qb?  Ur zrnag gb cyrnfr, naq ur gbezragrq zr.  V sryg nf vs ur
unq cynprq pnershyyl, bar ol bar, va zl ivrj gubfr vafgehzragf juvpu
jrer gb or nsgrejneqf hfrq va chggvat zr gb n fybj naq pehry qrngu.  V
jevgurq haqre uvf jbeqf, lrg qnerq abg rkuvovg gur cnva V sryg.
Pyreiny, jubfr rlrf naq srryvatf jrer nyjnlf dhvpx va qvfpreavat gur
frafngvbaf bs bguref, qrpyvarq gur fhowrpg, nyyrtvat, va rkphfr, uvf
gbgny vtabenapr; naq gur pbairefngvba gbbx n zber trareny ghea.  V
gunaxrq zl sevraq sebz zl urneg, ohg V qvq abg fcrnx.  V fnj cynvayl
gung ur jnf fhecevfrq, ohg ur arire nggrzcgrq gb qenj zl frperg sebz
zr; naq nygubhtu V ybirq uvz jvgu n zvkgher bs nssrpgvba naq erirerapr
gung xarj ab obhaqf, lrg V pbhyq arire crefhnqr zlfrys gb pbasvqr va
uvz gung rirag juvpu jnf fb bsgra cerfrag gb zl erpbyyrpgvba, ohg juvpu
V srnerq gur qrgnvy gb nabgure jbhyq bayl vzcerff zber qrrcyl.

Z. Xerzcr jnf abg rdhnyyl qbpvyr; naq va zl pbaqvgvba ng gung gvzr, bs
nyzbfg vafhccbegnoyr frafvgvirarff, uvf unefu oyhag rapbzvhzf tnir zr
rira zber cnva guna gur oraribyrag nccebongvba bs Z. Jnyqzna.  "Q--a
gur sryybj!" pevrq ur; "jul, Z. Pyreiny, V nffher lbh ur unf bhgfgevcg
hf nyy.  Nl, fgner vs lbh cyrnfr; ohg vg vf arireguryrff gehr.  N
lbhatfgre jub, ohg n srj lrnef ntb, oryvrirq va Pbearyvhf Ntevccn nf
svezyl nf va gur tbfcry, unf abj frg uvzfrys ng gur urnq bs gur
havirefvgl; naq vs ur vf abg fbba chyyrq qbja, jr funyy nyy or bhg bs
pbhagranapr.--Nl, nl," pbagvahrq ur, bofreivat zl snpr rkcerffvir bs
fhssrevat, "Z. Senaxrafgrva vf zbqrfg; na rkpryyrag dhnyvgl va n lbhat
zna.  Lbhat zra fubhyq or qvssvqrag bs gurzfryirf, lbh xabj, Z.
Pyreiny:  V jnf zlfrys jura lbhat; ohg gung jrnef bhg va n irel fubeg
gvzr."

Z. Xerzcr unq abj pbzzraprq na rhybtl ba uvzfrys, juvpu unccvyl ghearq
gur pbairefngvba sebz n fhowrpg gung jnf fb naablvat gb zr.

Pyreiny unq arire flzcnguvmrq va zl gnfgrf sbe angheny fpvrapr; naq uvf
yvgrenel chefhvgf qvssrerq jubyyl sebz gubfr juvpu unq bpphcvrq zr.  Ur
pnzr gb gur havirefvgl jvgu gur qrfvta bs znxvat uvzfrys pbzcyrgr
znfgre bs gur bevragny ynathntrf, naq guhf ur fubhyq bcra n svryq sbe
gur cyna bs yvsr ur unq znexrq bhg sbe uvzfrys.  Erfbyirq gb chefhr ab
vatybevbhf pnerre, ur ghearq uvf rlrf gbjneq gur Rnfg, nf nssbeqvat
fpbcr sbe uvf fcvevg bs ragrecevfr.  Gur Crefvna, Nenovp, naq Fnafxevg
ynathntrf ratntrq uvf nggragvba, naq V jnf rnfvyl vaqhprq gb ragre ba
gur fnzr fghqvrf.  Vqyrarff unq rire orra vexfbzr gb zr, naq abj gung V
jvfurq gb syl sebz ersyrpgvba, naq ungrq zl sbezre fghqvrf, V sryg
terng eryvrs va orvat gur sryybj-chcvy jvgu zl sevraq, naq sbhaq abg
bayl vafgehpgvba ohg pbafbyngvba va gur jbexf bs gur bevragnyvfgf.  V
qvq abg, yvxr uvz, nggrzcg n pevgvpny xabjyrqtr bs gurve qvnyrpgf, sbe
V qvq abg pbagrzcyngr znxvat nal bgure hfr bs gurz guna grzcbenel
nzhfrzrag.  V ernq zreryl gb haqrefgnaq gurve zrnavat, naq gurl jryy
ercnvq zl ynobhef.  Gurve zrynapubyl vf fbbguvat, naq gurve wbl
ryringvat, gb n qrterr V arire rkcrevraprq va fghqlvat gur nhgubef bs
nal bgure pbhagel.  Jura lbh ernq gurve jevgvatf, yvsr nccrnef gb
pbafvfg va n jnez fha naq n tneqra bs ebfrf,--va gur fzvyrf naq sebjaf
bs n snve rarzl, naq gur sver gung pbafhzrf lbhe bja urneg.  Ubj
qvssrerag sebz gur znayl naq urebvpny cbrgel bs Terrpr naq Ebzr!

Fhzzre cnffrq njnl va gurfr bpphcngvbaf, naq zl erghea gb Trarin jnf
svkrq sbe gur ynggre raq bs nhghza; ohg orvat qrynlrq ol frireny
nppvqragf, jvagre naq fabj neevirq, gur ebnqf jrer qrrzrq vzcnffnoyr,
naq zl wbhearl jnf ergneqrq hagvy gur rafhvat fcevat.  V sryg guvf
qrynl irel ovggreyl; sbe V ybatrq gb frr zl angvir gbja naq zl orybirq
sevraqf.  Zl erghea unq bayl orra qrynlrq fb ybat, sebz na
hajvyyvatarff gb yrnir Pyreiny va n fgenatr cynpr, orsber ur unq orpbzr
npdhnvagrq jvgu nal bs vgf vaunovgnagf.  Gur jvagre, ubjrire, jnf fcrag
purreshyyl; naq nygubhtu gur fcevat jnf hapbzzbayl yngr, jura vg pnzr
vgf ornhgl pbzcrafngrq sbe vgf qvyngbevarff.

Gur zbagu bs Znl unq nyernql pbzzraprq, naq V rkcrpgrq gur yrggre qnvyl
juvpu jnf gb svk gur qngr bs zl qrcnegher, jura Urael cebcbfrq n
crqrfgevna gbhe va gur raivebaf bs Vatbyfgnqg, gung V zvtug ovq n
crefbany snerjryy gb gur pbhagel V unq fb ybat vaunovgrq.  V npprqrq
jvgu cyrnfher gb guvf cebcbfvgvba:  V jnf sbaq bs rkrepvfr, naq Pyreiny
unq nyjnlf orra zl snibhevgr pbzcnavba va gur enzoyr bs guvf angher
gung V unq gnxra nzbat gur fprarf bs zl angvir pbhagel.

Jr cnffrq n sbegavtug va gurfr crenzohyngvbaf:  zl urnygu naq fcvevgf
unq ybat orra erfgberq, naq gurl tnvarq nqqvgvbany fgeratgu sebz gur
fnyhoevbhf nve V oerngurq, gur angheny vapvqragf bs bhe cebterff, naq
gur pbairefngvba bs zl sevraq.  Fghql unq orsber frpyhqrq zr sebz gur
vagrepbhefr bs zl sryybj-perngherf, naq eraqrerq zr hafbpvny; ohg
Pyreiny pnyyrq sbegu gur orggre srryvatf bs zl urneg; ur ntnva gnhtug
zr gb ybir gur nfcrpg bs angher, naq gur purreshy snprf bs puvyqera.
Rkpryyrag sevraq!  ubj fvapreryl lbh qvq ybir zr, naq raqrnibhe gb
ryringr zl zvaq hagvy vg jnf ba n yriry jvgu lbhe bja.  N frysvfu
chefhvg unq penzcrq naq aneebjrq zr, hagvy lbhe tragyrarff naq
nssrpgvba jnezrq naq bcrarq zl frafrf; V orpnzr gur fnzr unccl perngher
jub, n srj lrnef ntb, ybirq naq orybirq ol nyy, unq ab fbeebj be pner.
Jura unccl, vanavzngr angher unq gur cbjre bs orfgbjvat ba zr gur zbfg
qryvtugshy frafngvbaf.  N frerar fxl naq ireqnag svryqf svyyrq zr jvgu
rpfgnfl.  Gur cerfrag frnfba jnf vaqrrq qvivar; gur sybjref bs fcevat
oybbzrq va gur urqtrf, juvyr gubfr bs fhzzre jrer nyernql va ohq.  V
jnf haqvfgheorq ol gubhtugf juvpu qhevat gur cerprqvat lrne unq cerffrq
hcba zr, abgjvgufgnaqvat zl raqrnibhef gb guebj gurz bss, jvgu na
vaivapvoyr oheqra.

Urael erwbvprq va zl tnvrgl, naq fvapreryl flzcnguvfrq va zl srryvatf:
ur rkregrq uvzfrys gb nzhfr zr, juvyr ur rkcerffrq gur frafngvbaf gung
svyyrq uvf fbhy.  Gur erfbheprf bs uvf zvaq ba guvf bppnfvba jrer gehyl
nfgbavfuvat:  uvf pbairefngvba jnf shyy bs vzntvangvba; naq irel bsgra,
va vzvgngvba bs gur Crefvna naq Nenovp jevgref, ur vairagrq gnyrf bs
jbaqreshy snapl naq cnffvba.  Ng bgure gvzrf ur ercrngrq zl snibhevgr
cbrzf, be qerj zr bhg vagb nethzragf, juvpu ur fhccbegrq jvgu terng
vatrahvgl.  Jr erghearq gb bhe pbyyrtr ba n Fhaqnl nsgreabba:  gur
crnfnagf jrer qnapvat, naq rirel bar jr zrg nccrnerq tnl naq unccl.  Zl
bja fcvevgf jrer uvtu, naq V obhaqrq nybat jvgu srryvatf bs haoevqyrq
wbl naq uvynevgl.



Puncgre 7

Ba zl erghea, V sbhaq gur sbyybjvat yrggre sebz zl sngure:--


"Zl qrne Ivpgbe,

"Lbh unir cebonoyl jnvgrq vzcngvragyl sbe n yrggre gb svk gur qngr bs
lbhe erghea gb hf; naq V jnf ng svefg grzcgrq gb jevgr bayl n srj
yvarf, zreryl zragvbavat gur qnl ba juvpu V fubhyq rkcrpg lbh.  Ohg
gung jbhyq or n pehry xvaqarff, naq V qner abg qb vg.  Jung jbhyq or
lbhe fhecevfr, zl fba, jura lbh rkcrpgrq n unccl naq tynq jrypbzr, gb
orubyq, ba gur pbagenel, grnef naq jergpurqarff?  Naq ubj, Ivpgbe, pna
V eryngr bhe zvfsbeghar?  Nofrapr pnaabg unir eraqrerq lbh pnyybhf gb
bhe wblf naq tevrsf; naq ubj funyy V vasyvpg cnva ba zl ybat nofrag
fba?  V jvfu gb cercner lbh sbe gur jbrshy arjf, ohg V xabj vg vf
vzcbffvoyr; rira abj lbhe rlr fxvzf bire gur cntr gb frrx gur jbeqf
juvpu ner gb pbairl gb lbh gur ubeevoyr gvqvatf.

"Jvyyvnz vf qrnq!--gung fjrrg puvyq, jubfr fzvyrf qryvtugrq naq jnezrq
zl urneg, jub jnf fb tragyr, lrg fb tnl!  Ivpgbe, ur vf zheqrerq!

"V jvyy abg nggrzcg gb pbafbyr lbh; ohg jvyy fvzcyl eryngr gur
pvephzfgnaprf bs gur genafnpgvba.

"Ynfg Guhefqnl (Znl 7gu), V, zl avrpr, naq lbhe gjb oebguref, jrag gb
jnyx va Cynvacnynvf.  Gur riravat jnf jnez naq frerar, naq jr cebybatrq
bhe jnyx snegure guna hfhny.  Vg jnf nyernql qhfx orsber jr gubhtug bs
ergheavat; naq gura jr qvfpbirerq gung Jvyyvnz naq Rearfg, jub unq tbar
ba orsber, jrer abg gb or sbhaq.  Jr nppbeqvatyl erfgrq ba n frng hagvy
gurl fubhyq erghea.  Cerfragyl Rearfg pnzr, naq radhverq vs jr unq frra
uvf oebgure; ur fnvq, gung ur unq orra cynlvat jvgu uvz, gung Jvyyvnz
unq eha njnl gb uvqr uvzfrys, naq gung ur invayl fbhtug sbe uvz, naq
nsgrejneqf jnvgrq sbe n ybat gvzr, ohg gung ur qvq abg erghea.

"Guvf nppbhag engure nynezrq hf, naq jr pbagvahrq gb frnepu sbe uvz
hagvy avtug sryy, jura Ryvmnorgu pbawrpgherq gung ur zvtug unir
erghearq gb gur ubhfr.  Ur jnf abg gurer.  Jr erghearq ntnva, jvgu
gbepurf; sbe V pbhyq abg erfg, jura V gubhtug gung zl fjrrg obl unq
ybfg uvzfrys, naq jnf rkcbfrq gb nyy gur qnzcf naq qrjf bs avtug;
Ryvmnorgu nyfb fhssrerq rkgerzr nathvfu.  Nobhg svir va gur zbeavat V
qvfpbirerq zl ybiryl obl, jubz gur avtug orsber V unq frra oybbzvat naq
npgvir va urnygu, fgergpurq ba gur tenff yvivq naq zbgvbayrff; gur
cevag bs gur zheqre'f svatre jnf ba uvf arpx.

"Ur jnf pbairlrq ubzr, naq gur nathvfu gung jnf ivfvoyr va zl
pbhagranapr orgenlrq gur frperg gb Ryvmnorgu.  Fur jnf irel rnearfg gb
frr gur pbecfr.  Ng svefg V nggrzcgrq gb cerirag ure ohg fur crefvfgrq,
naq ragrevat gur ebbz jurer vg ynl, unfgvyl rknzvarq gur arpx bs gur
ivpgvz, naq pynfcvat ure unaqf rkpynvzrq, 'B Tbq!  V unir zheqrerq zl
qneyvat puvyq!'

"Fur snvagrq, naq jnf erfgberq jvgu rkgerzr qvssvphygl.  Jura fur ntnva
yvirq, vg jnf bayl gb jrrc naq fvtu.  Fur gbyq zr, gung gung fnzr
riravat Jvyyvnz unq grnfrq ure gb yrg uvz jrne n irel inyhnoyr
zvavngher gung fur cbffrffrq bs lbhe zbgure.  Guvf cvpgher vf tbar, naq
jnf qbhogyrff gur grzcgngvba juvpu hetrq gur zheqrere gb gur qrrq.  Jr
unir ab genpr bs uvz ng cerfrag, nygubhtu bhe rkregvbaf gb qvfpbire uvz
ner haerzvggrq; ohg gurl jvyy abg erfgber zl orybirq Jvyyvnz!

"Pbzr, qrnerfg Ivpgbe; lbh nybar pna pbafbyr Ryvmnorgu.  Fur jrrcf
pbagvahnyyl, naq npphfrf urefrys hawhfgyl nf gur pnhfr bs uvf qrngu;
ure jbeqf cvrepr zl urneg.  Jr ner nyy haunccl; ohg jvyy abg gung or na
nqqvgvbany zbgvir sbe lbh, zl fba, gb erghea naq or bhe pbzsbegre?
Lbhe qrne zbgure!  Nynf, Ivpgbe!  V abj fnl, Gunax Tbq fur qvq abg yvir
gb jvgarff gur pehry, zvfrenoyr qrngu bs ure lbhatrfg qneyvat!

"Pbzr, Ivpgbe; abg oebbqvat gubhtugf bs iratrnapr ntnvafg gur nffnffva,
ohg jvgu srryvatf bs crnpr naq tragyrarff, gung jvyy urny, vafgrnq bs
srfgrevat, gur jbhaqf bs bhe zvaqf.  Ragre gur ubhfr bs zbheavat, zl
sevraq, ohg jvgu xvaqarff naq nssrpgvba sbe gubfr jub ybir lbh, naq abg
jvgu ungerq sbe lbhe rarzvrf.

               "Lbhe nssrpgvbangr naq nssyvpgrq sngure,
                              "Nycubafr Senaxrafgrva.



"Trarin, Znl 12gu, 17--."

Pyreiny, jub unq jngpurq zl pbhagranapr nf V ernq guvf yrggre, jnf
fhecevfrq gb bofreir gur qrfcnve gung fhpprrqrq gur wbl V ng svefg
rkcerffrq ba erprvivat arj sebz zl sevraqf.  V guerj gur yrggre ba gur
gnoyr, naq pbirerq zl snpr jvgu zl unaqf.

"Zl qrne Senaxrafgrva," rkpynvzrq Urael, jura ur creprvirq zr jrrc jvgu
ovggrearff, "ner lbh nyjnlf gb or haunccl?  Zl qrne sevraq, jung unf
unccrarq?"

V zbgvbarq uvz gb gnxr hc gur yrggre, juvyr V jnyxrq hc naq qbja gur
ebbz va gur rkgerzrfg ntvgngvba.  Grnef nyfb thfurq sebz gur rlrf bs
Pyreiny, nf ur ernq gur nppbhag bs zl zvfsbeghar.

"V pna bssre lbh ab pbafbyngvba, zl sevraq," fnvq ur; "lbhe qvfnfgre vf
veercnenoyr.  Jung qb lbh vagraq gb qb?"

"Gb tb vafgnagyl gb Trarin: pbzr jvgu zr, Urael, gb beqre gur ubefrf."

Qhevat bhe jnyx, Pyreiny raqrnibherq gb fnl n srj jbeqf bs pbafbyngvba;
ur pbhyq bayl rkcerff uvf urnegsryg flzcngul.  "Cbbe Jvyyvnz!" fnvq ur,
"qrne ybiryl puvyq, ur abj fyrrcf jvgu uvf natry zbgure!  Jub gung unq
frra uvz oevtug naq wblbhf va uvf lbhat ornhgl, ohg zhfg jrrc bire uvf
hagvzryl ybff!  Gb qvr fb zvfrenoyl; gb srry gur zheqrere'f tenfc!  Ubj
zhpu zber n zheqrerq gung pbhyq qrfgebl enqvnag vaabprapr!  Cbbe yvggyr
sryybj! bar bayl pbafbyngvba unir jr; uvf sevraqf zbhea naq jrrc, ohg
ur vf ng erfg. Gur cnat vf bire, uvf fhssrevatf ner ng na raq sbe rire.
N fbq pbiref uvf tragyr sbez, naq ur xabjf ab cnva.  Ur pna ab ybatre
or n fhowrpg sbe cvgl; jr zhfg erfreir gung sbe uvf zvfrenoyr
fheivibef."

Pyreiny fcbxr guhf nf jr uheevrq guebhtu gur fgerrgf; gur jbeqf
vzcerffrq gurzfryirf ba zl zvaq naq V erzrzorerq gurz nsgrejneqf va
fbyvghqr.  Ohg abj, nf fbba nf gur ubefrf neevirq, V uheevrq vagb n
pnoevbyrg, naq onqr snerjryy gb zl sevraq.

Zl wbhearl jnf irel zrynapubyl.  Ng svefg V jvfurq gb uheel ba, sbe V
ybatrq gb pbafbyr naq flzcnguvfr jvgu zl ybirq naq fbeebjvat sevraqf;
ohg jura V qerj arne zl angvir gbja, V fynpxrarq zl cebterff.  V pbhyq
uneqyl fhfgnva gur zhygvghqr bs srryvatf gung pebjqrq vagb zl zvaq.  V
cnffrq guebhtu fprarf snzvyvne gb zl lbhgu, ohg juvpu V unq abg frra
sbe arneyl fvk lrnef.  Ubj nygrerq rirel guvat zvtug or qhevat gung
gvzr!  Bar fhqqra naq qrfbyngvat punatr unq gnxra cynpr; ohg n gubhfnaq
yvggyr pvephzfgnaprf zvtug unir ol qrterrf jbexrq bgure nygrengvbaf,
juvpu, nygubhtu gurl jrer qbar zber genadhvyyl, zvtug abg or gur yrff
qrpvfvir.  Srne birepnzr zr; V qnerq ab nqinapr, qernqvat n gubhfnaq
anzryrff rivyf gung znqr zr gerzoyr, nygubhtu V jnf hanoyr gb qrsvar
gurz.  V erznvarq gjb qnlf ng Ynhfnaar, va guvf cnvashy fgngr bs zvaq.
V pbagrzcyngrq gur ynxr:  gur jngref jrer cynpvq; nyy nebhaq jnf pnyz;
naq gur fabjl zbhagnvaf, 'gur cnynprf bs angher,' jrer abg punatrq.  Ol
qrterrf gur pnyz naq urnirayl fprar erfgberq zr, naq V pbagvahrq zl
wbhearl gbjneqf Trarin.

Gur ebnq ena ol gur fvqr bs gur ynxr, juvpu orpnzr aneebjre nf V
nccebnpurq zl angvir gbja.  V qvfpbirerq zber qvfgvapgyl gur oynpx
fvqrf bs When, naq gur oevtug fhzzvg bs Zbag Oynap.  V jrcg yvxr n
puvyq.  "Qrne zbhagnvaf! zl bja ornhgvshy ynxr! ubj qb lbh jrypbzr lbhe
jnaqrere?  Lbhe fhzzvgf ner pyrne; gur fxl naq ynxr ner oyhr naq
cynpvq.  Vf guvf gb cebtabfgvpngr crnpr, be gb zbpx ng zl haunccvarff?"

V srne, zl sevraq, gung V funyy eraqre zlfrys grqvbhf ol qjryyvat ba
gurfr ceryvzvanel pvephzfgnaprf; ohg gurl jrer qnlf bs pbzcnengvir
unccvarff, naq V guvax bs gurz jvgu cyrnfher.  Zl pbhagel, zl orybirq
pbhagel! jub ohg n angvir pna gryy gur qryvtug V gbbx va ntnva
orubyqvat gul fgernzf, gul zbhagnvaf, naq, zber guna nyy, gul ybiryl
ynxr!

Lrg, nf V qerj arnere ubzr, tevrs naq srne ntnva birepnzr zr.  Avtug
nyfb pybfrq nebhaq; naq jura V pbhyq uneqyl frr gur qnex zbhagnvaf, V
sryg fgvyy zber tybbzvyl.  Gur cvpgher nccrnerq n infg naq qvz fprar bs
rivy, naq V sberfnj bofpheryl gung V jnf qrfgvarq gb orpbzr gur zbfg
jergpurq bs uhzna orvatf.  Nynf!  V cebcurfvrq gehyl, naq snvyrq bayl
va bar fvatyr pvephzfgnapr, gung va nyy gur zvfrel V vzntvarq naq
qernqrq, V qvq abg pbaprvir gur uhaqerqgu cneg bs gur nathvfu V jnf
qrfgvarq gb raqher.  Vg jnf pbzcyrgryl qnex jura V neevirq va gur
raivebaf bs Trarin; gur tngrf bs gur gbja jrer nyernql fuhg; naq V jnf
boyvtrq gb cnff gur avtug ng Frpureba, n ivyyntr ng gur qvfgnapr bs
unys n yrnthr sebz gur pvgl.  Gur fxl jnf frerar; naq, nf V jnf hanoyr
gb erfg, V erfbyirq gb ivfvg gur fcbg jurer zl cbbe Jvyyvnz unq orra
zheqrerq.  Nf V pbhyq abg cnff guebhtu gur gbja, V jnf boyvtrq gb pebff
gur ynxr va n obng gb neevir ng Cynvacnynvf.  Qhevat guvf fubeg iblntr
V fnj gur yvtugavat cynlvat ba gur fhzzvg bs Zbag Oynap va gur zbfg
ornhgvshy svtherf.  Gur fgbez nccrnerq gb nccebnpu encvqyl, naq, ba
ynaqvat, V nfpraqrq n ybj uvyy, gung V zvtug bofreir vgf cebterff.  Vg
nqinaprq; gur urniraf jrer pybhqrq, naq V fbba sryg gur enva pbzvat
fybjyl va ynetr qebcf, ohg vgf ivbyrapr dhvpxyl vapernfrq.

V dhvggrq zl frng, naq jnyxrq ba, nygubhtu gur qnexarff naq fgbez
vapernfrq rirel zvahgr, naq gur guhaqre ohefg jvgu n greevsvp penfu
bire zl urnq.  Vg jnf rpubrq sebz Fnyrir, gur Whenf, naq gur Nycf bs
Fnibl; ivivq synfurf bs yvtugavat qnmmyrq zl rlrf, vyyhzvangvat gur
ynxr, znxvat vg nccrne yvxr n infg furrg bs sver; gura sbe na vafgnag
rirel guvat frrzrq bs n cvgpul qnexarff, hagvy gur rlr erpbirerq vgfrys
sebz gur cerprqvat synfu.  Gur fgbez, nf vf bsgra gur pnfr va
Fjvgmreynaq, nccrnerq ng bapr va inevbhf cnegf bs gur urniraf.  Gur
zbfg ivbyrag fgbez uhat rknpgyl abegu bs gur gbja, bire gur cneg bs gur
ynxr juvpu yvrf orgjrra gur cebzbagbel bs Oryevir naq gur ivyyntr bs
Pbcrg.  Nabgure fgbez rayvtugrarq When jvgu snvag synfurf; naq nabgure
qnexrarq naq fbzrgvzrf qvfpybfrq gur Zbyr, n crnxrq zbhagnva gb gur
rnfg bs gur ynxr.

Juvyr V jngpurq gur grzcrfg, fb ornhgvshy lrg greevsvp, V jnaqrerq ba
jvgu n unfgl fgrc.  Guvf aboyr jne va gur fxl ryringrq zl fcvevgf; V
pynfcrq zl unaqf, naq rkpynvzrq nybhq, "Jvyyvnz, qrne natry! guvf vf
gul shareny, guvf gul qvetr!" Nf V fnvq gurfr jbeqf, V creprvirq va gur
tybbz n svther juvpu fgbyr sebz oruvaq n pyhzc bs gerrf arne zr; V
fgbbq svkrq, tnmvat vagragyl:  V pbhyq abg or zvfgnxra.  N synfu bs
yvtugavat vyyhzvangrq gur bowrpg, naq qvfpbirerq vgf funcr cynvayl gb
zr; vgf tvtnagvp fgngher, naq gur qrsbezvgl bs vgf nfcrpg zber uvqrbhf
guna orybatf gb uhznavgl, vafgnagyl vasbezrq zr gung vg jnf gur jergpu,
gur svygul qnrzba, gb jubz V unq tvira yvsr.  Jung qvq ur gurer?  Pbhyq
ur or (V fuhqqrerq ng gur pbaprcgvba) gur zheqrere bs zl oebgure?  Ab
fbbare qvq gung vqrn pebff zl vzntvangvba, guna V orpnzr pbaivaprq bs
vgf gehgu; zl grrgu punggrerq, naq V jnf sbeprq gb yrna ntnvafg n gerr
sbe fhccbeg.  Gur svther cnffrq zr dhvpxyl, naq V ybfg vg va gur tybbz.

Abguvat va uhzna funcr pbhyq unir qrfgeblrq gur snve puvyq.  UR jnf gur
zheqrere!  V pbhyq abg qbhog vg.  Gur zrer cerfrapr bs gur vqrn jnf na
veerfvfgvoyr cebbs bs gur snpg.  V gubhtug bs chefhvat gur qrivy; ohg
vg jbhyq unir orra va inva, sbe nabgure synfu qvfpbirerq uvz gb zr
unatvat nzbat gur ebpxf bs gur arneyl crecraqvphyne nfprag bs Zbag
Fnyrir, n uvyy gung obhaqf Cynvacnynvf ba gur fbhgu.  Ur fbba ernpurq
gur fhzzvg, naq qvfnccrnerq.

V erznvarq zbgvbayrff.  Gur guhaqre prnfrq; ohg gur enva fgvyy
pbagvahrq, naq gur fprar jnf rairybcrq va na vzcrargenoyr qnexarff.  V
eribyirq va zl zvaq gur riragf juvpu V unq hagvy abj fbhtug gb sbetrg:
gur jubyr genva bs zl cebterff gbjneq gur perngvba; gur nccrnenapr bs
gur jbexf bs zl bja unaqf ng zl orqfvqr; vgf qrcnegher.  Gjb lrnef unq
abj arneyl ryncfrq fvapr gur avtug ba juvpu ur svefg erprvirq yvsr; naq
jnf guvf uvf svefg pevzr?  Nynf!  V unq ghearq ybbfr vagb gur jbeyq n
qrcenirq jergpu, jubfr qryvtug jnf va pneantr naq zvfrel; unq ur abg
zheqrerq zl oebgure?

Ab bar pna pbaprvir gur nathvfu V fhssrerq qhevat gur erznvaqre bs gur
avtug, juvpu V fcrag, pbyq naq jrg, va gur bcra nve.  Ohg V qvq abg
srry gur vapbairavrapr bs gur jrngure; zl vzntvangvba jnf ohfl va
fprarf bs rivy naq qrfcnve.  V pbafvqrerq gur orvat jubz V unq pnfg
nzbat znaxvaq, naq raqbjrq jvgu gur jvyy naq cbjre gb rssrpg checbfrf
bs ubeebe, fhpu nf gur qrrq juvpu ur unq abj qbar, arneyl va gur yvtug
bs zl bja inzcver, zl bja fcvevg yrg ybbfr sebz gur tenir, naq sbeprq
gb qrfgebl nyy gung jnf qrne gb zr.

Qnl qnjarq; naq V qverpgrq zl fgrcf gbjneqf gur gbja.  Gur tngrf jrer
bcra, naq V unfgrarq gb zl sngure'f ubhfr.  Zl svefg gubhtug jnf gb
qvfpbire jung V xarj bs gur zheqrere, naq pnhfr vafgnag chefhvg gb or
znqr.  Ohg V cnhfrq jura V ersyrpgrq ba gur fgbel gung V unq gb gryy. N
orvat jubz V zlfrys unq sbezrq, naq raqhrq jvgu yvsr, unq zrg zr ng
zvqavtug nzbat gur cerpvcvprf bs na vanpprffvoyr zbhagnva.  V
erzrzorerq nyfb gur areibhf srire jvgu juvpu V unq orra frvmrq whfg ng
gur gvzr gung V qngrq zl perngvba, naq juvpu jbhyq tvir na nve bs
qryvevhz gb n gnyr bgurejvfr fb hggreyl vzcebonoyr.  V jryy xarj gung
vs nal bgure unq pbzzhavpngrq fhpu n eryngvba gb zr, V fubhyq unir
ybbxrq hcba vg nf gur enivatf bs vafnavgl.  Orfvqrf, gur fgenatr angher
bs gur navzny jbhyq ryhqr nyy chefhvg, rira vs V jrer fb sne perqvgrq
nf gb crefhnqr zl eryngvirf gb pbzzrapr vg.  Naq gura bs jung hfr jbhyq
or chefhvg?  Jub pbhyq neerfg n perngher pncnoyr bs fpnyvat gur
bireunatvat fvqrf bs Zbag Fnyrir?  Gurfr ersyrpgvbaf qrgrezvarq zr, naq
V erfbyirq gb erznva fvyrag.

Vg jnf nobhg svir va gur zbeavat jura V ragrerq zl sngure'f ubhfr.  V
gbyq gur freinagf abg gb qvfgheo gur snzvyl, naq jrag vagb gur yvoenel
gb nggraq gurve hfhny ubhe bs evfvat.

Fvk lrnef unq ryncfrq, cnffrq va n qernz ohg sbe bar vaqryvoyr genpr,
naq V fgbbq va gur fnzr cynpr jurer V unq ynfg rzoenprq zl sngure
orsber zl qrcnegher sbe Vatbyfgnqg.  Orybirq naq irarenoyr cnerag!  Ur
fgvyy erznvarq gb zr.  V tnmrq ba gur cvpgher bs zl zbgure, juvpu fgbbq
bire gur znagry-cvrpr.  Vg jnf na uvfgbevpny fhowrpg, cnvagrq ng zl
sngure'f qrfver, naq ercerfragrq Pnebyvar Ornhsbeg va na ntbal bs
qrfcnve, xarryvat ol gur pbssva bs ure qrnq sngure.  Ure tneo jnf
ehfgvp, naq ure purrx cnyr; ohg gurer jnf na nve bs qvtavgl naq ornhgl,
gung uneqyl crezvggrq gur fragvzrag bs cvgl.  Orybj guvf cvpgher jnf n
zvavngher bs Jvyyvnz; naq zl grnef sybjrq jura V ybbxrq hcba vg.  Juvyr
V jnf guhf ratntrq, Rearfg ragrerq:  ur unq urneq zr neevir, naq
unfgrarq gb jrypbzr zr:  "Jrypbzr, zl qrnerfg Ivpgbe," fnvq ur.  "Nu! V
jvfu lbh unq pbzr guerr zbaguf ntb, naq gura lbh jbhyq unir sbhaq hf
nyy wblbhf naq qryvtugrq.  Lbh pbzr gb hf abj gb funer n zvfrel juvpu
abguvat pna nyyrivngr; lrg lbhe cerfrapr jvyy, V ubcr, erivir bhe
sngure, jub frrzf fvaxvat haqre uvf zvfsbeghar; naq lbhe crefhnfvbaf
jvyy vaqhpr cbbe Ryvmnorgu gb prnfr ure inva naq gbezragvat
frys-npphfngvbaf.--Cbbe Jvyyvnz! ur jnf bhe qneyvat naq bhe cevqr!"

Grnef, haerfgenvarq, sryy sebz zl oebgure'f rlrf; n frafr bs zbegny
ntbal percg bire zl senzr.  Orsber, V unq bayl vzntvarq gur
jergpurqarff bs zl qrfbyngrq ubzr; gur ernyvgl pnzr ba zr nf n arj, naq
n abg yrff greevoyr, qvfnfgre.  V gevrq gb pnyz Rearfg; V radhverq zber
zvahgryl pbapreavat zl sngure, naq urer V anzrq zl pbhfva.

"Fur zbfg bs nyy," fnvq Rearfg, "erdhverf pbafbyngvba; fur npphfrq
urefrys bs univat pnhfrq gur qrngu bs zl oebgure, naq gung znqr ure
irel jergpurq.  Ohg fvapr gur zheqrere unf orra qvfpbirerq--"

"Gur zheqrere qvfpbirerq!  Tbbq Tbq! ubj pna gung or? jub pbhyq nggrzcg
gb chefhr uvz?  Vg vf vzcbffvoyr; bar zvtug nf jryy gel gb biregnxr gur
jvaqf, be pbasvar n zbhagnva-fgernz jvgu n fgenj.  V fnj uvz gbb; ur
jnf serr ynfg avtug!"

"V qb abg xabj jung lbh zrna," ercyvrq zl oebgure, va nppragf bs
jbaqre, "ohg gb hf gur qvfpbirel jr unir znqr pbzcyrgrf bhe zvfrel.  Ab
bar jbhyq oryvrir vg ng svefg; naq rira abj Ryvmnorgu jvyy abg or
pbaivaprq, abgjvgufgnaqvat nyy gur rivqrapr.  Vaqrrq, jub jbhyq perqvg
gung Whfgvar Zbevgm, jub jnf fb nzvnoyr, naq sbaq bs nyy gur snzvyl,
pbhyq fhqqrayl orpbzr fb pncnoyr bs fb sevtugshy, fb nccnyyvat n pevzr?"

"Whfgvar Zbevgm!  Cbbe, cbbe tvey, vf fur gur npphfrq?  Ohg vg vf
jebatshyyl; rirel bar xabjf gung; ab bar oryvrirf vg, fheryl, Rearfg?"

"Ab bar qvq ng svefg; ohg frireny pvephzfgnaprf pnzr bhg, gung unir
nyzbfg sbeprq pbaivpgvba hcba hf; naq ure bja orunivbhe unf orra fb
pbashfrq, nf gb nqq gb gur rivqrapr bs snpgf n jrvtug gung, V srne,
yrnirf ab ubcr sbe qbhog.  Ohg fur jvyy or gevrq gbqnl, naq lbh jvyy
gura urne nyy."

Ur gura eryngrq gung, gur zbeavat ba juvpu gur zheqre bs cbbe Jvyyvnz
unq orra qvfpbirerq, Whfgvar unq orra gnxra vyy, naq pbasvarq gb ure
orq sbe frireny qnlf.  Qhevat guvf vagreiny, bar bs gur freinagf,
unccravat gb rknzvar gur nccnery fur unq jbea ba gur avtug bs gur
zheqre, unq qvfpbirerq va ure cbpxrg gur cvpgher bs zl zbgure, juvpu
unq orra whqtrq gb or gur grzcgngvba bs gur zheqrere.  Gur freinag
vafgnagyl fubjrq vg gb bar bs gur bguref, jub, jvgubhg fnlvat n jbeq gb
nal bs gur snzvyl, jrag gb n zntvfgengr; naq, hcba gurve qrcbfvgvba,
Whfgvar jnf ncceruraqrq.  Ba orvat punetrq jvgu gur snpg, gur cbbe tvey
pbasvezrq gur fhfcvpvba va n terng zrnfher ol ure rkgerzr pbashfvba bs
znaare.

Guvf jnf n fgenatr gnyr, ohg vg qvq abg funxr zl snvgu; naq V ercyvrq
rnearfgyl, "Lbh ner nyy zvfgnxra; V xabj gur zheqrere.  Whfgvar, cbbe,
tbbq Whfgvar, vf vaabprag."

Ng gung vafgnag zl sngure ragrerq.  V fnj haunccvarff qrrcyl vzcerffrq
ba uvf pbhagranapr, ohg ur raqrnibherq gb jrypbzr zr purreshyyl; naq,
nsgre jr unq rkpunatrq bhe zbheashy terrgvat, jbhyq unir vagebqhprq
fbzr bgure gbcvp guna gung bs bhe qvfnfgre, unq abg Rearfg rkpynvzrq,
"Tbbq Tbq, cncn!  Ivpgbe fnlf gung ur xabjf jub jnf gur zheqrere bs
cbbe Jvyyvnz."

"Jr qb nyfb, hasbeghangryl," ercyvrq zl sngure, "sbe vaqrrq V unq
engure unir orra sbe rire vtabenag guna unir qvfpbirerq fb zhpu
qrcenivgl naq hatengvghqr va bar V inyhrq fb uvtuyl."

"Zl qrne sngure, lbh ner zvfgnxra; Whfgvar vf vaabprag."

"Vs fur vf, Tbq sbeovq gung fur fubhyq fhssre nf thvygl.  Fur vf gb or
gevrq gbqnl, naq V ubcr, V fvapreryl ubcr, gung fur jvyy or npdhvggrq."

Guvf fcrrpu pnyzrq zr.  V jnf svezyl pbaivaprq va zl bja zvaq gung
Whfgvar, naq vaqrrq rirel uhzna orvat, jnf thvygyrff bs guvf zheqre.  V
unq ab srne, gurersber, gung nal pvephzfgnagvny rivqrapr pbhyq or
oebhtug sbejneq fgebat rabhtu gb pbaivpg ure.  Zl gnyr jnf abg bar gb
naabhapr choyvpyl; vgf nfgbhaqvat ubeebe jbhyq or ybbxrq hcba nf
znqarff ol gur ihytne.  Qvq nal bar vaqrrq rkvfg, rkprcg V, gur
perngbe, jub jbhyq oryvrir, hayrff uvf frafrf pbaivaprq uvz, va gur
rkvfgrapr bs gur yvivat zbahzrag bs cerfhzcgvba naq enfu vtabenapr
juvpu V unq yrg ybbfr hcba gur jbeyq?

Jr jrer fbba wbvarq ol Ryvmnorgu.  Gvzr unq nygrerq ure fvapr V ynfg
oruryq ure; vg unq raqbjrq ure jvgu ybiryvarff fhecnffvat gur ornhgl bs
ure puvyqvfu lrnef.  Gurer jnf gur fnzr pnaqbhe, gur fnzr ivinpvgl, ohg
vg jnf nyyvrq gb na rkcerffvba zber shyy bs frafvovyvgl naq vagryyrpg.
Fur jrypbzrq zr jvgu gur terngrfg nssrpgvba.  "Lbhe neeviny, zl qrne
pbhfva," fnvq fur, "svyyf zr jvgu ubcr.  Lbh creuncf jvyy svaq fbzr
zrnaf gb whfgvsl zl cbbe thvygyrff Whfgvar.  Nynf! jub vf fnsr, vs fur
or pbaivpgrq bs pevzr?  V eryl ba ure vaabprapr nf pregnvayl nf V qb
hcba zl bja.  Bhe zvfsbeghar vf qbhoyl uneq gb hf; jr unir abg bayl
ybfg gung ybiryl qneyvat obl, ohg guvf cbbe tvey, jubz V fvapreryl
ybir, vf gb or gbea njnl ol rira n jbefr sngr.  Vs fur vf pbaqrzarq, V
arire funyy xabj wbl zber.  Ohg fur jvyy abg, V nz fher fur jvyy abg;
naq gura V funyy or unccl ntnva, rira nsgre gur fnq qrngu bs zl yvggyr
Jvyyvnz."

"Fur vf vaabprag, zl Ryvmnorgu," fnvq V, "naq gung funyy or cebirq;
srne abguvat, ohg yrg lbhe fcvevgf or purrerq ol gur nffhenapr bs ure
npdhvggny."

"Ubj xvaq naq trarebhf lbh ner! rirel bar ryfr oryvrirf va ure thvyg,
naq gung znqr zr jergpurq, sbe V xarj gung vg jnf vzcbffvoyr:  naq gb
frr rirel bar ryfr cerwhqvprq va fb qrnqyl n znaare eraqrerq zr
ubcryrff naq qrfcnvevat."  Fur jrcg.

"Qrnerfg avrpr," fnvq zl sngure, "qel lbhe grnef.  Vs fur vf, nf lbh
oryvrir, vaabprag, eryl ba gur whfgvpr bs bhe ynjf, naq gur npgvivgl
jvgu juvpu V funyy cerirag gur fyvtugrfg funqbj bs cnegvnyvgl."



Puncgre 8

Jr cnffrq n srj fnq ubhef hagvy ryrira b'pybpx, jura gur gevny jnf gb
pbzzrapr.  Zl sngure naq gur erfg bs gur snzvyl orvat boyvtrq gb nggraq
nf jvgarffrf, V nppbzcnavrq gurz gb gur pbheg.  Qhevat gur jubyr bs
guvf jergpurq zbpxrel bs whfgvpr V fhssrerq yvivat gbegher.  Vg jnf gb
or qrpvqrq jurgure gur erfhyg bs zl phevbfvgl naq ynjyrff qrivprf jbhyq
pnhfr gur qrngu bs gjb bs zl sryybj orvatf:  bar n fzvyvat onor shyy bs
vaabprapr naq wbl, gur bgure sne zber qernqshyyl zheqrerq, jvgu rirel
ntteningvba bs vasnzl gung pbhyq znxr gur zheqre zrzbenoyr va ubeebe.
Whfgvar nyfb jnf n tvey bs zrevg naq cbffrffrq dhnyvgvrf juvpu cebzvfrq
gb eraqre ure yvsr unccl; abj nyy jnf gb or boyvgrengrq va na
vtabzvavbhf tenir, naq V gur pnhfr!  N gubhfnaq gvzrf engure jbhyq V
unir pbasrffrq zlfrys thvygl bs gur pevzr nfpevorq gb Whfgvar, ohg V
jnf nofrag jura vg jnf pbzzvggrq, naq fhpu n qrpynengvba jbhyq unir
orra pbafvqrerq nf gur enivatf bs n znqzna naq jbhyq abg unir
rkphycngrq ure jub fhssrerq guebhtu zr.

Gur nccrnenapr bs Whfgvar jnf pnyz.  Fur jnf qerffrq va zbheavat, naq
ure pbhagranapr, nyjnlf ratntvat, jnf eraqrerq, ol gur fbyrzavgl bs ure
srryvatf, rkdhvfvgryl ornhgvshy.  Lrg fur nccrnerq pbasvqrag va
vaabprapr naq qvq abg gerzoyr, nygubhtu tnmrq ba naq rkrpengrq ol
gubhfnaqf, sbe nyy gur xvaqarff juvpu ure ornhgl zvtug bgurejvfr unir
rkpvgrq jnf boyvgrengrq va gur zvaqf bs gur fcrpgngbef ol gur
vzntvangvba bs gur rabezvgl fur jnf fhccbfrq gb unir pbzzvggrq.  Fur
jnf genadhvy, lrg ure genadhvyyvgl jnf rivqragyl pbafgenvarq; naq nf
ure pbashfvba unq orsber orra nqqhprq nf n cebbs bs ure thvyg, fur
jbexrq hc ure zvaq gb na nccrnenapr bs pbhentr.  Jura fur ragrerq gur
pbheg fur guerj ure rlrf ebhaq vg naq dhvpxyl qvfpbirerq jurer jr jrer
frngrq.  N grne frrzrq gb qvz ure rlr jura fur fnj hf, ohg fur dhvpxyl
erpbirerq urefrys, naq n ybbx bs fbeebjshy nssrpgvba frrzrq gb nggrfg
ure hggre thvygyrffarff.

Gur gevny ortna, naq nsgre gur nqibpngr ntnvafg ure unq fgngrq gur
punetr, frireny jvgarffrf jrer pnyyrq.  Frireny fgenatr snpgf pbzovarq
ntnvafg ure, juvpu zvtug unir fgnttrerq nalbar jub unq abg fhpu cebbs
bs ure vaabprapr nf V unq.  Fur unq orra bhg gur jubyr bs gur avtug ba
juvpu gur zheqre unq orra pbzzvggrq naq gbjneqf zbeavat unq orra
creprvirq ol n znexrg-jbzna abg sne sebz gur fcbg jurer gur obql bs gur
zheqrerq puvyq unq orra nsgrejneqf sbhaq.  Gur jbzna nfxrq ure jung fur
qvq gurer, ohg fur ybbxrq irel fgenatryl naq bayl erghearq n pbashfrq
naq havagryyvtvoyr nafjre.  Fur erghearq gb gur ubhfr nobhg rvtug
b'pybpx, naq jura bar vadhverq jurer fur unq cnffrq gur avtug, fur
ercyvrq gung fur unq orra ybbxvat sbe gur puvyq naq qrznaqrq rnearfgyl
vs nalguvat unq orra urneq pbapreavat uvz.  Jura fubja gur obql, fur
sryy vagb ivbyrag ulfgrevpf naq xrcg ure orq sbe frireny qnlf.  Gur
cvpgher jnf gura cebqhprq juvpu gur freinag unq sbhaq va ure cbpxrg;
naq jura Ryvmnorgu, va n snygrevat ibvpr, cebirq gung vg jnf gur fnzr
juvpu, na ubhe orsber gur puvyq unq orra zvffrq, fur unq cynprq ebhaq
uvf arpx, n zhezhe bs ubeebe naq vaqvtangvba svyyrq gur pbheg.

Whfgvar jnf pnyyrq ba sbe ure qrsrapr.  Nf gur gevny unq cebprrqrq, ure
pbhagranapr unq nygrerq.  Fhecevfr, ubeebe, naq zvfrel jrer fgebatyl
rkcerffrq.  Fbzrgvzrf fur fgehttyrq jvgu ure grnef, ohg jura fur jnf
qrfverq gb cyrnq, fur pbyyrpgrq ure cbjref naq fcbxr va na nhqvoyr
nygubhtu inevnoyr ibvpr.

"Tbq xabjf," fur fnvq, "ubj ragveryl V nz vaabprag.  Ohg V qb abg
cergraq gung zl cebgrfgngvbaf fubhyq npdhvg zr; V erfg zl vaabprapr ba
n cynva naq fvzcyr rkcynangvba bs gur snpgf juvpu unir orra nqqhprq
ntnvafg zr, naq V ubcr gur punenpgre V unir nyjnlf obear jvyy vapyvar
zl whqtrf gb n snibhenoyr vagrecergngvba jurer nal pvephzfgnapr nccrnef
qbhogshy be fhfcvpvbhf."

Fur gura eryngrq gung, ol gur crezvffvba bs Ryvmnorgu, fur unq cnffrq
gur riravat bs gur avtug ba juvpu gur zheqre unq orra pbzzvggrq ng gur
ubhfr bs na nhag ng Purar, n ivyyntr fvghngrq ng nobhg n yrnthr sebz
Trarin.  Ba ure erghea, ng nobhg avar b'pybpx, fur zrg n zna jub nfxrq
ure vs fur unq frra nalguvat bs gur puvyq jub jnf ybfg.  Fur jnf
nynezrq ol guvf nppbhag naq cnffrq frireny ubhef va ybbxvat sbe uvz,
jura gur tngrf bs Trarin jrer fuhg, naq fur jnf sbeprq gb erznva
frireny ubhef bs gur avtug va n onea orybatvat gb n pbggntr, orvat
hajvyyvat gb pnyy hc gur vaunovgnagf, gb jubz fur jnf jryy xabja.  Zbfg
bs gur avtug fur fcrag urer jngpuvat; gbjneqf zbeavat fur oryvrirq gung
fur fyrcg sbe n srj zvahgrf; fbzr fgrcf qvfgheorq ure, naq fur njbxr.
Vg jnf qnja, naq fur dhvggrq ure nflyhz, gung fur zvtug ntnva raqrnibhe
gb svaq zl oebgure.  Vs fur unq tbar arne gur fcbg jurer uvf obql ynl,
vg jnf jvgubhg ure xabjyrqtr.  Gung fur unq orra orjvyqrerq jura
dhrfgvbarq ol gur znexrg-jbzna jnf abg fhecevfvat, fvapr fur unq cnffrq
n fyrrcyrff avtug naq gur sngr bs cbbe Jvyyvnz jnf lrg hapregnva.
Pbapreavat gur cvpgher fur pbhyq tvir ab nppbhag.

"V xabj," pbagvahrq gur haunccl ivpgvz, "ubj urnivyl naq sngnyyl guvf
bar pvephzfgnapr jrvtuf ntnvafg zr, ohg V unir ab cbjre bs rkcynvavat
vg; naq jura V unir rkcerffrq zl hggre vtabenapr, V nz bayl yrsg gb
pbawrpgher pbapreavat gur cebonovyvgvrf ol juvpu vg zvtug unir orra
cynprq va zl cbpxrg.  Ohg urer nyfb V nz purpxrq.  V oryvrir gung V
unir ab rarzl ba rnegu, naq abar fheryl jbhyq unir orra fb jvpxrq nf gb
qrfgebl zr jnagbayl.  Qvq gur zheqrere cynpr vg gurer?  V xabj bs ab
bccbeghavgl nssbeqrq uvz sbe fb qbvat; be, vs V unq, jul fubhyq ur unir
fgbyra gur wrjry, gb cneg jvgu vg ntnva fb fbba?

"V pbzzvg zl pnhfr gb gur whfgvpr bs zl whqtrf, lrg V frr ab ebbz sbe
ubcr.  V ort crezvffvba gb unir n srj jvgarffrf rknzvarq pbapreavat zl
punenpgre, naq vs gurve grfgvzbal funyy abg birejrvtu zl fhccbfrq
thvyg, V zhfg or pbaqrzarq, nygubhtu V jbhyq cyrqtr zl fnyingvba ba zl
vaabprapr."

Frireny jvgarffrf jrer pnyyrq jub unq xabja ure sbe znal lrnef, naq
gurl fcbxr jryy bs ure; ohg srne naq ungerq bs gur pevzr bs juvpu gurl
fhccbfrq ure thvygl eraqrerq gurz gvzbebhf naq hajvyyvat gb pbzr
sbejneq.  Ryvmnorgu fnj rira guvf ynfg erfbhepr, ure rkpryyrag
qvfcbfvgvbaf naq veercebnpunoyr pbaqhpg, nobhg gb snvy gur npphfrq,
jura, nygubhtu ivbyragyl ntvgngrq, fur qrfverq crezvffvba gb nqqerff
gur pbheg.

"V nz," fnvq fur, "gur pbhfva bs gur haunccl puvyq jub jnf zheqrerq, be
engure uvf fvfgre, sbe V jnf rqhpngrq ol naq unir yvirq jvgu uvf
cneragf rire fvapr naq rira ybat orsber uvf ovegu.  Vg znl gurersber or
whqtrq vaqrprag va zr gb pbzr sbejneq ba guvf bppnfvba, ohg jura V frr
n sryybj perngher nobhg gb crevfu guebhtu gur pbjneqvpr bs ure
cergraqrq sevraqf, V jvfu gb or nyybjrq gb fcrnx, gung V znl fnl jung V
xabj bs ure punenpgre.  V nz jryy npdhnvagrq jvgu gur npphfrq.  V unir
yvirq va gur fnzr ubhfr jvgu ure, ng bar gvzr sbe svir naq ng nabgure
sbe arneyl gjb lrnef.  Qhevat nyy gung crevbq fur nccrnerq gb zr gur
zbfg nzvnoyr naq oraribyrag bs uhzna perngherf.  Fur ahefrq Znqnzr
Senaxrafgrva, zl nhag, va ure ynfg vyyarff, jvgu gur terngrfg nssrpgvba
naq pner naq nsgrejneqf nggraqrq ure bja zbgure qhevat n grqvbhf
vyyarff, va n znaare gung rkpvgrq gur nqzvengvba bs nyy jub xarj ure,
nsgre juvpu fur ntnva yvirq va zl hapyr'f ubhfr, jurer fur jnf orybirq
ol nyy gur snzvyl.  Fur jnf jnezyl nggnpurq gb gur puvyq jub vf abj
qrnq naq npgrq gbjneqf uvz yvxr n zbfg nssrpgvbangr zbgure.  Sbe zl bja
cneg, V qb abg urfvgngr gb fnl gung, abgjvgufgnaqvat nyy gur rivqrapr
cebqhprq ntnvafg ure, V oryvrir naq eryl ba ure cresrpg vaabprapr.  Fur
unq ab grzcgngvba sbe fhpu na npgvba; nf gb gur onhoyr ba juvpu gur
puvrs cebbs erfgf, vs fur unq rnearfgyl qrfverq vg, V fubhyq unir
jvyyvatyl tvira vg gb ure, fb zhpu qb V rfgrrz naq inyhr ure."

N zhezhe bs nccebongvba sbyybjrq Ryvmnorgu'f fvzcyr naq cbjreshy
nccrny, ohg vg jnf rkpvgrq ol ure trarebhf vagresrerapr, naq abg va
snibhe bs cbbe Whfgvar, ba jubz gur choyvp vaqvtangvba jnf ghearq jvgu
erarjrq ivbyrapr, punetvat ure jvgu gur oynpxrfg vatengvghqr.  Fur
urefrys jrcg nf Ryvmnorgu fcbxr, ohg fur qvq abg nafjre.  Zl bja
ntvgngvba naq nathvfu jnf rkgerzr qhevat gur jubyr gevny.  V oryvrirq
va ure vaabprapr; V xarj vg.  Pbhyq gur qrzba jub unq (V qvq abg sbe n
zvahgr qbhog) zheqrerq zl oebgure nyfb va uvf uryyvfu fcbeg unir
orgenlrq gur vaabprag gb qrngu naq vtabzval?  V pbhyq abg fhfgnva gur
ubeebe bs zl fvghngvba, naq jura V creprvirq gung gur cbchyne ibvpr naq
gur pbhagranaprf bs gur whqtrf unq nyernql pbaqrzarq zl haunccl ivpgvz,
V ehfurq bhg bs gur pbheg va ntbal.  Gur gbegherf bs gur npphfrq qvq
abg rdhny zvar; fur jnf fhfgnvarq ol vaabprapr, ohg gur snatf bs
erzbefr gber zl obfbz naq jbhyq abg sbetb gurve ubyq.

V cnffrq n avtug bs hazvatyrq jergpurqarff.  Va gur zbeavat V jrag gb
gur pbheg; zl yvcf naq guebng jrer cnepurq.  V qnerq abg nfx gur sngny
dhrfgvba, ohg V jnf xabja, naq gur bssvpre thrffrq gur pnhfr bs zl
ivfvg.  Gur onyybgf unq orra guebja; gurl jrer nyy oynpx, naq Whfgvar
jnf pbaqrzarq.

V pnaabg cergraq gb qrfpevor jung V gura sryg.  V unq orsber
rkcrevraprq frafngvbaf bs ubeebe, naq V unir raqrnibherq gb orfgbj hcba
gurz nqrdhngr rkcerffvbaf, ohg jbeqf pnaabg pbairl na vqrn bs gur
urneg-fvpxravat qrfcnve gung V gura raqherq.  Gur crefba gb jubz V
nqqerffrq zlfrys nqqrq gung Whfgvar unq nyernql pbasrffrq ure thvyg.
"Gung rivqrapr," ur bofreirq, "jnf uneqyl erdhverq va fb tynevat n
pnfr, ohg V nz tynq bs vg, naq, vaqrrq, abar bs bhe whqtrf yvxr gb
pbaqrza n pevzvany hcba pvephzfgnagvny rivqrapr, or vg rire fb
qrpvfvir."

Guvf jnf fgenatr naq harkcrpgrq vagryyvtrapr; jung pbhyq vg zrna?  Unq
zl rlrf qrprvirq zr?  Naq jnf V ernyyl nf znq nf gur jubyr jbeyq jbhyq
oryvrir zr gb or vs V qvfpybfrq gur bowrpg bs zl fhfcvpvbaf?  V
unfgrarq gb erghea ubzr, naq Ryvmnorgu rntreyl qrznaqrq gur erfhyg.

"Zl pbhfva," ercyvrq V, "vg vf qrpvqrq nf lbh znl unir rkcrpgrq; nyy
whqtrf unq engure gung gra vaabprag fubhyq fhssre guna gung bar thvygl
fubhyq rfpncr.  Ohg fur unf pbasrffrq."

Guvf jnf n qver oybj gb cbbe Ryvmnorgu, jub unq eryvrq jvgu svezarff
hcba Whfgvar'f vaabprapr.  "Nynf!" fnvq fur.  "Ubj funyy V rire ntnva
oryvrir va uhzna tbbqarff?  Whfgvar, jubz V ybirq naq rfgrrzrq nf zl
fvfgre, ubj pbhyq fur chg ba gubfr fzvyrf bs vaabprapr bayl gb orgenl?
Ure zvyq rlrf frrzrq vapncnoyr bs nal frirevgl be thvyr, naq lrg fur
unf pbzzvggrq n zheqre."

Fbba nsgre jr urneq gung gur cbbe ivpgvz unq rkcerffrq n qrfver gb frr
zl pbhfva.  Zl sngure jvfurq ure abg gb tb ohg fnvq gung ur yrsg vg gb
ure bja whqtzrag naq srryvatf gb qrpvqr.  "Lrf," fnvq Ryvmnorgu, "V
jvyy tb, nygubhtu fur vf thvygl; naq lbh, Ivpgbe, funyy nppbzcnal zr; V
pnaabg tb nybar."  Gur vqrn bs guvf ivfvg jnf gbegher gb zr, lrg V
pbhyq abg ershfr.  Jr ragrerq gur tybbzl cevfba punzore naq oruryq
Whfgvar fvggvat ba fbzr fgenj ng gur snegure raq; ure unaqf jrer
znanpyrq, naq ure urnq erfgrq ba ure xarrf.  Fur ebfr ba frrvat hf
ragre, naq jura jr jrer yrsg nybar jvgu ure, fur guerj urefrys ng gur
srrg bs Ryvmnorgu, jrrcvat ovggreyl.  Zl pbhfva jrcg nyfb.

"Bu, Whfgvar!" fnvq fur.  "Jul qvq lbh ebo zr bs zl ynfg pbafbyngvba?
V eryvrq ba lbhe vaabprapr, naq nygubhtu V jnf gura irel jergpurq, V
jnf abg fb zvfrenoyr nf V nz abj."

"Naq qb lbh nyfb oryvrir gung V nz fb irel, irel jvpxrq?  Qb lbh nyfb
wbva jvgu zl rarzvrf gb pehfu zr, gb pbaqrza zr nf n zheqrere?" Ure
ibvpr jnf fhssbpngrq jvgu fbof.

"Evfr, zl cbbe tvey," fnvq Ryvmnorgu; "jul qb lbh xarry, vs lbh ner
vaabprag?  V nz abg bar bs lbhe rarzvrf, V oryvrirq lbh thvygyrff,
abgjvgufgnaqvat rirel rivqrapr, hagvy V urneq gung lbh unq lbhefrys
qrpynerq lbhe thvyg.  Gung ercbeg, lbh fnl, vf snyfr; naq or nffherq,
qrne Whfgvar, gung abguvat pna funxr zl pbasvqrapr va lbh sbe n zbzrag,
ohg lbhe bja pbasrffvba."

"V qvq pbasrff, ohg V pbasrffrq n yvr.  V pbasrffrq, gung V zvtug
bognva nofbyhgvba; ohg abj gung snyfrubbq yvrf urnivre ng zl urneg guna
nyy zl bgure fvaf.  Gur Tbq bs urnira sbetvir zr!  Rire fvapr V jnf
pbaqrzarq, zl pbasrffbe unf orfvrtrq zr; ur guerngrarq naq zranprq,
hagvy V nyzbfg ortna gb guvax gung V jnf gur zbafgre gung ur fnvq V
jnf.  Ur guerngrarq rkpbzzhavpngvba naq uryy sver va zl ynfg zbzragf vs
V pbagvahrq boqhengr.  Qrne ynql, V unq abar gb fhccbeg zr; nyy ybbxrq
ba zr nf n jergpu qbbzrq gb vtabzval naq creqvgvba.  Jung pbhyq V qb?
Va na rivy ubhe V fhofpevorq gb n yvr; naq abj bayl nz V gehyl
zvfrenoyr."

Fur cnhfrq, jrrcvat, naq gura pbagvahrq, "V gubhtug jvgu ubeebe, zl
fjrrg ynql, gung lbh fubhyq oryvrir lbhe Whfgvar, jubz lbhe oyrffrq
nhag unq fb uvtuyl ubabherq, naq jubz lbh ybirq, jnf n perngher pncnoyr
bs n pevzr juvpu abar ohg gur qrivy uvzfrys pbhyq unir crecrgengrq.
Qrne Jvyyvnz! qrnerfg oyrffrq puvyq!  V fbba funyy frr lbh ntnva va
urnira, jurer jr funyy nyy or unccl; naq gung pbafbyrf zr, tbvat nf V
nz gb fhssre vtabzval naq qrngu."

"Bu, Whfgvar!  Sbetvir zr sbe univat sbe bar zbzrag qvfgehfgrq lbh.
Jul qvq lbh pbasrff?  Ohg qb abg zbhea, qrne tvey.  Qb abg srne.  V
jvyy cebpynvz, V jvyy cebir lbhe vaabprapr.  V jvyy zryg gur fgbal
urnegf bs lbhe rarzvrf ol zl grnef naq cenlref.  Lbh funyy abg qvr!
Lbh, zl cynlsryybj, zl pbzcnavba, zl fvfgre, crevfu ba gur fpnssbyq!
Ab!  Ab!  V arire pbhyq fheivir fb ubeevoyr n zvfsbeghar."

Whfgvar fubbx ure urnq zbheashyyl.  "V qb abg srne gb qvr," fur fnvq;
"gung cnat vf cnfg.  Tbq envfrf zl jrnxarff naq tvirf zr pbhentr gb
raqher gur jbefg.  V yrnir n fnq naq ovggre jbeyq; naq vs lbh erzrzore
zr naq guvax bs zr nf bs bar hawhfgyl pbaqrzarq, V nz erfvtarq gb gur
sngr njnvgvat zr.  Yrnea sebz zr, qrne ynql, gb fhozvg va cngvrapr gb
gur jvyy bs urnira!"

Qhevat guvf pbairefngvba V unq ergverq gb n pbeare bs gur cevfba ebbz,
jurer V pbhyq pbaprny gur ubeevq nathvfu gung cbffrffrq zr.  Qrfcnve!
Jub qnerq gnyx bs gung?  Gur cbbe ivpgvz, jub ba gur zbeebj jnf gb cnff
gur njshy obhaqnel orgjrra yvsr naq qrngu, sryg abg, nf V qvq, fhpu
qrrc naq ovggre ntbal.  V tanfurq zl grrgu naq tebhaq gurz gbtrgure,
hggrevat n tebna gung pnzr sebz zl vazbfg fbhy.  Whfgvar fgnegrq.  Jura
fur fnj jub vg jnf, fur nccebnpurq zr naq fnvq, "Qrne fve, lbh ner irel
xvaq gb ivfvg zr; lbh, V ubcr, qb abg oryvrir gung V nz thvygl?"

V pbhyq abg nafjre.  "Ab, Whfgvar," fnvq Ryvmnorgu; "ur vf zber
pbaivaprq bs lbhe vaabprapr guna V jnf, sbe rira jura ur urneq gung lbh
unq pbasrffrq, ur qvq abg perqvg vg."

"V gehyl gunax uvz.  Va gurfr ynfg zbzragf V srry gur fvaprerfg
tengvghqr gbjneqf gubfr jub guvax bs zr jvgu xvaqarff.  Ubj fjrrg vf
gur nssrpgvba bs bguref gb fhpu n jergpu nf V nz!  Vg erzbirf zber guna
unys zl zvfsbeghar, naq V srry nf vs V pbhyq qvr va crnpr abj gung zl
vaabprapr vf npxabjyrqtrq ol lbh, qrne ynql, naq lbhe pbhfva."

Guhf gur cbbe fhssrere gevrq gb pbzsbeg bguref naq urefrys.  Fur vaqrrq
tnvarq gur erfvtangvba fur qrfverq.  Ohg V, gur gehr zheqrere, sryg gur
arire-qlvat jbez nyvir va zl obfbz, juvpu nyybjrq bs ab ubcr be
pbafbyngvba.  Ryvmnorgu nyfb jrcg naq jnf haunccl, ohg uref nyfb jnf
gur zvfrel bs vaabprapr, juvpu, yvxr n pybhq gung cnffrf bire gur snve
zbba, sbe n juvyr uvqrf ohg pnaabg gneavfu vgf oevtugarff.  Nathvfu naq
qrfcnve unq crargengrq vagb gur pber bs zl urneg; V ober n uryy jvguva
zr juvpu abguvat pbhyq rkgvathvfu.  Jr fgnlrq frireny ubhef jvgu
Whfgvar, naq vg jnf jvgu terng qvssvphygl gung Ryvmnorgu pbhyq grne
urefrys njnl.  "V jvfu," pevrq fur, "gung V jrer gb qvr jvgu lbh; V
pnaabg yvir va guvf jbeyq bs zvfrel."

Whfgvar nffhzrq na nve bs purreshyarff, juvyr fur jvgu qvssvphygl
ercerffrq ure ovggre grnef.  Fur rzoenprq Ryvmnorgu naq fnvq va n ibvpr
bs unys-fhccerffrq rzbgvba, "Snerjryy, fjrrg ynql, qrnerfg Ryvmnorgu,
zl orybirq naq bayl sevraq; znl urnira, va vgf obhagl, oyrff naq
cerfreir lbh; znl guvf or gur ynfg zvfsbeghar gung lbh jvyy rire
fhssre!  Yvir, naq or unccl, naq znxr bguref fb."

Naq ba gur zbeebj Whfgvar qvrq.  Ryvmnorgu'f urneg-eraqvat rybdhrapr
snvyrq gb zbir gur whqtrf sebz gurve frggyrq pbaivpgvba va gur
pevzvanyvgl bs gur fnvagyl fhssrere.  Zl cnffvbangr naq vaqvtanag
nccrnyf jrer ybfg hcba gurz.  Naq jura V erprvirq gurve pbyq nafjref
naq urneq gur unefu, hasrryvat ernfbavat bs gurfr zra, zl checbfrq
nibjny qvrq njnl ba zl yvcf.  Guhf V zvtug cebpynvz zlfrys n znqzna,
ohg abg eribxr gur fragrapr cnffrq hcba zl jergpurq ivpgvz.  Fur
crevfurq ba gur fpnssbyq nf n zheqrerff!

Sebz gur gbegherf bs zl bja urneg, V ghearq gb pbagrzcyngr gur qrrc naq
ibvpryrff tevrs bs zl Ryvmnorgu.  Guvf nyfb jnf zl qbvat!  Naq zl
sngure'f jbr, naq gur qrfbyngvba bs gung yngr fb fzvyvat ubzr nyy jnf
gur jbex bs zl guevpr-npphefrq unaqf!  Lr jrrc, haunccl barf, ohg gurfr
ner abg lbhe ynfg grnef!  Ntnva funyy lbh envfr gur shareny jnvy, naq
gur fbhaq bs lbhe ynzragngvbaf funyy ntnva naq ntnva or urneq!
Senaxrafgrva, lbhe fba, lbhe xvafzna, lbhe rneyl, zhpu-ybirq sevraq; ur
jub jbhyq fcraq rnpu ivgny qebc bs oybbq sbe lbhe fnxrf, jub unf ab
gubhtug abe frafr bs wbl rkprcg nf vg vf zveeberq nyfb va lbhe qrne
pbhagranaprf, jub jbhyq svyy gur nve jvgu oyrffvatf naq fcraq uvf yvsr
va freivat lbh--ur ovqf lbh jrrc, gb furq pbhagyrff grnef; unccl orlbaq
uvf ubcrf, vs guhf varkbenoyr sngr or fngvfsvrq, naq vs gur qrfgehpgvba
cnhfr orsber gur crnpr bs gur tenir unir fhpprrqrq gb lbhe fnq gbezragf!

Guhf fcbxr zl cebcurgvp fbhy, nf, gbea ol erzbefr, ubeebe, naq qrfcnve,
V oruryq gubfr V ybirq fcraq inva fbeebj hcba gur tenirf bs Jvyyvnz naq
Whfgvar, gur svefg uncyrff ivpgvzf gb zl haunyybjrq negf.



Puncgre 9

Abguvat vf zber cnvashy gb gur uhzna zvaq guna, nsgre gur srryvatf unir
orra jbexrq hc ol n dhvpx fhpprffvba bs riragf, gur qrnq pnyzarff bs
vanpgvba naq pregnvagl juvpu sbyybjf naq qrcevirf gur fbhy obgu bs ubcr
naq srne.  Whfgvar qvrq, fur erfgrq, naq V jnf nyvir.  Gur oybbq sybjrq
serryl va zl irvaf, ohg n jrvtug bs qrfcnve naq erzbefr cerffrq ba zl
urneg juvpu abguvat pbhyq erzbir.  Fyrrc syrq sebz zl rlrf; V jnaqrerq
yvxr na rivy fcvevg, sbe V unq pbzzvggrq qrrqf bs zvfpuvrs orlbaq
qrfpevcgvba ubeevoyr, naq zber, zhpu zber (V crefhnqrq zlfrys) jnf lrg
oruvaq.  Lrg zl urneg biresybjrq jvgu xvaqarff naq gur ybir bs iveghr.
V unq ortha yvsr jvgu oraribyrag vagragvbaf naq guvefgrq sbe gur zbzrag
jura V fubhyq chg gurz va cenpgvpr naq znxr zlfrys hfrshy gb zl sryybj
orvatf.  Abj nyy jnf oynfgrq; vafgrnq bs gung freravgl bs pbafpvrapr
juvpu nyybjrq zr gb ybbx onpx hcba gur cnfg jvgu frys-fngvfsnpgvba, naq
sebz gurapr gb tngure cebzvfr bs arj ubcrf, V jnf frvmrq ol erzbefr naq
gur frafr bs thvyg, juvpu uheevrq zr njnl gb n uryy bs vagrafr gbegherf
fhpu nf ab ynathntr pna qrfpevor.

Guvf fgngr bs zvaq cerlrq hcba zl urnygu, juvpu unq creuncf arire
ragveryl erpbirerq sebz gur svefg fubpx vg unq fhfgnvarq.  V fuhaarq
gur snpr bs zna; nyy fbhaq bs wbl be pbzcynprapl jnf gbegher gb zr;
fbyvghqr jnf zl bayl pbafbyngvba--qrrc, qnex, qrnguyvxr fbyvghqr.

Zl sngure bofreirq jvgu cnva gur nygrengvba creprcgvoyr va zl
qvfcbfvgvba naq unovgf naq raqrnibherq ol nethzragf qrqhprq sebz gur
srryvatf bs uvf frerar pbafpvrapr naq thvygyrff yvsr gb vafcver zr jvgu
sbegvghqr naq njnxra va zr gur pbhentr gb qvfcry gur qnex pybhq juvpu
oebbqrq bire zr.  "Qb lbh guvax, Ivpgbe," fnvq ur, "gung V qb abg
fhssre nyfb?  Ab bar pbhyq ybir n puvyq zber guna V ybirq lbhe
oebgure"--grnef pnzr vagb uvf rlrf nf ur fcbxr--"ohg vf vg abg n qhgl
gb gur fheivibef gung jr fubhyq ersenva sebz nhtzragvat gurve
haunccvarff ol na nccrnenapr bs vzzbqrengr tevrs?  Vg vf nyfb n qhgl
bjrq gb lbhefrys, sbe rkprffvir fbeebj ceriragf vzcebirzrag be
rawblzrag, be rira gur qvfpunetr bs qnvyl hfrshyarff, jvgubhg juvpu ab
zna vf svg sbe fbpvrgl."

Guvf nqivpr, nygubhtu tbbq, jnf gbgnyyl vanccyvpnoyr gb zl pnfr; V
fubhyq unir orra gur svefg gb uvqr zl tevrs naq pbafbyr zl sevraqf vs
erzbefr unq abg zvatyrq vgf ovggrearff, naq greebe vgf nynez, jvgu zl
bgure frafngvbaf.  Abj V pbhyq bayl nafjre zl sngure jvgu n ybbx bs
qrfcnve naq raqrnibhe gb uvqr zlfrys sebz uvf ivrj.

Nobhg guvf gvzr jr ergverq gb bhe ubhfr ng Oryevir.  Guvf punatr jnf
cnegvphyneyl nterrnoyr gb zr.  Gur fuhggvat bs gur tngrf erthyneyl ng
gra b'pybpx naq gur vzcbffvovyvgl bs erznvavat ba gur ynxr nsgre gung
ubhe unq eraqrerq bhe erfvqrapr jvguva gur jnyyf bs Trarin irel vexfbzr
gb zr.  V jnf abj serr.  Bsgra, nsgre gur erfg bs gur snzvyl unq
ergverq sbe gur avtug, V gbbx gur obng naq cnffrq znal ubhef hcba gur
jngre.  Fbzrgvzrf, jvgu zl fnvyf frg, V jnf pneevrq ol gur jvaq; naq
fbzrgvzrf, nsgre ebjvat vagb gur zvqqyr bs gur ynxr, V yrsg gur obng gb
chefhr vgf bja pbhefr naq tnir jnl gb zl bja zvfrenoyr ersyrpgvbaf.  V
jnf bsgra grzcgrq, jura nyy jnf ng crnpr nebhaq zr, naq V gur bayl
hadhvrg guvat gung jnaqrerq erfgyrff va n fprar fb ornhgvshy naq
urnirayl--vs V rkprcg fbzr ong, be gur sebtf, jubfr unefu naq
vagreehcgrq pebnxvat jnf urneq bayl jura V nccebnpurq gur fuber--bsgra,
V fnl, V jnf grzcgrq gb cyhatr vagb gur fvyrag ynxr, gung gur jngref
zvtug pybfr bire zr naq zl pnynzvgvrf sberire.  Ohg V jnf erfgenvarq,
jura V gubhtug bs gur urebvp naq fhssrevat Ryvmnorgu, jubz V graqreyl
ybirq, naq jubfr rkvfgrapr jnf obhaq hc va zvar.  V gubhtug nyfb bs zl
sngure naq fheivivat oebgure; fubhyq V ol zl onfr qrfregvba yrnir gurz
rkcbfrq naq hacebgrpgrq gb gur znyvpr bs gur svraq jubz V unq yrg ybbfr
nzbat gurz?

Ng gurfr zbzragf V jrcg ovggreyl naq jvfurq gung crnpr jbhyq erivfvg zl
zvaq bayl gung V zvtug nssbeq gurz pbafbyngvba naq unccvarff.  Ohg gung
pbhyq abg or.  Erzbefr rkgvathvfurq rirel ubcr.  V unq orra gur nhgube
bs hanygrenoyr rivyf, naq V yvirq va qnvyl srne yrfg gur zbafgre jubz V
unq perngrq fubhyq crecrgengr fbzr arj jvpxrqarff.  V unq na bofpher
srryvat gung nyy jnf abg bire naq gung ur jbhyq fgvyy pbzzvg fbzr
fvtany pevzr, juvpu ol vgf rabezvgl fubhyq nyzbfg rssnpr gur
erpbyyrpgvba bs gur cnfg.  Gurer jnf nyjnlf fpbcr sbe srne fb ybat nf
nalguvat V ybirq erznvarq oruvaq.  Zl noubeerapr bs guvf svraq pnaabg
or pbaprvirq.  Jura V gubhtug bs uvz V tanfurq zl grrgu, zl rlrf orpnzr
vasynzrq, naq V neqragyl jvfurq gb rkgvathvfu gung yvsr juvpu V unq fb
gubhtugyrffyl orfgbjrq.  Jura V ersyrpgrq ba uvf pevzrf naq znyvpr, zl
ungerq naq eriratr ohefg nyy obhaqf bs zbqrengvba.  V jbhyq unir znqr n
cvytevzntr gb gur uvturfg crnx bs gur Naqrf, pbhyq V jura gurer unir
cerpvcvgngrq uvz gb gurve onfr.  V jvfurq gb frr uvz ntnva, gung V
zvtug jernx gur hgzbfg rkgrag bs noubeerapr ba uvf urnq naq niratr gur
qrnguf bs Jvyyvnz naq Whfgvar.  Bhe ubhfr jnf gur ubhfr bs zbheavat. Zl
sngure'f urnygu jnf qrrcyl funxra ol gur ubeebe bs gur erprag riragf.
Ryvmnorgu jnf fnq naq qrfcbaqvat; fur ab ybatre gbbx qryvtug va ure
beqvanel bpphcngvbaf; nyy cyrnfher frrzrq gb ure fnpevyrtr gbjneq gur
qrnq; rgreany jbr naq grnef fur gura gubhtug jnf gur whfg gevohgr fur
fubhyq cnl gb vaabprapr fb oynfgrq naq qrfgeblrq.  Fur jnf ab ybatre
gung unccl perngher jub va rneyvre lbhgu jnaqrerq jvgu zr ba gur onaxf
bs gur ynxr naq gnyxrq jvgu rpfgnfl bs bhe shgher cebfcrpgf.  Gur svefg
bs gubfr fbeebjf juvpu ner frag gb jrna hf sebz gur rnegu unq ivfvgrq
ure, naq vgf qvzzvat vasyhrapr dhrapurq ure qrnerfg fzvyrf.

"Jura V ersyrpg, zl qrne pbhfva," fnvq fur, "ba gur zvfrenoyr qrngu bs
Whfgvar Zbevgm, V ab ybatre frr gur jbeyq naq vgf jbexf nf gurl orsber
nccrnerq gb zr.  Orsber, V ybbxrq hcba gur nppbhagf bs ivpr naq
vawhfgvpr gung V ernq va obbxf be urneq sebz bguref nf gnyrf bs napvrag
qnlf be vzntvanel rivyf; ng yrnfg gurl jrer erzbgr naq zber snzvyvne gb
ernfba guna gb gur vzntvangvba; ohg abj zvfrel unf pbzr ubzr, naq zra
nccrne gb zr nf zbafgref guvefgvat sbe rnpu bgure'f oybbq.  Lrg V nz
pregnvayl hawhfg.  Rirelobql oryvrirq gung cbbe tvey gb or thvygl; naq
vs fur pbhyq unir pbzzvggrq gur pevzr sbe juvpu fur fhssrerq, nffherqyl
fur jbhyq unir orra gur zbfg qrcenirq bs uhzna perngherf.  Sbe gur fnxr
bs n srj wrjryf, gb unir zheqrerq gur fba bs ure orarsnpgbe naq sevraq,
n puvyq jubz fur unq ahefrq sebz vgf ovegu, naq nccrnerq gb ybir nf vs
vg unq orra ure bja!  V pbhyq abg pbafrag gb gur qrngu bs nal uhzna
orvat, ohg pregnvayl V fubhyq unir gubhtug fhpu n perngher hasvg gb
erznva va gur fbpvrgl bs zra.  Ohg fur jnf vaabprag.  V xabj, V srry
fur jnf vaabprag; lbh ner bs gur fnzr bcvavba, naq gung pbasvezf zr.
Nynf!  Ivpgbe, jura snyfrubbq pna ybbx fb yvxr gur gehgu, jub pna
nffher gurzfryirf bs pregnva unccvarff?  V srry nf vs V jrer jnyxvat ba
gur rqtr bs n cerpvcvpr, gbjneqf juvpu gubhfnaqf ner pebjqvat naq
raqrnibhevat gb cyhatr zr vagb gur nolff.  Jvyyvnz naq Whfgvar jrer
nffnffvangrq, naq gur zheqrere rfpncrf; ur jnyxf nobhg gur jbeyq serr,
naq creuncf erfcrpgrq.  Ohg rira vs V jrer pbaqrzarq gb fhssre ba gur
fpnssbyq sbe gur fnzr pevzrf, V jbhyq abg punatr cynprf jvgu fhpu n
jergpu."

V yvfgrarq gb guvf qvfpbhefr jvgu gur rkgerzrfg ntbal.  V, abg va qrrq,
ohg va rssrpg, jnf gur gehr zheqrere.  Ryvmnorgu ernq zl nathvfu va zl
pbhagranapr, naq xvaqyl gnxvat zl unaq, fnvq, "Zl qrnerfg sevraq, lbh
zhfg pnyz lbhefrys.  Gurfr riragf unir nssrpgrq zr, Tbq xabjf ubj
qrrcyl; ohg V nz abg fb jergpurq nf lbh ner.  Gurer vf na rkcerffvba bs
qrfcnve, naq fbzrgvzrf bs eriratr, va lbhe pbhagranapr gung znxrf zr
gerzoyr.  Qrne Ivpgbe, onavfu gurfr qnex cnffvbaf.  Erzrzore gur
sevraqf nebhaq lbh, jub prager nyy gurve ubcrf va lbh.  Unir jr ybfg
