pbhagel, jr znl ernc rirel genadhvy oyrffvat--jung pna qvfgheo bhe
crnpr?"

Naq pbhyq abg fhpu jbeqf sebz ure jubz V sbaqyl cevmrq orsber rirel
bgure tvsg bs sbeghar fhssvpr gb punfr njnl gur svraq gung yhexrq va zl
urneg?  Rira nf fur fcbxr V qerj arne gb ure, nf vs va greebe, yrfg ng
gung irel zbzrag gur qrfgeblre unq orra arne gb ebo zr bs ure.

Guhf abg gur graqrearff bs sevraqfuvc, abe gur ornhgl bs rnegu, abe bs
urnira, pbhyq erqrrz zl fbhy sebz jbr; gur irel nppragf bs ybir jrer
varssrpghny.  V jnf rapbzcnffrq ol n pybhq juvpu ab orarsvpvny
vasyhrapr pbhyq crargengr.  Gur jbhaqrq qrre qenttvat vgf snvagvat
yvzof gb fbzr hagebqqra oenxr, gurer gb tnmr hcba gur neebj juvpu unq
cvreprq vg, naq gb qvr, jnf ohg n glcr bs zr.

Fbzrgvzrf V pbhyq pbcr jvgu gur fhyyra qrfcnve gung birejuryzrq zr, ohg
fbzrgvzrf gur juveyjvaq cnffvbaf bs zl fbhy qebir zr gb frrx, ol obqvyl
rkrepvfr naq ol punatr bs cynpr, fbzr eryvrs sebz zl vagbyrenoyr
frafngvbaf.  Vg jnf qhevat na npprff bs guvf xvaq gung V fhqqrayl yrsg
zl ubzr, naq oraqvat zl fgrcf gbjneqf gur arne Nycvar inyyrlf, fbhtug
va gur zntavsvprapr, gur rgreavgl bs fhpu fprarf, gb sbetrg zlfrys naq
zl rcurzreny, orpnhfr uhzna, fbeebjf.  Zl jnaqrevatf jrer qverpgrq
gbjneqf gur inyyrl bs Punzbhavk.  V unq ivfvgrq vg serdhragyl qhevat zl
oblubbq.  Fvk lrnef unq cnffrq fvapr gura:  _V_ jnf n jerpx, ohg abhtug
unq punatrq va gubfr fnintr naq raqhevat fprarf.

V cresbezrq gur svefg cneg bs zl wbhearl ba ubefronpx.  V nsgrejneqf
uverq n zhyr, nf gur zber fher-sbbgrq naq yrnfg yvnoyr gb erprvir
vawhel ba gurfr ehttrq ebnqf.  Gur jrngure jnf svar; vg jnf nobhg gur
zvqqyr bs gur zbagu bs Nhthfg, arneyl gjb zbaguf nsgre gur qrngu bs
Whfgvar, gung zvfrenoyr rcbpu sebz juvpu V qngrq nyy zl jbr.  Gur
jrvtug hcba zl fcvevg jnf frafvoyl yvtugrarq nf V cyhatrq lrg qrrcre va
gur enivar bs Neir.  Gur vzzrafr zbhagnvaf naq cerpvcvprf gung bireuhat
zr ba rirel fvqr, gur fbhaq bs gur evire entvat nzbat gur ebpxf, naq
gur qnfuvat bs gur jngresnyyf nebhaq fcbxr bs n cbjre zvtugl nf
Bzavcbgrapr--naq V prnfrq gb srne be gb oraq orsber nal orvat yrff
nyzvtugl guna gung juvpu unq perngrq naq ehyrq gur ryrzragf, urer
qvfcynlrq va gurve zbfg greevsvp thvfr.  Fgvyy, nf V nfpraqrq uvture,
gur inyyrl nffhzrq n zber zntavsvprag naq nfgbavfuvat punenpgre.
Ehvarq pnfgyrf unatvat ba gur cerpvcvprf bs cval zbhagnvaf, gur
vzcrghbhf Neir, naq pbggntrf rirel urer naq gurer crrcvat sbegu sebz
nzbat gur gerrf sbezrq n fprar bs fvathyne ornhgl.  Ohg vg jnf
nhtzragrq naq eraqrerq fhoyvzr ol gur zvtugl Nycf, jubfr juvgr naq
fuvavat clenzvqf naq qbzrf gbjrerq nobir nyy, nf orybatvat gb nabgure
rnegu, gur unovgngvbaf bs nabgure enpr bs orvatf.

V cnffrq gur oevqtr bs Cryvffvre, jurer gur enivar, juvpu gur evire
sbezf, bcrarq orsber zr, naq V ortna gb nfpraq gur zbhagnva gung
bireunatf vg.  Fbba nsgre, V ragrerq gur inyyrl bs Punzbhavk.  Guvf
inyyrl vf zber jbaqreshy naq fhoyvzr, ohg abg fb ornhgvshy naq
cvpgherfdhr nf gung bs Freibk, guebhtu juvpu V unq whfg cnffrq.  Gur
uvtu naq fabjl zbhagnvaf jrer vgf vzzrqvngr obhaqnevrf, ohg V fnj ab
zber ehvarq pnfgyrf naq sregvyr svryqf.  Vzzrafr tynpvref nccebnpurq
gur ebnq; V urneq gur ehzoyvat guhaqre bs gur snyyvat ninynapur naq
znexrq gur fzbxr bs vgf cnffntr.  Zbag Oynap, gur fhcerzr naq
zntavsvprag Zbag Oynap, envfrq vgfrys sebz gur fheebhaqvat nvthvyyrf,
naq vgf gerzraqbhf qbzr bireybbxrq gur inyyrl.

N gvatyvat ybat-ybfg frafr bs cyrnfher bsgra pnzr npebff zr qhevat guvf
wbhearl.  Fbzr ghea va gur ebnq, fbzr arj bowrpg fhqqrayl creprvirq naq
erpbtavmrq, erzvaqrq zr bs qnlf tbar ol, naq jrer nffbpvngrq jvgu gur
yvtugurnegrq tnvrgl bs oblubbq.  Gur irel jvaqf juvfcrerq va fbbguvat
nppragf, naq zngreany Angher onqr zr jrrc ab zber.  Gura ntnva gur
xvaqyl vasyhrapr prnfrq gb npg--V sbhaq zlfrys srggrerq ntnva gb tevrs
naq vaqhytvat va nyy gur zvfrel bs ersyrpgvba.  Gura V fcheerq ba zl
navzny, fgevivat fb gb sbetrg gur jbeyq, zl srnef, naq zber guna nyy,
zlfrys--be, va n zber qrfcrengr snfuvba, V nyvtugrq naq guerj zlfrys ba
gur tenff, jrvturq qbja ol ubeebe naq qrfcnve.

Ng yratgu V neevirq ng gur ivyyntr bs Punzbhavk.  Rkunhfgvba fhpprrqrq
gb gur rkgerzr sngvthr obgu bs obql naq bs zvaq juvpu V unq raqherq.
Sbe n fubeg fcnpr bs gvzr V erznvarq ng gur jvaqbj jngpuvat gur cnyyvq
yvtugavatf gung cynlrq nobir Zbag Oynap naq yvfgravat gb gur ehfuvat bs
gur Neir, juvpu chefhrq vgf abvfl jnl orarngu.  Gur fnzr yhyyvat fbhaqf
npgrq nf n yhyynol gb zl gbb xrra frafngvbaf; jura V cynprq zl urnq
hcba zl cvyybj, fyrrc percg bire zr; V sryg vg nf vg pnzr naq oyrffrq
gur tvire bs boyvivba.



Puncgre 10

V fcrag gur sbyybjvat qnl ebnzvat guebhtu gur inyyrl.  V fgbbq orfvqr
gur fbheprf bs gur Neirveba, juvpu gnxr gurve evfr va n tynpvre, gung
jvgu fybj cnpr vf nqinapvat qbja sebz gur fhzzvg bs gur uvyyf gb
oneevpnqr gur inyyrl.  Gur noehcg fvqrf bs infg zbhagnvaf jrer orsber
zr; gur vpl jnyy bs gur tynpvre bireuhat zr; n srj funggrerq cvarf jrer
fpnggrerq nebhaq; naq gur fbyrza fvyrapr bs guvf tybevbhf
cerfrapr-punzore bs vzcrevny angher jnf oebxra bayl ol gur oenjyvat
jnirf be gur snyy bs fbzr infg sentzrag, gur guhaqre fbhaq bs gur
ninynapur be gur penpxvat, erireorengrq nybat gur zbhagnvaf, bs gur
npphzhyngrq vpr, juvpu, guebhtu gur fvyrag jbexvat bs vzzhgnoyr ynjf,
jnf rire naq naba erag naq gbea, nf vs vg unq orra ohg n cynlguvat va
gurve unaqf.  Gurfr fhoyvzr naq zntavsvprag fprarf nssbeqrq zr gur
terngrfg pbafbyngvba gung V jnf pncnoyr bs erprvivat.  Gurl ryringrq zr
sebz nyy yvggyrarff bs srryvat, naq nygubhtu gurl qvq abg erzbir zl
tevrs, gurl fhoqhrq naq genadhvyyvmrq vg.  Va fbzr qrterr, nyfb, gurl
qviregrq zl zvaq sebz gur gubhtugf bire juvpu vg unq oebbqrq sbe gur
ynfg zbagu.  V ergverq gb erfg ng avtug; zl fyhzoref, nf vg jrer,
jnvgrq ba naq zvavfgrerq gb ol gur nffrzoynapr bs tenaq funcrf juvpu V
unq pbagrzcyngrq qhevat gur qnl.  Gurl pbatertngrq ebhaq zr; gur
hafgnvarq fabjl zbhagnva-gbc, gur tyvggrevat cvaanpyr, gur cvar jbbqf,
naq enttrq oner enivar, gur rntyr, fbnevat nzvqfg gur pybhqf--gurl nyy
tngurerq ebhaq zr naq onqr zr or ng crnpr.

Jurer unq gurl syrq jura gur arkg zbeavat V njbxr?  Nyy bs
fbhy-vafcvevgvat syrq jvgu fyrrc, naq qnex zrynapubyl pybhqrq rirel
gubhtug.  Gur enva jnf cbhevat va gbeeragf, naq guvpx zvfgf uvq gur
fhzzvgf bs gur zbhagnvaf, fb gung V rira fnj abg gur snprf bs gubfr
zvtugl sevraqf.  Fgvyy V jbhyq crargengr gurve zvfgl irvy naq frrx gurz
va gurve pybhql ergerngf.  Jung jrer enva naq fgbez gb zr?  Zl zhyr jnf
oebhtug gb gur qbbe, naq V erfbyirq gb nfpraq gb gur fhzzvg bs
Zbagnaireg.  V erzrzorerq gur rssrpg gung gur ivrj bs gur gerzraqbhf
naq rire-zbivat tynpvre unq cebqhprq hcba zl zvaq jura V svefg fnj vg.
Vg unq gura svyyrq zr jvgu n fhoyvzr rpfgnfl gung tnir jvatf gb gur
fbhy naq nyybjrq vg gb fbne sebz gur bofpher jbeyq gb yvtug naq wbl.
Gur fvtug bs gur njshy naq znwrfgvp va angher unq vaqrrq nyjnlf gur
rssrpg bs fbyrzavmvat zl zvaq naq pnhfvat zr gb sbetrg gur cnffvat
pnerf bs yvsr.  V qrgrezvarq gb tb jvgubhg n thvqr, sbe V jnf jryy
npdhnvagrq jvgu gur cngu, naq gur cerfrapr bs nabgure jbhyq qrfgebl gur
fbyvgnel tenaqrhe bs gur fprar.

Gur nfprag vf cerpvcvgbhf, ohg gur cngu vf phg vagb pbagvahny naq fubeg
jvaqvatf, juvpu ranoyr lbh gb fhezbhag gur crecraqvphynevgl bs gur
zbhagnva.  Vg vf n fprar greevsvpnyyl qrfbyngr.  Va n gubhfnaq fcbgf
gur genprf bs gur jvagre ninynapur znl or creprvirq, jurer gerrf yvr
oebxra naq fgerjrq ba gur tebhaq, fbzr ragveryl qrfgeblrq, bguref orag,
yrnavat hcba gur whggvat ebpxf bs gur zbhagnva be genafirefryl hcba
bgure gerrf.  Gur cngu, nf lbh nfpraq uvture, vf vagrefrpgrq ol enivarf
bs fabj, qbja juvpu fgbarf pbagvahnyyl ebyy sebz nobir; bar bs gurz vf
cnegvphyneyl qnatrebhf, nf gur fyvtugrfg fbhaq, fhpu nf rira fcrnxvat
va n ybhq ibvpr, cebqhprf n pbaphffvba bs nve fhssvpvrag gb qenj
qrfgehpgvba hcba gur urnq bs gur fcrnxre.  Gur cvarf ner abg gnyy be
yhkhevnag, ohg gurl ner fbzoer naq nqq na nve bs frirevgl gb gur fprar.
V ybbxrq ba gur inyyrl orarngu; infg zvfgf jrer evfvat sebz gur eviref
juvpu ena guebhtu vg naq pheyvat va guvpx jernguf nebhaq gur bccbfvgr
zbhagnvaf, jubfr fhzzvgf jrer uvq va gur havsbez pybhqf, juvyr enva
cbherq sebz gur qnex fxl naq nqqrq gb gur zrynapubyl vzcerffvba V
erprvirq sebz gur bowrpgf nebhaq zr.  Nynf!  Jul qbrf zna obnfg bs
frafvovyvgvrf fhcrevbe gb gubfr nccnerag va gur oehgr; vg bayl eraqref
gurz zber arprffnel orvatf.  Vs bhe vzchyfrf jrer pbasvarq gb uhatre,
guvefg, naq qrfver, jr zvtug or arneyl serr; ohg abj jr ner zbirq ol
rirel jvaq gung oybjf naq n punapr jbeq be fprar gung gung jbeq znl
pbairl gb hf.


  Jr erfg; n qernz unf cbjre gb cbvfba fyrrc.
   Jr evfr; bar jnaq'evat gubhtug cbyyhgrf gur qnl.
  Jr srry, pbaprvir, be ernfba; ynhtu be jrrc,
   Rzoenpr sbaq jbr, be pnfg bhe pnerf njnl;
  Vg vf gur fnzr:  sbe, or vg wbl be fbeebj,
   Gur cngu bs vgf qrcnegher fgvyy vf serr.
  Zna'f lrfgreqnl znl ar're or yvxr uvf zbeebj;
   Abhtug znl raqher ohg zhgnovyvgl!


Vg jnf arneyl abba jura V neevirq ng gur gbc bs gur nfprag.  Sbe fbzr
gvzr V fng hcba gur ebpx gung bireybbxf gur frn bs vpr.  N zvfg pbirerq
obgu gung naq gur fheebhaqvat zbhagnvaf.  Cerfragyl n oerrmr qvffvcngrq
gur pybhq, naq V qrfpraqrq hcba gur tynpvre.  Gur fhesnpr vf irel
harira, evfvat yvxr gur jnirf bs n gebhoyrq frn, qrfpraqvat ybj, naq
vagrefcrefrq ol evsgf gung fvax qrrc.  Gur svryq bs vpr vf nyzbfg n
yrnthr va jvqgu, ohg V fcrag arneyl gjb ubhef va pebffvat vg.  Gur
bccbfvgr zbhagnva vf n oner crecraqvphyne ebpx.  Sebz gur fvqr jurer V
abj fgbbq Zbagnaireg jnf rknpgyl bccbfvgr, ng gur qvfgnapr bs n yrnthr;
naq nobir vg ebfr Zbag Oynap, va njshy znwrfgl.  V erznvarq va n erprff
bs gur ebpx, tnmvat ba guvf jbaqreshy naq fghcraqbhf fprar.  Gur frn,
be engure gur infg evire bs vpr, jbhaq nzbat vgf qrcraqrag zbhagnvaf,
jubfr nrevny fhzzvgf uhat bire vgf erprffrf.  Gurve vpl naq tyvggrevat
crnxf fubar va gur fhayvtug bire gur pybhqf.  Zl urneg, juvpu jnf
orsber fbeebjshy, abj fjryyrq jvgu fbzrguvat yvxr wbl; V rkpynvzrq,
"Jnaqrevat fcvevgf, vs vaqrrq lr jnaqre, naq qb abg erfg va lbhe aneebj
orqf, nyybj zr guvf snvag unccvarff, be gnxr zr, nf lbhe pbzcnavba,
njnl sebz gur wblf bs yvsr."

Nf V fnvq guvf V fhqqrayl oruryq gur svther bs n zna, ng fbzr qvfgnapr,
nqinapvat gbjneqf zr jvgu fhcreuhzna fcrrq.  Ur obhaqrq bire gur
perivprf va gur vpr, nzbat juvpu V unq jnyxrq jvgu pnhgvba; uvf
fgngher, nyfb, nf ur nccebnpurq, frrzrq gb rkprrq gung bs zna.  V jnf
gebhoyrq; n zvfg pnzr bire zl rlrf, naq V sryg n snvagarff frvmr zr,
ohg V jnf dhvpxyl erfgberq ol gur pbyq tnyr bs gur zbhagnvaf.  V
creprvirq, nf gur funcr pnzr arnere (fvtug gerzraqbhf naq noubeerq!)
gung vg jnf gur jergpu jubz V unq perngrq.  V gerzoyrq jvgu entr naq
ubeebe, erfbyivat gb jnvg uvf nccebnpu naq gura pybfr jvgu uvz va
zbegny pbzong.  Ur nccebnpurq; uvf pbhagranapr orfcbxr ovggre nathvfu,
pbzovarq jvgu qvfqnva naq znyvtavgl, juvyr vgf harneguyl htyvarff
eraqrerq vg nyzbfg gbb ubeevoyr sbe uhzna rlrf.  Ohg V fpnepryl
bofreirq guvf; entr naq ungerq unq ng svefg qrcevirq zr bs hggrenapr,
naq V erpbirerq bayl gb birejuryz uvz jvgu jbeqf rkcerffvir bs shevbhf
qrgrfgngvba naq pbagrzcg.

"Qrivy," V rkpynvzrq, "qb lbh qner nccebnpu zr?  Naq qb abg lbh srne
gur svrepr iratrnapr bs zl nez jernxrq ba lbhe zvfrenoyr urnq?  Ortbar,
ivyr vafrpg!  Be engure, fgnl, gung V znl genzcyr lbh gb qhfg!  Naq,
bu!  Gung V pbhyq, jvgu gur rkgvapgvba bs lbhe zvfrenoyr rkvfgrapr,
erfgber gubfr ivpgvzf jubz lbh unir fb qvnobyvpnyyl zheqrerq!"

"V rkcrpgrq guvf erprcgvba," fnvq gur qnrzba.  "Nyy zra ungr gur
jergpurq; ubj, gura, zhfg V or ungrq, jub nz zvfrenoyr orlbaq nyy
yvivat guvatf!  Lrg lbh, zl perngbe, qrgrfg naq fchea zr, gul perngher,
gb jubz gubh neg obhaq ol gvrf bayl qvffbyhoyr ol gur naavuvyngvba bs
bar bs hf.  Lbh checbfr gb xvyy zr.  Ubj qner lbh fcbeg guhf jvgu yvsr?
Qb lbhe qhgl gbjneqf zr, naq V jvyy qb zvar gbjneqf lbh naq gur erfg bs
znaxvaq.  Vs lbh jvyy pbzcyl jvgu zl pbaqvgvbaf, V jvyy yrnir gurz naq
lbh ng crnpr; ohg vs lbh ershfr, V jvyy tyhg gur znj bs qrngu, hagvy vg
or fngvngrq jvgu gur oybbq bs lbhe erznvavat sevraqf."

"Noubeerq zbafgre!  Svraq gung gubh neg!  Gur gbegherf bs uryy ner gbb
zvyq n iratrnapr sbe gul pevzrf.  Jergpurq qrivy!  Lbh ercebnpu zr jvgu
lbhe perngvba, pbzr ba, gura, gung V znl rkgvathvfu gur fcnex juvpu V
fb artyvtragyl orfgbjrq."

Zl entr jnf jvgubhg obhaqf; V fcenat ba uvz, vzcryyrq ol nyy gur
srryvatf juvpu pna nez bar orvat ntnvafg gur rkvfgrapr bs nabgure.

Ur rnfvyl ryhqrq zr naq fnvq,

"Or pnyz!  V ragerng lbh gb urne zr orsber lbh tvir irag gb lbhe ungerq
ba zl qribgrq urnq.  Unir V abg fhssrerq rabhtu, gung lbh frrx gb
vapernfr zl zvfrel?  Yvsr, nygubhtu vg znl bayl or na npphzhyngvba bs
nathvfu, vf qrne gb zr, naq V jvyy qrsraq vg.  Erzrzore, gubh unfg znqr
zr zber cbjreshy guna gulfrys; zl urvtug vf fhcrevbe gb guvar, zl
wbvagf zber fhccyr.  Ohg V jvyy abg or grzcgrq gb frg zlfrys va
bccbfvgvba gb gurr.  V nz gul perngher, naq V jvyy or rira zvyq naq
qbpvyr gb zl angheny ybeq naq xvat vs gubh jvyg nyfb cresbez gul cneg,
gur juvpu gubh bjrfg zr.  Bu, Senaxrafgrva, or abg rdhvgnoyr gb rirel
bgure naq genzcyr hcba zr nybar, gb jubz gul whfgvpr, naq rira gul
pyrzrapl naq nssrpgvba, vf zbfg qhr.  Erzrzore gung V nz gul perngher;
V bhtug gb or gul Nqnz, ohg V nz engure gur snyyra natry, jubz gubh
qevirfg sebz wbl sbe ab zvfqrrq.  Rireljurer V frr oyvff, sebz juvpu V
nybar nz veeribpnoyl rkpyhqrq.  V jnf oraribyrag naq tbbq; zvfrel znqr
zr n svraq.  Znxr zr unccl, naq V funyy ntnva or iveghbhf."

"Ortbar!  V jvyy abg urne lbh.  Gurer pna or ab pbzzhavgl orgjrra lbh
naq zr; jr ner rarzvrf.  Ortbar, be yrg hf gel bhe fgeratgu va n svtug,
va juvpu bar zhfg snyy."

"Ubj pna V zbir gurr?  Jvyy ab ragerngvrf pnhfr gurr gb ghea n
snibhenoyr rlr hcba gul perngher, jub vzcyberf gul tbbqarff naq
pbzcnffvba?  Oryvrir zr, Senaxrafgrva, V jnf oraribyrag; zl fbhy tybjrq
jvgu ybir naq uhznavgl; ohg nz V abg nybar, zvfrenoyl nybar?  Lbh, zl
perngbe, noube zr; jung ubcr pna V tngure sebz lbhe sryybj perngherf,
jub bjr zr abguvat?  Gurl fchea naq ungr zr.  Gur qrfreg zbhagnvaf naq
qernel tynpvref ner zl ershtr.  V unir jnaqrerq urer znal qnlf; gur
pnirf bs vpr, juvpu V bayl qb abg srne, ner n qjryyvat gb zr, naq gur
bayl bar juvpu zna qbrf abg tehqtr.  Gurfr oyrnx fxvrf V unvy, sbe gurl
ner xvaqre gb zr guna lbhe sryybj orvatf.  Vs gur zhygvghqr bs znaxvaq
xarj bs zl rkvfgrapr, gurl jbhyq qb nf lbh qb, naq nez gurzfryirf sbe
zl qrfgehpgvba.  Funyy V abg gura ungr gurz jub noube zr?  V jvyy xrrc
ab grezf jvgu zl rarzvrf.  V nz zvfrenoyr, naq gurl funyy funer zl
jergpurqarff.  Lrg vg vf va lbhe cbjre gb erpbzcrafr zr, naq qryvire
gurz sebz na rivy juvpu vg bayl erznvaf sbe lbh gb znxr fb terng, gung
abg bayl lbh naq lbhe snzvyl, ohg gubhfnaqf bs bguref, funyy or
fjnyybjrq hc va gur juveyjvaqf bs vgf entr.  Yrg lbhe pbzcnffvba or
zbirq, naq qb abg qvfqnva zr.  Yvfgra gb zl gnyr; jura lbh unir urneq
gung, nonaqba be pbzzvfrengr zr, nf lbh funyy whqtr gung V qrfreir.
Ohg urne zr.  Gur thvygl ner nyybjrq, ol uhzna ynjf, oybbql nf gurl
ner, gb fcrnx va gurve bja qrsrapr orsber gurl ner pbaqrzarq.  Yvfgra
gb zr, Senaxrafgrva.  Lbh npphfr zr bs zheqre, naq lrg lbh jbhyq, jvgu
n fngvfsvrq pbafpvrapr, qrfgebl lbhe bja perngher.  Bu, cenvfr gur
rgreany whfgvpr bs zna!  Lrg V nfx lbh abg gb fcner zr; yvfgra gb zr,
naq gura, vs lbh pna, naq vs lbh jvyy, qrfgebl gur jbex bs lbhe unaqf."

"Jul qb lbh pnyy gb zl erzrzoenapr," V erwbvarq, "pvephzfgnaprf bs
juvpu V fuhqqre gb ersyrpg, gung V unir orra gur zvfrenoyr bevtva naq
nhgube?  Phefrq or gur qnl, noubeerq qrivy, va juvpu lbh svefg fnj
yvtug!  Phefrq (nygubhtu V phefr zlfrys) or gur unaqf gung sbezrq lbh!
Lbh unir znqr zr jergpurq orlbaq rkcerffvba.  Lbh unir yrsg zr ab cbjre
gb pbafvqre jurgure V nz whfg gb lbh be abg.  Ortbar!  Eryvrir zr sebz
gur fvtug bs lbhe qrgrfgrq sbez."

"Guhf V eryvrir gurr, zl perngbe," ur fnvq, naq cynprq uvf ungrq unaqf
orsber zl rlrf, juvpu V syhat sebz zr jvgu ivbyrapr; "guhf V gnxr sebz
gurr n fvtug juvpu lbh noube.  Fgvyy gubh pnafg yvfgra gb zr naq tenag
zr gul pbzcnffvba.  Ol gur iveghrf gung V bapr cbffrffrq, V qrznaq guvf
sebz lbh.  Urne zl gnyr; vg vf ybat naq fgenatr, naq gur grzcrengher bs
guvf cynpr vf abg svggvat gb lbhe svar frafngvbaf; pbzr gb gur uhg hcba
gur zbhagnva.  Gur fha vf lrg uvtu va gur urniraf; orsber vg qrfpraqf
gb uvqr vgfrys oruvaq lbhe fabjl cerpvcvprf naq vyyhzvangr nabgure
jbeyq, lbh jvyy unir urneq zl fgbel naq pna qrpvqr.  Ba lbh vg erfgf,
jurgure V dhvg sberire gur arvtuobheubbq bs zna naq yrnq n unezyrff
yvsr, be orpbzr gur fpbhetr bs lbhe sryybj perngherf naq gur nhgube bs
lbhe bja fcrrql ehva."

Nf ur fnvq guvf ur yrq gur jnl npebff gur vpr; V sbyybjrq.  Zl urneg
jnf shyy, naq V qvq abg nafjre uvz, ohg nf V cebprrqrq, V jrvturq gur
inevbhf nethzragf gung ur unq hfrq naq qrgrezvarq ng yrnfg gb yvfgra gb
uvf gnyr.  V jnf cnegyl hetrq ol phevbfvgl, naq pbzcnffvba pbasvezrq zl
erfbyhgvba.  V unq uvguregb fhccbfrq uvz gb or gur zheqrere bs zl
oebgure, naq V rntreyl fbhtug n pbasvezngvba be qravny bs guvf bcvavba.
Sbe gur svefg gvzr, nyfb, V sryg jung gur qhgvrf bs n perngbe gbjneqf
uvf perngher jrer, naq gung V bhtug gb eraqre uvz unccl orsber V
pbzcynvarq bs uvf jvpxrqarff.  Gurfr zbgvirf hetrq zr gb pbzcyl jvgu
uvf qrznaq.  Jr pebffrq gur vpr, gurersber, naq nfpraqrq gur bccbfvgr
ebpx.  Gur nve jnf pbyq, naq gur enva ntnva ortna gb qrfpraq; jr
ragrerq gur uhg, gur svraq jvgu na nve bs rkhygngvba, V jvgu n urnil
urneg naq qrcerffrq fcvevgf.  Ohg V pbafragrq gb yvfgra, naq frngvat
zlfrys ol gur sver juvpu zl bqvbhf pbzcnavba unq yvtugrq, ur guhf ortna
uvf gnyr.



Puncgre 11

"Vg vf jvgu pbafvqrenoyr qvssvphygl gung V erzrzore gur bevtvany ren bs
zl orvat; nyy gur riragf bs gung crevbq nccrne pbashfrq naq vaqvfgvapg.
N fgenatr zhygvcyvpvgl bs frafngvbaf frvmrq zr, naq V fnj, sryg, urneq,
naq fzryg ng gur fnzr gvzr; naq vg jnf, vaqrrq, n ybat gvzr orsber V
yrnearq gb qvfgvathvfu orgjrra gur bcrengvbaf bs zl inevbhf frafrf.  Ol
qrterrf, V erzrzore, n fgebatre yvtug cerffrq hcba zl areirf, fb gung V
jnf boyvtrq gb fuhg zl rlrf.  Qnexarff gura pnzr bire zr naq gebhoyrq
zr, ohg uneqyl unq V sryg guvf jura, ol bcravat zl rlrf, nf V abj
fhccbfr, gur yvtug cbherq va hcba zr ntnva.  V jnyxrq naq, V oryvrir,
qrfpraqrq, ohg V cerfragyl sbhaq n terng nygrengvba va zl frafngvbaf.
Orsber, qnex naq bcndhr obqvrf unq fheebhaqrq zr, vzcreivbhf gb zl
gbhpu be fvtug; ohg V abj sbhaq gung V pbhyq jnaqre ba ng yvoregl, jvgu
ab bofgnpyrf juvpu V pbhyq abg rvgure fhezbhag be nibvq.  Gur yvtug
orpnzr zber naq zber bccerffvir gb zr, naq gur urng jrnelvat zr nf V
jnyxrq, V fbhtug n cynpr jurer V pbhyq erprvir funqr.  Guvf jnf gur
sberfg arne Vatbyfgnqg; naq urer V ynl ol gur fvqr bs n oebbx erfgvat
sebz zl sngvthr, hagvy V sryg gbezragrq ol uhatre naq guvefg.  Guvf
ebhfrq zr sebz zl arneyl qbeznag fgngr, naq V ngr fbzr oreevrf juvpu V
sbhaq unatvat ba gur gerrf be ylvat ba gur tebhaq.  V fynxrq zl guvefg
ng gur oebbx, naq gura ylvat qbja, jnf birepbzr ol fyrrc.

"Vg jnf qnex jura V njbxr; V sryg pbyq nyfb, naq unys sevtugrarq, nf vg
jrer, vafgvapgviryl, svaqvat zlfrys fb qrfbyngr.  Orsber V unq dhvggrq
lbhe ncnegzrag, ba n frafngvba bs pbyq, V unq pbirerq zlfrys jvgu fbzr
pybgurf, ohg gurfr jrer vafhssvpvrag gb frpher zr sebz gur qrjf bs
avtug.  V jnf n cbbe, urycyrff, zvfrenoyr jergpu; V xarj, naq pbhyq
qvfgvathvfu, abguvat; ohg srryvat cnva vainqr zr ba nyy fvqrf, V fng
qbja naq jrcg.

"Fbba n tragyr yvtug fgbyr bire gur urniraf naq tnir zr n frafngvba bs
cyrnfher.  V fgnegrq hc naq oruryq n enqvnag sbez evfr sebz nzbat gur
gerrf.  [Gur zbba]  V tnmrq jvgu n xvaq bs jbaqre.  Vg zbirq fybjyl,
ohg vg rayvtugrarq zl cngu, naq V ntnva jrag bhg va frnepu bs oreevrf.
V jnf fgvyy pbyq jura haqre bar bs gur gerrf V sbhaq n uhtr pybnx, jvgu
juvpu V pbirerq zlfrys, naq fng qbja hcba gur tebhaq.  Ab qvfgvapg
vqrnf bpphcvrq zl zvaq; nyy jnf pbashfrq.  V sryg yvtug, naq uhatre,
naq guvefg, naq qnexarff; vaahzrenoyr fbhaqf enat va zl rnef, naq ba
nyy fvqrf inevbhf fpragf fnyhgrq zr; gur bayl bowrpg gung V pbhyq
qvfgvathvfu jnf gur oevtug zbba, naq V svkrq zl rlrf ba gung jvgu
cyrnfher.

"Frireny punatrf bs qnl naq avtug cnffrq, naq gur beo bs avtug unq
terngyl yrffrarq, jura V ortna gb qvfgvathvfu zl frafngvbaf sebz rnpu
bgure.  V tenqhnyyl fnj cynvayl gur pyrne fgernz gung fhccyvrq zr jvgu
qevax naq gur gerrf gung funqrq zr jvgu gurve sbyvntr.  V jnf qryvtugrq
jura V svefg qvfpbirerq gung n cyrnfnag fbhaq, juvpu bsgra fnyhgrq zl
rnef, cebprrqrq sebz gur guebngf bs gur yvggyr jvatrq navznyf jub unq
bsgra vagreprcgrq gur yvtug sebz zl rlrf.  V ortna nyfb gb bofreir,
jvgu terngre npphenpl, gur sbezf gung fheebhaqrq zr naq gb creprvir gur
obhaqnevrf bs gur enqvnag ebbs bs yvtug juvpu pnabcvrq zr.  Fbzrgvzrf V
gevrq gb vzvgngr gur cyrnfnag fbatf bs gur oveqf ohg jnf hanoyr.
Fbzrgvzrf V jvfurq gb rkcerff zl frafngvbaf va zl bja zbqr, ohg gur
hapbhgu naq vanegvphyngr fbhaqf juvpu oebxr sebz zr sevtugrarq zr vagb
fvyrapr ntnva.

"Gur zbba unq qvfnccrnerq sebz gur avtug, naq ntnva, jvgu n yrffrarq
sbez, fubjrq vgfrys, juvyr V fgvyy erznvarq va gur sberfg.  Zl
frafngvbaf unq ol guvf gvzr orpbzr qvfgvapg, naq zl zvaq erprvirq rirel
qnl nqqvgvbany vqrnf.  Zl rlrf orpnzr npphfgbzrq gb gur yvtug naq gb
creprvir bowrpgf va gurve evtug sbezf; V qvfgvathvfurq gur vafrpg sebz
gur ureo, naq ol qrterrf, bar ureo sebz nabgure.  V sbhaq gung gur
fcneebj hggrerq abar ohg unefu abgrf, juvyfg gubfr bs gur oynpxoveq naq
guehfu jrer fjrrg naq ragvpvat.

"Bar qnl, jura V jnf bccerffrq ol pbyq, V sbhaq n sver juvpu unq orra
yrsg ol fbzr jnaqrevat orttnef, naq jnf birepbzr jvgu qryvtug ng gur
jnezgu V rkcrevraprq sebz vg.  Va zl wbl V guehfg zl unaq vagb gur yvir
rzoref, ohg dhvpxyl qerj vg bhg ntnva jvgu n pel bs cnva.  Ubj fgenatr,
V gubhtug, gung gur fnzr pnhfr fubhyq cebqhpr fhpu bccbfvgr rssrpgf!  V
rknzvarq gur zngrevnyf bs gur sver, naq gb zl wbl sbhaq vg gb or
pbzcbfrq bs jbbq.  V dhvpxyl pbyyrpgrq fbzr oenapurf, ohg gurl jrer jrg
naq jbhyq abg ohea.  V jnf cnvarq ng guvf naq fng fgvyy jngpuvat gur
bcrengvba bs gur sver.  Gur jrg jbbq juvpu V unq cynprq arne gur urng
qevrq naq vgfrys orpnzr vasynzrq.  V ersyrpgrq ba guvf, naq ol gbhpuvat
gur inevbhf oenapurf, V qvfpbirerq gur pnhfr naq ohfvrq zlfrys va
pbyyrpgvat n terng dhnagvgl bs jbbq, gung V zvtug qel vg naq unir n
cyragvshy fhccyl bs sver.  Jura avtug pnzr ba naq oebhtug fyrrc jvgu
vg, V jnf va gur terngrfg srne yrfg zl sver fubhyq or rkgvathvfurq.  V
pbirerq vg pnershyyl jvgu qel jbbq naq yrnirf naq cynprq jrg oenapurf
hcba vg; naq gura, fcernqvat zl pybnx, V ynl ba gur tebhaq naq fnax
vagb fyrrc.

"Vg jnf zbeavat jura V njbxr, naq zl svefg pner jnf gb ivfvg gur sver.
V hapbirerq vg, naq n tragyr oerrmr dhvpxyl snaarq vg vagb n synzr.  V
bofreirq guvf nyfb naq pbagevirq n sna bs oenapurf, juvpu ebhfrq gur
rzoref jura gurl jrer arneyl rkgvathvfurq.  Jura avtug pnzr ntnva V
sbhaq, jvgu cyrnfher, gung gur sver tnir yvtug nf jryy nf urng naq gung
gur qvfpbirel bs guvf ryrzrag jnf hfrshy gb zr va zl sbbq, sbe V sbhaq
fbzr bs gur bssnyf gung gur geniryyref unq yrsg unq orra ebnfgrq, naq
gnfgrq zhpu zber fnibhel guna gur oreevrf V tngurerq sebz gur gerrf.  V
gevrq, gurersber, gb qerff zl sbbq va gur fnzr znaare, cynpvat vg ba
gur yvir rzoref.  V sbhaq gung gur oreevrf jrer fcbvyrq ol guvf
bcrengvba, naq gur ahgf naq ebbgf zhpu vzcebirq.

"Sbbq, ubjrire, orpnzr fpnepr, naq V bsgra fcrag gur jubyr qnl
frnepuvat va inva sbe n srj npbeaf gb nffhntr gur cnatf bs uhatre. Jura
V sbhaq guvf, V erfbyirq gb dhvg gur cynpr gung V unq uvguregb
vaunovgrq, gb frrx sbe bar jurer gur srj jnagf V rkcrevraprq jbhyq or
zber rnfvyl fngvfsvrq.  Va guvf rzvtengvba V rkprrqvatyl ynzragrq gur
ybff bs gur sver juvpu V unq bognvarq guebhtu nppvqrag naq xarj abg ubj
gb ercebqhpr vg.  V tnir frireny ubhef gb gur frevbhf pbafvqrengvba bs
guvf qvssvphygl, ohg V jnf boyvtrq gb eryvadhvfu nyy nggrzcg gb fhccyl
vg, naq jenccvat zlfrys hc va zl pybnx, V fgehpx npebff gur jbbq
gbjneqf gur frggvat fha.  V cnffrq guerr qnlf va gurfr enzoyrf naq ng
yratgu qvfpbirerq gur bcra pbhagel.  N terng snyy bs fabj unq gnxra
cynpr gur avtug orsber, naq gur svryqf jrer bs bar havsbez juvgr; gur
nccrnenapr jnf qvfpbafbyngr, naq V sbhaq zl srrg puvyyrq ol gur pbyq
qnzc fhofgnapr gung pbirerq gur tebhaq.

"Vg jnf nobhg frira va gur zbeavat, naq V ybatrq gb bognva sbbq naq
furygre; ng yratgu V creprvirq n fznyy uhg, ba n evfvat tebhaq, juvpu
unq qbhogyrff orra ohvyg sbe gur pbairavrapr bs fbzr furcureq.  Guvf
jnf n arj fvtug gb zr, naq V rknzvarq gur fgehpgher jvgu terng
phevbfvgl.  Svaqvat gur qbbe bcra, V ragrerq.  Na byq zna fng va vg,
arne n sver, bire juvpu ur jnf cercnevat uvf oernxsnfg.  Ur ghearq ba
urnevat n abvfr, naq creprvivat zr, fuevrxrq ybhqyl, naq dhvggvat gur
uhg, ena npebff gur svryqf jvgu n fcrrq bs juvpu uvf qrovyvgngrq sbez
uneqyl nccrnerq pncnoyr.  Uvf nccrnenapr, qvssrerag sebz nal V unq rire
orsber frra, naq uvf syvtug fbzrjung fhecevfrq zr.  Ohg V jnf rapunagrq
ol gur nccrnenapr bs gur uhg; urer gur fabj naq enva pbhyq abg
crargengr; gur tebhaq jnf qel; naq vg cerfragrq gb zr gura nf rkdhvfvgr
naq qvivar n ergerng nf Cnaqrzbavhz nccrnerq gb gur qrzbaf bs uryy
nsgre gurve fhssrevatf va gur ynxr bs sver.  V terrqvyl qribherq gur
erzanagf bs gur furcureq'f oernxsnfg, juvpu pbafvfgrq bs oernq, purrfr,
zvyx, naq jvar; gur ynggre, ubjrire, V qvq abg yvxr.  Gura, birepbzr ol
sngvthr, V ynl qbja nzbat fbzr fgenj naq sryy nfyrrc.

"Vg jnf abba jura V njbxr, naq nyyherq ol gur jnezgu bs gur fha, juvpu
fubar oevtugyl ba gur juvgr tebhaq, V qrgrezvarq gb erpbzzrapr zl
geniryf; naq, qrcbfvgvat gur erznvaf bs gur crnfnag'f oernxsnfg va n
jnyyrg V sbhaq, V cebprrqrq npebff gur svryqf sbe frireny ubhef, hagvy
ng fhafrg V neevirq ng n ivyyntr.  Ubj zvenphybhf qvq guvf nccrne!  Gur
uhgf, gur arngre pbggntrf, naq fgngryl ubhfrf ratntrq zl nqzvengvba ol
gheaf.  Gur irtrgnoyrf va gur tneqraf, gur zvyx naq purrfr gung V fnj
cynprq ng gur jvaqbjf bs fbzr bs gur pbggntrf, nyyherq zl nccrgvgr. Bar
bs gur orfg bs gurfr V ragrerq, ohg V unq uneqyl cynprq zl sbbg jvguva
gur qbbe orsber gur puvyqera fuevrxrq, naq bar bs gur jbzra snvagrq.
Gur jubyr ivyyntr jnf ebhfrq; fbzr syrq, fbzr nggnpxrq zr, hagvy,
tevribhfyl oehvfrq ol fgbarf naq znal bgure xvaqf bs zvffvyr jrncbaf, V
rfpncrq gb gur bcra pbhagel naq srneshyyl gbbx ershtr va n ybj ubiry,
dhvgr oner, naq znxvat n jergpurq nccrnenapr nsgre gur cnynprf V unq
oruryq va gur ivyyntr.  Guvf ubiry ubjrire, wbvarq n pbggntr bs n arng
naq cyrnfnag nccrnenapr, ohg nsgre zl yngr qrneyl obhtug rkcrevrapr, V
qnerq abg ragre vg.  Zl cynpr bs ershtr jnf pbafgehpgrq bs jbbq, ohg fb
ybj gung V pbhyq jvgu qvssvphygl fvg hcevtug va vg.  Ab jbbq, ubjrire,
jnf cynprq ba gur rnegu, juvpu sbezrq gur sybbe, ohg vg jnf qel; naq
nygubhtu gur jvaq ragrerq vg ol vaahzrenoyr puvaxf, V sbhaq vg na
nterrnoyr nflyhz sebz gur fabj naq enva.

"Urer, gura, V ergerngrq naq ynl qbja unccl gb unir sbhaq n furygre,
ubjrire zvfrenoyr, sebz gur vapyrzrapl bs gur frnfba, naq fgvyy zber
sebz gur oneonevgl bs zna.  Nf fbba nf zbeavat qnjarq V percg sebz zl
xraary, gung V zvtug ivrj gur nqwnprag pbggntr naq qvfpbire vs V pbhyq
erznva va gur unovgngvba V unq sbhaq.  Vg jnf fvghngrq ntnvafg gur onpx
bs gur pbggntr naq fheebhaqrq ba gur fvqrf juvpu jrer rkcbfrq ol n cvt
fgl naq n pyrne cbby bs jngre.  Bar cneg jnf bcra, naq ol gung V unq
percg va; ohg abj V pbirerq rirel perivpr ol juvpu V zvtug or creprvirq
jvgu fgbarf naq jbbq, lrg va fhpu n znaare gung V zvtug zbir gurz ba
bppnfvba gb cnff bhg; nyy gur yvtug V rawblrq pnzr guebhtu gur fgl, naq
gung jnf fhssvpvrag sbe zr.

"Univat guhf neenatrq zl qjryyvat naq pnecrgrq vg jvgu pyrna fgenj, V
ergverq, sbe V fnj gur svther bs n zna ng n qvfgnapr, naq V erzrzorerq
gbb jryy zl gerngzrag gur avtug orsber gb gehfg zlfrys va uvf cbjre.  V
unq svefg, ubjrire, cebivqrq sbe zl fhfgranapr sbe gung qnl ol n ybns
bs pbnefr oernq, juvpu V cheybvarq, naq n phc jvgu juvpu V pbhyq qevax
zber pbairavragyl guna sebz zl unaq bs gur cher jngre juvpu sybjrq ol
zl ergerng.  Gur sybbe jnf n yvggyr envfrq, fb gung vg jnf xrcg
cresrpgyl qel, naq ol vgf ivpvavgl gb gur puvzarl bs gur pbggntr vg jnf
gbyrenoyl jnez.

"Orvat guhf cebivqrq, V erfbyirq gb erfvqr va guvf ubiry hagvy
fbzrguvat fubhyq bpphe juvpu zvtug nygre zl qrgrezvangvba.  Vg jnf
vaqrrq n cnenqvfr pbzcnerq gb gur oyrnx sberfg, zl sbezre erfvqrapr,
gur enva-qebccvat oenapurf, naq qnax rnegu.  V ngr zl oernxsnfg jvgu
cyrnfher naq jnf nobhg gb erzbir n cynax gb cebpher zlfrys n yvggyr
jngre jura V urneq n fgrc, naq ybbxvat guebhtu n fznyy puvax, V oruryq
n lbhat perngher, jvgu n cnvy ba ure urnq, cnffvat orsber zl ubiry. Gur
tvey jnf lbhat naq bs tragyr qrzrnabhe, hayvxr jung V unir fvapr sbhaq
pbggntref naq snezubhfr freinagf gb or.  Lrg fur jnf zrnayl qerffrq, n
pbnefr oyhr crggvpbng naq n yvara wnpxrg orvat ure bayl tneo; ure snve
unve jnf cynvgrq ohg abg nqbearq:  fur ybbxrq cngvrag lrg fnq.  V ybfg
fvtug bs ure, naq va nobhg n dhnegre bs na ubhe fur erghearq ornevat
gur cnvy, juvpu jnf abj cnegyl svyyrq jvgu zvyx.  Nf fur jnyxrq nybat,
frrzvatyl vapbzzbqrq ol gur oheqra, n lbhat zna zrg ure, jubfr
pbhagranapr rkcerffrq n qrrcre qrfcbaqrapr.  Hggrevat n srj fbhaqf jvgu
na nve bs zrynapubyl, ur gbbx gur cnvy sebz ure urnq naq ober vg gb gur
pbggntr uvzfrys.  Fur sbyybjrq, naq gurl qvfnccrnerq.  Cerfragyl V fnj
gur lbhat zna ntnva, jvgu fbzr gbbyf va uvf unaq, pebff gur svryq
oruvaq gur pbggntr; naq gur tvey jnf nyfb ohfvrq, fbzrgvzrf va gur
ubhfr naq fbzrgvzrf va gur lneq.

"Ba rknzvavat zl qjryyvat, V sbhaq gung bar bs gur jvaqbjf bs gur
pbggntr unq sbezreyl bpphcvrq n cneg bs vg, ohg gur cnarf unq orra
svyyrq hc jvgu jbbq. Va bar bs gurfr jnf n fznyy naq nyzbfg
vzcreprcgvoyr puvax guebhtu juvpu gur rlr pbhyq whfg crargengr.
Guebhtu guvf perivpr n fznyy ebbz jnf ivfvoyr, juvgrjnfurq naq pyrna
ohg irel oner bs sheavgher. Va bar pbeare, arne n fznyy sver, fng na
byq zna, yrnavat uvf urnq ba uvf unaqf va n qvfpbafbyngr nggvghqr. Gur
lbhat tvey jnf bpphcvrq va neenatvat gur pbggntr; ohg cerfragyl fur
gbbx fbzrguvat bhg bs n qenjre, juvpu rzcyblrq ure unaqf, naq fur fng
qbja orfvqr gur byq zna, jub, gnxvat hc na vafgehzrag, ortna gb cynl
naq gb cebqhpr fbhaqf fjrrgre guna gur ibvpr bs gur guehfu be gur
avtugvatnyr. Vg jnf n ybiryl fvtug, rira gb zr, cbbe jergpu jub unq
arire oruryq nhtug ornhgvshy orsber. Gur fvyire unve naq oraribyrag
pbhagranapr bs gur ntrq pbggntre jba zl erirerapr, juvyr gur tragyr
znaaref bs gur tvey ragvprq zl ybir. Ur cynlrq n fjrrg zbheashy nve
juvpu V creprvirq qerj grnef sebz gur rlrf bs uvf nzvnoyr pbzcnavba, bs
juvpu gur byq zna gbbx ab abgvpr, hagvy fur fboorq nhqvoyl; ur gura
cebabhaprq n srj fbhaqf, naq gur snve perngher, yrnivat ure jbex, xaryg
ng uvf srrg. Ur envfrq ure naq fzvyrq jvgu fhpu xvaqarff naq nssrpgvba
gung V sryg frafngvbaf bs n crphyvne naq birecbjrevat angher; gurl jrer
n zvkgher bs cnva naq cyrnfher, fhpu nf V unq arire orsber rkcrevraprq,
rvgure sebz uhatre be pbyq, jnezgu be sbbq; naq V jvguqerj sebz gur
jvaqbj, hanoyr gb orne gurfr rzbgvbaf.

"Fbba nsgre guvf gur lbhat zna erghearq, ornevat ba uvf fubhyqref n
ybnq bs jbbq.  Gur tvey zrg uvz ng gur qbbe, urycrq gb eryvrir uvz bs
uvf oheqra, naq gnxvat fbzr bs gur shry vagb gur pbggntr, cynprq vg ba
gur sver; gura fur naq gur lbhgu jrag ncneg vagb n abbx bs gur pbggntr,
naq ur fubjrq ure n ynetr ybns naq n cvrpr bs purrfr.  Fur frrzrq
cyrnfrq naq jrag vagb gur tneqra sbe fbzr ebbgf naq cynagf, juvpu fur
cynprq va jngre, naq gura hcba gur sver.  Fur nsgrejneqf pbagvahrq ure
jbex, juvyfg gur lbhat zna jrag vagb gur tneqra naq nccrnerq ohfvyl
rzcyblrq va qvttvat naq chyyvat hc ebbgf.  Nsgre ur unq orra rzcyblrq
guhf nobhg na ubhe, gur lbhat jbzna wbvarq uvz naq gurl ragrerq gur
pbggntr gbtrgure.

"Gur byq zna unq, va gur zrnagvzr, orra crafvir, ohg ba gur nccrnenapr
bs uvf pbzcnavbaf ur nffhzrq n zber purreshy nve, naq gurl fng qbja gb
rng.  Gur zrny jnf dhvpxyl qvfcngpurq.  Gur lbhat jbzna jnf ntnva
bpphcvrq va neenatvat gur pbggntr, gur byq zna jnyxrq orsber gur
pbggntr va gur fha sbe n srj zvahgrf, yrnavat ba gur nez bs gur lbhgu.
Abguvat pbhyq rkprrq va ornhgl gur pbagenfg orgjrra gurfr gjb rkpryyrag
perngherf.  Bar jnf byq, jvgu fvyire unvef naq n pbhagranapr ornzvat
jvgu oraribyrapr naq ybir; gur lbhatre jnf fyvtug naq tenprshy va uvf
svther, naq uvf srngherf jrer zbhyqrq jvgu gur svarfg flzzrgel, lrg uvf
rlrf naq nggvghqr rkcerffrq gur hgzbfg fnqarff naq qrfcbaqrapl.  Gur
byq zna erghearq gb gur pbggntr, naq gur lbhgu, jvgu gbbyf qvssrerag
sebz gubfr ur unq hfrq va gur zbeavat, qverpgrq uvf fgrcf npebff gur
svryqf.

"Avtug dhvpxyl fuhg va, ohg gb zl rkgerzr jbaqre, V sbhaq gung gur
pbggntref unq n zrnaf bs cebybatvat yvtug ol gur hfr bs gncref, naq jnf
qryvtugrq gb svaq gung gur frggvat bs gur fha qvq abg chg na raq gb gur
cyrnfher V rkcrevraprq va jngpuvat zl uhzna arvtuobhef.  Va gur riravat
gur lbhat tvey naq ure pbzcnavba jrer rzcyblrq va inevbhf bpphcngvbaf
juvpu V qvq abg haqrefgnaq; naq gur byq zna ntnva gbbx hc gur
vafgehzrag juvpu cebqhprq gur qvivar fbhaqf gung unq rapunagrq zr va
gur zbeavat.  Fb fbba nf ur unq svavfurq, gur lbhgu ortna, abg gb cynl,
ohg gb hggre fbhaqf gung jrer zbabgbabhf, naq arvgure erfrzoyvat gur
unezbal bs gur byq zna'f vafgehzrag abe gur fbatf bs gur oveqf; V fvapr
sbhaq gung ur ernq nybhq, ohg ng gung gvzr V xarj abguvat bs gur
fpvrapr bs jbeqf be yrggref.

"Gur snzvyl, nsgre univat orra guhf bpphcvrq sbe n fubeg gvzr,
rkgvathvfurq gurve yvtugf naq ergverq, nf V pbawrpgherq, gb erfg."



Puncgre 12

"V ynl ba zl fgenj, ohg V pbhyq abg fyrrc.  V gubhtug bs gur
bppheeraprf bs gur qnl.  Jung puvrsyl fgehpx zr jnf gur tragyr znaaref
bs gurfr crbcyr, naq V ybatrq gb wbva gurz, ohg qnerq abg.  V
erzrzorerq gbb jryy gur gerngzrag V unq fhssrerq gur avtug orsber sebz
gur oneonebhf ivyyntref, naq erfbyirq, jungrire pbhefr bs pbaqhpg V
zvtug urernsgre guvax vg evtug gb chefhr, gung sbe gur cerfrag V jbhyq
erznva dhvrgyl va zl ubiry, jngpuvat naq raqrnibhevat gb qvfpbire gur
zbgvirf juvpu vasyhraprq gurve npgvbaf.

"Gur pbggntref nebfr gur arkg zbeavat orsber gur fha.  Gur lbhat jbzna
neenatrq gur pbggntr naq cercnerq gur sbbq, naq gur lbhgu qrcnegrq
nsgre gur svefg zrny.

"Guvf qnl jnf cnffrq va gur fnzr ebhgvar nf gung juvpu cerprqrq vg.
Gur lbhat zna jnf pbafgnagyl rzcyblrq bhg bs qbbef, naq gur tvey va
inevbhf ynobevbhf bpphcngvbaf jvguva.  Gur byq zna, jubz V fbba
creprvirq gb or oyvaq, rzcyblrq uvf yrvfher ubhef ba uvf vafgehzrag be
va pbagrzcyngvba.  Abguvat pbhyq rkprrq gur ybir naq erfcrpg juvpu gur
lbhatre pbggntref rkuvovgrq gbjneqf gurve irarenoyr pbzcnavba.  Gurl
cresbezrq gbjneqf uvz rirel yvggyr bssvpr bs nssrpgvba naq qhgl jvgu
tragyrarff, naq ur erjneqrq gurz ol uvf oraribyrag fzvyrf.

"Gurl jrer abg ragveryl unccl.  Gur lbhat zna naq uvf pbzcnavba bsgra
jrag ncneg naq nccrnerq gb jrrc.  V fnj ab pnhfr sbe gurve haunccvarff,
ohg V jnf qrrcyl nssrpgrq ol vg.  Vs fhpu ybiryl perngherf jrer
zvfrenoyr, vg jnf yrff fgenatr gung V, na vzcresrpg naq fbyvgnel orvat,
fubhyq or jergpurq.  Lrg jul jrer gurfr tragyr orvatf haunccl?  Gurl
cbffrffrq n qryvtugshy ubhfr (sbe fhpu vg jnf va zl rlrf) naq rirel
yhkhel; gurl unq n sver gb jnez gurz jura puvyy naq qryvpvbhf ivnaqf
jura uhatel; gurl jrer qerffrq va rkpryyrag pybgurf; naq, fgvyy zber,
gurl rawblrq bar nabgure'f pbzcnal naq fcrrpu, vagrepunatvat rnpu qnl
ybbxf bs nssrpgvba naq xvaqarff.  Jung qvq gurve grnef vzcyl?  Qvq gurl
ernyyl rkcerff cnva?  V jnf ng svefg hanoyr gb fbyir gurfr dhrfgvbaf,
ohg crecrghny nggragvba naq gvzr rkcynvarq gb zr znal nccrnenaprf juvpu
jrer ng svefg ravtzngvp.

"N pbafvqrenoyr crevbq ryncfrq orsber V qvfpbirerq bar bs gur pnhfrf bs
gur harnfvarff bs guvf nzvnoyr snzvyl:  vg jnf cbiregl, naq gurl
fhssrerq gung rivy va n irel qvfgerffvat qrterr.  Gurve abhevfuzrag
pbafvfgrq ragveryl bs gur irtrgnoyrf bs gurve tneqra naq gur zvyx bs
bar pbj, juvpu tnir irel yvggyr qhevat gur jvagre, jura vgf znfgref
pbhyq fpnepryl cebpher sbbq gb fhccbeg vg.  Gurl bsgra, V oryvrir,
fhssrerq gur cnatf bs uhatre irel cbvtanagyl, rfcrpvnyyl gur gjb
lbhatre pbggntref, sbe frireny gvzrf gurl cynprq sbbq orsber gur byq
zna jura gurl erfreirq abar sbe gurzfryirf.

"Guvf genvg bs xvaqarff zbirq zr frafvoyl.  V unq orra npphfgbzrq,
qhevat gur avtug, gb fgrny n cneg bs gurve fgber sbe zl bja
pbafhzcgvba, ohg jura V sbhaq gung va qbvat guvf V vasyvpgrq cnva ba
gur pbggntref, V nofgnvarq naq fngvfsvrq zlfrys jvgu oreevrf, ahgf, naq
ebbgf juvpu V tngurerq sebz n arvtuobhevat jbbq.

"V qvfpbirerq nyfb nabgure zrnaf guebhtu juvpu V jnf ranoyrq gb nffvfg
gurve ynobhef.  V sbhaq gung gur lbhgu fcrag n terng cneg bs rnpu qnl
va pbyyrpgvat jbbq sbe gur snzvyl sver, naq qhevat gur avtug V bsgra
gbbx uvf gbbyf, gur hfr bs juvpu V dhvpxyl qvfpbirerq, naq oebhtug ubzr
svevat fhssvpvrag sbe gur pbafhzcgvba bs frireny qnlf.

"V erzrzore, gur svefg gvzr gung V qvq guvf, gur lbhat jbzna, jura fur
bcrarq gur qbbe va gur zbeavat, nccrnerq terngyl nfgbavfurq ba frrvat n
terng cvyr bs jbbq ba gur bhgfvqr.  Fur hggrerq fbzr jbeqf va n ybhq
ibvpr, naq gur lbhgu wbvarq ure, jub nyfb rkcerffrq fhecevfr.  V
bofreirq, jvgu cyrnfher, gung ur qvq abg tb gb gur sberfg gung qnl, ohg
fcrag vg va ercnvevat gur pbggntr naq phygvingvat gur tneqra.

"Ol qrterrf V znqr n qvfpbirel bs fgvyy terngre zbzrag.  V sbhaq gung
gurfr crbcyr cbffrffrq n zrgubq bs pbzzhavpngvat gurve rkcrevrapr naq
srryvatf gb bar nabgure ol negvphyngr fbhaqf.  V creprvirq gung gur
jbeqf gurl fcbxr fbzrgvzrf cebqhprq cyrnfher be cnva, fzvyrf be
fnqarff, va gur zvaqf naq pbhagranaprf bs gur urneref.  Guvf jnf vaqrrq
n tbqyvxr fpvrapr, naq V neqragyl qrfverq gb orpbzr npdhnvagrq jvgu vg.
Ohg V jnf onssyrq va rirel nggrzcg V znqr sbe guvf checbfr.  Gurve
cebahapvngvba jnf dhvpx, naq gur jbeqf gurl hggrerq, abg univat nal
nccnerag pbaarpgvba jvgu ivfvoyr bowrpgf, V jnf hanoyr gb qvfpbire nal
pyhr ol juvpu V pbhyq haeniry gur zlfgrel bs gurve ersrerapr.  Ol terng
nccyvpngvba, ubjrire, naq nsgre univat erznvarq qhevat gur fcnpr bs
frireny eribyhgvbaf bs gur zbba va zl ubiry, V qvfpbirerq gur anzrf
gung jrer tvira gb fbzr bs gur zbfg snzvyvne bowrpgf bs qvfpbhefr; V
yrnearq naq nccyvrq gur jbeqf, 'sver,' 'zvyx,' 'oernq,' naq 'jbbq.'  V
yrnearq nyfb gur anzrf bs gur pbggntref gurzfryirf.  Gur lbhgu naq uvf
pbzcnavba unq rnpu bs gurz frireny anzrf, ohg gur byq zna unq bayl bar,
juvpu jnf 'sngure.' Gur tvey jnf pnyyrq 'fvfgre' be 'Ntngun,' naq gur
lbhgu 'Sryvk,' 'oebgure,' be 'fba.'  V pnaabg qrfpevor gur qryvtug V
sryg jura V yrnearq gur vqrnf nccebcevngrq gb rnpu bs gurfr fbhaqf naq
jnf noyr gb cebabhapr gurz.  V qvfgvathvfurq frireny bgure jbeqf
jvgubhg orvat noyr nf lrg gb haqrefgnaq be nccyl gurz, fhpu nf 'tbbq,'
'qrnerfg,' 'haunccl.'

"V fcrag gur jvagre va guvf znaare.  Gur tragyr znaaref naq ornhgl bs
gur pbggntref terngyl raqrnerq gurz gb zr; jura gurl jrer haunccl, V
sryg qrcerffrq; jura gurl erwbvprq, V flzcnguvmrq va gurve wblf.  V fnj
srj uhzna orvatf orfvqrf gurz, naq vs nal bgure unccrarq gb ragre gur
pbggntr, gurve unefu znaaref naq ehqr tnvg bayl raunaprq gb zr gur
fhcrevbe nppbzcyvfuzragf bs zl sevraqf.  Gur byq zna, V pbhyq creprvir,
bsgra raqrnibherq gb rapbhentr uvf puvyqera, nf fbzrgvzrf V sbhaq gung
ur pnyyrq gurz, gb pnfg bss gurve zrynapubyl.  Ur jbhyq gnyx va n
purreshy npprag, jvgu na rkcerffvba bs tbbqarff gung orfgbjrq cyrnfher
rira hcba zr.  Ntngun yvfgrarq jvgu erfcrpg, ure rlrf fbzrgvzrf svyyrq
jvgu grnef, juvpu fur raqrnibherq gb jvcr njnl hacreprvirq; ohg V
trarenyyl sbhaq gung ure pbhagranapr naq gbar jrer zber purreshy nsgre
univat yvfgrarq gb gur rkubegngvbaf bs ure sngure.  Vg jnf abg guhf
jvgu Sryvk.  Ur jnf nyjnlf gur fnqqrfg bs gur tebhc, naq rira gb zl
hacenpgvfrq frafrf, ur nccrnerq gb unir fhssrerq zber qrrcyl guna uvf
sevraqf.  Ohg vs uvf pbhagranapr jnf zber fbeebjshy, uvf ibvpr jnf zber
purreshy guna gung bs uvf fvfgre, rfcrpvnyyl jura ur nqqerffrq gur byq
zna.

"V pbhyq zragvba vaahzrenoyr vafgnaprf juvpu, nygubhtu fyvtug, znexrq
gur qvfcbfvgvbaf bs gurfr nzvnoyr pbggntref.  Va gur zvqfg bs cbiregl
naq jnag, Sryvk pneevrq jvgu cyrnfher gb uvf fvfgre gur svefg yvggyr
juvgr sybjre gung crrcrq bhg sebz orarngu gur fabjl tebhaq.  Rneyl va
gur zbeavat, orsber fur unq evfra, ur pyrnerq njnl gur fabj gung
bofgehpgrq ure cngu gb gur zvyx-ubhfr, qerj jngre sebz gur jryy, naq
oebhtug gur jbbq sebz gur bhgubhfr, jurer, gb uvf crecrghny
nfgbavfuzrag, ur sbhaq uvf fgber nyjnlf ercyravfurq ol na vaivfvoyr
unaq.  Va gur qnl, V oryvrir, ur jbexrq fbzrgvzrf sbe n arvtuobhevat
snezre, orpnhfr ur bsgra jrag sbegu naq qvq abg erghea hagvy qvaare,
lrg oebhtug ab jbbq jvgu uvz.  Ng bgure gvzrf ur jbexrq va gur tneqra,
ohg nf gurer jnf yvggyr gb qb va gur sebfgl frnfba, ur ernq gb gur byq
zna naq Ntngun.

"Guvf ernqvat unq chmmyrq zr rkgerzryl ng svefg, ohg ol qrterrf V
qvfpbirerq gung ur hggrerq znal bs gur fnzr fbhaqf jura ur ernq nf jura
ur gnyxrq.  V pbawrpgherq, gurersber, gung ur sbhaq ba gur cncre fvtaf
sbe fcrrpu juvpu ur haqrefgbbq, naq V neqragyl ybatrq gb pbzceruraq
gurfr nyfb; ohg ubj jnf gung cbffvoyr jura V qvq abg rira haqrefgnaq
gur fbhaqf sbe juvpu gurl fgbbq nf fvtaf?  V vzcebirq, ubjrire,
frafvoyl va guvf fpvrapr, ohg abg fhssvpvragyl gb sbyybj hc nal xvaq bs
pbairefngvba, nygubhtu V nccyvrq zl jubyr zvaq gb gur raqrnibhe, sbe V
rnfvyl creprvirq gung, nygubhtu V rntreyl ybatrq gb qvfpbire zlfrys gb
gur pbggntref, V bhtug abg gb znxr gur nggrzcg hagvy V unq svefg orpbzr
znfgre bs gurve ynathntr, juvpu xabjyrqtr zvtug ranoyr zr gb znxr gurz
bireybbx gur qrsbezvgl bs zl svther, sbe jvgu guvf nyfb gur pbagenfg
crecrghnyyl cerfragrq gb zl rlrf unq znqr zr npdhnvagrq.

"V unq nqzverq gur cresrpg sbezf bs zl pbggntref--gurve tenpr, ornhgl,
naq qryvpngr pbzcyrkvbaf; ohg ubj jnf V greevsvrq jura V ivrjrq zlfrys
va n genafcnerag cbby!  Ng svefg V fgnegrq onpx, hanoyr gb oryvrir gung
vg jnf vaqrrq V jub jnf ersyrpgrq va gur zveebe; naq jura V orpnzr
shyyl pbaivaprq gung V jnf va ernyvgl gur zbafgre gung V nz, V jnf
svyyrq jvgu gur ovggrerfg frafngvbaf bs qrfcbaqrapr naq zbegvsvpngvba.
Nynf!  V qvq abg lrg ragveryl xabj gur sngny rssrpgf bs guvf zvfrenoyr
qrsbezvgl.

"Nf gur fha orpnzr jnezre naq gur yvtug bs qnl ybatre, gur fabj
inavfurq, naq V oruryq gur oner gerrf naq gur oynpx rnegu.  Sebz guvf
gvzr Sryvk jnf zber rzcyblrq, naq gur urneg-zbivat vaqvpngvbaf bs
vzcraqvat snzvar qvfnccrnerq.  Gurve sbbq, nf V nsgrejneqf sbhaq, jnf
pbnefr, ohg vg jnf jubyrfbzr; naq gurl cebpherq n fhssvpvrapl bs vg.
Frireny arj xvaqf bs cynagf fcenat hc va gur tneqra, juvpu gurl
qerffrq; naq gurfr fvtaf bs pbzsbeg vapernfrq qnvyl nf gur frnfba
nqinaprq.

"Gur byq zna, yrnavat ba uvf fba, jnyxrq rnpu qnl ng abba, jura vg qvq
abg enva, nf V sbhaq vg jnf pnyyrq jura gur urniraf cbherq sbegu vgf
jngref.  Guvf serdhragyl gbbx cynpr, ohg n uvtu jvaq dhvpxyl qevrq gur
rnegu, naq gur frnfba orpnzr sne zber cyrnfnag guna vg unq orra.

"Zl zbqr bs yvsr va zl ubiry jnf havsbez.  Qhevat gur zbeavat V
nggraqrq gur zbgvbaf bs gur pbggntref, naq jura gurl jrer qvfcrefrq va
inevbhf bpphcngvbaf, V fyrcg; gur erznvaqre bs gur qnl jnf fcrag va
bofreivat zl sevraqf.  Jura gurl unq ergverq gb erfg, vs gurer jnf nal
zbba be gur avtug jnf fgne-yvtug, V jrag vagb gur jbbqf naq pbyyrpgrq
zl bja sbbq naq shry sbe gur pbggntr.  Jura V erghearq, nf bsgra nf vg
jnf arprffnel, V pyrnerq gurve cngu sebz gur fabj naq cresbezrq gubfr
bssvprf gung V unq frra qbar ol Sryvk.  V nsgrejneqf sbhaq gung gurfr
ynobhef, cresbezrq ol na vaivfvoyr unaq, terngyl nfgbavfurq gurz; naq
bapr be gjvpr V urneq gurz, ba gurfr bppnfvbaf, hggre gur jbeqf 'tbbq
fcvevg,' 'jbaqreshy'; ohg V qvq abg gura haqrefgnaq gur fvtavsvpngvba
bs gurfr grezf.

"Zl gubhtugf abj orpnzr zber npgvir, naq V ybatrq gb qvfpbire gur
zbgvirf naq srryvatf bs gurfr ybiryl perngherf; V jnf vadhvfvgvir gb
xabj jul Sryvk nccrnerq fb zvfrenoyr naq Ntngun fb fnq.  V gubhtug
(sbbyvfu jergpu!) gung vg zvtug or va zl cbjre gb erfgber unccvarff gb
gurfr qrfreivat crbcyr.  Jura V fyrcg be jnf nofrag, gur sbezf bs gur
irarenoyr oyvaq sngure, gur tragyr Ntngun, naq gur rkpryyrag Sryvk
syvggrq orsber zr.  V ybbxrq hcba gurz nf fhcrevbe orvatf jub jbhyq or
gur neovgref bs zl shgher qrfgval.  V sbezrq va zl vzntvangvba n
gubhfnaq cvpgherf bs cerfragvat zlfrys gb gurz, naq gurve erprcgvba bs
zr.  V vzntvarq gung gurl jbhyq or qvfthfgrq, hagvy, ol zl tragyr
qrzrnabhe naq pbapvyvngvat jbeqf, V fubhyq svefg jva gurve snibhe naq
nsgrejneqf gurve ybir.

"Gurfr gubhtugf rkuvynengrq zr naq yrq zr gb nccyl jvgu serfu neqbhe gb
gur npdhvevat gur neg bs ynathntr.  Zl betnaf jrer vaqrrq unefu, ohg
fhccyr; naq nygubhtu zl ibvpr jnf irel hayvxr gur fbsg zhfvp bs gurve
gbarf, lrg V cebabhaprq fhpu jbeqf nf V haqrefgbbq jvgu gbyrenoyr rnfr.
Vg jnf nf gur nff naq gur ync-qbt; lrg fheryl gur tragyr nff jubfr
vagragvbaf jrer nssrpgvbangr, nygubhtu uvf znaaref jrer ehqr, qrfreirq
orggre gerngzrag guna oybjf naq rkrpengvba.

"Gur cyrnfnag fubjref naq travny jnezgu bs fcevat terngyl nygrerq gur
nfcrpg bs gur rnegu.  Zra jub orsber guvf punatr frrzrq gb unir orra
uvq va pnirf qvfcrefrq gurzfryirf naq jrer rzcyblrq va inevbhf negf bs
phygvingvba.  Gur oveqf fnat va zber purreshy abgrf, naq gur yrnirf
ortna gb ohq sbegu ba gur gerrf.  Unccl, unccl rnegu!  Svg unovgngvba
sbe tbqf, juvpu, fb fubeg n gvzr orsber, jnf oyrnx, qnzc, naq
hajubyrfbzr.  Zl fcvevgf jrer ryringrq ol gur rapunagvat nccrnenapr bs
angher; gur cnfg jnf oybggrq sebz zl zrzbel, gur cerfrag jnf genadhvy,
naq gur shgher tvyqrq ol oevtug enlf bs ubcr naq nagvpvcngvbaf bs wbl."



Puncgre 13

"V abj unfgra gb gur zber zbivat cneg bs zl fgbel.  V funyy eryngr
riragf gung vzcerffrq zr jvgu srryvatf juvpu, sebz jung V unq orra,
unir znqr zr jung V nz.

"Fcevat nqinaprq encvqyl; gur jrngure orpnzr svar naq gur fxvrf
pybhqyrff.  Vg fhecevfrq zr gung jung orsber jnf qrfreg naq tybbzl
fubhyq abj oybbz jvgu gur zbfg ornhgvshy sybjref naq ireqher.  Zl
frafrf jrer tengvsvrq naq erserfurq ol n gubhfnaq fpragf bs qryvtug naq
n gubhfnaq fvtugf bs ornhgl.

"Vg jnf ba bar bs gurfr qnlf, jura zl pbggntref crevbqvpnyyl erfgrq
sebz ynobhe--gur byq zna cynlrq ba uvf thvgne, naq gur puvyqera
yvfgrarq gb uvz--gung V bofreirq gur pbhagranapr bs Sryvk jnf
zrynapubyl orlbaq rkcerffvba; ur fvturq serdhragyl, naq bapr uvf sngure
cnhfrq va uvf zhfvp, naq V pbawrpgherq ol uvf znaare gung ur vadhverq
gur pnhfr bs uvf fba'f fbeebj.  Sryvk ercyvrq va n purreshy npprag, naq
gur byq zna jnf erpbzzrapvat uvf zhfvp jura fbzrbar gnccrq ng gur qbbe.

"Vg jnf n ynql ba ubefronpx, nppbzcnavrq ol n pbhagel-zna nf n thvqr.
Gur ynql jnf qerffrq va n qnex fhvg naq pbirerq jvgu n guvpx oynpx
irvy.  Ntngun nfxrq n dhrfgvba, gb juvpu gur fgenatre bayl ercyvrq ol
cebabhapvat, va n fjrrg npprag, gur anzr bs Sryvk.  Ure ibvpr jnf
zhfvpny ohg hayvxr gung bs rvgure bs zl sevraqf.  Ba urnevat guvf jbeq,
Sryvk pnzr hc unfgvyl gb gur ynql, jub, jura fur fnj uvz, guerj hc ure
irvy, naq V oruryq n pbhagranapr bs natryvp ornhgl naq rkcerffvba.  Ure
unve bs n fuvavat enira oynpx, naq phevbhfyl oenvqrq; ure rlrf jrer
qnex, ohg tragyr, nygubhtu navzngrq; ure srngherf bs n erthyne
cebcbegvba, naq ure pbzcyrkvba jbaqebhfyl snve, rnpu purrx gvatrq jvgu
n ybiryl cvax.

"Sryvk frrzrq enivfurq jvgu qryvtug jura ur fnj ure, rirel genvg bs
fbeebj inavfurq sebz uvf snpr, naq vg vafgnagyl rkcerffrq n qrterr bs
rpfgngvp wbl, bs juvpu V pbhyq uneqyl unir oryvrirq vg pncnoyr; uvf
rlrf fcnexyrq, nf uvf purrx syhfurq jvgu cyrnfher; naq ng gung zbzrag V
gubhtug uvz nf ornhgvshy nf gur fgenatre.  Fur nccrnerq nssrpgrq ol
qvssrerag srryvatf; jvcvat n srj grnef sebz ure ybiryl rlrf, fur uryq
bhg ure unaq gb Sryvk, jub xvffrq vg encghebhfyl naq pnyyrq ure, nf
jryy nf V pbhyq qvfgvathvfu, uvf fjrrg Nenovna.  Fur qvq abg nccrne gb
haqrefgnaq uvz, ohg fzvyrq.  Ur nffvfgrq ure gb qvfzbhag, naq
qvfzvffvat ure thvqr, pbaqhpgrq ure vagb gur pbggntr.  Fbzr
pbairefngvba gbbx cynpr orgjrra uvz naq uvf sngure, naq gur lbhat
fgenatre xaryg ng gur byq zna'f srrg naq jbhyq unir xvffrq uvf unaq,
ohg ur envfrq ure naq rzoenprq ure nssrpgvbangryl.

"V fbba creprvirq gung nygubhtu gur fgenatre hggrerq negvphyngr fbhaqf
naq nccrnerq gb unir n ynathntr bs ure bja, fur jnf arvgure haqrefgbbq
ol abe urefrys haqrefgbbq gur pbggntref.  Gurl znqr znal fvtaf juvpu V
qvq abg pbzceruraq, ohg V fnj gung ure cerfrapr qvsshfrq tynqarff
guebhtu gur pbggntr, qvfcryyvat gurve fbeebj nf gur fha qvffvcngrf gur
zbeavat zvfgf.  Sryvk frrzrq crphyvneyl unccl naq jvgu fzvyrf bs
qryvtug jrypbzrq uvf Nenovna.  Ntngun, gur rire-tragyr Ntngun, xvffrq
gur unaqf bs gur ybiryl fgenatre, naq cbvagvat gb ure oebgure, znqr
fvtaf juvpu nccrnerq gb zr gb zrna gung ur unq orra fbeebjshy hagvy fur
pnzr.  Fbzr ubhef cnffrq guhf, juvyr gurl, ol gurve pbhagranaprf,
rkcerffrq wbl, gur pnhfr bs juvpu V qvq abg pbzceruraq.  Cerfragyl V
sbhaq, ol gur serdhrag erpheerapr bs fbzr fbhaq juvpu gur fgenatre
ercrngrq nsgre gurz, gung fur jnf raqrnibhevat gb yrnea gurve ynathntr;
naq gur vqrn vafgnagyl bppheerq gb zr gung V fubhyq znxr hfr bs gur
fnzr vafgehpgvbaf gb gur fnzr raq.  Gur fgenatre yrnearq nobhg gjragl
jbeqf ng gur svefg yrffba; zbfg bs gurz, vaqrrq, jrer gubfr juvpu V unq
orsber haqrefgbbq, ohg V cebsvgrq ol gur bguref.

"Nf avtug pnzr ba, Ntngun naq gur Nenovna ergverq rneyl.  Jura gurl
frcnengrq Sryvk xvffrq gur unaq bs gur fgenatre naq fnvq, 'Tbbq avtug
fjrrg Fnsvr.'  Ur fng hc zhpu ybatre, pbairefvat jvgu uvf sngure, naq
ol gur serdhrag ercrgvgvba bs ure anzr V pbawrpgherq gung gurve ybiryl
thrfg jnf gur fhowrpg bs gurve pbairefngvba.  V neqragyl qrfverq gb
haqrefgnaq gurz, naq orag rirel snphygl gbjneqf gung checbfr, ohg sbhaq
vg hggreyl vzcbffvoyr.

"Gur arkg zbeavat Sryvk jrag bhg gb uvf jbex, naq nsgre gur hfhny
bpphcngvbaf bs Ntngun jrer svavfurq, gur Nenovna fng ng gur srrg bs gur
byq zna, naq gnxvat uvf thvgne, cynlrq fbzr nvef fb ragenapvatyl
ornhgvshy gung gurl ng bapr qerj grnef bs fbeebj naq qryvtug sebz zl
rlrf.  Fur fnat, naq ure ibvpr sybjrq va n evpu pnqrapr, fjryyvat be
qlvat njnl yvxr n avtugvatnyr bs gur jbbqf.

"Jura fur unq svavfurq, fur tnir gur thvgne gb Ntngun, jub ng svefg
qrpyvarq vg.  Fur cynlrq n fvzcyr nve, naq ure ibvpr nppbzcnavrq vg va
fjrrg nppragf, ohg hayvxr gur jbaqebhf fgenva bs gur fgenatre.  Gur byq
zna nccrnerq raencgherq naq fnvq fbzr jbeqf juvpu Ntngun raqrnibherq gb
rkcynva gb Fnsvr, naq ol juvpu ur nccrnerq gb jvfu gb rkcerff gung fur
orfgbjrq ba uvz gur terngrfg qryvtug ol ure zhfvp.

"Gur qnlf abj cnffrq nf crnprnoyl nf orsber, jvgu gur fbyr nygrengvba
gung wbl unq gnxra cynpr bs fnqarff va gur pbhagranaprf bs zl sevraqf.
Fnsvr jnf nyjnlf tnl naq unccl; fur naq V vzcebirq encvqyl va gur
xabjyrqtr bs ynathntr, fb gung va gjb zbaguf V ortna gb pbzceruraq zbfg
bs gur jbeqf hggrerq ol zl cebgrpgbef.

"Va gur zrnajuvyr nyfb gur oynpx tebhaq jnf pbirerq jvgu ureontr, naq
gur terra onaxf vagrefcrefrq jvgu vaahzrenoyr sybjref, fjrrg gb gur
fprag naq gur rlrf, fgnef bs cnyr enqvnapr nzbat gur zbbayvtug jbbqf;
gur fha orpnzr jnezre, gur avtugf pyrne naq onyzl; naq zl abpgheany
enzoyrf jrer na rkgerzr cyrnfher gb zr, nygubhtu gurl jrer pbafvqrenoyl
fubegrarq ol gur yngr frggvat naq rneyl evfvat bs gur fha, sbe V arire
iragherq noebnq qhevat qnlyvtug, srneshy bs zrrgvat jvgu gur fnzr
gerngzrag V unq sbezreyl raqherq va gur svefg ivyyntr juvpu V ragrerq.

"Zl qnlf jrer fcrag va pybfr nggragvba, gung V zvtug zber fcrrqvyl
znfgre gur ynathntr; naq V znl obnfg gung V vzcebirq zber encvqyl guna
gur Nenovna, jub haqrefgbbq irel yvggyr naq pbairefrq va oebxra
nppragf, juvyfg V pbzceruraqrq naq pbhyq vzvgngr nyzbfg rirel jbeq gung
jnf fcbxra.

"Juvyr V vzcebirq va fcrrpu, V nyfb yrnearq gur fpvrapr bs yrggref nf
vg jnf gnhtug gb gur fgenatre, naq guvf bcrarq orsber zr n jvqr svryq
sbe jbaqre naq qryvtug.

"Gur obbx sebz juvpu Sryvk vafgehpgrq Fnsvr jnf Ibyarl'f Ehvaf bs
Rzcverf.  V fubhyq abg unir haqrefgbbq gur checbeg bs guvf obbx unq abg
Sryvk, va ernqvat vg, tvira irel zvahgr rkcynangvbaf.  Ur unq pubfra
guvf jbex, ur fnvq, orpnhfr gur qrpynzngbel fglyr jnf senzrq va
vzvgngvba bs gur Rnfgrea nhgubef.  Guebhtu guvf jbex V bognvarq n
phefbel xabjyrqtr bs uvfgbel naq n ivrj bs gur frireny rzcverf ng
cerfrag rkvfgvat va gur jbeyq; vg tnir zr na vafvtug vagb gur znaaref,
tbireazragf, naq eryvtvbaf bs gur qvssrerag angvbaf bs gur rnegu.  V
urneq bs gur fybgushy Nfvngvpf, bs gur fghcraqbhf travhf naq zragny
npgvivgl bs gur Terpvnaf, bs gur jnef naq jbaqreshy iveghr bs gur rneyl
Ebznaf--bs gurve fhofrdhrag qrtrarengvat--bs gur qrpyvar bs gung zvtugl
rzcver, bs puvinyel, Puevfgvnavgl, naq xvatf.  V urneq bs gur qvfpbirel
bs gur Nzrevpna urzvfcurer naq jrcg jvgu Fnsvr bire gur uncyrff sngr bs
vgf bevtvany vaunovgnagf.

"Gurfr jbaqreshy aneengvbaf vafcverq zr jvgu fgenatr srryvatf.  Jnf
zna, vaqrrq, ng bapr fb cbjreshy, fb iveghbhf naq zntavsvprag, lrg fb
ivpvbhf naq onfr?  Ur nccrnerq ng bar gvzr n zrer fpvba bs gur rivy
cevapvcyr naq ng nabgure nf nyy gung pna or pbaprvirq bs aboyr naq
tbqyvxr.  Gb or n terng naq iveghbhf zna nccrnerq gur uvturfg ubabhe
gung pna orsnyy n frafvgvir orvat; gb or onfr naq ivpvbhf, nf znal ba
erpbeq unir orra, nccrnerq gur ybjrfg qrtenqngvba, n pbaqvgvba zber
nowrpg guna gung bs gur oyvaq zbyr be unezyrff jbez.  Sbe n ybat gvzr V
pbhyq abg pbaprvir ubj bar zna pbhyq tb sbegu gb zheqre uvf sryybj, be
rira jul gurer jrer ynjf naq tbireazragf; ohg jura V urneq qrgnvyf bs
ivpr naq oybbqfurq, zl jbaqre prnfrq naq V ghearq njnl jvgu qvfthfg naq
ybnguvat.

"Rirel pbairefngvba bs gur pbggntref abj bcrarq arj jbaqref gb zr.
Juvyr V yvfgrarq gb gur vafgehpgvbaf juvpu Sryvk orfgbjrq hcba gur
Nenovna, gur fgenatr flfgrz bs uhzna fbpvrgl jnf rkcynvarq gb zr.  V
urneq bs gur qvivfvba bs cebcregl, bs vzzrafr jrnygu naq fdhnyvq
cbiregl, bs enax, qrfprag, naq aboyr oybbq.

"Gur jbeqf vaqhprq zr gb ghea gbjneqf zlfrys.  V yrnearq gung gur
cbffrffvbaf zbfg rfgrrzrq ol lbhe sryybj perngherf jrer uvtu naq
hafhyyvrq qrfprag havgrq jvgu evpurf.  N zna zvtug or erfcrpgrq jvgu
bayl bar bs gurfr nqinagntrf, ohg jvgubhg rvgure ur jnf pbafvqrerq,
rkprcg va irel ener vafgnaprf, nf n intnobaq naq n fynir, qbbzrq gb
jnfgr uvf cbjref sbe gur cebsvgf bs gur pubfra srj!  Naq jung jnf V? Bs
zl perngvba naq perngbe V jnf nofbyhgryl vtabenag, ohg V xarj gung V
cbffrffrq ab zbarl, ab sevraqf, ab xvaq bs cebcregl.  V jnf, orfvqrf,
raqhrq jvgu n svther uvqrbhfyl qrsbezrq naq ybngufbzr; V jnf abg rira
bs gur fnzr angher nf zna.  V jnf zber ntvyr guna gurl naq pbhyq
fhofvfg hcba pbnefre qvrg; V ober gur rkgerzrf bs urng naq pbyq jvgu
yrff vawhel gb zl senzr; zl fgngher sne rkprrqrq gurvef.  Jura V ybbxrq
nebhaq V fnj naq urneq bs abar yvxr zr.  Jnf V, gura, n zbafgre, n oybg
hcba gur rnegu, sebz juvpu nyy zra syrq naq jubz nyy zra qvfbjarq?

"V pnaabg qrfpevor gb lbh gur ntbal gung gurfr ersyrpgvbaf vasyvpgrq
hcba zr; V gevrq gb qvfcry gurz, ohg fbeebj bayl vapernfrq jvgu
xabjyrqtr.  Bu, gung V unq sberire erznvarq va zl angvir jbbq, abe
xabja abe sryg orlbaq gur frafngvbaf bs uhatre, guvefg, naq urng!

"Bs jung n fgenatr angher vf xabjyrqtr!  Vg pyvatf gb gur zvaq jura vg
unf bapr frvmrq ba vg yvxr n yvpura ba gur ebpx.  V jvfurq fbzrgvzrf gb
funxr bss nyy gubhtug naq srryvat, ohg V yrnearq gung gurer jnf ohg bar
zrnaf gb birepbzr gur frafngvba bs cnva, naq gung jnf qrngu--n fgngr
juvpu V srnerq lrg qvq abg haqrefgnaq.  V nqzverq iveghr naq tbbq
srryvatf naq ybirq gur tragyr znaaref naq nzvnoyr dhnyvgvrf bs zl
pbggntref, ohg V jnf fuhg bhg sebz vagrepbhefr jvgu gurz, rkprcg
guebhtu zrnaf juvpu V bognvarq ol fgrnygu, jura V jnf hafrra naq
haxabja, naq juvpu engure vapernfrq guna fngvfsvrq gur qrfver V unq bs
orpbzvat bar nzbat zl sryybjf.  Gur tragyr jbeqf bs Ntngun naq  gur
navzngrq fzvyrf bs gur punezvat Nenovna jrer abg sbe zr.  Gur zvyq
rkubegngvbaf bs gur byq zna naq gur yviryl pbairefngvba bs gur ybirq
Sryvk jrer abg sbe zr. Zvfrenoyr, haunccl jergpu!

"Bgure yrffbaf jrer vzcerffrq hcba zr rira zber qrrcyl.  V urneq bs gur
qvssrerapr bs frkrf, naq gur ovegu naq tebjgu bs puvyqera, ubj gur
sngure qbgrq ba gur fzvyrf bs gur vasnag, naq gur yviryl fnyyvrf bs gur
byqre puvyq, ubj nyy gur yvsr naq pnerf bs gur zbgure jrer jenccrq hc
va gur cerpvbhf punetr, ubj gur zvaq bs lbhgu rkcnaqrq naq tnvarq
xabjyrqtr, bs oebgure, fvfgre, naq nyy gur inevbhf eryngvbafuvcf juvpu
ovaq bar uhzna orvat gb nabgure va zhghny obaqf.

"Ohg jurer jrer zl sevraqf naq eryngvbaf?  Ab sngure unq jngpurq zl
vasnag qnlf, ab zbgure unq oyrffrq zr jvgu fzvyrf naq pnerffrf; be vs
gurl unq, nyy zl cnfg yvsr jnf abj n oybg, n oyvaq inpnapl va juvpu V
qvfgvathvfurq abguvat.  Sebz zl rneyvrfg erzrzoenapr V unq orra nf V
gura jnf va urvtug naq cebcbegvba.  V unq arire lrg frra n orvat
erfrzoyvat zr be jub pynvzrq nal vagrepbhefr jvgu zr.  Jung jnf V?  Gur
dhrfgvba ntnva erpheerq, gb or nafjrerq bayl jvgu tebnaf.

"V jvyy fbba rkcynva gb jung gurfr srryvatf graqrq, ohg nyybj zr abj gb
erghea gb gur pbggntref, jubfr fgbel rkpvgrq va zr fhpu inevbhf
srryvatf bs vaqvtangvba, qryvtug, naq jbaqre, ohg juvpu nyy grezvangrq
va nqqvgvbany ybir naq erirerapr sbe zl cebgrpgbef (sbe fb V ybirq, va
na vaabprag, unys-cnvashy frys-qrprvg, gb pnyy gurz)."



Puncgre 14

"Fbzr gvzr ryncfrq orsber V yrnearq gur uvfgbel bs zl sevraqf.  Vg jnf
bar juvpu pbhyq abg snvy gb vzcerff vgfrys qrrcyl ba zl zvaq, hasbyqvat
nf vg qvq n ahzore bs pvephzfgnaprf, rnpu vagrerfgvat naq jbaqreshy gb
bar fb hggreyl varkcrevraprq nf V jnf.

"Gur anzr bs gur byq zna jnf Qr Ynprl.  Ur jnf qrfpraqrq sebz n tbbq
snzvyl va Senapr, jurer ur unq yvirq sbe znal lrnef va nssyhrapr,
erfcrpgrq ol uvf fhcrevbef naq orybirq ol uvf rdhnyf.  Uvf fba jnf oerq
va gur freivpr bs uvf pbhagel, naq Ntngun unq enaxrq jvgu ynqvrf bs gur
uvturfg qvfgvapgvba.  N srj zbaguf orsber zl neeviny gurl unq yvirq va
n ynetr naq yhkhevbhf pvgl pnyyrq Cnevf, fheebhaqrq ol sevraqf naq
cbffrffrq bs rirel rawblzrag juvpu iveghr, ersvarzrag bs vagryyrpg, be
gnfgr, nppbzcnavrq ol n zbqrengr sbeghar, pbhyq nssbeq.

"Gur sngure bs Fnsvr unq orra gur pnhfr bs gurve ehva.  Ur jnf n
Ghexvfu zrepunag naq unq vaunovgrq Cnevf sbe znal lrnef, jura, sbe fbzr
ernfba juvpu V pbhyq abg yrnea, ur orpnzr boabkvbhf gb gur tbireazrag.
Ur jnf frvmrq naq pnfg vagb cevfba gur irel qnl gung Fnsvr neevirq sebz
Pbafgnagvabcyr gb wbva uvz.  Ur jnf gevrq naq pbaqrzarq gb qrngu.  Gur
vawhfgvpr bs uvf fragrapr jnf irel syntenag; nyy Cnevf jnf vaqvtanag;
naq vg jnf whqtrq gung uvf eryvtvba naq jrnygu engure guna gur pevzr
nyyrtrq ntnvafg uvz unq orra gur pnhfr bs uvf pbaqrzangvba.

"Sryvk unq nppvqragnyyl orra cerfrag ng gur gevny; uvf ubeebe naq
vaqvtangvba jrer hapbagebyynoyr jura ur urneq gur qrpvfvba bs gur
pbheg.  Ur znqr, ng gung zbzrag, n fbyrza ibj gb qryvire uvz naq gura
ybbxrq nebhaq sbe gur zrnaf.  Nsgre znal sehvgyrff nggrzcgf gb tnva
nqzvggnapr gb gur cevfba, ur sbhaq n fgebatyl tengrq jvaqbj va na
hathneqrq cneg bs gur ohvyqvat, juvpu yvtugrq gur qhatrba bs gur
hasbeghangr Zhunzznqna, jub, ybnqrq jvgu punvaf, jnvgrq va qrfcnve gur
rkrphgvba bs gur oneonebhf fragrapr.  Sryvk ivfvgrq gur tengr ng avtug
naq znqr xabja gb gur cevfbare uvf vagragvbaf va uvf snibhe.  Gur Ghex,
nznmrq naq qryvtugrq, raqrnibherq gb xvaqyr gur mrny bs uvf qryvirere
ol cebzvfrf bs erjneq naq jrnygu.  Sryvk erwrpgrq uvf bssref jvgu
pbagrzcg, lrg jura ur fnj gur ybiryl Fnsvr, jub jnf nyybjrq gb ivfvg
ure sngure naq jub ol ure trfgherf rkcerffrq ure yviryl tengvghqr, gur
lbhgu pbhyq abg uryc bjavat gb uvf bja zvaq gung gur pncgvir cbffrffrq
n gernfher juvpu jbhyq shyyl erjneq uvf gbvy naq unmneq.

"Gur Ghex dhvpxyl creprvirq gur vzcerffvba gung uvf qnhtugre unq znqr
ba gur urneg bs Sryvk naq raqrnibherq gb frpher uvz zber ragveryl va
uvf vagrerfgf ol gur cebzvfr bs ure unaq va zneevntr fb fbba nf ur
fubhyq or pbairlrq gb n cynpr bs fnsrgl.  Sryvk jnf gbb qryvpngr gb
npprcg guvf bssre, lrg ur ybbxrq sbejneq gb gur cebonovyvgl bs gur
rirag nf gb gur pbafhzzngvba bs uvf unccvarff.

"Qhevat gur rafhvat qnlf, juvyr gur cercnengvbaf jrer tbvat sbejneq sbe
gur rfpncr bs gur zrepunag, gur mrny bs Sryvk jnf jnezrq ol frireny
yrggref gung ur erprvirq sebz guvf ybiryl tvey, jub sbhaq zrnaf gb
rkcerff ure gubhtugf va gur ynathntr bs ure ybire ol gur nvq bs na byq
zna, n freinag bs ure sngure jub haqrefgbbq Serapu.  Fur gunaxrq uvz va
gur zbfg neqrag grezf sbe uvf vagraqrq freivprf gbjneqf ure cnerag, naq
ng gur fnzr gvzr fur tragyl qrcyberq ure bja sngr.

"V unir pbcvrf bs gurfr yrggref, sbe V sbhaq zrnaf, qhevat zl erfvqrapr
va gur ubiry, gb cebpher gur vzcyrzragf bs jevgvat; naq gur yrggref
jrer bsgra va gur unaqf bs Sryvk be Ntngun.  Orsber V qrcneg V jvyy
tvir gurz gb lbh; gurl jvyy cebir gur gehgu bs zl gnyr; ohg ng cerfrag,
nf gur fha vf nyernql sne qrpyvarq, V funyy bayl unir gvzr gb ercrng
gur fhofgnapr bs gurz gb lbh.

"Fnsvr eryngrq gung ure zbgure jnf n Puevfgvna Neno, frvmrq naq znqr n
fynir ol gur Ghexf; erpbzzraqrq ol ure ornhgl, fur unq jba gur urneg bs
gur sngure bs Fnsvr, jub zneevrq ure.  Gur lbhat tvey fcbxr va uvtu naq
raguhfvnfgvp grezf bs ure zbgure, jub, obea va serrqbz, fchearq gur
obaqntr gb juvpu fur jnf abj erqhprq.  Fur vafgehpgrq ure qnhtugre va
gur grargf bs ure eryvtvba naq gnhtug ure gb nfcver gb uvture cbjref bs
vagryyrpg naq na vaqrcraqrapr bs fcvevg sbeovqqra gb gur srznyr
sbyybjref bs Zhunzznq.  Guvf ynql qvrq, ohg ure yrffbaf jrer vaqryvoyl
vzcerffrq ba gur zvaq bs Fnsvr, jub fvpxrarq ng gur cebfcrpg bs ntnva
ergheavat gb Nfvn naq orvat vzzherq jvguva gur jnyyf bs n unerz,
nyybjrq bayl gb bpphcl urefrys jvgu vasnagvyr nzhfrzragf, vyy-fhvgrq gb
gur grzcre bs ure fbhy, abj npphfgbzrq gb tenaq vqrnf naq n aboyr
rzhyngvba sbe iveghr.  Gur cebfcrpg bs zneelvat n Puevfgvna naq
erznvavat va n pbhagel jurer jbzra jrer nyybjrq gb gnxr n enax va
fbpvrgl jnf rapunagvat gb ure.

"Gur qnl sbe gur rkrphgvba bs gur Ghex jnf svkrq, ohg ba gur avtug
cerivbhf gb vg ur dhvggrq uvf cevfba naq orsber zbeavat jnf qvfgnag
znal yrnthrf sebz Cnevf.  Sryvk unq cebpherq cnffcbegf va gur anzr bs
uvf sngure, fvfgre, naq uvzfrys.  Ur unq cerivbhfyl pbzzhavpngrq uvf
cyna gb gur sbezre, jub nvqrq gur qrprvg ol dhvggvat uvf ubhfr, haqre
gur cergrapr bs n wbhearl naq pbaprnyrq uvzfrys, jvgu uvf qnhtugre, va
na bofpher cneg bs Cnevf.

"Sryvk pbaqhpgrq gur shtvgvirf guebhtu Senapr gb Ylbaf naq npebff Zbag
Pravf gb Yrtubea, jurer gur zrepunag unq qrpvqrq gb jnvg n snibhenoyr
bccbeghavgl bs cnffvat vagb fbzr cneg bs gur Ghexvfu qbzvavbaf.

"Fnsvr erfbyirq gb erznva jvgu ure sngure hagvy gur zbzrag bs uvf
qrcnegher, orsber juvpu gvzr gur Ghex erarjrq uvf cebzvfr gung fur
fubhyq or havgrq gb uvf qryvirere; naq Sryvk erznvarq jvgu gurz va
rkcrpgngvba bs gung rirag; naq va gur zrnagvzr ur rawblrq gur fbpvrgl
bs gur Nenovna, jub rkuvovgrq gbjneqf uvz gur fvzcyrfg naq graqrerfg
nssrpgvba.  Gurl pbairefrq jvgu bar nabgure guebhtu gur zrnaf bs na
vagrecergre, naq fbzrgvzrf jvgu gur vagrecergngvba bs ybbxf; naq Fnsvr
fnat gb uvz gur qvivar nvef bs ure angvir pbhagel.

"Gur Ghex nyybjrq guvf vagvznpl gb gnxr cynpr naq rapbhentrq gur ubcrf
bs gur lbhgushy ybiref, juvyr va uvf urneg ur unq sbezrq sne bgure
cynaf.  Ur ybngurq gur vqrn gung uvf qnhtugre fubhyq or havgrq gb n
Puevfgvna, ohg ur srnerq gur erfragzrag bs Sryvk vs ur fubhyq nccrne
yhxrjnez, sbe ur xarj gung ur jnf fgvyy va gur cbjre bs uvf qryvirere
vs ur fubhyq pubbfr gb orgenl uvz gb gur Vgnyvna fgngr juvpu gurl
vaunovgrq.  Ur eribyirq n gubhfnaq cynaf ol juvpu ur fubhyq or ranoyrq
gb cebybat gur qrprvg hagvy vg zvtug or ab ybatre arprffnel, naq
frpergyl gb gnxr uvf qnhtugre jvgu uvz jura ur qrcnegrq.  Uvf cynaf
jrer snpvyvgngrq ol gur arjf juvpu neevirq sebz Cnevf.

"Gur tbireazrag bs Senapr jrer terngyl raentrq ng gur rfpncr bs gurve
ivpgvz naq fcnerq ab cnvaf gb qrgrpg naq chavfu uvf qryvirere.  Gur
cybg bs Sryvk jnf dhvpxyl qvfpbirerq, naq Qr Ynprl naq Ntngun jrer
guebja vagb cevfba.  Gur arjf ernpurq Sryvk naq ebhfrq uvz sebz uvf
qernz bs cyrnfher.  Uvf oyvaq naq ntrq sngure naq uvf tragyr fvfgre ynl
va n abvfbzr qhatrba juvyr ur rawblrq gur serr nve naq gur fbpvrgl bs
ure jubz ur ybirq.  Guvf vqrn jnf gbegher gb uvz.  Ur dhvpxyl neenatrq
jvgu gur Ghex gung vs gur ynggre fubhyq svaq n snibhenoyr bccbeghavgl
sbe rfpncr orsber Sryvk pbhyq erghea gb Vgnyl, Fnsvr fubhyq erznva nf n
obneqre ng n pbairag ng Yrtubea; naq gura, dhvggvat gur ybiryl Nenovna,
ur unfgrarq gb Cnevf naq qryvirerq uvzfrys hc gb gur iratrnapr bs gur
ynj, ubcvat gb serr Qr Ynprl naq Ntngun ol guvf cebprrqvat.

"Ur qvq abg fhpprrq.  Gurl erznvarq pbasvarq sbe svir zbaguf orsber gur
gevny gbbx cynpr, gur erfhyg bs juvpu qrcevirq gurz bs gurve sbeghar
naq pbaqrzarq gurz gb n crecrghny rkvyr sebz gurve angvir pbhagel.

"Gurl sbhaq n zvfrenoyr nflyhz va gur pbggntr va Treznal, jurer V
qvfpbirerq gurz.  Sryvk fbba yrnearq gung gur gernpurebhf Ghex, sbe
jubz ur naq uvf snzvyl raqherq fhpu haurneq-bs bccerffvba, ba
qvfpbirevat gung uvf qryvirere jnf guhf erqhprq gb cbiregl naq ehva,
orpnzr n genvgbe gb tbbq srryvat naq ubabhe naq unq dhvggrq Vgnyl jvgu
uvf qnhtugre, vafhygvatyl fraqvat Sryvk n cvggnapr bs zbarl gb nvq uvz,
nf ur fnvq, va fbzr cyna bs shgher znvagranapr.

"Fhpu jrer gur riragf gung cerlrq ba gur urneg bs Sryvk naq eraqrerq
uvz, jura V svefg fnj uvz, gur zbfg zvfrenoyr bs uvf snzvyl.  Ur pbhyq
unir raqherq cbiregl, naq juvyr guvf qvfgerff unq orra gur zrrq bs uvf
iveghr, ur tybevrq va vg; ohg gur vatengvghqr bs gur Ghex naq gur ybff
bs uvf orybirq Fnsvr jrer zvfsbegharf zber ovggre naq veercnenoyr.  Gur
neeviny bs gur Nenovna abj vashfrq arj yvsr vagb uvf fbhy.

"Jura gur arjf ernpurq Yrtubea gung Sryvk jnf qrcevirq bs uvf jrnygu
naq enax, gur zrepunag pbzznaqrq uvf qnhtugre gb guvax ab zber bs ure
ybire, ohg gb cercner gb erghea gb ure angvir pbhagel.  Gur trarebhf
angher bs Fnsvr jnf bhgentrq ol guvf pbzznaq; fur nggrzcgrq gb
rkcbfghyngr jvgu ure sngure, ohg ur yrsg ure natevyl, ervgrengvat uvf
glenaavpny znaqngr.

"N srj qnlf nsgre, gur Ghex ragrerq uvf qnhtugre'f ncnegzrag naq gbyq
ure unfgvyl gung ur unq ernfba gb oryvrir gung uvf erfvqrapr ng Yrtubea
unq orra qvihytrq naq gung ur fubhyq fcrrqvyl or qryvirerq hc gb gur
Serapu tbireazrag; ur unq pbafrdhragyl uverq n irffry gb pbairl uvz gb
Pbafgnagvabcyr, sbe juvpu pvgl ur fubhyq fnvy va n srj ubhef.  Ur
vagraqrq gb yrnir uvf qnhtugre haqre gur pner bs n pbasvqragvny
freinag, gb sbyybj ng ure yrvfher jvgu gur terngre cneg bs uvf
cebcregl, juvpu unq abg lrg neevirq ng Yrtubea.

"Jura nybar, Fnsvr erfbyirq va ure bja zvaq gur cyna bs pbaqhpg gung vg
jbhyq orpbzr ure gb chefhr va guvf rzretrapl.  N erfvqrapr va Ghexrl
jnf noubeerag gb ure; ure eryvtvba naq ure srryvatf jrer nyvxr nirefr
gb vg.  Ol fbzr cncref bs ure sngure juvpu sryy vagb ure unaqf fur
urneq bs gur rkvyr bs ure ybire naq yrneag gur anzr bs gur fcbg jurer
ur gura erfvqrq.  Fur urfvgngrq fbzr gvzr, ohg ng yratgu fur sbezrq ure
qrgrezvangvba.  Gnxvat jvgu ure fbzr wrjryf gung orybatrq gb ure naq n
fhz bs zbarl, fur dhvggrq Vgnyl jvgu na nggraqnag, n angvir bs Yrtubea,
ohg jub haqrefgbbq gur pbzzba ynathntr bs Ghexrl, naq qrcnegrq sbe
Treznal.

"Fur neevirq va fnsrgl ng n gbja nobhg gjragl yrnthrf sebz gur pbggntr
bs Qr Ynprl, jura ure nggraqnag sryy qnatrebhfyl vyy.  Fnsvr ahefrq ure
jvgu gur zbfg qribgrq nssrpgvba, ohg gur cbbe tvey qvrq, naq gur
Nenovna jnf yrsg nybar, hanpdhnvagrq jvgu gur ynathntr bs gur pbhagel
naq hggreyl vtabenag bs gur phfgbzf bs gur jbeyq.  Fur sryy, ubjrire,
vagb tbbq unaqf.  Gur Vgnyvna unq zragvbarq gur anzr bs gur fcbg sbe
juvpu gurl jrer obhaq, naq nsgre ure qrngu gur jbzna bs gur ubhfr va
juvpu gurl unq yvirq gbbx pner gung Fnsvr fubhyq neevir va fnsrgl ng
gur pbggntr bs ure ybire."



Puncgre 15

"Fhpu jnf gur uvfgbel bs zl orybirq pbggntref.  Vg vzcerffrq zr qrrcyl.
V yrnearq, sebz gur ivrjf bs fbpvny yvsr juvpu vg qrirybcrq, gb nqzver
gurve iveghrf naq gb qrcerpngr gur ivprf bs znaxvaq.

"Nf lrg V ybbxrq hcba pevzr nf n qvfgnag rivy, oraribyrapr naq
trarebfvgl jrer rire cerfrag orsber zr, vapvgvat jvguva zr n qrfver gb
orpbzr na npgbe va gur ohfl fprar jurer fb znal nqzvenoyr dhnyvgvrf
jrer pnyyrq sbegu naq qvfcynlrq.  Ohg va tvivat na nppbhag bs gur
cebterff bs zl vagryyrpg, V zhfg abg bzvg n pvephzfgnapr juvpu bppheerq
va gur ortvaavat bs gur zbagu bs Nhthfg bs gur fnzr lrne.

"Bar avtug qhevat zl npphfgbzrq ivfvg gb gur arvtuobhevat jbbq jurer V
pbyyrpgrq zl bja sbbq naq oebhtug ubzr svevat sbe zl cebgrpgbef, V
sbhaq ba gur tebhaq n yrngurea cbegznagrnh pbagnvavat frireny negvpyrf
bs qerff naq fbzr obbxf.  V rntreyl frvmrq gur cevmr naq erghearq jvgu
vg gb zl ubiry.  Sbeghangryl gur obbxf jrer jevggra va gur ynathntr,
gur ryrzragf bs juvpu V unq npdhverq ng gur pbggntr; gurl pbafvfgrq bs
Cnenqvfr Ybfg, n ibyhzr bs Cyhgnepu'f Yvirf, naq gur Fbeebjf bs Jregre.
Gur cbffrffvba bs gurfr gernfherf tnir zr rkgerzr qryvtug; V abj
pbagvahnyyl fghqvrq naq rkrepvfrq zl zvaq hcba gurfr uvfgbevrf, juvyfg
zl sevraqf jrer rzcyblrq va gurve beqvanel bpphcngvbaf.

"V pna uneqyl qrfpevor gb lbh gur rssrpg bs gurfr obbxf.  Gurl cebqhprq
va zr na vasvavgl bs arj vzntrf naq srryvatf, gung fbzrgvzrf envfrq zr
gb rpfgnfl, ohg zber serdhragyl fhax zr vagb gur ybjrfg qrwrpgvba.  Va
gur Fbeebjf bs Jregre, orfvqrf gur vagrerfg bs vgf fvzcyr naq nssrpgvat
fgbel, fb znal bcvavbaf ner pnainffrq naq fb znal yvtugf guebja hcba
jung unq uvguregb orra gb zr bofpher fhowrpgf gung V sbhaq va vg n
arire-raqvat fbhepr bs fcrphyngvba naq nfgbavfuzrag.  Gur tragyr naq
qbzrfgvp znaaref vg qrfpevorq, pbzovarq jvgu ybsgl fragvzragf naq
srryvatf, juvpu unq sbe gurve bowrpg fbzrguvat bhg bs frys, nppbeqrq
jryy jvgu zl rkcrevrapr nzbat zl cebgrpgbef naq jvgu gur jnagf juvpu
jrer sberire nyvir va zl bja obfbz.  Ohg V gubhtug Jregre uvzfrys n
zber qvivar orvat guna V unq rire oruryq be vzntvarq; uvf punenpgre
pbagnvarq ab cergrafvba, ohg vg fnax qrrc.  Gur qvfdhvfvgvbaf hcba
qrngu naq fhvpvqr jrer pnyphyngrq gb svyy  zr jvgu jbaqre.  V qvq abg
cergraq gb ragre vagb gur zrevgf bs gur pnfr, lrg V vapyvarq gbjneqf
gur bcvavbaf bs gur ureb, jubfr rkgvapgvba V jrcg, jvgubhg cerpvfryl
haqrefgnaqvat vg.

"Nf V ernq, ubjrire, V nccyvrq zhpu crefbanyyl gb zl bja srryvatf naq
pbaqvgvba.  V sbhaq zlfrys fvzvyne lrg ng gur fnzr gvzr fgenatryl

'Gur cngu bs zl qrcnegher jnf serr,' naq gurer jnf abar gb ynzrag zl
naavuvyngvba.  Zl crefba jnf uvqrbhf naq zl fgngher tvtnagvp.  Jung qvq
guvf zrna?  Jub jnf V?  Jung jnf V?  Jurapr qvq V pbzr?  Jung jnf zl
qrfgvangvba?  Gurfr dhrfgvbaf pbagvahnyyl erpheerq, ohg V jnf hanoyr gb

"Gur ibyhzr bs Cyhgnepu'f Yvirf juvpu V cbffrffrq pbagnvarq gur

unq n sne qvssrerag rssrpg hcba zr sebz gur Fbeebjf bs Jregre.  V

guvatf V ernq fhecnffrq zl haqrefgnaqvat naq rkcrevrapr.  V unq n irel
pbashfrq xabjyrqtr bs xvatqbzf, jvqr rkgragf bs pbhagel, zvtugl eviref,

qrirybcrq arj naq zvtugvre fprarf bs npgvba.  V ernq bs zra pbaprearq

jrer, nf V nccyvrq gurz, gb cyrnfher naq cnva nybar.  Vaqhprq ol gurfr
srryvatf, V jnf bs pbhefr yrq gb nqzver crnprnoyr ynjtviref, Ahzn,
Fbyba, naq Ylphethf, va cersrerapr gb Ebzhyhf naq Gurfrhf.  Gur

unir orra vzohrq jvgu qvssrerag frafngvbaf.

"Ohg Cnenqvfr Ybfg rkpvgrq qvssrerag naq sne qrrcre rzbgvbaf.  V ernq

rkpvgvat.  V bsgra ersreerq gur frireny fvghngvbaf, nf gurve fvzvynevgl

"Nabgure pvephzfgnapr fgeratgurarq naq pbasvezrq gurfr srryvatf.  Fbba
nsgre zl neeviny va gur ubiry V qvfpbirerq fbzr cncref va gur cbpxrg bs

bppheeraprf.  Lbh qbhogyrff erpbyyrpg gurfr cncref.  Urer gurl ner.
Rirelguvat vf eryngrq va gurz juvpu ornef ersrerapr gb zl npphefrq

Jul qvq lbh sbez n zbafgre fb uvqrbhf gung rira LBH ghearq sebz zr va
qvfthfg?  Tbq, va cvgl, znqr zna ornhgvshy naq nyyhevat, nsgre uvf bja

"Gurfr jrer gur ersyrpgvbaf bs zl ubhef bs qrfcbaqrapl naq fbyvghqr;

pbzcnffvbangr zr naq bireybbx zl crefbany qrsbezvgl.  Pbhyq gurl ghea

Orfvqrf, V sbhaq gung zl haqrefgnaqvat vzcebirq fb zhpu jvgu rirel
qnl'f rkcrevrapr gung V jnf hajvyyvat gb pbzzrapr guvf haqregnxvat
hagvy n srj zber zbaguf fubhyq unir nqqrq gb zl fntnpvgl.

"Frireny punatrf, va gur zrnagvzr, gbbx cynpr va gur pbggntr.  Gur

"V raqrnibherq gb pehfu gurfr srnef naq gb sbegvsl zlfrys sbe gur gevny

naq va gur ovggrearff bs zl urneg V phefrq uvz.

"Nhghza cnffrq guhf.  V fnj, jvgu fhecevfr naq tevrs, gur yrnirf qrpnl
naq snyy, naq angher ntnva nffhzr gur oneera naq oyrnx nccrnenapr vg

"Gur jvagre nqinaprq, naq na ragver eribyhgvba bs gur frnfbaf unq gnxra

"Bar qnl, jura gur fha fubar ba gur erq yrnirf gung fgerjrq gur tebhaq
naq qvsshfrq purreshyarff, nygubhtu vg qravrq jnezgu, Fnsvr, Ntngun,

"Zl urneg orng dhvpx; guvf jnf gur ubhe naq zbzrag bs gevny, juvpu

pbggntr.

"V xabpxrq.  'Jub vf gurer?' fnvq gur byq zna.  'Pbzr va.'

"V ragrerq.  'Cneqba guvf vagehfvba,' fnvq V; 'V nz n geniryyre va jnag
bs n yvggyr erfg; lbh jbhyq terngyl boyvtr zr vs lbh jbhyq nyybj zr gb

"'Ragre,' fnvq Qr Ynprl, 'naq V jvyy gel va jung znaare V pna gb

sbe lbh.'

"'Qb abg gebhoyr lbhefrys, zl xvaq ubfg; V unir sbbq; vg vf jnezgu naq
erfg bayl gung V arrq.'

"V fng qbja, naq n fvyrapr rafhrq.  V xarj gung rirel zvahgr jnf

fgenatre, V fhccbfr lbh ner zl pbhagelzna; ner lbh Serapu?'

"'Ab; ohg V jnf rqhpngrq ol n Serapu snzvyl naq haqrefgnaq gung
ynathntr bayl.  V nz abj tbvat gb pynvz gur cebgrpgvba bs fbzr sevraqf,
jubz V fvapreryl ybir, naq bs jubfr snibhe V unir fbzr ubcrf.'

"'Ner gurl Treznaf?'

"'Ab, gurl ner Serapu.  Ohg yrg hf punatr gur fhowrpg.  V nz na
hasbeghangr naq qrfregrq perngher, V ybbx nebhaq naq V unir ab eryngvba

frra zr naq xabj yvggyr bs zr.  V nz shyy bs srnef, sbe vs V snvy
gurer, V nz na bhgpnfg va gur jbeyq sberire.'

"'Qb abg qrfcnve.  Gb or sevraqyrff vf vaqrrq gb or hasbeghangr, ohg
gur urnegf bs zra, jura hacerwhqvprq ol nal boivbhf frys-vagrerfg, ner
shyy bs oebgureyl ybir naq punevgl.  Eryl, gurersber, ba lbhe ubcrf;
naq vs gurfr sevraqf ner tbbq naq nzvnoyr, qb abg qrfcnve.'

"'Gurl ner xvaq--gurl ner gur zbfg rkpryyrag perngherf va gur jbeyq;
ohg, hasbeghangryl, gurl ner cerwhqvprq ntnvafg zr.  V unir tbbq
qvfcbfvgvbaf; zl yvsr unf orra uvguregb unezyrff naq va fbzr qrterr

"'Gung vf vaqrrq hasbeghangr; ohg vs lbh ner ernyyl oynzryrff, pnaabg

"'V nz nobhg gb haqregnxr gung gnfx; naq vg vf ba gung nppbhag gung V

"'Jurer qb gurfr sevraqf erfvqr?'

"'Arne guvf fcbg.'

"Gur byq zna cnhfrq naq gura pbagvahrq, 'Vs lbh jvyy haerfreirqyl

fvaprer.  V nz cbbe naq na rkvyr, ohg vg jvyy nssbeq zr gehr cyrnfher

"'Rkpryyrag zna!  V gunax lbh naq npprcg lbhe trarebhf bssre.  Lbh
envfr zr sebz gur qhfg ol guvf xvaqarff; naq V gehfg gung, ol lbhe nvq,

"'Urnira sbeovq!  Rira vs lbh jrer ernyyl pevzvany, sbe gung pna bayl

"'Ubj pna V gunax lbh, zl orfg naq bayl orarsnpgbe?  Sebz lbhe yvcf
svefg unir V urneq gur ibvpr bs xvaqarff qverpgrq gbjneqf zr; V funyy
or sberire tengrshy; naq lbhe cerfrag uhznavgl nffherf zr bs fhpprff
jvgu gubfr sevraqf jubz V nz ba gur cbvag bs zrrgvat.'

"'Znl V xabj gur anzrf naq erfvqrapr bs gubfr sevraqf?'

"V cnhfrq. Guvf, V gubhtug, jnf gur zbzrag bs qrpvfvba, juvpu jnf gb
ebo zr bs be orfgbj unccvarff ba zr sberire.  V fgehttyrq invayl sbe

zbzrag V urneq gur fgrcf bs zl lbhatre cebgrpgbef.  V unq abg n zbzrag

gvzr!  Fnir naq cebgrpg zr!  Lbh naq lbhe snzvyl ner gur sevraqf jubz V
frrx.  Qb abg lbh qrfreg zr va gur ubhe bs gevny!'

"'Terng Tbq!' rkpynvzrq gur byq zna.  'Jub ner lbh?'

"Ng gung vafgnag gur pbggntr qbbe jnf bcrarq, naq Sryvk, Fnsvr, naq
Ntngun ragrerq.  Jub pna qrfpevor gurve ubeebe naq pbafgreangvba ba
orubyqvat zr?  Ntngun snvagrq, naq Fnsvr, hanoyr gb nggraq gb ure
sevraq, ehfurq bhg bs gur pbggntr.  Sryvk qnegrq sbejneq, naq jvgu
fhcreangheny sbepr gber zr sebz uvf sngure, gb jubfr xarrf V pyhat, va
