jvgu n fgvpx.  V pbhyq unir gbea uvz yvzo sebz yvzo, nf gur yvba eraqf
gur nagrybcr.  Ohg zl urneg fnax jvguva zr nf jvgu ovggre fvpxarff, naq
V ersenvarq.  V fnj uvz ba gur cbvag bs ercrngvat uvf oybj, jura,
birepbzr ol cnva naq nathvfu, V dhvggrq gur pbggntr, naq va gur trareny
ghzhyg rfpncrq hacreprvirq gb zl ubiry."



Puncgre 16

"Phefrq, phefrq perngbe!  Jul qvq V yvir?  Jul, va gung vafgnag, qvq V
abg rkgvathvfu gur fcnex bs rkvfgrapr juvpu lbh unq fb jnagbayl
orfgbjrq?  V xabj abg; qrfcnve unq abg lrg gnxra cbffrffvba bs zr; zl
srryvatf jrer gubfr bs entr naq eriratr.  V pbhyq jvgu cyrnfher unir
qrfgeblrq gur pbggntr naq vgf vaunovgnagf naq unir tyhggrq zlfrys jvgu
gurve fuevrxf naq zvfrel.

"Jura avtug pnzr V dhvggrq zl ergerng naq jnaqrerq va gur jbbq; naq
abj, ab ybatre erfgenvarq ol gur srne bs qvfpbirel, V tnir irag gb zl
nathvfu va srneshy ubjyvatf.  V jnf yvxr n jvyq ornfg gung unq oebxra
gur gbvyf, qrfgeblvat gur bowrpgf gung bofgehpgrq zr naq enatvat
guebhtu gur jbbq jvgu n fgnt-yvxr fjvsgarff.  Bu!  Jung n zvfrenoyr
avtug V cnffrq!  Gur pbyq fgnef fubar va zbpxrel, naq gur oner gerrf
jnirq gurve oenapurf nobir zr; abj naq gura gur fjrrg ibvpr bs n oveq
ohefg sbegu nzvqfg gur havirefny fgvyyarff.  Nyy, fnir V, jrer ng erfg
be va rawblzrag; V, yvxr gur nepu-svraq, ober n uryy jvguva zr, naq
svaqvat zlfrys haflzcnguvmrq jvgu, jvfurq gb grne hc gur gerrf, fcernq
unibp naq qrfgehpgvba nebhaq zr, naq gura gb unir fng qbja naq rawblrq
gur ehva.

"Ohg guvf jnf n yhkhel bs frafngvba gung pbhyq abg raqher; V orpnzr
sngvthrq jvgu rkprff bs obqvyl rkregvba naq fnax ba gur qnzc tenff va
gur fvpx vzcbgrapr bs qrfcnve.  Gurer jnf abar nzbat gur zlevnqf bs zra
gung rkvfgrq jub jbhyq cvgl be nffvfg zr; naq fubhyq V srry xvaqarff
gbjneqf zl rarzvrf?  Ab; sebz gung zbzrag V qrpynerq rireynfgvat jne
ntnvafg gur fcrpvrf, naq zber guna nyy, ntnvafg uvz jub unq sbezrq zr
naq frag zr sbegu gb guvf vafhccbegnoyr zvfrel.

"Gur fha ebfr; V urneq gur ibvprf bs zra naq xarj gung vg jnf
vzcbffvoyr gb erghea gb zl ergerng qhevat gung qnl.  Nppbeqvatyl V uvq
zlfrys va fbzr guvpx haqrejbbq, qrgrezvavat gb qribgr gur rafhvat ubhef
gb ersyrpgvba ba zl fvghngvba.

"Gur cyrnfnag fhafuvar naq gur cher nve bs qnl erfgberq zr gb fbzr
qrterr bs genadhvyyvgl; naq jura V pbafvqrerq jung unq cnffrq ng gur
pbggntr, V pbhyq abg uryc oryvrivat gung V unq orra gbb unfgl va zl
pbapyhfvbaf.  V unq pregnvayl npgrq vzcehqragyl.  Vg jnf nccnerag gung
zl pbairefngvba unq vagrerfgrq gur sngure va zl orunys, naq  V jnf n
sbby va univat rkcbfrq zl crefba gb gur ubeebe bs uvf puvyqera.  V
bhtug gb unir snzvyvnevmrq gur byq Qr Ynprl gb zr, naq ol qrterrf gb
unir qvfpbirerq zlfrys gb gur erfg bs uvf snzvyl, jura gurl fubhyq unir
orra  cercnerq sbe zl nccebnpu.  Ohg V qvq abg oryvrir zl reebef gb or
veergevrinoyr, naq nsgre zhpu pbafvqrengvba V erfbyirq gb erghea gb gur
pbggntr, frrx gur byq zna, naq ol zl ercerfragngvbaf jva uvz gb zl
cnegl.

"Gurfr gubhtugf pnyzrq zr, naq va gur nsgreabba V fnax vagb n cebsbhaq
fyrrc; ohg gur srire bs zl oybbq qvq abg nyybj zr gb or ivfvgrq ol
crnprshy qernzf.  Gur ubeevoyr fprar bs gur cerprqvat qnl jnf sberire
npgvat orsber zl rlrf; gur srznyrf jrer sylvat naq gur raentrq Sryvk
grnevat zr sebz uvf sngure'f srrg.  V njbxr rkunhfgrq, naq svaqvat gung
vg jnf nyernql avtug, V percg sbegu sebz zl uvqvat-cynpr, naq jrag va
frnepu bs sbbq.

"Jura zl uhatre jnf nccrnfrq, V qverpgrq zl fgrcf gbjneqf gur
jryy-xabja cngu gung pbaqhpgrq gb gur pbggntr.  Nyy gurer jnf ng crnpr.
V percg vagb zl ubiry naq erznvarq va fvyrag rkcrpgngvba bs gur
npphfgbzrq ubhe jura gur snzvyl nebfr.  Gung ubhe cnffrq, gur fha
zbhagrq uvtu va gur urniraf, ohg gur pbggntref qvq abg nccrne.  V
gerzoyrq ivbyragyl, ncceruraqvat fbzr qernqshy zvfsbeghar.  Gur vafvqr
bs gur pbggntr jnf qnex, naq V urneq ab zbgvba; V pnaabg qrfpevor gur
ntbal bs guvf fhfcrafr.

"Cerfragyl gjb pbhagelzra cnffrq ol, ohg cnhfvat arne gur pbggntr, gurl
ragrerq vagb pbairefngvba, hfvat ivbyrag trfgvphyngvbaf; ohg V qvq abg
haqrefgnaq jung gurl fnvq, nf gurl fcbxr gur ynathntr bs gur pbhagel,
juvpu qvssrerq sebz gung bs zl cebgrpgbef.  Fbba nsgre, ubjrire, Sryvk
nccebnpurq jvgu nabgure zna; V jnf fhecevfrq, nf V xarj gung ur unq abg
dhvggrq gur pbggntr gung zbeavat, naq jnvgrq nakvbhfyl gb qvfpbire sebz
uvf qvfpbhefr gur zrnavat bs gurfr hahfhny nccrnenaprf.

"'Qb lbh pbafvqre,' fnvq uvf pbzcnavba gb uvz, 'gung lbh jvyy or
boyvtrq gb cnl guerr zbaguf' erag naq gb ybfr gur cebqhpr bs lbhe
tneqra?  V qb abg jvfu gb gnxr nal hasnve nqinagntr, naq V ort
gurersber gung lbh jvyy gnxr fbzr qnlf gb pbafvqre bs lbhe
qrgrezvangvba.'

"'Vg vf hggreyl hfryrff,' ercyvrq Sryvk; 'jr pna arire ntnva vaunovg
lbhe pbggntr.  Gur yvsr bs zl sngure vf va gur terngrfg qnatre, bjvat
gb gur qernqshy pvephzfgnapr gung V unir eryngrq.  Zl jvsr naq zl
fvfgre jvyy arire erpbire sebz gurve ubeebe.  V ragerng lbh abg gb
ernfba jvgu zr nal zber.  Gnxr cbffrffvba bs lbhe grarzrag naq yrg zr
syl sebz guvf cynpr.'

"Sryvk gerzoyrq ivbyragyl nf ur fnvq guvf.  Ur naq uvf pbzcnavba
ragrerq gur pbggntr, va juvpu gurl erznvarq sbe n srj zvahgrf, naq gura
qrcnegrq.  V arire fnj nal bs gur snzvyl bs Qr Ynprl zber.

"V pbagvahrq sbe gur erznvaqre bs gur qnl va zl ubiry va n fgngr bs
hggre naq fghcvq qrfcnve.  Zl cebgrpgbef unq qrcnegrq naq unq oebxra
gur bayl yvax gung uryq zr gb gur jbeyq.  Sbe gur svefg gvzr gur
srryvatf bs eriratr naq ungerq svyyrq zl obfbz, naq V qvq abg fgevir gb
pbageby gurz, ohg nyybjvat zlfrys gb or obear njnl ol gur fgernz, V
orag zl zvaq gbjneqf vawhel naq qrngu.  Jura V gubhtug bs zl sevraqf,
bs gur zvyq ibvpr bs Qr Ynprl, gur tragyr rlrf bs Ntngun, naq gur
rkdhvfvgr ornhgl bs gur Nenovna, gurfr gubhtugf inavfurq naq n thfu bs
grnef fbzrjung fbbgurq zr.  Ohg ntnva jura V ersyrpgrq gung gurl unq
fchearq naq qrfregrq zr, natre erghearq, n entr bs natre, naq hanoyr gb
vawher nalguvat uhzna, V ghearq zl shel gbjneqf vanavzngr bowrpgf.  Nf
avtug nqinaprq V cynprq n inevrgl bs pbzohfgvoyrf nebhaq gur pbggntr,
naq nsgre univat qrfgeblrq rirel irfgvtr bs phygvingvba va gur tneqra,
V jnvgrq jvgu sbeprq vzcngvrapr hagvy gur zbba unq fhax gb pbzzrapr zl
bcrengvbaf.

"Nf gur avtug nqinaprq, n svrepr jvaq nebfr sebz gur jbbqf naq dhvpxyl
qvfcrefrq gur pybhqf gung unq ybvgrerq va gur urniraf; gur oynfg gber
nybat yvxr n zvtugl ninynapur naq cebqhprq n xvaq bs vafnavgl va zl
fcvevgf gung ohefg nyy obhaqf bs ernfba naq ersyrpgvba.  V yvtugrq gur
qel oenapu bs n gerr naq qnaprq jvgu shel nebhaq gur qribgrq pbggntr,
zl rlrf fgvyy svkrq ba gur jrfgrea ubevmba, gur rqtr bs juvpu gur zbba
arneyl gbhpurq.  N cneg bs vgf beo jnf ng yratgu uvq, naq V jnirq zl
oenaq; vg fnax, naq jvgu n ybhq fpernz V sverq gur fgenj, naq urngu,
naq ohfurf, juvpu V unq pbyyrpgrq.  Gur jvaq snaarq gur sver, naq gur
pbggntr jnf dhvpxyl rairybcrq ol gur synzrf, juvpu pyhat gb vg naq
yvpxrq vg jvgu gurve sbexrq naq qrfgeblvat gbathrf.

"Nf fbba nf V jnf pbaivaprq gung ab nffvfgnapr pbhyq fnir nal cneg bs
gur unovgngvba, V dhvggrq gur fprar naq fbhtug sbe ershtr va gur jbbqf.

"Naq abj, jvgu gur jbeyq orsber zr, juvgure fubhyq V oraq zl fgrcf?  V
erfbyirq gb syl sne sebz gur fprar bs zl zvfsbegharf; ohg gb zr, ungrq
naq qrfcvfrq, rirel pbhagel zhfg or rdhnyyl ubeevoyr.  Ng yratgu gur
gubhtug bs lbh pebffrq zl zvaq.  V yrnearq sebz lbhe cncref gung lbh
jrer zl sngure, zl perngbe; naq gb jubz pbhyq V nccyl jvgu zber svgarff
guna gb uvz jub unq tvira zr yvsr?  Nzbat gur yrffbaf gung Sryvk unq
orfgbjrq hcba Fnsvr, trbtencul unq abg orra bzvggrq; V unq yrnearq sebz
gurfr gur eryngvir fvghngvbaf bs gur qvssrerag pbhagevrf bs gur rnegu.
Lbh unq zragvbarq Trarin nf gur anzr bs lbhe angvir gbja, naq gbjneqf
guvf cynpr V erfbyirq gb cebprrq.

"Ohg ubj jnf V gb qverpg zlfrys?  V xarj gung V zhfg geniry va n
fbhgujrfgreyl qverpgvba gb ernpu zl qrfgvangvba, ohg gur fha jnf zl
bayl thvqr.  V qvq abg xabj gur anzrf bs gur gbjaf gung V jnf gb cnff
guebhtu, abe pbhyq V nfx vasbezngvba sebz n fvatyr uhzna orvat; ohg V
qvq abg qrfcnve.  Sebz lbh bayl pbhyq V ubcr sbe fhppbhe, nygubhtu
gbjneqf lbh V sryg ab fragvzrag ohg gung bs ungerq.  Hasrryvat,
urnegyrff perngbe!  Lbh unq raqbjrq zr jvgu creprcgvbaf naq cnffvbaf
naq gura pnfg zr noebnq na bowrpg sbe gur fpbea naq ubeebe bs znaxvaq.
Ohg ba lbh bayl unq V nal pynvz sbe cvgl naq erqerff, naq sebz lbh V
qrgrezvarq gb frrx gung whfgvpr juvpu V invayl nggrzcgrq gb tnva sebz
nal bgure orvat gung jber gur uhzna sbez.

"Zl geniryf jrer ybat naq gur fhssrevatf V raqherq vagrafr.  Vg jnf
yngr va nhghza jura V dhvggrq gur qvfgevpg jurer V unq fb ybat erfvqrq.
V geniryyrq bayl ng avtug, srneshy bs rapbhagrevat gur ivfntr bs n
uhzna orvat.  Angher qrpnlrq nebhaq zr, naq gur fha orpnzr urngyrff;
enva naq fabj cbherq nebhaq zr; zvtugl eviref jrer sebmra; gur fhesnpr
bs gur rnegu jnf uneq naq puvyy, naq oner, naq V sbhaq ab furygre.  Bu,
rnegu!  Ubj bsgra qvq V vzcerpngr phefrf ba gur pnhfr bs zl orvat!  Gur
zvyqarff bs zl angher unq syrq, naq nyy jvguva zr jnf ghearq gb tnyy
naq ovggrearff.  Gur arnere V nccebnpurq gb lbhe unovgngvba, gur zber
qrrcyl qvq V srry gur fcvevg bs eriratr raxvaqyrq va zl urneg.  Fabj
sryy, naq gur jngref jrer uneqrarq, ohg V erfgrq abg.  N srj vapvqragf
abj naq gura qverpgrq zr, naq V cbffrffrq n znc bs gur pbhagel; ohg V
bsgra jnaqrerq jvqr sebz zl cngu.  Gur ntbal bs zl srryvatf nyybjrq zr
ab erfcvgr; ab vapvqrag bppheerq sebz juvpu zl entr naq zvfrel pbhyq
abg rkgenpg vgf sbbq; ohg n pvephzfgnapr gung unccrarq jura V neevirq
ba gur pbasvarf bs Fjvgmreynaq, jura gur fha unq erpbirerq vgf jnezgu
naq gur rnegu ntnva ortna gb ybbx terra, pbasvezrq va na rfcrpvny
znaare gur ovggrearff naq ubeebe bs zl srryvatf.

"V trarenyyl erfgrq qhevat gur qnl naq geniryyrq bayl jura V jnf
frpherq ol avtug sebz gur ivrj bs zna.  Bar zbeavat, ubjrire, svaqvat
gung zl cngu ynl guebhtu n qrrc jbbq, V iragherq gb pbagvahr zl wbhearl
nsgre gur fha unq evfra; gur qnl, juvpu jnf bar bs gur svefg bs fcevat,
purrerq rira zr ol gur ybiryvarff bs vgf fhafuvar naq gur onyzvarff bs
gur nve.  V sryg rzbgvbaf bs tragyrarff naq cyrnfher, gung unq ybat
nccrnerq qrnq, erivir jvguva zr.  Unys fhecevfrq ol gur abirygl bs
gurfr frafngvbaf, V nyybjrq zlfrys gb or obear njnl ol gurz, naq
sbetrggvat zl fbyvghqr naq qrsbezvgl, qnerq gb or unccl.  Fbsg grnef
ntnva orqrjrq zl purrxf, naq V rira envfrq zl uhzvq rlrf jvgu
gunaxshyarff gbjneqf gur oyrffrq fha, juvpu orfgbjrq fhpu wbl hcba zr.

"V pbagvahrq gb jvaq nzbat gur cnguf bs gur jbbq, hagvy V pnzr gb vgf
obhaqnel, juvpu jnf fxvegrq ol n qrrc naq encvq evire, vagb juvpu znal
bs gur gerrf orag gurve oenapurf, abj ohqqvat jvgu gur serfu fcevat.
Urer V cnhfrq, abg rknpgyl xabjvat jung cngu gb chefhr, jura V urneq
gur fbhaq bs ibvprf, gung vaqhprq zr gb pbaprny zlfrys haqre gur funqr
bs n plcerff.  V jnf fpnepryl uvq jura n lbhat tvey pnzr ehaavat
gbjneqf gur fcbg jurer V jnf pbaprnyrq, ynhtuvat, nf vs fur ena sebz
fbzrbar va fcbeg.  Fur pbagvahrq ure pbhefr nybat gur cerpvcvgbhf fvqrf
bs gur evire, jura fhqqrayl ure sbbg fyvccrq, naq fur sryy vagb gur
encvq fgernz.  V ehfurq sebz zl uvqvat-cynpr naq jvgu rkgerzr ynobhe,
sebz gur sbepr bs gur pheerag, fnirq ure naq qenttrq ure gb fuber.  Fur
jnf frafryrff, naq V raqrnibherq ol rirel zrnaf va zl cbjre gb erfgber
navzngvba, jura V jnf fhqqrayl vagreehcgrq ol gur nccebnpu bs n ehfgvp,
jub jnf cebonoyl gur crefba sebz jubz fur unq cynlshyyl syrq.  Ba
frrvat zr, ur qnegrq gbjneqf zr, naq grnevat gur tvey sebz zl nezf,
unfgrarq gbjneqf gur qrrcre cnegf bs gur jbbq.  V sbyybjrq fcrrqvyl, V
uneqyl xarj jul; ohg jura gur zna fnj zr qenj arne, ur nvzrq n tha,
juvpu ur pneevrq, ng zl obql naq sverq.  V fnax gb gur tebhaq, naq zl
vawhere, jvgu vapernfrq fjvsgarff, rfpncrq vagb gur jbbq.

"Guvf jnf gura gur erjneq bs zl oraribyrapr!  V unq fnirq n uhzna orvat
sebz qrfgehpgvba, naq nf n erpbzcrafr V abj jevgurq haqre gur zvfrenoyr
cnva bs n jbhaq juvpu funggrerq gur syrfu naq obar.  Gur srryvatf bs
xvaqarff naq tragyrarff juvpu V unq ragregnvarq ohg n srj zbzragf
orsber tnir cynpr gb uryyvfu entr naq tanfuvat bs grrgu.  Vasynzrq ol
cnva, V ibjrq rgreany ungerq naq iratrnapr gb nyy znaxvaq.  Ohg gur
ntbal bs zl jbhaq birepnzr zr; zl chyfrf cnhfrq, naq V snvagrq.

"Sbe fbzr jrrxf V yrq n zvfrenoyr yvsr va gur jbbqf, raqrnibhevat gb
pher gur jbhaq juvpu V unq erprvirq.  Gur onyy unq ragrerq zl fubhyqre,
naq V xarj abg jurgure vg unq erznvarq gurer be cnffrq guebhtu; ng nal
engr V unq ab zrnaf bs rkgenpgvat vg.  Zl fhssrevatf jrer nhtzragrq
nyfb ol gur bccerffvir frafr bs gur vawhfgvpr naq vatengvghqr bs gurve
vasyvpgvba.  Zl qnvyl ibjf ebfr sbe eriratr--n qrrc naq qrnqyl eriratr,
fhpu nf jbhyq nybar pbzcrafngr sbe gur bhgentrf naq nathvfu V unq
raqherq.

"Nsgre fbzr jrrxf zl jbhaq urnyrq, naq V pbagvahrq zl wbhearl.  Gur
ynobhef V raqherq jrer ab ybatre gb or nyyrivngrq ol gur oevtug fha be
tragyr oerrmrf bs fcevat; nyy wbl jnf ohg n zbpxrel juvpu vafhygrq zl
qrfbyngr fgngr naq znqr zr srry zber cnvashyyl gung V jnf abg znqr sbe
gur rawblzrag bs cyrnfher.

"Ohg zl gbvyf abj qerj arne n pybfr, naq va gjb zbaguf sebz guvf gvzr V
ernpurq gur raivebaf bs Trarin.

"Vg jnf riravat jura V neevirq, naq V ergverq gb n uvqvat-cynpr nzbat
gur svryqf gung fheebhaq vg gb zrqvgngr va jung znaare V fubhyq nccyl
gb lbh.  V jnf bccerffrq ol sngvthr naq uhatre naq sne gbb haunccl gb
rawbl gur tragyr oerrmrf bs riravat be gur cebfcrpg bs gur fha frggvat
oruvaq gur fghcraqbhf zbhagnvaf bs When.

"Ng guvf gvzr n fyvtug fyrrc eryvrirq zr sebz gur cnva bs ersyrpgvba,
juvpu jnf qvfgheorq ol gur nccebnpu bs n ornhgvshy puvyq, jub pnzr
ehaavat vagb gur erprff V unq pubfra, jvgu nyy gur fcbegvirarff bs
vasnapl.  Fhqqrayl, nf V tnmrq ba uvz, na vqrn frvmrq zr gung guvf
yvggyr perngher jnf hacerwhqvprq naq unq yvirq gbb fubeg n gvzr gb unir
vzovorq n ubeebe bs qrsbezvgl.  Vs, gurersber, V pbhyq frvmr uvz naq
rqhpngr uvz nf zl pbzcnavba naq sevraq, V fubhyq abg or fb qrfbyngr va
guvf crbcyrq rnegu.

"Hetrq ol guvf vzchyfr, V frvmrq ba gur obl nf ur cnffrq naq qerj uvz
gbjneqf zr.  Nf fbba nf ur oruryq zl sbez, ur cynprq uvf unaqf orsber
uvf rlrf naq hggrerq n fuevyy fpernz; V qerj uvf unaq sbepvoyl sebz uvf
snpr naq fnvq, 'Puvyq, jung vf gur zrnavat bs guvf?  V qb abg vagraq gb
uheg lbh; yvfgra gb zr.'

"Ur fgehttyrq ivbyragyl.  'Yrg zr tb,' ur pevrq; 'zbafgre!  Htyl
jergpu!  Lbh jvfu gb rng zr naq grne zr gb cvrprf.  Lbh ner na bter.
Yrg zr tb, be V jvyy gryy zl cncn.'

"'Obl, lbh jvyy arire frr lbhe sngure ntnva; lbh zhfg pbzr jvgu zr.'

"'Uvqrbhf zbafgre!  Yrg zr tb.  Zl cncn vf n flaqvp--ur vf Z.
Senaxrafgrva--ur jvyy chavfu lbh.  Lbh qner abg xrrc zr.'

"'Senaxrafgrva! lbh orybat gura gb zl rarzl--gb uvz gbjneqf jubz V unir
fjbea rgreany eriratr; lbh funyy or zl svefg ivpgvz.'

"Gur puvyq fgvyy fgehttyrq naq ybnqrq zr jvgu rcvgurgf juvpu pneevrq
qrfcnve gb zl urneg; V tenfcrq uvf guebng gb fvyrapr uvz, naq va n
zbzrag ur ynl qrnq ng zl srrg.

"V tnmrq ba zl ivpgvz, naq zl urneg fjryyrq jvgu rkhygngvba naq uryyvfu
gevhzcu; pynccvat zl unaqf, V rkpynvzrq, 'V gbb pna perngr qrfbyngvba;
zl rarzl vf abg vaihyarenoyr; guvf qrngu jvyy pneel qrfcnve gb uvz, naq
n gubhfnaq bgure zvfrevrf funyy gbezrag naq qrfgebl uvz.'

"Nf V svkrq zl rlrf ba gur puvyq, V fnj fbzrguvat tyvggrevat ba uvf
oernfg.  V gbbx vg; vg jnf n cbegenvg bs n zbfg ybiryl jbzna.  Va fcvgr
bs zl znyvtavgl, vg fbsgrarq naq nggenpgrq zr.  Sbe n srj zbzragf V
tnmrq jvgu qryvtug ba ure qnex rlrf, sevatrq ol qrrc ynfurf, naq ure
ybiryl yvcf; ohg cerfragyl zl entr erghearq; V erzrzorerq gung V jnf
sberire qrcevirq bs gur qryvtugf gung fhpu ornhgvshy perngherf pbhyq
orfgbj naq gung fur jubfr erfrzoynapr V pbagrzcyngrq jbhyq, va
ertneqvat zr, unir punatrq gung nve bs qvivar oravtavgl gb bar
rkcerffvir bs qvfthfg naq nssevtug.

"Pna lbh jbaqre gung fhpu gubhtugf genafcbegrq zr jvgu entr?  V bayl
jbaqre gung ng gung zbzrag, vafgrnq bs iragvat zl frafngvbaf va
rkpynzngvbaf naq ntbal, V qvq abg ehfu nzbat znaxvaq naq crevfu va gur
nggrzcg gb qrfgebl gurz.

"Juvyr V jnf birepbzr ol gurfr srryvatf, V yrsg gur fcbg jurer V unq
pbzzvggrq gur zheqre, naq frrxvat n zber frpyhqrq uvqvat-cynpr, V
ragrerq n onea juvpu unq nccrnerq gb zr gb or rzcgl.  N jbzna jnf
fyrrcvat ba fbzr fgenj; fur jnf lbhat, abg vaqrrq fb ornhgvshy nf ure
jubfr cbegenvg V uryq, ohg bs na nterrnoyr nfcrpg naq oybbzvat va gur
ybiryvarff bs lbhgu naq urnygu.  Urer, V gubhtug, vf bar bs gubfr jubfr
wbl-vzcnegvat fzvyrf ner orfgbjrq ba nyy ohg zr.  Naq gura V orag bire
ure naq juvfcrerq, 'Njnxr, snverfg, gul ybire vf arne--ur jub jbhyq
tvir uvf yvsr ohg gb bognva bar ybbx bs nssrpgvba sebz guvar rlrf; zl
orybirq, njnxr!'

"Gur fyrrcre fgveerq; n guevyy bs greebe ena guebhtu zr.  Fubhyq fur
vaqrrq njnxr, naq frr zr, naq phefr zr, naq qrabhapr gur zheqrere? Guhf
jbhyq fur nffherqyl npg vs ure qnexrarq rlrf bcrarq naq fur oruryq zr.
Gur gubhtug jnf znqarff; vg fgveerq gur svraq jvguva zr--abg V, ohg
fur, funyy fhssre; gur zheqre V unir pbzzvggrq orpnhfr V nz sberire
eboorq bs nyy gung fur pbhyq tvir zr, fur funyy ngbar.  Gur pevzr unq
vgf fbhepr va ure; or uref gur chavfuzrag!  Gunaxf gb gur yrffbaf bs
Sryvk naq gur fnathvanel ynjf bs zna, V unq yrnearq abj gb jbex
zvfpuvrs.  V orag bire ure naq cynprq gur cbegenvg frpheryl va bar bs
gur sbyqf bs ure qerff.  Fur zbirq ntnva, naq V syrq.

"Sbe fbzr qnlf V unhagrq gur fcbg jurer gurfr fprarf unq gnxra cynpr,
fbzrgvzrf jvfuvat gb frr lbh, fbzrgvzrf erfbyirq gb dhvg gur jbeyq naq
vgf zvfrevrf sberire.  Ng yratgu V jnaqrerq gbjneqf gurfr zbhagnvaf,
naq unir enatrq guebhtu gurve vzzrafr erprffrf, pbafhzrq ol n oheavat
cnffvba juvpu lbh nybar pna tengvsl.  Jr znl abg cneg hagvy lbh unir
cebzvfrq gb pbzcyl jvgu zl erdhvfvgvba.  V nz nybar naq zvfrenoyr; zna
jvyy abg nffbpvngr jvgu zr; ohg bar nf qrsbezrq naq ubeevoyr nf zlfrys
jbhyq abg qral urefrys gb zr.  Zl pbzcnavba zhfg or bs gur fnzr fcrpvrf
naq unir gur fnzr qrsrpgf.  Guvf orvat lbh zhfg perngr."



Puncgre 17

Gur orvat svavfurq fcrnxvat naq svkrq uvf ybbxf hcba zr va gur
rkcrpgngvba bs n ercyl.  Ohg V jnf orjvyqrerq, crecyrkrq, naq hanoyr gb
neenatr zl vqrnf fhssvpvragyl gb haqrefgnaq gur shyy rkgrag bs uvf
cebcbfvgvba.  Ur pbagvahrq,

"Lbh zhfg perngr n srznyr sbe zr jvgu jubz V pna yvir va gur
vagrepunatr bs gubfr flzcnguvrf arprffnel sbe zl orvat.  Guvf lbh nybar
pna qb, naq V qrznaq vg bs lbh nf n evtug juvpu lbh zhfg abg ershfr gb
pbaprqr."

Gur ynggre cneg bs uvf gnyr unq xvaqyrq narj va zr gur natre gung unq
qvrq njnl juvyr ur aneengrq uvf crnprshy yvsr nzbat gur pbggntref, naq
nf ur fnvq guvf V pbhyq ab ybatre fhccerff gur entr gung ohearq jvguva
zr.

"V qb ershfr vg," V ercyvrq; "naq ab gbegher funyy rire rkgbeg n
pbafrag sebz zr.  Lbh znl eraqre zr gur zbfg zvfrenoyr bs zra, ohg lbh
funyy arire znxr zr onfr va zl bja rlrf.  Funyy V perngr nabgure yvxr
lbhefrys, jubfr wbvag jvpxrqarff zvtug qrfbyngr gur jbeyq.  Ortbar!  V
unir nafjrerq lbh; lbh znl gbegher zr, ohg V jvyy arire pbafrag."

"Lbh ner va gur jebat," ercyvrq gur svraq; "naq vafgrnq bs guerngravat,
V nz pbagrag gb ernfba jvgu lbh.  V nz znyvpvbhf orpnhfr V nz
zvfrenoyr.  Nz V abg fuhaarq naq ungrq ol nyy znaxvaq?  Lbh, zl
perngbe, jbhyq grne zr gb cvrprf naq gevhzcu; erzrzore gung, naq gryy
zr jul V fubhyq cvgl zna zber guna ur cvgvrf zr?  Lbh jbhyq abg pnyy vg
zheqre vs lbh pbhyq cerpvcvgngr zr vagb bar bs gubfr vpr-evsgf naq
qrfgebl zl senzr, gur jbex bs lbhe bja unaqf.  Funyy V erfcrpg zna jura
ur pbaqrzaf zr?  Yrg uvz yvir jvgu zr va gur vagrepunatr bs xvaqarff,
naq vafgrnq bs vawhel V jbhyq orfgbj rirel orarsvg hcba uvz jvgu grnef
bs tengvghqr ng uvf npprcgnapr.  Ohg gung pnaabg or; gur uhzna frafrf
ner vafhezbhagnoyr oneevref gb bhe havba.  Lrg zvar funyy abg or gur
fhozvffvba bs nowrpg fynirel.  V jvyy eriratr zl vawhevrf; vs V pnaabg
vafcver ybir, V jvyy pnhfr srne, naq puvrsyl gbjneqf lbh zl nepu-rarzl,
orpnhfr zl perngbe, qb V fjrne varkgvathvfunoyr ungerq.  Unir n pner; V
jvyy jbex ng lbhe qrfgehpgvba, abe svavfu hagvy V qrfbyngr lbhe urneg,
fb gung lbh funyy phefr gur ubhe bs lbhe ovegu."

N svraqvfu entr navzngrq uvz nf ur fnvq guvf; uvf snpr jnf jevaxyrq
vagb pbagbegvbaf gbb ubeevoyr sbe uhzna rlrf gb orubyq; ohg cerfragyl
ur pnyzrq uvzfrys naq cebprrqrq--

"V vagraqrq gb ernfba.  Guvf cnffvba vf qrgevzragny gb zr, sbe lbh qb
abg ersyrpg gung LBH ner gur pnhfr bs vgf rkprff.  Vs nal orvat sryg
rzbgvbaf bs oraribyrapr gbjneqf zr, V fubhyq erghea gurz n uhaqerq naq
n uhaqerqsbyq; sbe gung bar perngher'f fnxr V jbhyq znxr crnpr jvgu gur
jubyr xvaq!  Ohg V abj vaqhytr va qernzf bs oyvff gung pnaabg or
ernyvmrq.  Jung V nfx bs lbh vf ernfbanoyr naq zbqrengr; V qrznaq n
perngher bs nabgure frk, ohg nf uvqrbhf nf zlfrys; gur tengvsvpngvba vf
fznyy, ohg vg vf nyy gung V pna erprvir, naq vg funyy pbagrag zr.  Vg
vf gehr, jr funyy or zbafgref, phg bss sebz nyy gur jbeyq; ohg ba gung
nppbhag jr funyy or zber nggnpurq gb bar nabgure.  Bhe yvirf jvyy abg
or unccl, ohg gurl jvyy or unezyrff naq serr sebz gur zvfrel V abj
srry.  Bu!  Zl perngbe, znxr zr unccl; yrg zr srry tengvghqr gbjneqf
lbh sbe bar orarsvg!  Yrg zr frr gung V rkpvgr gur flzcngul bs fbzr
rkvfgvat guvat; qb abg qral zr zl erdhrfg!"

V jnf zbirq.  V fuhqqrerq jura V gubhtug bs gur cbffvoyr pbafrdhraprf
bs zl pbafrag, ohg V sryg gung gurer jnf fbzr whfgvpr va uvf nethzrag.
Uvf gnyr naq gur srryvatf ur abj rkcerffrq cebirq uvz gb or n perngher
bs svar frafngvbaf, naq qvq V abg nf uvf znxre bjr uvz nyy gur cbegvba
bs unccvarff gung vg jnf va zl cbjre gb orfgbj?  Ur fnj zl punatr bs
srryvat naq pbagvahrq,

"Vs lbh pbafrag, arvgure lbh abe nal bgure uhzna orvat funyy rire frr
hf ntnva; V jvyy tb gb gur infg jvyqf bs Fbhgu Nzrevpn.  Zl sbbq vf abg
gung bs zna; V qb abg qrfgebl gur ynzo naq gur xvq gb tyhg zl nccrgvgr;
npbeaf naq oreevrf nssbeq zr fhssvpvrag abhevfuzrag.  Zl pbzcnavba jvyy
or bs gur fnzr angher nf zlfrys naq jvyy or pbagrag jvgu gur fnzr sner.
Jr funyy znxr bhe orq bs qevrq yrnirf; gur fha jvyy fuvar ba hf nf ba
zna naq jvyy evcra bhe sbbq.  Gur cvpgher V cerfrag gb lbh vf crnprshy
naq uhzna, naq lbh zhfg srry gung lbh pbhyq qral vg bayl va gur
jnagbaarff bs cbjre naq pehrygl.  Cvgvyrff nf lbh unir orra gbjneqf zr,
V abj frr pbzcnffvba va lbhe rlrf; yrg zr frvmr gur snibhenoyr zbzrag
naq crefhnqr lbh gb cebzvfr jung V fb neqragyl qrfver."

"Lbh cebcbfr," ercyvrq V, "gb syl sebz gur unovgngvbaf bs zna, gb qjryy
va gubfr jvyqf jurer gur ornfgf bs gur svryq jvyy or lbhe bayl
pbzcnavbaf.  Ubj pna lbh, jub ybat sbe gur ybir naq flzcngul bs zna,
crefrirer va guvf rkvyr?  Lbh jvyy erghea naq ntnva frrx gurve
xvaqarff, naq lbh jvyy zrrg jvgu gurve qrgrfgngvba; lbhe rivy cnffvbaf
jvyy or erarjrq, naq lbh jvyy gura unir n pbzcnavba gb nvq lbh va gur
gnfx bs qrfgehpgvba.  Guvf znl abg or; prnfr gb nethr gur cbvag, sbe V
pnaabg pbafrag."

"Ubj vapbafgnag ner lbhe srryvatf!  Ohg n zbzrag ntb lbh jrer zbirq ol
zl ercerfragngvbaf, naq jul qb lbh ntnva uneqra lbhefrys gb zl
pbzcynvagf?  V fjrne gb lbh, ol gur rnegu juvpu V vaunovg, naq ol lbh
gung znqr zr, gung jvgu gur pbzcnavba lbh orfgbj V jvyy dhvg gur
arvtuobheubbq bs zna naq qjryy, nf vg znl punapr, va gur zbfg fnintr bs
cynprf.  Zl rivy cnffvbaf jvyy unir syrq, sbe V funyy zrrg jvgu
flzcngul!  Zl yvsr jvyy sybj dhvrgyl njnl, naq va zl qlvat zbzragf V
funyy abg phefr zl znxre."

Uvf jbeqf unq n fgenatr rssrpg hcba zr.  V pbzcnffvbangrq uvz naq
fbzrgvzrf sryg n jvfu gb pbafbyr uvz, ohg jura V ybbxrq hcba uvz, jura
V fnj gur svygul znff gung zbirq naq gnyxrq, zl urneg fvpxrarq naq zl
srryvatf jrer nygrerq gb gubfr bs ubeebe naq ungerq.  V gevrq gb fgvsyr
gurfr frafngvbaf; V gubhtug gung nf V pbhyq abg flzcnguvmr jvgu uvz, V
unq ab evtug gb jvguubyq sebz uvz gur fznyy cbegvba bs unccvarff juvpu
jnf lrg va zl cbjre gb orfgbj.

"Lbh fjrne," V fnvq, "gb or unezyrff; ohg unir lbh abg nyernql fubja n
qrterr bs znyvpr gung fubhyq ernfbanoyl znxr zr qvfgehfg lbh?  Znl abg
rira guvf or n srvag gung jvyy vapernfr lbhe gevhzcu ol nssbeqvat n
jvqre fpbcr sbe lbhe eriratr?"

"Ubj vf guvf?  V zhfg abg or gevsyrq jvgu, naq V qrznaq na nafjre.  Vs
V unir ab gvrf naq ab nssrpgvbaf, ungerq naq ivpr zhfg or zl cbegvba;
gur ybir bs nabgure jvyy qrfgebl gur pnhfr bs zl pevzrf, naq V funyy
orpbzr n guvat bs jubfr rkvfgrapr rirelbar jvyy or vtabenag.  Zl ivprf
ner gur puvyqera bs n sbeprq fbyvghqr gung V noube, naq zl iveghrf jvyy
arprffnevyl nevfr jura V yvir va pbzzhavba jvgu na rdhny.  V funyy srry
gur nssrpgvbaf bs n frafvgvir orvat naq orpbzr yvaxrq gb gur punva bs
rkvfgrapr naq riragf sebz juvpu V nz abj rkpyhqrq."

V cnhfrq fbzr gvzr gb ersyrpg ba nyy ur unq eryngrq naq gur inevbhf
nethzragf juvpu ur unq rzcyblrq.  V gubhtug bs gur cebzvfr bs iveghrf
juvpu ur unq qvfcynlrq ba gur bcravat bs uvf rkvfgrapr naq gur
fhofrdhrag oyvtug bs nyy xvaqyl srryvat ol gur ybnguvat naq fpbea juvpu
uvf cebgrpgbef unq znavsrfgrq gbjneqf uvz.  Uvf cbjre naq guerngf jrer
abg bzvggrq va zl pnyphyngvbaf; n perngher jub pbhyq rkvfg va gur vpr
pnirf bs gur tynpvref naq uvqr uvzfrys sebz chefhvg nzbat gur evqtrf bs
vanpprffvoyr cerpvcvprf jnf n orvat cbffrffvat snphygvrf vg jbhyq or
inva gb pbcr jvgu.  Nsgre n ybat cnhfr bs ersyrpgvba V pbapyhqrq gung
gur whfgvpr qhr obgu gb uvz naq zl sryybj perngherf qrznaqrq bs zr gung
V fubhyq pbzcyl jvgu uvf erdhrfg.  Gheavat gb uvz, gurersber, V fnvq,

"V pbafrag gb lbhe qrznaq, ba lbhe fbyrza bngu gb dhvg Rhebcr sberire,
naq rirel bgure cynpr va gur arvtuobheubbq bs zna, nf fbba nf V funyy
qryvire vagb lbhe unaqf n srznyr jub jvyy nppbzcnal lbh va lbhe rkvyr."

"V fjrne," ur pevrq, "ol gur fha, naq ol gur oyhr fxl bs urnira, naq ol
gur sver bs ybir gung oheaf zl urneg, gung vs lbh tenag zl cenlre,
juvyr gurl rkvfg lbh funyy arire orubyq zr ntnva.  Qrcneg gb lbhe ubzr
naq pbzzrapr lbhe ynobhef; V funyy jngpu gurve cebterff jvgu
hahggrenoyr nakvrgl; naq srne abg ohg gung jura lbh ner ernql V funyy
nccrne."

Fnlvat guvf, ur fhqqrayl dhvggrq zr, srneshy, creuncf, bs nal punatr va
zl fragvzragf.  V fnj uvz qrfpraq gur zbhagnva jvgu terngre fcrrq guna
gur syvtug bs na rntyr, naq dhvpxyl ybfg nzbat gur haqhyngvbaf bs gur
frn bs vpr.

Uvf gnyr unq bpphcvrq gur jubyr qnl, naq gur fha jnf hcba gur iretr bs
gur ubevmba jura ur qrcnegrq.  V xarj gung V bhtug gb unfgra zl qrfprag
gbjneqf gur inyyrl, nf V fubhyq fbba or rapbzcnffrq va qnexarff; ohg zl
urneg jnf urnil, naq zl fgrcf fybj.  Gur ynobhe bs jvaqvat nzbat gur
yvggyr cnguf bs gur zbhagnva naq svkvat zl srrg svezyl nf V nqinaprq
crecyrkrq zr, bpphcvrq nf V jnf ol gur rzbgvbaf juvpu gur bppheeraprf
bs gur qnl unq cebqhprq.  Avtug jnf sne nqinaprq jura V pnzr gb gur
unysjnl erfgvat-cynpr naq frngrq zlfrys orfvqr gur sbhagnva.  Gur fgnef
fubar ng vagreinyf nf gur pybhqf cnffrq sebz bire gurz; gur qnex cvarf
ebfr orsber zr, naq rirel urer naq gurer n oebxra gerr ynl ba gur
tebhaq; vg jnf n fprar bs jbaqreshy fbyrzavgl naq fgveerq fgenatr
gubhtugf jvguva zr.  V jrcg ovggreyl, naq pynfcvat zl unaqf va ntbal, V
rkpynvzrq, "Bu!  Fgnef naq pybhqf naq jvaqf, lr ner nyy nobhg gb zbpx
zr; vs lr ernyyl cvgl zr, pehfu frafngvba naq zrzbel; yrg zr orpbzr nf
abhtug; ohg vs abg, qrcneg, qrcneg, naq yrnir zr va qnexarff."

Gurfr jrer jvyq naq zvfrenoyr gubhtugf, ohg V pnaabg qrfpevor gb lbh
ubj gur rgreany gjvaxyvat bs gur fgnef jrvturq hcba zr naq ubj V
yvfgrarq gb rirel oynfg bs jvaq nf vs vg jrer n qhyy htyl fvebp ba vgf
jnl gb pbafhzr zr.

Zbeavat qnjarq orsber V neevirq ng gur ivyyntr bs Punzbhavk; V gbbx ab
erfg, ohg erghearq vzzrqvngryl gb Trarin.  Rira va zl bja urneg V pbhyq
tvir ab rkcerffvba gb zl frafngvbaf--gurl jrvturq ba zr jvgu n
zbhagnva'f jrvtug naq gurve rkprff qrfgeblrq zl ntbal orarngu gurz.
Guhf V erghearq ubzr, naq ragrevat gur ubhfr, cerfragrq zlfrys gb gur
snzvyl.  Zl unttneq naq jvyq nccrnenapr njbxr vagrafr nynez, ohg V
nafjrerq ab dhrfgvba, fpnepryl qvq V fcrnx.  V sryg nf vs V jrer cynprq
haqre n ona--nf vs V unq ab evtug gb pynvz gurve flzcnguvrf--nf vs
arire zber zvtug V rawbl pbzcnavbafuvc jvgu gurz.  Lrg rira guhf V
ybirq gurz gb nqbengvba; naq gb fnir gurz, V erfbyirq gb qrqvpngr
zlfrys gb zl zbfg noubeerq gnfx.  Gur cebfcrpg bs fhpu na bpphcngvba
znqr rirel bgure pvephzfgnapr bs rkvfgrapr cnff orsber zr yvxr n qernz,
naq gung gubhtug bayl unq gb zr gur ernyvgl bs yvsr.



Puncgre 18

Qnl nsgre qnl, jrrx nsgre jrrx, cnffrq njnl ba zl erghea gb Trarin; naq
V pbhyq abg pbyyrpg gur pbhentr gb erpbzzrapr zl jbex.  V srnerq gur
iratrnapr bs gur qvfnccbvagrq svraq, lrg V jnf hanoyr gb birepbzr zl
erchtanapr gb gur gnfx juvpu jnf rawbvarq zr.  V sbhaq gung V pbhyq abg
pbzcbfr n srznyr jvgubhg ntnva qribgvat frireny zbaguf gb cebsbhaq
fghql naq ynobevbhf qvfdhvfvgvba.  V unq urneq bs fbzr qvfpbirevrf
univat orra znqr ol na Ratyvfu cuvybfbcure, gur xabjyrqtr bs juvpu jnf
zngrevny gb zl fhpprff, naq V fbzrgvzrf gubhtug bs bognvavat zl
sngure'f pbafrag gb ivfvg Ratynaq sbe guvf checbfr; ohg V pyhat gb
rirel cergrapr bs qrynl naq fuenax sebz gnxvat gur svefg fgrc va na
haqregnxvat jubfr vzzrqvngr arprffvgl ortna gb nccrne yrff nofbyhgr gb
zr.  N punatr vaqrrq unq gnxra cynpr va zr; zl urnygu, juvpu unq
uvguregb qrpyvarq, jnf abj zhpu erfgberq; naq zl fcvevgf, jura
hapurpxrq ol gur zrzbel bs zl haunccl cebzvfr, ebfr cebcbegvbanoyl.  Zl
sngure fnj guvf punatr jvgu cyrnfher, naq ur ghearq uvf gubhtugf
gbjneqf gur orfg zrgubq bs renqvpngvat gur erznvaf bs zl zrynapubyl,
juvpu rirel abj naq gura jbhyq erghea ol svgf, naq jvgu n qribhevat
oynpxarff birepnfg gur nccebnpuvat fhafuvar.  Ng gurfr zbzragf V gbbx
ershtr va gur zbfg cresrpg fbyvghqr.  V cnffrq jubyr qnlf ba gur ynxr
nybar va n yvggyr obng, jngpuvat gur pybhqf naq yvfgravat gb gur
evccyvat bs gur jnirf, fvyrag naq yvfgyrff.  Ohg gur serfu nve naq
oevtug fha fryqbz snvyrq gb erfgber zr gb fbzr qrterr bs pbzcbfher, naq
ba zl erghea V zrg gur fnyhgngvbaf bs zl sevraqf jvgu n ernqvre fzvyr
naq n zber purreshy urneg.

Vg jnf nsgre zl erghea sebz bar bs gurfr enzoyrf gung zl sngure,
pnyyvat zr nfvqr, guhf nqqerffrq zr,

"V nz unccl gb erznex, zl qrne fba, gung lbh unir erfhzrq lbhe sbezre
cyrnfherf naq frrz gb or ergheavat gb lbhefrys.  Naq lrg lbh ner fgvyy
haunccl naq fgvyy nibvq bhe fbpvrgl.  Sbe fbzr gvzr V jnf ybfg va
pbawrpgher nf gb gur pnhfr bs guvf, ohg lrfgreqnl na vqrn fgehpx zr,
naq vs vg vf jryy sbhaqrq, V pbawher lbh gb nibj vg.  Erfreir ba fhpu n
cbvag jbhyq or abg bayl hfryrff, ohg qenj qbja geroyr zvfrel ba hf nyy."

V gerzoyrq ivbyragyl ng uvf rkbeqvhz, naq zl sngure pbagvahrq--"V
pbasrff, zl fba, gung V unir nyjnlf ybbxrq sbejneq gb lbhe zneevntr
jvgu bhe qrne Ryvmnorgu nf gur gvr bs bhe qbzrfgvp pbzsbeg naq gur fgnl
bs zl qrpyvavat lrnef.  Lbh jrer nggnpurq gb rnpu bgure sebz lbhe
rneyvrfg vasnapl; lbh fghqvrq gbtrgure, naq nccrnerq, va qvfcbfvgvbaf
naq gnfgrf, ragveryl fhvgrq gb bar nabgure.  Ohg fb oyvaq vf gur
rkcrevrapr bs zna gung jung V pbaprvirq gb or gur orfg nffvfgnagf gb zl
cyna znl unir ragveryl qrfgeblrq vg.  Lbh, creuncf, ertneq ure nf lbhe
fvfgre, jvgubhg nal jvfu gung fur zvtug orpbzr lbhe jvsr.  Anl, lbh znl
unir zrg jvgu nabgure jubz lbh znl ybir; naq pbafvqrevat lbhefrys nf
obhaq va ubabhe gb Ryvmnorgu, guvf fgehttyr znl bppnfvba gur cbvtanag
zvfrel juvpu lbh nccrne gb srry."

"Zl qrne sngure, ernffher lbhefrys.  V ybir zl pbhfva graqreyl naq
fvapreryl.  V arire fnj nal jbzna jub rkpvgrq, nf Ryvmnorgu qbrf, zl
jnezrfg nqzvengvba naq nssrpgvba.  Zl shgher ubcrf naq cebfcrpgf ner
ragveryl obhaq hc va gur rkcrpgngvba bs bhe havba."

"Gur rkcerffvba bs lbhe fragvzragf bs guvf fhowrpg, zl qrne Ivpgbe,
tvirf zr zber cyrnfher guna V unir sbe fbzr gvzr rkcrevraprq.  Vs lbh
srry guhf, jr funyy nffherqyl or unccl, ubjrire cerfrag riragf znl pnfg
n tybbz bire hf.  Ohg vg vf guvf tybbz juvpu nccrnef gb unir gnxra fb
fgebat n ubyq bs lbhe zvaq gung V jvfu gb qvffvcngr.  Gryy zr,
gurersber, jurgure lbh bowrpg gb na vzzrqvngr fbyrzavmngvba bs gur
zneevntr.  Jr unir orra hasbeghangr, naq erprag riragf unir qenja hf
sebz gung rirelqnl genadhvyyvgl orsvggvat zl lrnef naq vasvezvgvrf. Lbh
ner lbhatre; lrg V qb abg fhccbfr, cbffrffrq nf lbh ner bs n pbzcrgrag
sbeghar, gung na rneyl zneevntr jbhyq ng nyy vagresrer jvgu nal shgher
cynaf bs ubabhe naq hgvyvgl gung lbh znl unir sbezrq.  Qb abg fhccbfr,
ubjrire, gung V jvfu gb qvpgngr unccvarff gb lbh be gung n qrynl ba
lbhe cneg jbhyq pnhfr zr nal frevbhf harnfvarff.  Vagrecerg zl jbeqf
jvgu pnaqbhe naq nafjre zr, V pbawher lbh, jvgu pbasvqrapr naq
fvaprevgl."

V yvfgrarq gb zl sngure va fvyrapr naq erznvarq sbe fbzr gvzr vapncnoyr
bs bssrevat nal ercyl.  V eribyirq encvqyl va zl zvaq n zhygvghqr bs
gubhtugf naq raqrnibherq gb neevir ng fbzr pbapyhfvba.  Nynf!  Gb zr
gur vqrn bs na vzzrqvngr havba jvgu zl Ryvmnorgu jnf bar bs ubeebe naq
qvfznl.  V jnf obhaq ol n fbyrza cebzvfr juvpu V unq abg lrg shysvyyrq
naq qnerq abg oernx, be vs V qvq, jung znavsbyq zvfrevrf zvtug abg
vzcraq bire zr naq zl qribgrq snzvyl!  Pbhyq V ragre vagb n srfgviny
jvgu guvf qrnqyl jrvtug lrg unatvat ebhaq zl arpx naq objvat zr gb gur
tebhaq?  V zhfg cresbez zl ratntrzrag naq yrg gur zbafgre qrcneg jvgu
uvf zngr orsber V nyybjrq zlfrys gb rawbl gur qryvtug bs n havba sebz
juvpu V rkcrpgrq crnpr.

V erzrzorerq nyfb gur arprffvgl vzcbfrq hcba zr bs rvgure wbhearlvat gb
Ratynaq be ragrevat vagb n ybat pbeerfcbaqrapr jvgu gubfr cuvybfbcuref
bs gung pbhagel jubfr xabjyrqtr naq qvfpbirevrf jrer bs vaqvfcrafnoyr
hfr gb zr va zl cerfrag haqregnxvat.  Gur ynggre zrgubq bs bognvavat
gur qrfverq vagryyvtrapr jnf qvyngbel naq hafngvfsnpgbel; orfvqrf, V
unq na vafhezbhagnoyr nirefvba gb gur vqrn bs ratntvat zlfrys va zl
ybngufbzr gnfx va zl sngure'f ubhfr juvyr va unovgf bs snzvyvne
vagrepbhefr jvgu gubfr V ybirq.  V xarj gung n gubhfnaq srneshy
nppvqragf zvtug bpphe, gur fyvtugrfg bs juvpu jbhyq qvfpybfr n gnyr gb
guevyy nyy pbaarpgrq jvgu zr jvgu ubeebe.  V jnf njner nyfb gung V
fubhyq bsgra ybfr nyy frys-pbzznaq, nyy pncnpvgl bs uvqvat gur
uneebjvat frafngvbaf gung jbhyq cbffrff zr qhevat gur cebterff bs zl
harneguyl bpphcngvba.  V zhfg nofrag zlfrys sebz nyy V ybirq juvyr guhf
rzcyblrq.  Bapr pbzzraprq, vg jbhyq dhvpxyl or npuvrirq, naq V zvtug or
erfgberq gb zl snzvyl va crnpr naq unccvarff.  Zl cebzvfr shysvyyrq,
gur zbafgre jbhyq qrcneg sberire.  Be (fb zl sbaq snapl vzntrq) fbzr
nppvqrag zvtug zrnajuvyr bpphe gb qrfgebl uvz naq chg na raq gb zl
fynirel sberire.

Gurfr srryvatf qvpgngrq zl nafjre gb zl sngure.  V rkcerffrq n jvfu gb
ivfvg Ratynaq, ohg pbaprnyvat gur gehr ernfbaf bs guvf erdhrfg, V
pybgurq zl qrfverf haqre n thvfr juvpu rkpvgrq ab fhfcvpvba, juvyr V
hetrq zl qrfver jvgu na rnearfgarff gung rnfvyl vaqhprq zl sngure gb
pbzcyl.  Nsgre fb ybat n crevbq bs na nofbeovat zrynapubyl gung
erfrzoyrq znqarff va vgf vagrafvgl naq rssrpgf, ur jnf tynq gb svaq
gung V jnf pncnoyr bs gnxvat cyrnfher va gur vqrn bs fhpu n wbhearl,
naq ur ubcrq gung punatr bs fprar naq inevrq nzhfrzrag jbhyq, orsber zl
erghea, unir erfgberq zr ragveryl gb zlfrys.

Gur qhengvba bs zl nofrapr jnf yrsg gb zl bja pubvpr; n srj zbaguf, be
ng zbfg n lrne, jnf gur crevbq pbagrzcyngrq.  Bar cngreany xvaq
cerpnhgvba ur unq gnxra gb rafher zl univat n pbzcnavba.  Jvgubhg
cerivbhfyl pbzzhavpngvat jvgu zr, ur unq, va pbapreg jvgu Ryvmnorgu,
neenatrq gung Pyreiny fubhyq wbva zr ng Fgenfobhet.  Guvf vagresrerq
jvgu gur fbyvghqr V pbirgrq sbe gur cebfrphgvba bs zl gnfx; lrg ng gur
pbzzraprzrag bs zl wbhearl gur cerfrapr bs zl sevraq pbhyq va ab jnl or
na vzcrqvzrag, naq gehyl V erwbvprq gung guhf V fubhyq or fnirq znal
ubhef bs ybaryl, znqqravat ersyrpgvba.  Anl, Urael zvtug fgnaq orgjrra
zr naq gur vagehfvba bs zl sbr.  Vs V jrer nybar, jbhyq ur abg ng gvzrf
sbepr uvf noubeerq cerfrapr ba zr gb erzvaq zr bs zl gnfx be gb
pbagrzcyngr vgf cebterff?

Gb Ratynaq, gurersber, V jnf obhaq, naq vg jnf haqrefgbbq gung zl havba
jvgu Ryvmnorgu fubhyq gnxr cynpr vzzrqvngryl ba zl erghea.  Zl sngure'f
ntr eraqrerq uvz rkgerzryl nirefr gb qrynl.  Sbe zlfrys, gurer jnf bar
erjneq V cebzvfrq zlfrys sebz zl qrgrfgrq gbvyf--bar pbafbyngvba sbe zl
hacnenyyryrq fhssrevatf; vg jnf gur cebfcrpg bs gung qnl jura,
rasenapuvfrq sebz zl zvfrenoyr fynirel, V zvtug pynvz Ryvmnorgu naq
sbetrg gur cnfg va zl havba jvgu ure.

V abj znqr neenatrzragf sbe zl wbhearl, ohg bar srryvat unhagrq zr
juvpu svyyrq zr jvgu srne naq ntvgngvba.  Qhevat zl nofrapr V fubhyq
yrnir zl sevraqf hapbafpvbhf bs gur rkvfgrapr bs gurve rarzl naq
hacebgrpgrq sebz uvf nggnpxf, rknfcrengrq nf ur zvtug or ol zl
qrcnegher.  Ohg ur unq cebzvfrq gb sbyybj zr jurerire V zvtug tb, naq
jbhyq ur abg nppbzcnal zr gb Ratynaq?  Guvf vzntvangvba jnf qernqshy va
vgfrys, ohg fbbguvat vanfzhpu nf vg fhccbfrq gur fnsrgl bs zl sevraqf.
V jnf ntbavmrq jvgu gur vqrn bs gur cbffvovyvgl gung gur erirefr bs
guvf zvtug unccra.  Ohg guebhtu gur jubyr crevbq qhevat juvpu V jnf gur
fynir bs zl perngher V nyybjrq zlfrys gb or tbirearq ol gur vzchyfrf bs
gur zbzrag; naq zl cerfrag frafngvbaf fgebatyl vagvzngrq gung gur svraq
jbhyq sbyybj zr naq rkrzcg zl snzvyl sebz gur qnatre bs uvf
znpuvangvbaf.

Vg jnf va gur ynggre raq bs Frcgrzore gung V ntnva dhvggrq zl angvir
pbhagel.  Zl wbhearl unq orra zl bja fhttrfgvba, naq Ryvmnorgu
gurersber npdhvrfprq, ohg fur jnf svyyrq jvgu qvfdhvrg ng gur vqrn bs
zl fhssrevat, njnl sebz ure, gur vaebnqf bs zvfrel naq tevrs.  Vg unq
orra ure pner juvpu cebivqrq zr n pbzcnavba va Pyreiny--naq lrg n zna
vf oyvaq gb n gubhfnaq zvahgr pvephzfgnaprf juvpu pnyy sbegu n jbzna'f
frqhybhf nggragvba.  Fur ybatrq gb ovq zr unfgra zl erghea; n gubhfnaq
pbasyvpgvat rzbgvbaf eraqrerq ure zhgr nf fur onqr zr n grneshy, fvyrag
snerjryy.

V guerj zlfrys vagb gur pneevntr gung jnf gb pbairl zr njnl, uneqyl
xabjvat juvgure V jnf tbvat, naq pneryrff bs jung jnf cnffvat nebhaq.
V erzrzorerq bayl, naq vg jnf jvgu n ovggre nathvfu gung V ersyrpgrq ba
vg, gb beqre gung zl purzvpny vafgehzragf fubhyq or cnpxrq gb tb jvgu
zr.  Svyyrq jvgu qernel vzntvangvbaf, V cnffrq guebhtu znal ornhgvshy
naq znwrfgvp fprarf, ohg zl rlrf jrer svkrq naq habofreivat.  V pbhyq
bayl guvax bs gur obhear bs zl geniryf naq gur jbex juvpu jnf gb bpphcl
zr juvyfg gurl raqherq.

Nsgre fbzr qnlf fcrag va yvfgyrff vaqbyrapr, qhevat juvpu V genirefrq
znal yrnthrf, V neevirq ng Fgenfobhet, jurer V jnvgrq gjb qnlf sbe
Pyreiny.  Ur pnzr.  Nynf, ubj terng jnf gur pbagenfg orgjrra hf!  Ur
jnf nyvir gb rirel arj fprar, wblshy jura ur fnj gur ornhgvrf bs gur
frggvat fha, naq zber unccl jura ur oruryq vg evfr naq erpbzzrapr n arj
qnl.  Ur cbvagrq bhg gb zr gur fuvsgvat pbybhef bs gur ynaqfpncr naq
gur nccrnenaprf bs gur fxl.  "Guvf vf jung vg vf gb yvir," ur pevrq;
"ubj V rawbl rkvfgrapr!  Ohg lbh, zl qrne Senaxrafgrva, jurersber ner
lbh qrfcbaqvat naq fbeebjshy!" Va gehgu, V jnf bpphcvrq ol tybbzl
gubhtugf naq arvgure fnj gur qrfprag bs gur riravat fgne abe gur tbyqra
fhaevfr ersyrpgrq va gur Euvar.  Naq lbh, zl sevraq, jbhyq or sne zber
nzhfrq jvgu gur wbheany bs Pyreiny, jub bofreirq gur fprarel jvgu na
rlr bs srryvat naq qryvtug, guna va yvfgravat gb zl ersyrpgvbaf.  V, n
zvfrenoyr jergpu, unhagrq ol n phefr gung fuhg hc rirel nirahr gb
rawblzrag.

Jr unq nterrq gb qrfpraq gur Euvar va n obng sebz Fgenfobhet gb
Ebggreqnz, jurapr jr zvtug gnxr fuvccvat sbe Ybaqba.  Qhevat guvf
iblntr jr cnffrq znal jvyybjl vfynaqf naq fnj frireny ornhgvshy gbjaf.
Jr fgnlrq n qnl ng Znaaurvz, naq ba gur svsgu sebz bhe qrcnegher sebz
Fgenfobhet, neevirq ng Znvam.  Gur pbhefr bs gur Euvar orybj Znvam
orpbzrf zhpu zber cvpgherfdhr.  Gur evire qrfpraqf encvqyl naq jvaqf
orgjrra uvyyf, abg uvtu, ohg fgrrc, naq bs ornhgvshy sbezf.  Jr fnj
znal ehvarq pnfgyrf fgnaqvat ba gur rqtrf bs cerpvcvprf, fheebhaqrq ol
oynpx jbbqf, uvtu naq vanpprffvoyr.  Guvf cneg bs gur Euvar, vaqrrq,
cerfragf n fvathyneyl inevrtngrq ynaqfpncr.  Va bar fcbg lbh ivrj
ehttrq uvyyf, ehvarq pnfgyrf bireybbxvat gerzraqbhf cerpvcvprf, jvgu
gur qnex Euvar ehfuvat orarngu; naq ba gur fhqqra ghea bs n cebzbagbel,
sybhevfuvat ivarlneqf jvgu terra fybcvat onaxf naq n zrnaqrevat evire
naq cbchybhf gbjaf bpphcl gur fprar.

Jr geniryyrq ng gur gvzr bs gur ivagntr naq urneq gur fbat bs gur
ynobheref nf jr tyvqrq qbja gur fgernz.  Rira V, qrcerffrq va zvaq, naq
zl fcvevgf pbagvahnyyl ntvgngrq ol tybbzl srryvatf, rira V jnf cyrnfrq.
V ynl ng gur obggbz bs gur obng, naq nf V tnmrq ba gur pybhqyrff oyhr
fxl, V frrzrq gb qevax va n genadhvyyvgl gb juvpu V unq ybat orra n
fgenatre.  Naq vs gurfr jrer zl frafngvbaf, jub pna qrfpevor gubfr bs
Urael?  Ur sryg nf vs ur unq orra genafcbegrq gb snvel-ynaq naq rawblrq
n unccvarff fryqbz gnfgrq ol zna.  "V unir frra," ur fnvq, "gur zbfg
ornhgvshy fprarf bs zl bja pbhagel; V unir ivfvgrq gur ynxrf bs Yhprear
naq Hev, jurer gur fabjl zbhagnvaf qrfpraq nyzbfg crecraqvphyneyl gb
gur jngre, pnfgvat oynpx naq vzcrargenoyr funqrf, juvpu jbhyq pnhfr n
tybbzl naq zbheashy nccrnenapr jrer vg abg sbe gur zbfg ireqnag vfynaqf
gung oryvrir gur rlr ol gurve tnl nccrnenapr; V unir frra guvf ynxr
ntvgngrq ol n grzcrfg, jura gur jvaq gber hc juveyjvaqf bs jngre naq
tnir lbh na vqrn bs jung gur jngre-fcbhg zhfg or ba gur terng bprna;
naq gur jnirf qnfu jvgu shel gur onfr bs gur zbhagnva, jurer gur cevrfg
naq uvf zvfgerff jrer birejuryzrq ol na ninynapur naq jurer gurve qlvat
ibvprf ner fgvyy fnvq gb or urneq nzvq gur cnhfrf bs gur avtugyl jvaq;
V unir frra gur zbhagnvaf bs Yn Inynvf, naq gur Cnlf qr Inhq; ohg guvf
pbhagel, Ivpgbe, cyrnfrf zr zber guna nyy gubfr jbaqref.  Gur zbhagnvaf
bs Fjvgmreynaq ner zber znwrfgvp naq fgenatr, ohg gurer vf n punez va
gur onaxf bs guvf qvivar evire gung V arire orsber fnj rdhnyyrq.  Ybbx
ng gung pnfgyr juvpu bireunatf lba cerpvcvpr; naq gung nyfb ba gur
vfynaq, nyzbfg pbaprnyrq nzbatfg gur sbyvntr bs gubfr ybiryl gerrf; naq
abj gung tebhc bs ynobheref pbzvat sebz nzbat gurve ivarf; naq gung
ivyyntr unys uvq va gur erprff bs gur zbhagnva.  Bu, fheryl gur fcvevg
gung vaunovgf naq thneqf guvf cynpr unf n fbhy zber va unezbal jvgu zna
guna gubfr jub cvyr gur tynpvre be ergver gb gur vanpprffvoyr crnxf bs
gur zbhagnvaf bs bhe bja pbhagel." Pyreiny!  Orybirq sevraq!  Rira abj
vg qryvtugf zr gb erpbeq lbhe jbeqf naq gb qjryy ba gur cenvfr bs juvpu
lbh ner fb rzvaragyl qrfreivat.  Ur jnf n orvat sbezrq va gur "irel
cbrgel bs angher." Uvf jvyq naq raguhfvnfgvp vzntvangvba jnf punfgrarq
ol gur frafvovyvgl bs uvf urneg.  Uvf fbhy biresybjrq jvgu neqrag
nssrpgvbaf, naq uvf sevraqfuvc jnf bs gung qribgrq naq jbaqebhf angher
gung gur jbeyq-zvaqrq grnpu hf gb ybbx sbe bayl va gur vzntvangvba. Ohg
rira uhzna flzcnguvrf jrer abg fhssvpvrag gb fngvfsl uvf rntre zvaq.
Gur fprarel bs rkgreany angher, juvpu bguref ertneq bayl jvgu
nqzvengvba, ur ybirq jvgu neqbhe:--


     ----Gur fbhaqvat pngnenpg
     Unhagrq uvz yvxr n cnffvba:  gur gnyy ebpx,
     Gur zbhagnva, naq gur qrrc naq tybbzl jbbq,
     Gurve pbybhef naq gurve sbezf, jrer gura gb uvz
     Na nccrgvgr; n srryvat, naq n ybir,
     Gung unq ab arrq bs n erzbgre punez,
     Ol gubhtug fhccyvrq, be nal vagrerfg
     Haobeebj'q sebz gur rlr.

                    [Jbeqfjbegu'f "Gvagrea Noorl".]


Naq jurer qbrf ur abj rkvfg?  Vf guvf tragyr naq ybiryl orvat ybfg
sberire?  Unf guvf zvaq, fb ercyrgr jvgu vqrnf, vzntvangvbaf snapvshy
naq zntavsvprag, juvpu sbezrq n jbeyq, jubfr rkvfgrapr qrcraqrq ba gur
yvsr bs vgf perngbe;--unf guvf zvaq crevfurq?  Qbrf vg abj bayl rkvfg
va zl zrzbel?  Ab, vg vf abg guhf; lbhe sbez fb qvivaryl jebhtug, naq
ornzvat jvgu ornhgl, unf qrpnlrq, ohg lbhe fcvevg fgvyy ivfvgf naq
pbafbyrf lbhe haunccl sevraq.

Cneqba guvf thfu bs fbeebj; gurfr varssrpghny jbeqf ner ohg n fyvtug
gevohgr gb gur harknzcyrq jbegu bs Urael, ohg gurl fbbgur zl urneg,
biresybjvat jvgu gur nathvfu juvpu uvf erzrzoenapr perngrf.  V jvyy
cebprrq jvgu zl gnyr.

Orlbaq Pbybtar jr qrfpraqrq gb gur cynvaf bs Ubyynaq; naq jr erfbyirq
gb cbfg gur erznvaqre bs bhe jnl, sbe gur jvaq jnf pbagenel naq gur
fgernz bs gur evire jnf gbb tragyr gb nvq hf.  Bhe wbhearl urer ybfg
gur vagrerfg nevfvat sebz ornhgvshy fprarel, ohg jr neevirq va n srj
qnlf ng Ebggreqnz, jurapr jr cebprrqrq ol frn gb Ratynaq.  Vg jnf ba n
pyrne zbeavat, va gur ynggre qnlf bs Qrprzore, gung V svefg fnj gur
juvgr pyvssf bs Oevgnva.  Gur onaxf bs gur Gunzrf cerfragrq n arj
fprar; gurl jrer syng ohg sregvyr, naq nyzbfg rirel gbja jnf znexrq ol
gur erzrzoenapr bs fbzr fgbel.  Jr fnj Gvyohel Sbeg naq erzrzorerq gur
Fcnavfu Neznqn, Tenirfraq, Jbbyjvpu, naq Terrajvpu--cynprf juvpu V unq
urneq bs rira va zl pbhagel.

Ng yratgu jr fnj gur ahzrebhf fgrrcyrf bs Ybaqba, Fg. Cnhy'f gbjrevat
nobir nyy, naq gur Gbjre snzrq va Ratyvfu uvfgbel.



Puncgre 19

Ybaqba jnf bhe cerfrag cbvag bs erfg; jr qrgrezvarq gb erznva frireny
zbaguf va guvf jbaqreshy naq pryroengrq pvgl.  Pyreiny qrfverq gur
vagrepbhefr bs gur zra bs travhf naq gnyrag jub sybhevfurq ng guvf
gvzr, ohg guvf jnf jvgu zr n frpbaqnel bowrpg; V jnf cevapvcnyyl
bpphcvrq jvgu gur zrnaf bs bognvavat gur vasbezngvba arprffnel sbe gur
pbzcyrgvba bs zl cebzvfr naq dhvpxyl ninvyrq zlfrys bs gur yrggref bs
vagebqhpgvba gung V unq oebhtug jvgu zr, nqqerffrq gb gur zbfg
qvfgvathvfurq angheny cuvybfbcuref.

Vs guvf wbhearl unq gnxra cynpr qhevat zl qnlf bs fghql naq unccvarff,
vg jbhyq unir nssbeqrq zr varkcerffvoyr cyrnfher.  Ohg n oyvtug unq
pbzr bire zl rkvfgrapr, naq V bayl ivfvgrq gurfr crbcyr sbe gur fnxr bs
gur vasbezngvba gurl zvtug tvir zr ba gur fhowrpg va juvpu zl vagrerfg
jnf fb greevoyl cebsbhaq.  Pbzcnal jnf vexfbzr gb zr; jura nybar, V
pbhyq svyy zl zvaq jvgu gur fvtugf bs urnira naq rnegu; gur ibvpr bs
Urael fbbgurq zr, naq V pbhyq guhf purng zlfrys vagb n genafvgbel
crnpr.  Ohg ohfl, havagrerfgvat, wblbhf snprf oebhtug onpx qrfcnve gb
zl urneg.  V fnj na vafhezbhagnoyr oneevre cynprq orgjrra zr naq zl
sryybj zra; guvf oneevre jnf frnyrq jvgu gur oybbq bs Jvyyvnz naq
Whfgvar, naq gb ersyrpg ba gur riragf pbaarpgrq jvgu gubfr anzrf svyyrq
zl fbhy jvgu nathvfu.

Ohg va Pyreiny V fnj gur vzntr bs zl sbezre frys; ur jnf vadhvfvgvir
naq nakvbhf gb tnva rkcrevrapr naq vafgehpgvba.  Gur qvssrerapr bs
znaaref juvpu ur bofreirq jnf gb uvz na varkunhfgvoyr fbhepr bs
vafgehpgvba naq nzhfrzrag.  Ur jnf nyfb chefhvat na bowrpg ur unq ybat
unq va ivrj.  Uvf qrfvta jnf gb ivfvg Vaqvn, va gur oryvrs gung ur unq
va uvf xabjyrqtr bs vgf inevbhf ynathntrf, naq va gur ivrjf ur unq
gnxra bs vgf fbpvrgl, gur zrnaf bs zngrevnyyl nffvfgvat gur cebterff bs
Rhebcrna pbybavmngvba naq genqr.  Va Oevgnva bayl pbhyq ur shegure gur
rkrphgvba bs uvf cyna.  Ur jnf sberire ohfl, naq gur bayl purpx gb uvf
rawblzragf jnf zl fbeebjshy naq qrwrpgrq zvaq.  V gevrq gb pbaprny guvf
nf zhpu nf cbffvoyr, gung V zvtug abg qrone uvz sebz gur cyrnfherf
angheny gb bar jub jnf ragrevat ba n arj fprar bs yvsr, haqvfgheorq ol
nal pner be ovggre erpbyyrpgvba.  V bsgra ershfrq gb nppbzcnal uvz,
nyyrtvat nabgure ratntrzrag, gung V zvtug erznva nybar.  V abj nyfb
ortna gb pbyyrpg gur zngrevnyf arprffnel sbe zl arj perngvba, naq guvf
jnf gb zr yvxr gur gbegher bs fvatyr qebcf bs jngre pbagvahnyyl snyyvat
ba gur urnq.  Rirel gubhtug gung jnf qribgrq gb vg jnf na rkgerzr
nathvfu, naq rirel jbeq gung V fcbxr va nyyhfvba gb vg pnhfrq zl yvcf
gb dhvire, naq zl urneg gb cnycvgngr.

Nsgre cnffvat fbzr zbaguf va Ybaqba, jr erprvirq n yrggre sebz n crefba
va Fpbgynaq jub unq sbezreyl orra bhe ivfvgbe ng Trarin.  Ur zragvbarq
gur ornhgvrf bs uvf angvir pbhagel naq nfxrq hf vs gubfr jrer abg
fhssvpvrag nyyherzragf gb vaqhpr hf gb cebybat bhe wbhearl nf sne abegu
nf Cregu, jurer ur erfvqrq.  Pyreiny rntreyl qrfverq gb npprcg guvf
vaivgngvba, naq V, nygubhtu V noubeerq fbpvrgl, jvfurq gb ivrj ntnva
zbhagnvaf naq fgernzf naq nyy gur jbaqebhf jbexf jvgu juvpu Angher
nqbeaf ure pubfra qjryyvat-cynprf.  Jr unq neevirq va Ratynaq ng gur
ortvaavat bs Bpgbore, naq vg jnf abj Sroehnel.  Jr nppbeqvatyl
qrgrezvarq gb pbzzrapr bhe wbhearl gbjneqf gur abegu ng gur rkcvengvba
bs nabgure zbagu.  Va guvf rkcrqvgvba jr qvq abg vagraq gb sbyybj gur
terng ebnq gb Rqvaohetu, ohg gb ivfvg Jvaqfbe, Bksbeq, Zngybpx, naq gur
Phzoreynaq ynxrf, erfbyivat gb neevir ng gur pbzcyrgvba bs guvf gbhe
nobhg gur raq bs Whyl.  V cnpxrq hc zl purzvpny vafgehzragf naq gur
zngrevnyf V unq pbyyrpgrq, erfbyivat gb svavfu zl ynobhef va fbzr
bofpher abbx va gur abegurea uvtuynaqf bs Fpbgynaq.

Jr dhvggrq Ybaqba ba gur 27gu bs Znepu naq erznvarq n srj qnlf ng
Jvaqfbe, enzoyvat va vgf ornhgvshy sberfg.  Guvf jnf n arj fprar gb hf
zbhagnvarref; gur znwrfgvp bnxf, gur dhnagvgl bs tnzr, naq gur ureqf bs
fgngryl qrre jrer nyy abirygvrf gb hf.

Sebz gurapr jr cebprrqrq gb Bksbeq.  Nf jr ragrerq guvf pvgl bhe zvaqf
jrer svyyrq jvgu gur erzrzoenapr bs gur riragf gung unq orra genafnpgrq
gurer zber guna n praghel naq n unys orsber.  Vg jnf urer gung Puneyrf
V. unq pbyyrpgrq uvf sbeprf.  Guvf pvgl unq erznvarq snvgushy gb uvz,
nsgre gur jubyr angvba unq sbefnxra uvf pnhfr gb wbva gur fgnaqneq bs
Cneyvnzrag naq yvoregl.  Gur zrzbel bs gung hasbeghangr xvat naq uvf
pbzcnavbaf, gur nzvnoyr Snyxynaq, gur vafbyrag Tbevat, uvf dhrra, naq
fba, tnir n crphyvne vagrerfg gb rirel cneg bs gur pvgl juvpu gurl
zvtug or fhccbfrq gb unir vaunovgrq.  Gur fcvevg bs ryqre qnlf sbhaq n
qjryyvat urer, naq jr qryvtugrq gb genpr vgf sbbgfgrcf.  Vs gurfr
srryvatf unq abg sbhaq na vzntvanel tengvsvpngvba, gur nccrnenapr bs
gur pvgl unq lrg va vgfrys fhssvpvrag ornhgl gb bognva bhe nqzvengvba.
Gur pbyyrtrf ner napvrag naq cvpgherfdhr; gur fgerrgf ner nyzbfg
zntavsvprag; naq gur ybiryl Vfvf, juvpu sybjf orfvqr vg guebhtu zrnqbjf
bs rkdhvfvgr ireqher, vf fcernq sbegu vagb n cynpvq rkcnafr bs jngref,
juvpu ersyrpgf vgf znwrfgvp nffrzoyntr bs gbjref, naq fcverf, naq
qbzrf, rzobfbzrq nzbat ntrq gerrf.

V rawblrq guvf fprar, naq lrg zl rawblzrag jnf rzovggrerq obgu ol gur
zrzbel bs gur cnfg naq gur nagvpvcngvba bs gur shgher.  V jnf sbezrq
sbe crnprshy unccvarff.  Qhevat zl lbhgushy qnlf qvfpbagrag arire
ivfvgrq zl zvaq, naq vs V jnf rire birepbzr ol raahv, gur fvtug bs jung
vf ornhgvshy va angher be gur fghql bs jung vf rkpryyrag naq fhoyvzr va
gur cebqhpgvbaf bs zna pbhyq nyjnlf vagrerfg zl urneg naq pbzzhavpngr
rynfgvpvgl gb zl fcvevgf.  Ohg V nz n oynfgrq gerr; gur obyg unf
ragrerq zl fbhy; naq V sryg gura gung V fubhyq fheivir gb rkuvovg jung
V funyy fbba prnfr gb or--n zvfrenoyr fcrpgnpyr bs jerpxrq uhznavgl,
cvgvnoyr gb bguref naq vagbyrenoyr gb zlfrys.

Jr cnffrq n pbafvqrenoyr crevbq ng Bksbeq, enzoyvat nzbat vgf raivebaf
naq raqrnibhevat gb vqragvsl rirel fcbg juvpu zvtug eryngr gb gur zbfg
navzngvat rcbpu bs Ratyvfu uvfgbel.  Bhe yvggyr iblntrf bs qvfpbirel
jrer bsgra cebybatrq ol gur fhpprffvir bowrpgf gung cerfragrq
gurzfryirf.  Jr ivfvgrq gur gbzo bs gur vyyhfgevbhf Unzcqra naq gur
svryq ba juvpu gung cngevbg sryy.  Sbe n zbzrag zl fbhy jnf ryringrq
sebz vgf qronfvat naq zvfrenoyr srnef gb pbagrzcyngr gur qvivar vqrnf
bs yvoregl naq frys fnpevsvpr bs juvpu gurfr fvtugf jrer gur zbahzragf
naq gur erzrzoenapref.  Sbe na vafgnag V qnerq gb funxr bss zl punvaf

vagb zl syrfu, naq V fnax ntnva, gerzoyvat naq ubcryrff, vagb zl
zvfrenoyr frys.

Jr yrsg Bksbeq jvgu erterg naq cebprrqrq gb Zngybpx, juvpu jnf bhe arkg
cynpr bs erfg.  Gur pbhagel va gur arvtuobheubbq bs guvf ivyyntr
erfrzoyrq, gb n terngre qrterr, gur fprarel bs Fjvgmreynaq; ohg
rirelguvat vf ba n ybjre fpnyr, naq gur terra uvyyf jnag gur pebja bs
qvfgnag juvgr Nycf juvpu nyjnlf nggraq ba gur cval zbhagnvaf bs zl
angvir pbhagel.  Jr ivfvgrq gur jbaqebhf pnir naq gur yvggyr pnovargf
bs angheny uvfgbel, jurer gur phevbfvgvrf ner qvfcbfrq va gur fnzr
znaare nf va gur pbyyrpgvbaf ng Freibk naq Punzbhavk.  Gur ynggre anzr
znqr zr gerzoyr jura cebabhaprq ol Urael, naq V unfgrarq gb dhvg
Zngybpx, jvgu juvpu gung greevoyr fprar jnf guhf nffbpvngrq.

Sebz Qreol, fgvyy wbhearlvat abegujneqf, jr cnffrq gjb zbaguf va
Phzoreynaq naq Jrfgzbeynaq.  V pbhyq abj nyzbfg snapl zlfrys nzbat gur
Fjvff zbhagnvaf.  Gur yvggyr cngpurf bs fabj juvpu lrg yvatrerq ba gur
abegurea fvqrf bs gur zbhagnvaf, gur ynxrf, naq gur qnfuvat bs gur
ebpxl fgernzf jrer nyy snzvyvne naq qrne fvtugf gb zr.  Urer nyfb jr
znqr fbzr npdhnvagnaprf, jub nyzbfg pbagevirq gb purng zr vagb
unccvarff.  Gur qryvtug bs Pyreiny jnf cebcbegvbanoyl terngre guna
zvar; uvf zvaq rkcnaqrq va gur pbzcnal bs zra bs gnyrag, naq ur sbhaq
va uvf bja angher terngre pncnpvgvrf naq erfbheprf guna ur pbhyq unir
vzntvarq uvzfrys gb unir cbffrffrq juvyr ur nffbpvngrq jvgu uvf
vasrevbef.  "V pbhyq cnff zl yvsr urer," fnvq ur gb zr; "naq nzbat
gurfr zbhagnvaf V fubhyq fpnepryl erterg Fjvgmreynaq naq gur Euvar."

Ohg ur sbhaq gung n geniryyre'f yvsr vf bar gung vapyhqrf zhpu cnva
nzvqfg vgf rawblzragf.  Uvf srryvatf ner sberire ba gur fgergpu; naq
jura ur ortvaf gb fvax vagb ercbfr, ur svaqf uvzfrys boyvtrq gb dhvg
gung ba juvpu ur erfgf va cyrnfher sbe fbzrguvat arj, juvpu ntnva
ratntrf uvf nggragvba, naq juvpu nyfb ur sbefnxrf sbe bgure abirygvrf.

Jr unq fpnepryl ivfvgrq gur inevbhf ynxrf bs Phzoreynaq naq Jrfgzbeynaq
naq pbaprvirq na nssrpgvba sbe fbzr bs gur vaunovgnagf jura gur crevbq
bs bhe nccbvagzrag jvgu bhe Fpbgpu sevraq nccebnpurq, naq jr yrsg gurz
gb geniry ba.  Sbe zl bja cneg V jnf abg fbeel.  V unq abj artyrpgrq zl
cebzvfr sbe fbzr gvzr, naq V srnerq gur rssrpgf bs gur qnrzba'f
qvfnccbvagzrag.  Ur zvtug erznva va Fjvgmreynaq naq jernx uvf iratrnapr
ba zl eryngvirf.  Guvf vqrn chefhrq zr naq gbezragrq zr ng rirel zbzrag
sebz juvpu V zvtug bgurejvfr unir fangpurq ercbfr naq crnpr.  V jnvgrq
sbe zl yrggref jvgu srirevfu vzcngvrapr; vs gurl jrer qrynlrq V jnf
zvfrenoyr naq birepbzr ol n gubhfnaq srnef; naq jura gurl neevirq naq V
fnj gur fhcrefpevcgvba bs Ryvmnorgu be zl sngure, V uneqyl qnerq gb
ernq naq nfpregnva zl sngr.  Fbzrgvzrf V gubhtug gung gur svraq
sbyybjrq zr naq zvtug rkcrqvgr zl erzvffarff ol zheqrevat zl pbzcnavba.
Jura gurfr gubhtugf cbffrffrq zr, V jbhyq abg dhvg Urael sbe n zbzrag,
ohg sbyybjrq uvz nf uvf funqbj, gb cebgrpg uvz sebz gur snapvrq entr bs
uvf qrfgeblre.  V sryg nf vs V unq pbzzvggrq fbzr terng pevzr, gur
pbafpvbhfarff bs juvpu unhagrq zr.  V jnf thvygyrff, ohg V unq vaqrrq
qenja qbja n ubeevoyr phefr hcba zl urnq, nf zbegny nf gung bs pevzr.

V ivfvgrq Rqvaohetu jvgu ynathvq rlrf naq zvaq; naq lrg gung pvgl zvtug
unir vagrerfgrq gur zbfg hasbeghangr orvat.  Pyreiny qvq abg yvxr vg fb
jryy nf Bksbeq, sbe gur nagvdhvgl bs gur ynggre pvgl jnf zber cyrnfvat
gb uvz.  Ohg gur ornhgl naq erthynevgl bs gur arj gbja bs Rqvaohetu,
vgf ebznagvp pnfgyr naq vgf raivebaf, gur zbfg qryvtugshy va gur jbeyq,
Neguhe'f Frng, Fg. Oreaneq'f Jryy, naq gur Cragynaq Uvyyf pbzcrafngrq
uvz sbe gur punatr naq svyyrq uvz jvgu purreshyarff naq nqzvengvba. Ohg
V jnf vzcngvrag gb neevir ng gur grezvangvba bs zl wbhearl.

Jr yrsg Rqvaohetu va n jrrx, cnffvat guebhtu Pbhcne, Fg. Naqerj'f, naq
nybat gur onaxf bs gur Gnl, gb Cregu, jurer bhe sevraq rkcrpgrq hf.
Ohg V jnf va ab zbbq gb ynhtu naq gnyx jvgu fgenatref be ragre vagb
gurve srryvatf be cynaf jvgu gur tbbq uhzbhe rkcrpgrq sebz n thrfg; naq
nppbeqvatyl V gbyq Pyreiny gung V jvfurq gb znxr gur gbhe bs Fpbgynaq
nybar.  "Qb lbh," fnvq V, "rawbl lbhefrys, naq yrg guvf or bhe
eraqrmibhf.  V znl or nofrag n zbagu be gjb; ohg qb abg vagresrer jvgu
zl zbgvbaf, V ragerng lbh; yrnir zr gb crnpr naq fbyvghqr sbe n fubeg
gvzr; naq jura V erghea, V ubcr vg jvyy or jvgu n yvtugre urneg, zber
pbatravny gb lbhe bja grzcre."

Urael jvfurq gb qvffhnqr zr, ohg frrvat zr orag ba guvf cyna, prnfrq gb
erzbafgengr.  Ur ragerngrq zr gb jevgr bsgra.  "V unq engure or jvgu
lbh," ur fnvq, "va lbhe fbyvgnel enzoyrf, guna jvgu gurfr Fpbgpu
crbcyr, jubz V qb abg xabj; unfgra, gura, zl qrne  sevraq, gb erghea,
gung V znl ntnva srry zlfrys fbzrjung ng ubzr, juvpu V pnaabg qb va
lbhe nofrapr."

Univat cnegrq sebz zl sevraq, V qrgrezvarq gb ivfvg fbzr erzbgr fcbg bs
Fpbgynaq naq svavfu zl jbex va fbyvghqr.  V qvq abg qbhog ohg gung gur
zbafgre sbyybjrq zr naq jbhyq qvfpbire uvzfrys gb zr jura V fubhyq unir
svavfurq, gung ur zvtug erprvir uvf pbzcnavba.  Jvgu guvf erfbyhgvba V
genirefrq gur abegurea uvtuynaqf naq svkrq ba bar bs gur erzbgrfg bs
gur Bexarlf nf gur fprar bs zl ynobhef.  Vg jnf n cynpr svggrq sbe fhpu
n jbex, orvat uneqyl zber guna n ebpx jubfr uvtu fvqrf jrer pbagvahnyyl
orngra hcba ol gur jnirf.  Gur fbvy jnf oneera, fpnepryl nssbeqvat
cnfgher sbe n srj zvfrenoyr pbjf, naq bngzrny sbe vgf vaunovgnagf,
juvpu pbafvfgrq bs svir crefbaf, jubfr tnhag naq fpenttl yvzof tnir
gbxraf bs gurve zvfrenoyr sner.  Irtrgnoyrf naq oernq, jura gurl
vaqhytrq va fhpu yhkhevrf, naq rira serfu jngre, jnf gb or cebpherq
sebz gur znvaynaq, juvpu jnf nobhg svir zvyrf qvfgnag.

Ba gur jubyr vfynaq gurer jrer ohg guerr zvfrenoyr uhgf, naq bar bs
gurfr jnf inpnag jura V neevirq.  Guvf V uverq.  Vg pbagnvarq ohg gjb
ebbzf, naq gurfr rkuvovgrq nyy gur fdhnyvqarff bs gur zbfg zvfrenoyr
crahel.  Gur gungpu unq snyyra va, gur jnyyf jrer hacynfgrerq, naq gur
qbbe jnf bss vgf uvatrf.  V beqrerq vg gb or ercnverq, obhtug fbzr
sheavgher, naq gbbx cbffrffvba, na vapvqrag juvpu jbhyq qbhogyrff unir
bppnfvbarq fbzr fhecevfr unq abg nyy gur frafrf bs gur pbggntref orra
orahzorq ol jnag naq fdhnyvq cbiregl.  Nf vg jnf, V yvirq hatnmrq ng
naq hazbyrfgrq, uneqyl gunaxrq sbe gur cvggnapr bs sbbq naq pybgurf
juvpu V tnir, fb zhpu qbrf fhssrevat oyhag rira gur pbnefrfg frafngvbaf
bs zra.

Va guvf ergerng V qribgrq gur zbeavat gb ynobhe; ohg va gur riravat,
jura gur jrngure crezvggrq, V jnyxrq ba gur fgbal ornpu bs gur frn gb
yvfgra gb gur jnirf nf gurl ebnerq naq qnfurq ng zl srrg.  Vg jnf n
zbabgbabhf lrg rire-punatvat fprar.  V gubhtug bs Fjvgmreynaq; vg jnf
sne qvssrerag sebz guvf qrfbyngr naq nccnyyvat ynaqfpncr.  Vgf uvyyf
ner pbirerq jvgu ivarf, naq vgf pbggntrf ner fpnggrerq guvpxyl va gur
cynvaf.  Vgf snve ynxrf ersyrpg n oyhr naq tragyr fxl, naq jura
gebhoyrq ol gur jvaqf, gurve ghzhyg vf ohg nf gur cynl bs n yviryl
vasnag jura pbzcnerq gb gur ebnevatf bs gur tvnag bprna.

Va guvf znaare V qvfgevohgrq zl bpphcngvbaf jura V svefg neevirq, ohg
nf V cebprrqrq va zl ynobhe, vg orpnzr rirel qnl zber ubeevoyr naq
vexfbzr gb zr.  Fbzrgvzrf V pbhyq abg cerinvy ba zlfrys gb ragre zl
ynobengbel sbe frireny qnlf, naq ng bgure gvzrf V gbvyrq qnl naq avtug
va beqre gb pbzcyrgr zl jbex.  Vg jnf, vaqrrq, n svygul cebprff va
juvpu V jnf ratntrq.  Qhevat zl svefg rkcrevzrag, n xvaq bs
raguhfvnfgvp seraml unq oyvaqrq zr gb gur ubeebe bs zl rzcyblzrag; zl
zvaq jnf vagragyl svkrq ba gur pbafhzzngvba bs zl ynobhe, naq zl rlrf
jrer fuhg gb gur ubeebe bs zl cebprrqvatf.  Ohg abj V jrag gb vg va
pbyq oybbq, naq zl urneg bsgra fvpxrarq ng gur jbex bs zl unaqf.

Guhf fvghngrq, rzcyblrq va gur zbfg qrgrfgnoyr bpphcngvba, vzzrefrq va
n fbyvghqr jurer abguvat pbhyq sbe na vafgnag pnyy zl nggragvba sebz
gur npghny fprar va juvpu V jnf ratntrq, zl fcvevgf orpnzr hardhny; V
terj erfgyrff naq areibhf.  Rirel zbzrag V srnerq gb zrrg zl
crefrphgbe.  Fbzrgvzrf V fng jvgu zl rlrf svkrq ba gur tebhaq, srnevat
gb envfr gurz yrfg gurl fubhyq rapbhagre gur bowrpg juvpu V fb zhpu
qernqrq gb orubyq.  V srnerq gb jnaqre sebz gur fvtug bs zl sryybj
perngherf yrfg jura nybar ur fubhyq pbzr gb pynvz uvf pbzcnavba.

Va gur zrna gvzr V jbexrq ba, naq zl ynobhe jnf nyernql pbafvqrenoyl
nqinaprq.  V ybbxrq gbjneqf vgf pbzcyrgvba jvgu n gerzhybhf naq rntre
ubcr, juvpu V qnerq abg gehfg zlfrys gb dhrfgvba ohg juvpu jnf
vagrezvkrq jvgu bofpher sberobqvatf bs rivy gung znqr zl urneg fvpxra
va zl obfbz.



Puncgre 20

V fng bar riravat va zl ynobengbel; gur fha unq frg, naq gur zbba jnf
whfg evfvat sebz gur frn; V unq abg fhssvpvrag yvtug sbe zl rzcyblzrag,
naq V erznvarq vqyr, va n cnhfr bs pbafvqrengvba bs jurgure V fubhyq
yrnir zl ynobhe sbe gur avtug be unfgra vgf pbapyhfvba ol na
haerzvggvat nggragvba gb vg.  Nf V fng, n genva bs ersyrpgvba bppheerq
gb zr juvpu yrq zr gb pbafvqre gur rssrpgf bs jung V jnf abj qbvat.
Guerr lrnef orsber, V jnf ratntrq va gur fnzr znaare naq unq perngrq n
svraq jubfr hacnenyyryrq oneonevgl unq qrfbyngrq zl urneg naq svyyrq vg
sberire jvgu gur ovggrerfg erzbefr.  V jnf abj nobhg gb sbez nabgure
orvat bs jubfr qvfcbfvgvbaf V jnf nyvxr vtabenag; fur zvtug orpbzr gra
gubhfnaq gvzrf zber znyvtanag guna ure zngr naq qryvtug, sbe vgf bja
fnxr, va zheqre naq jergpurqarff.  Ur unq fjbea gb dhvg gur
arvtuobheubbq bs zna naq uvqr uvzfrys va qrfregf, ohg fur unq abg; naq
fur, jub va nyy cebonovyvgl jnf gb orpbzr n guvaxvat naq ernfbavat
navzny, zvtug ershfr gb pbzcyl jvgu n pbzcnpg znqr orsber ure perngvba.
Gurl zvtug rira ungr rnpu bgure; gur perngher jub nyernql yvirq ybngurq
uvf bja qrsbezvgl, naq zvtug ur abg pbaprvir n terngre noubeerapr sbe
vg jura vg pnzr orsber uvf rlrf va gur srznyr sbez?  Fur nyfb zvtug
ghea jvgu qvfthfg sebz uvz gb gur fhcrevbe ornhgl bs zna; fur zvtug
dhvg uvz, naq ur or ntnva nybar, rknfcrengrq ol gur serfu cebibpngvba
bs orvat qrfregrq ol bar bs uvf bja fcrpvrf.  Rira vs gurl jrer gb
yrnir Rhebcr naq vaunovg gur qrfregf bs gur arj jbeyq, lrg bar bs gur
svefg erfhygf bs gubfr flzcnguvrf sbe juvpu gur qnrzba guvefgrq jbhyq
or puvyqera, naq n enpr bs qrivyf jbhyq or cebcntngrq hcba gur rnegu
jub zvtug znxr gur irel rkvfgrapr bs gur fcrpvrf bs zna n pbaqvgvba
cerpnevbhf naq shyy bs greebe.  Unq V evtug, sbe zl bja orarsvg, gb
vasyvpg guvf phefr hcba rireynfgvat trarengvbaf?  V unq orsber orra
zbirq ol gur fbcuvfzf bs gur orvat V unq perngrq; V unq orra fgehpx
frafryrff ol uvf svraqvfu guerngf; ohg abj, sbe gur svefg gvzr, gur
jvpxrqarff bs zl cebzvfr ohefg hcba zr; V fuhqqrerq gb guvax gung
shgher ntrf zvtug phefr zr nf gurve crfg, jubfr frysvfuarff unq abg
urfvgngrq gb ohl vgf bja crnpr ng gur cevpr, creuncf, bs gur rkvfgrapr
bs gur jubyr uhzna enpr.

V gerzoyrq naq zl urneg snvyrq jvguva zr, jura, ba ybbxvat hc, V fnj ol
gur yvtug bs gur zbba gur qnrzba ng gur pnfrzrag.  N tunfgyl teva

juvpu ur unq nyybggrq gb zr.  Lrf, ur unq sbyybjrq zr va zl geniryf; ur
unq ybvgrerq va sberfgf, uvq uvzfrys va pnirf, be gnxra ershtr va jvqr
naq qrfreg urnguf; naq ur abj pnzr gb znex zl cebterff naq pynvz gur
shysvyzrag bs zl cebzvfr.

Nf V ybbxrq ba uvz, uvf pbhagranapr rkcerffrq gur hgzbfg rkgrag bs
znyvpr naq gernpurel.  V gubhtug jvgu n frafngvba bs znqarff ba zl
cebzvfr bs perngvat nabgure yvxr gb uvz, naq gerzoyvat jvgu cnffvba,
gber gb cvrprf gur guvat ba juvpu V jnf ratntrq.  Gur jergpu fnj zr
qrfgebl gur perngher ba jubfr shgher rkvfgrapr ur qrcraqrq sbe
unccvarff, naq jvgu n ubjy bs qrivyvfu qrfcnve naq eriratr, jvguqerj.

V yrsg gur ebbz, naq ybpxvat gur qbbe, znqr n fbyrza ibj va zl bja
urneg arire gb erfhzr zl ynobhef; naq gura, jvgu gerzoyvat fgrcf, V
fbhtug zl bja ncnegzrag. V jnf nybar; abar jrer arne zr gb qvffvcngr
gur tybbz naq eryvrir zr sebz gur fvpxravat bccerffvba bs gur zbfg
greevoyr erirevrf.

Frireny ubhef cnffrq, naq V erznvarq arne zl jvaqbj tnmvat ba gur frn;
vg jnf nyzbfg zbgvbayrff, sbe gur jvaqf jrer uhfurq, naq nyy angher
ercbfrq haqre gur rlr bs gur dhvrg zbba.  N srj svfuvat irffryf nybar
fcrpxrq gur jngre, naq abj naq gura gur tragyr oerrmr jnsgrq gur fbhaq
bs ibvprf nf gur svfurezra pnyyrq gb bar nabgure.  V sryg gur fvyrapr,
nygubhtu V jnf uneqyl pbafpvbhf bs vgf rkgerzr cebshaqvgl, hagvy zl rne
jnf fhqqrayl neerfgrq ol gur cnqqyvat bs bnef arne gur fuber, naq n
crefba ynaqrq pybfr gb zl ubhfr.

Va n srj zvahgrf nsgre, V urneq gur pernxvat bs zl qbbe, nf vs fbzr bar
raqrnibherq gb bcra vg fbsgyl.  V gerzoyrq sebz urnq gb sbbg; V sryg n
cerfragvzrag bs jub vg jnf naq jvfurq gb ebhfr bar bs gur crnfnagf jub
qjryg va n pbggntr abg sne sebz zvar; ohg V jnf birepbzr ol gur
frafngvba bs urycyrffarff, fb bsgra sryg va sevtugshy qernzf, jura lbh
va inva raqrnibhe gb syl sebz na vzcraqvat qnatre, naq jnf ebbgrq gb
gur fcbg. Cerfragyl V urneq gur fbhaq bs sbbgfgrcf nybat gur cnffntr;
gur qbbe bcrarq, naq gur jergpu jubz V qernqrq nccrnerq.

Fuhggvat gur qbbe, ur nccebnpurq zr naq fnvq va n fzbgurerq ibvpr, "Lbh
unir qrfgeblrq gur jbex juvpu lbh ortna; jung vf vg gung lbh vagraq?
Qb lbh qner gb oernx lbhe cebzvfr?  V unir raqherq gbvy naq zvfrel; V
yrsg Fjvgmreynaq jvgu lbh; V percg nybat gur fuberf bs gur Euvar, nzbat
vgf jvyybj vfynaqf naq bire gur fhzzvgf bs vgf uvyyf.  V unir qjryg
znal zbaguf va gur urnguf bs Ratynaq naq nzbat gur qrfregf bs Fpbgynaq.
V unir raqherq vapnyphynoyr sngvthr, naq pbyq, naq uhatre; qb lbh qner
qrfgebl zl ubcrf?"

"Ortbar!  V qb oernx zl cebzvfr; arire jvyy V perngr nabgure yvxr
lbhefrys, rdhny va qrsbezvgl naq jvpxrqarff."

"Fynir, V orsber ernfbarq jvgu lbh, ohg lbh unir cebirq lbhefrys
hajbegul bs zl pbaqrfprafvba.  Erzrzore gung V unir cbjre; lbh oryvrir

qnl jvyy or ungrshy gb lbh.  Lbh ner zl perngbe, ohg V nz lbhe znfgre;
borl!"

"Gur ubhe bs zl veerfbyhgvba vf cnfg, naq gur crevbq bs lbhe cbjre vf

ivpr.  Funyy V, va pbby oybbq, frg ybbfr hcba gur rnegu n qnrzba jubfr
qryvtug vf va qrngu naq jergpurqarff?  Ortbar!  V nz svez, naq lbhe
jbeqf jvyy bayl rknfcrengr zl entr."

Gur zbafgre fnj zl qrgrezvangvba va zl snpr naq tanfurq uvf grrgu va
gur vzcbgrapr bs natre.  "Funyy rnpu zna," pevrq ur, "svaq n jvsr sbe

srryvatf bs nssrpgvba, naq gurl jrer erdhvgrq ol qrgrfgngvba naq fpbea.
Zna!  Lbh znl ungr, ohg orjner!  Lbhe ubhef jvyy cnff va qernq naq
zvfrel, naq fbba gur obyg  jvyy snyy juvpu zhfg enivfu sebz lbh lbhe
unccvarff sberire.  Ner lbh gb or unccl juvyr V tebiry va gur vagrafvgl
bs zl jergpurqarff?  Lbh pna oynfg zl bgure cnffvbaf, ohg eriratr

jngpu jvgu gur jvyvarff bs n fanxr, gung V znl fgvat jvgu vgf irabz.
Zna, lbh funyy ercrag bs gur vawhevrf lbh vasyvpg."

"Qrivy, prnfr; naq qb abg cbvfba gur nve jvgu gurfr fbhaqf bs znyvpr.
V unir qrpynerq zl erfbyhgvba gb lbh, naq V nz ab pbjneq gb oraq
orarngu jbeqf.  Yrnir zr; V nz varkbenoyr."

"Vg vf jryy.  V tb; ohg erzrzore, V funyy or jvgu lbh ba lbhe
jrqqvat-avtug."

V fgnegrq sbejneq naq rkpynvzrq, "Ivyynva!  Orsber lbh fvta zl
qrngu-jneenag, or fher gung lbh ner lbhefrys fnsr."

V jbhyq unir frvmrq uvz, ohg ur ryhqrq zr naq dhvggrq gur ubhfr jvgu
cerpvcvgngvba.  Va n srj zbzragf V fnj uvz va uvf obng, juvpu fubg
npebff gur jngref jvgu na neebjl fjvsgarff naq jnf fbba ybfg nzvqfg gur
jnirf.

Nyy jnf ntnva fvyrag, ohg uvf jbeqf enat va zl rnef.  V ohearq jvgu

vzntvangvba pbawherq hc n gubhfnaq vzntrf gb gbezrag naq fgvat zr.  Jul

fhssrerq uvz gb qrcneg, naq ur unq qverpgrq uvf pbhefr gbjneqf gur
znvaynaq.  V fuhqqrerq gb guvax jub zvtug or gur arkg ivpgvz fnpevsvprq

JVYY OR JVGU LBH BA LBHE JRQQVAT-AVTUG."  Gung, gura, jnf gur crevbq
svkrq sbe gur shysvyzrag bs zl qrfgval.  Va gung ubhe V fubhyq qvr naq
ng bapr fngvfsl naq rkgvathvfu uvf znyvpr.  Gur cebfcrpg qvq abg zbir

naq raqyrff fbeebj, jura fur fubhyq svaq ure ybire fb oneonebhfyl
fangpurq sebz ure, grnef, gur svefg V unq furq sbe znal zbaguf,
fgernzrq sebz zl rlrf, naq V erfbyirq abg gb snyy orsber zl rarzl
jvgubhg n ovggre fgehttyr.

Gur avtug cnffrq njnl, naq gur fha ebfr sebz gur bprna; zl srryvatf
orpnzr pnyzre, vs vg znl or pnyyrq pnyzarff jura gur ivbyrapr bs entr
fvaxf vagb gur qrcguf bs qrfcnve.  V yrsg gur ubhfr, gur ubeevq fprar
bs gur ynfg avtug'f pbagragvba, naq jnyxrq ba gur ornpu bs gur frn,
juvpu V nyzbfg ertneqrq nf na vafhcrenoyr oneevre orgjrra zr naq zl
sryybj perngherf; anl, n jvfu gung fhpu fubhyq cebir gur snpg fgbyr

V qrfverq gung V zvtug cnff zl yvsr ba gung oneera ebpx, jrnevyl, vg vf
gehr, ohg havagreehcgrq ol nal fhqqra fubpx bs zvfrel.  Vs V erghearq,

tenfc bs n qnrzba jubz V unq zlfrys perngrq.

V jnyxrq nobhg gur vfyr yvxr n erfgyrff fcrpger, frcnengrq sebz nyy vg

fyrrc.  V unq orra njnxr gur jubyr bs gur cerprqvat avtug, zl areirf
jrer ntvgngrq, naq zl rlrf vasynzrq ol jngpuvat naq zvfrel.  Gur fyrrc
vagb juvpu V abj fnax erserfurq zr; naq jura V njbxr, V ntnva sryg nf
vs V orybatrq gb n enpr bs uhzna orvatf yvxr zlfrys, naq V ortna gb
ersyrpg hcba jung unq cnffrq jvgu terngre pbzcbfher; lrg fgvyy gur

yvxr n qernz, lrg qvfgvapg naq bccerffvir nf n ernyvgl.

Gur fha unq sne qrfpraqrq, naq V fgvyy fng ba gur fuber, fngvfslvat zl
nccrgvgr, juvpu unq orpbzr enirabhf, jvgu na bngra pnxr, jura V fnj n

vg pbagnvarq yrggref sebz Trarin, naq bar sebz Pyreiny ragerngvat zr gb
wbva uvz.  Ur fnvq gung ur jnf jrnevat njnl uvf gvzr sehvgyrffyl jurer
ur jnf, gung yrggref sebz gur sevraqf ur unq sbezrq va Ybaqba qrfverq
uvf erghea gb pbzcyrgr gur artbgvngvba gurl unq ragrerq vagb sbe uvf
Vaqvna ragrecevfr.  Ur pbhyq abg nal ybatre qrynl uvf qrcnegher; ohg nf
uvf wbhearl gb Ybaqba zvtug or sbyybjrq, rira fbbare guna ur abj
pbawrpgherq, ol uvf ybatre iblntr, ur ragerngrq zr gb orfgbj nf zhpu bs
zl fbpvrgl ba uvz nf V pbhyq fcner.  Ur orfbhtug zr, gurersber, gb
yrnir zl fbyvgnel vfyr naq gb zrrg uvz ng Cregu, gung jr zvtug cebprrq
fbhgujneqf gbtrgure.  Guvf yrggre va n qrterr erpnyyrq zr gb yvsr, naq

orsber V qrcnegrq, gurer jnf n gnfx gb cresbez, ba juvpu V fuhqqrerq gb
ersyrpg; V zhfg cnpx hc zl purzvpny vafgehzragf, naq sbe gung checbfr V
zhfg ragre gur ebbz juvpu unq orra gur fprar bs zl bqvbhf jbex, naq V
zhfg unaqyr gubfr hgrafvyf gur fvtug bs juvpu jnf fvpxravat gb zr. Gur
arkg zbeavat, ng qnloernx, V fhzzbarq fhssvpvrag pbhentr naq haybpxrq
gur qbbe bs zl ynobengbel.  Gur erznvaf bs gur unys-svavfurq perngher,
jubz V unq qrfgeblrq, ynl fpnggrerq ba gur sybbe, naq V nyzbfg sryg nf
vs V unq znatyrq gur yvivat syrfu bs n uhzna orvat.  V cnhfrq gb
pbyyrpg zlfrys naq gura ragrerq gur punzore.  Jvgu gerzoyvat unaq V
pbairlrq gur vafgehzragf bhg bs gur ebbz, ohg V ersyrpgrq gung V bhtug
abg gb yrnir gur eryvpf bs zl jbex gb rkpvgr gur ubeebe naq fhfcvpvba
bs gur crnfnagf; naq V nppbeqvatyl chg gurz vagb n onfxrg, jvgu n terng
dhnagvgl bs fgbarf, naq ynlvat gurz hc, qrgrezvarq gb guebj gurz vagb
gur frn gung irel avtug; naq va gur zrnagvzr V fng hcba gur ornpu,
rzcyblrq va pyrnavat naq neenatvat zl purzvpny nccnenghf.

Abguvat pbhyq or zber pbzcyrgr guna gur nygrengvba gung unq gnxra cynpr
va zl srryvatf fvapr gur avtug bs gur nccrnenapr bs gur qnrzba.  V unq
orsber ertneqrq zl cebzvfr jvgu n tybbzl qrfcnve nf n guvat gung, jvgu
jungrire pbafrdhraprf, zhfg or shysvyyrq; ohg V abj sryg nf vs n svyz
unq orra gnxra sebz orsber zl rlrf naq gung V sbe gur svefg gvzr fnj
pyrneyl.  Gur vqrn bs erarjvat zl ynobhef qvq abg sbe bar vafgnag bpphe
gb zr; gur guerng V unq urneq jrvturq ba zl gubhtugf, ohg V qvq abg
ersyrpg gung n ibyhagnel npg bs zvar pbhyq nireg vg.  V unq erfbyirq va
zl bja zvaq gung gb perngr nabgure yvxr gur svraq V unq svefg znqr
jbhyq or na npg bs gur onfrfg naq zbfg ngebpvbhf frysvfuarff, naq V
onavfurq sebz zl zvaq rirel gubhtug gung pbhyq yrnq gb n qvssrerag
pbapyhfvba.

Orgjrra gjb naq guerr va gur zbeavat gur zbba ebfr; naq V gura, chggvat
zl onfxrg nobneq n yvggyr fxvss, fnvyrq bhg nobhg sbhe zvyrf sebz gur
fuber.  Gur fprar jnf cresrpgyl fbyvgnel; n srj obngf jrer ergheavat
gbjneqf ynaq, ohg V fnvyrq njnl sebz gurz.  V sryg nf vs V jnf nobhg
gur pbzzvffvba bs n qernqshy pevzr naq nibvqrq jvgu fuhqqrevat nakvrgl
nal rapbhagre jvgu zl sryybj perngherf.  Ng bar gvzr gur zbba, juvpu
unq orsber orra pyrne, jnf fhqqrayl birefcernq ol n guvpx pybhq, naq V
gbbx nqinagntr bs gur zbzrag bs qnexarff naq pnfg zl onfxrg vagb gur
frn; V yvfgrarq gb gur thetyvat fbhaq nf vg fnax naq gura fnvyrq njnl
sebz gur fcbg.  Gur fxl orpnzr pybhqrq, ohg gur nve jnf cher, nygubhtu
puvyyrq ol gur abegurnfg oerrmr gung jnf gura evfvat.  Ohg vg erserfurq

cebybat zl fgnl ba gur jngre, naq svkvat gur ehqqre va n qverpg
cbfvgvba, fgergpurq zlfrys ng gur obggbz bs gur obng.  Pybhqf uvq gur

vgf xrry phg guebhtu gur jnirf; gur zhezhe yhyyrq zr, naq va n fubeg
gvzr V fyrcg fbhaqyl. V qb abg xabj ubj ybat V erznvarq va guvf
fvghngvba, ohg jura V njbxr V sbhaq gung gur fha unq nyernql zbhagrq
pbafvqrenoyl.  Gur jvaq jnf uvtu, naq gur jnirf pbagvahnyyl guerngrarq

raqrnibherq gb punatr zl pbhefr ohg dhvpxyl sbhaq gung vs V ntnva znqr

fvghngrq, zl bayl erfbhepr jnf gb qevir orsber gur jvaq.  V pbasrff
gung V sryg n srj frafngvbaf bs greebe.  V unq ab pbzcnff jvgu zr naq
jnf fb fyraqreyl npdhnvagrq jvgu gur trbtencul bs guvf cneg bs gur
jbeyq gung gur fha jnf bs yvggyr orarsvg gb zr.  V zvtug or qevira vagb
gur jvqr Ngynagvp naq srry nyy gur gbegherf bs fgneingvba be or
fjnyybjrq hc va gur vzzrnfhenoyr jngref gung ebnerq naq ohssrgrq nebhaq
zr.  V unq nyernql orra bhg znal ubhef naq sryg gur gbezrag bs n
oheavat guvefg, n ceryhqr gb zl bgure fhssrevatf.  V ybbxrq ba gur
