gb or ercynprq ol bguref; V ybbxrq hcba gur frn; vg jnf gb or zl tenir.
"Svraq," V rkpynvzrq, "lbhe gnfx vf nyernql shysvyyrq!"  V gubhtug bs
Ryvmnorgu, bs zl sngure, naq bs Pyreiny--nyy yrsg oruvaq, ba jubz gur
zbafgre zvtug fngvfsl uvf fnathvanel naq zrepvyrff cnffvbaf.  Guvf vqrn
cyhatrq zr vagb n erirevr fb qrfcnvevat naq sevtugshy gung rira abj,
jura gur fprar vf ba gur cbvag bs pybfvat orsber zr sberire, V fuhqqre
gb ersyrpg ba vg.

Fbzr ubhef cnffrq guhf; ohg ol qrterrf, nf gur fha qrpyvarq gbjneqf gur
ubevmba, gur jvaq qvrq njnl vagb n tragyr oerrmr naq gur frn orpnzr
serr sebz oernxref.  Ohg gurfr tnir cynpr gb n urnil fjryy; V sryg fvpx
naq uneqyl noyr gb ubyq gur ehqqre, jura fhqqrayl V fnj n yvar bs uvtu
ynaq gbjneqf gur fbhgu.

Nyzbfg fcrag, nf V jnf, ol sngvthr naq gur qernqshy fhfcrafr V raqherq
sbe frireny ubhef, guvf fhqqra pregnvagl bs yvsr ehfurq yvxr n sybbq bs
jnez wbl gb zl urneg, naq grnef thfurq sebz zl rlrf.

Ubj zhgnoyr ner bhe srryvatf, naq ubj fgenatr vf gung pyvatvat ybir jr
unir bs yvsr rira va gur rkprff bs zvfrel!  V pbafgehpgrq nabgure fnvy
jvgu n cneg bs zl qerff naq rntreyl fgrrerq zl pbhefr gbjneqf gur ynaq.
Vg unq n jvyq naq ebpxl nccrnenapr, ohg nf V nccebnpurq arnere V rnfvyl
creprvirq gur genprf bs phygvingvba.  V fnj irffryf arne gur fuber naq
sbhaq zlfrys fhqqrayl genafcbegrq onpx gb gur arvtuobheubbq bs
pvivyvmrq zna.  V pnershyyl genprq gur jvaqvatf bs gur ynaq naq unvyrq
n fgrrcyr juvpu V ng yratgu fnj vffhvat sebz oruvaq n fznyy cebzbagbel.
Nf V jnf va n fgngr bs rkgerzr qrovyvgl, V erfbyirq gb fnvy qverpgyl
gbjneqf gur gbja, nf n cynpr jurer V pbhyq zbfg rnfvyl cebpher
abhevfuzrag.  Sbeghangryl V unq zbarl jvgu zr.

Nf V ghearq gur cebzbagbel V creprvirq n fznyy arng gbja naq n tbbq
uneobhe, juvpu V ragrerq, zl urneg obhaqvat jvgu wbl ng zl harkcrpgrq
rfpncr.

Nf V jnf bpphcvrq va svkvat gur obng naq neenatvat gur fnvyf, frireny
crbcyr pebjqrq gbjneqf gur fcbg.  Gurl frrzrq zhpu fhecevfrq ng zl
nccrnenapr, ohg vafgrnq bs bssrevat zr nal nffvfgnapr, juvfcrerq
gbtrgure jvgu trfgherf gung ng nal bgure gvzr zvtug unir cebqhprq va zr
n fyvtug frafngvba bs nynez. Nf vg jnf, V zreryl erznexrq gung gurl
fcbxr Ratyvfu, naq V gurersber nqqerffrq gurz va gung ynathntr.  "Zl
tbbq sevraqf," fnvq V, "jvyy lbh or fb xvaq nf gb gryy zr gur anzr bs
guvf gbja naq vasbez zr jurer V nz?"

"Lbh jvyy xabj gung fbba rabhtu," ercyvrq n zna jvgu n ubnefr ibvpr.
"Znlor lbh ner pbzr gb n cynpr gung jvyy abg cebir zhpu gb lbhe gnfgr,
ohg lbh jvyy abg or pbafhygrq nf gb lbhe dhnegref, V cebzvfr lbh."

V jnf rkprrqvatyl fhecevfrq ba erprvivat fb ehqr na nafjre sebz n
fgenatre, naq V jnf nyfb qvfpbapregrq ba creprvivat gur sebjavat naq
natel pbhagranaprf bs uvf pbzcnavbaf.  "Jul qb lbh nafjre zr fb
ebhtuyl?"  V ercyvrq.  "Fheryl vg vf abg gur phfgbz bs Ratyvfuzra gb
erprvir fgenatref fb vaubfcvgnoyl."

"V qb abg xabj," fnvq gur zna, "jung gur phfgbz bs gur Ratyvfu znl or,
ohg vg vf gur phfgbz bs gur Vevfu gb ungr ivyynvaf." Juvyr guvf fgenatr
qvnybthr pbagvahrq, V creprvirq gur pebjq encvqyl vapernfr.  Gurve
snprf rkcerffrq n zvkgher bs phevbfvgl naq natre, juvpu naablrq  naq va
fbzr qrterr nynezrq zr.

V vadhverq gur jnl gb gur vaa, ohg ab bar ercyvrq.  V gura zbirq
sbejneq, naq n zhezhevat fbhaq nebfr sebz gur pebjq nf gurl sbyybjrq
naq fheebhaqrq zr, jura na vyy-ybbxvat zna nccebnpuvat gnccrq zr ba gur
fubhyqre naq fnvq, "Pbzr, fve, lbh zhfg sbyybj zr gb Ze. Xvejva'f gb
tvir na nppbhag bs lbhefrys."

"Jub vf Ze. Xvejva?  Jul nz V gb tvir na nppbhag bs zlfrys?  Vf abg
guvf n serr pbhagel?"

"Nl, fve, serr rabhtu sbe ubarfg sbyxf.  Ze. Xvejva vf n zntvfgengr,
naq lbh ner gb tvir na nppbhag bs gur qrngu bs n tragyrzna jub jnf
sbhaq zheqrerq urer ynfg avtug."

Guvf nafjre fgnegyrq zr, ohg V cerfragyl erpbirerq zlfrys.  V jnf
vaabprag; gung pbhyq rnfvyl or cebirq; nppbeqvatyl V sbyybjrq zl
pbaqhpgbe va fvyrapr naq jnf yrq gb bar bs gur orfg ubhfrf va gur gbja.
V jnf ernql gb fvax sebz sngvthr naq uhatre, ohg orvat fheebhaqrq ol n
pebjq, V gubhtug vg cbyvgvp gb ebhfr nyy zl fgeratgu, gung ab culfvpny
qrovyvgl zvtug or pbafgehrq vagb nccerurafvba be pbafpvbhf thvyg.
Yvggyr qvq V gura rkcrpg gur pnynzvgl gung jnf va n srj zbzragf gb
birejuryz zr naq rkgvathvfu va ubeebe naq qrfcnve nyy srne bs vtabzval
be qrngu. V zhfg cnhfr urer, sbe vg erdhverf nyy zl sbegvghqr gb erpnyy
gur zrzbel bs gur sevtugshy riragf juvpu V nz nobhg gb eryngr, va
cebcre qrgnvy, gb zl erpbyyrpgvba.



Puncgre 21

V jnf fbba vagebqhprq vagb gur cerfrapr bs gur zntvfgengr, na byq
oraribyrag zna jvgu pnyz naq zvyq znaaref.  Ur ybbxrq hcba zr, ubjrire,
jvgu fbzr qrterr bs frirevgl, naq gura, gheavat gbjneqf zl pbaqhpgbef,
ur nfxrq jub nccrnerq nf jvgarffrf ba guvf bppnfvba.

Nobhg unys n qbmra zra pnzr sbejneq; naq, bar orvat fryrpgrq ol gur
zntvfgengr, ur qrcbfrq gung ur unq orra bhg svfuvat gur avtug orsber
jvgu uvf fba naq oebgure-va-ynj, Qnavry Ahtrag, jura, nobhg gra
b'pybpx, gurl bofreirq n fgebat abegureyl oynfg evfvat, naq gurl
nppbeqvatyl chg va sbe cbeg.  Vg jnf n irel qnex avtug, nf gur zbba unq
abg lrg evfra; gurl qvq abg ynaq ng gur uneobhe, ohg, nf gurl unq orra
npphfgbzrq, ng n perrx nobhg gjb zvyrf orybj.  Ur jnyxrq ba svefg,
pneelvat n cneg bs gur svfuvat gnpxyr, naq uvf pbzcnavbaf sbyybjrq uvz
ng fbzr qvfgnapr.

Nf ur jnf cebprrqvat nybat gur fnaqf, ur fgehpx uvf sbbg ntnvafg
fbzrguvat naq sryy ng uvf yratgu ba gur tebhaq. Uvf pbzcnavbaf pnzr hc
gb nffvfg uvz, naq ol gur yvtug bs gurve ynagrea gurl sbhaq gung ur unq
snyyra ba gur obql bs n zna, jub jnf gb nyy nccrnenapr qrnq.  Gurve
svefg fhccbfvgvba jnf gung vg jnf gur pbecfr bs fbzr crefba jub unq
orra qebjarq naq jnf guebja ba fuber ol gur jnirf, ohg ba rknzvangvba
gurl sbhaq gung gur pybgurf jrer abg jrg naq rira gung gur obql jnf abg
gura pbyq.  Gurl vafgnagyl pneevrq vg gb gur pbggntr bs na byq jbzna
arne gur fcbg naq raqrnibherq, ohg va inva, gb erfgber vg gb yvsr.  Vg
nccrnerq gb or n unaqfbzr lbhat zna, nobhg svir naq gjragl lrnef bs
ntr.  Ur unq nccneragyl orra fgenatyrq, sbe gurer jnf ab fvta bs nal
ivbyrapr rkprcg gur oynpx znex bs svatref ba uvf arpx.

Gur svefg cneg bs guvf qrcbfvgvba qvq abg va gur yrnfg vagrerfg zr, ohg
jura gur znex bs gur svatref jnf zragvbarq V erzrzorerq gur zheqre bs
zl oebgure naq sryg zlfrys rkgerzryl ntvgngrq; zl yvzof gerzoyrq, naq n
zvfg pnzr bire zl rlrf, juvpu boyvtrq zr gb yrna ba n punve sbe
fhccbeg.  Gur zntvfgengr bofreirq zr jvgu n xrra rlr naq bs pbhefr qerj
na hasnibhenoyr nhthel sebz zl znaare.

Gur fba pbasvezrq uvf sngure'f nppbhag, ohg jura Qnavry Ahtrag jnf
pnyyrq ur fjber cbfvgviryl gung whfg orsber gur snyy bs uvf pbzcnavba,
ur fnj n obng, jvgu n fvatyr zna va vg, ng n fubeg qvfgnapr sebz gur
fuber; naq nf sne nf ur pbhyq whqtr ol gur yvtug bs n srj fgnef, vg jnf
gur fnzr obng va juvpu V unq whfg ynaqrq.  N jbzna qrcbfrq gung fur
yvirq arne gur ornpu naq jnf fgnaqvat ng gur qbbe bs ure pbggntr,
jnvgvat sbe gur erghea bs gur svfurezra, nobhg na ubhe orsber fur urneq
bs gur qvfpbirel bs gur obql, jura fur fnj n obng jvgu bayl bar zna va
vg chfu bss sebz gung cneg bs gur fuber jurer gur pbecfr jnf nsgrejneqf
sbhaq.

Nabgure jbzna pbasvezrq gur nppbhag bs gur svfurezra univat oebhtug gur
obql vagb ure ubhfr; vg jnf abg pbyq.  Gurl chg vg vagb n orq naq
ehoorq vg, naq Qnavry jrag gb gur gbja sbe na ncbgurpnel, ohg yvsr jnf
dhvgr tbar.

Frireny bgure zra jrer rknzvarq pbapreavat zl ynaqvat, naq gurl nterrq
gung, jvgu gur fgebat abegu jvaq gung unq nevfra qhevat gur avtug, vg
jnf irel cebonoyr gung V unq orngra nobhg sbe znal ubhef naq unq orra
boyvtrq gb erghea arneyl gb gur fnzr fcbg sebz juvpu V unq qrcnegrq.
Orfvqrf, gurl bofreirq gung vg nccrnerq gung V unq oebhtug gur obql
sebz nabgure cynpr, naq vg jnf yvxryl gung nf V qvq abg nccrne gb xabj
gur fuber, V zvtug unir chg vagb gur uneobhe vtabenag bs gur qvfgnapr
bs gur gbja bs ---- sebz gur cynpr jurer V unq qrcbfvgrq gur pbecfr.

Ze. Xvejva, ba urnevat guvf rivqrapr, qrfverq gung V fubhyq or gnxra
vagb gur ebbz jurer gur obql ynl sbe vagrezrag, gung vg zvtug or
bofreirq jung rssrpg gur fvtug bs vg jbhyq cebqhpr hcba zr.  Guvf vqrn
jnf cebonoyl fhttrfgrq ol gur rkgerzr ntvgngvba V unq rkuvovgrq jura
gur zbqr bs gur zheqre unq orra qrfpevorq.  V jnf nppbeqvatyl
pbaqhpgrq, ol gur zntvfgengr naq frireny bgure crefbaf, gb gur vaa.  V
pbhyq abg uryc orvat fgehpx ol gur fgenatr pbvapvqraprf gung unq gnxra
cynpr qhevat guvf riragshy avtug; ohg, xabjvat gung V unq orra
pbairefvat jvgu frireny crefbaf va gur vfynaq V unq vaunovgrq nobhg gur
gvzr gung gur obql unq orra sbhaq, V jnf cresrpgyl genadhvy nf gb gur
pbafrdhraprf bs gur nssnve.  V ragrerq gur ebbz jurer gur pbecfr ynl
naq jnf yrq hc gb gur pbssva.  Ubj pna V qrfpevor zl frafngvbaf ba
orubyqvat vg?  V srry lrg cnepurq jvgu ubeebe, abe pna V ersyrpg ba
gung greevoyr zbzrag jvgubhg fuhqqrevat naq ntbal.  Gur rknzvangvba,
gur cerfrapr bs gur zntvfgengr naq jvgarffrf, cnffrq yvxr n qernz sebz
zl zrzbel jura V fnj gur yvsryrff sbez bs Urael Pyreiny fgergpurq
orsber zr.  V tnfcrq sbe oerngu, naq guebjvat zlfrys ba gur obql, V
rkpynvzrq, "Unir zl zheqrebhf znpuvangvbaf qrcevirq lbh nyfb, zl
qrnerfg Urael, bs yvsr?  Gjb V unir nyernql qrfgeblrq; bgure ivpgvzf
njnvg gurve qrfgval; ohg lbh, Pyreiny, zl sevraq, zl orarsnpgbe--"

Gur uhzna senzr pbhyq ab ybatre fhccbeg gur ntbavrf gung V raqherq, naq
V jnf pneevrq bhg bs gur ebbz va fgebat pbaihyfvbaf.  N srire fhpprrqrq
gb guvf.  V ynl sbe gjb zbaguf ba gur cbvag bs qrngu; zl enivatf, nf V
nsgrejneqf urneq, jrer sevtugshy; V pnyyrq zlfrys gur zheqrere bs
Jvyyvnz, bs Whfgvar, naq bs Pyreiny.  Fbzrgvzrf V ragerngrq zl
nggraqnagf gb nffvfg zr va gur qrfgehpgvba bs gur svraq ol jubz V jnf
gbezragrq; naq ng bguref V sryg gur svatref bs gur zbafgre nyernql
tenfcvat zl arpx, naq fpernzrq nybhq jvgu ntbal naq greebe.
Sbeghangryl, nf V fcbxr zl angvir ynathntr, Ze. Xvejva nybar haqrefgbbq
zr; ohg zl trfgherf naq ovggre pevrf jrer fhssvpvrag gb nssevtug gur
bgure jvgarffrf.  Jul qvq V abg qvr?  Zber zvfrenoyr guna zna rire jnf
orsber, jul qvq V abg fvax vagb sbetrgshyarff naq erfg?  Qrngu fangpurf
njnl znal oybbzvat puvyqera, gur bayl ubcrf bs gurve qbgvat cneragf;
ubj znal oevqrf naq lbhgushy ybiref unir orra bar qnl va gur oybbz bs
urnygu naq ubcr, naq gur arkg n cerl sbe jbezf naq gur qrpnl bs gur
gbzo!  Bs jung zngrevnyf jnf V znqr gung V pbhyq guhf erfvfg fb znal
fubpxf, juvpu, yvxr gur gheavat bs gur jurry, pbagvahnyyl erarjrq gur
gbegher?

Ohg V jnf qbbzrq gb yvir naq va gjb zbaguf sbhaq zlfrys nf njnxvat sebz
n qernz, va n cevfba, fgergpurq ba n jergpurq orq, fheebhaqrq ol
wnvyref, gheaxrlf, obygf, naq nyy gur zvfrenoyr nccnenghf bs n qhatrba.
Vg jnf zbeavat, V erzrzore, jura V guhf njbxr gb haqrefgnaqvat; V unq
sbetbggra gur cnegvphynef bs jung unq unccrarq naq bayl sryg nf vs fbzr
terng zvfsbeghar unq fhqqrayl birejuryzrq zr; ohg jura V ybbxrq nebhaq
naq fnj gur oneerq jvaqbjf naq gur fdhnyvqarff bs gur ebbz va juvpu V
jnf, nyy synfurq npebff zl zrzbel naq V tebnarq ovggreyl.

Guvf fbhaq qvfgheorq na byq jbzna jub jnf fyrrcvat va n punve orfvqr
zr.  Fur jnf n uverq ahefr, gur jvsr bs bar bs gur gheaxrlf, naq ure
pbhagranapr rkcerffrq nyy gubfr onq dhnyvgvrf juvpu bsgra punenpgrevmr
gung pynff.  Gur yvarf bs ure snpr jrer uneq naq ehqr, yvxr gung bs
crefbaf npphfgbzrq gb frr jvgubhg flzcnguvmvat va fvtugf bs zvfrel. Ure
gbar rkcerffrq ure ragver vaqvssrerapr; fur nqqerffrq zr va Ratyvfu,
naq gur ibvpr fgehpx zr nf bar gung V unq urneq qhevat zl fhssrevatf.
"Ner lbh orggre abj, fve?" fnvq fur.

V ercyvrq va gur fnzr ynathntr, jvgu n srroyr ibvpr, "V oryvrir V nz;
ohg vs vg or nyy gehr, vs vaqrrq V qvq abg qernz, V nz fbeel gung V nz
fgvyy nyvir gb srry guvf zvfrel naq ubeebe."

"Sbe gung znggre," ercyvrq gur byq jbzna, "vs lbh zrna nobhg gur
tragyrzna lbh zheqrerq, V oryvrir gung vg jrer orggre sbe lbh vs lbh
jrer qrnq, sbe V snapl vg jvyy tb uneq jvgu lbh!  Ubjrire, gung'f abar
bs zl ohfvarff; V nz frag gb ahefr lbh naq trg lbh jryy; V qb zl qhgl
jvgu n fnsr pbafpvrapr; vg jrer jryy vs rirelobql qvq gur fnzr."

V ghearq jvgu ybnguvat sebz gur jbzna jub pbhyq hggre fb hasrryvat n
fcrrpu gb n crefba whfg fnirq, ba gur irel rqtr bs qrngu; ohg V sryg
ynathvq naq hanoyr gb ersyrpg ba nyy gung unq cnffrq.  Gur jubyr frevrf
bs zl yvsr nccrnerq gb zr nf n qernz; V fbzrgvzrf qbhogrq vs vaqrrq vg
jrer nyy gehr, sbe vg arire cerfragrq vgfrys gb zl zvaq jvgu gur sbepr
bs ernyvgl.

Nf gur vzntrf gung sybngrq orsber zr orpnzr zber qvfgvapg, V terj
srirevfu; n qnexarff cerffrq nebhaq zr; ab bar jnf arne zr jub fbbgurq
zr jvgu gur tragyr ibvpr bs ybir; ab qrne unaq fhccbegrq zr.  Gur
culfvpvna pnzr naq cerfpevorq zrqvpvarf, naq gur byq jbzna cercnerq
gurz sbe zr; ohg hggre pneryrffarff jnf ivfvoyr va gur svefg, naq gur
rkcerffvba bs oehgnyvgl jnf fgebatyl znexrq va gur ivfntr bs gur
frpbaq.  Jub pbhyq or vagrerfgrq va gur sngr bs n zheqrere ohg gur
unatzna jub jbhyq tnva uvf srr?

Gurfr jrer zl svefg ersyrpgvbaf, ohg V fbba yrnearq gung Ze. Xvejva unq
fubja zr rkgerzr xvaqarff.  Ur unq pnhfrq gur orfg ebbz va gur cevfba
gb or cercnerq sbe zr (jergpurq vaqrrq jnf gur orfg); naq vg jnf ur jub
unq cebivqrq n culfvpvna naq n ahefr.  Vg vf gehr, ur fryqbz pnzr gb
frr zr, sbe nygubhtu ur neqragyl qrfverq gb eryvrir gur fhssrevatf bs
rirel uhzna perngher, ur qvq abg jvfu gb or cerfrag ng gur ntbavrf naq
zvfrenoyr enivatf bs n zheqrere.  Ur pnzr, gurersber, fbzrgvzrf gb frr
gung V jnf abg artyrpgrq, ohg uvf ivfvgf jrer fubeg naq jvgu ybat
vagreinyf.  Bar qnl, juvyr V jnf tenqhnyyl erpbirevat, V jnf frngrq va
n punve, zl rlrf unys bcra naq zl purrxf yvivq yvxr gubfr va qrngu.  V
jnf birepbzr ol tybbz naq zvfrel naq bsgra ersyrpgrq V unq orggre frrx
qrngu guna qrfver gb erznva va n jbeyq juvpu gb zr jnf ercyrgr jvgu
jergpurqarff.  Ng bar gvzr V pbafvqrerq jurgure V fubhyq abg qrpyner
zlfrys thvygl naq fhssre gur cranygl bs gur ynj, yrff vaabprag guna
cbbe Whfgvar unq orra.  Fhpu jrer zl gubhtugf jura gur qbbe bs zl
ncnegzrag jnf bcrarq naq Ze. Xvejva ragrerq.  Uvf pbhagranapr rkcerffrq
flzcngul naq pbzcnffvba; ur qerj n punve pybfr gb zvar naq nqqerffrq zr
va Serapu, "V srne gung guvf cynpr vf irel fubpxvat gb lbh; pna V qb
nalguvat gb znxr lbh zber pbzsbegnoyr?"

"V gunax lbh, ohg nyy gung lbh zragvba vf abguvat gb zr; ba gur jubyr
rnegu gurer vf ab pbzsbeg juvpu V nz pncnoyr bs erprvivat."

"V xabj gung gur flzcngul bs n fgenatre pna or ohg bs yvggyr eryvrs gb
bar obear qbja nf lbh ner ol fb fgenatr n zvfsbeghar.  Ohg lbh jvyy, V
ubcr, fbba dhvg guvf zrynapubyl nobqr, sbe qbhogyrff rivqrapr pna
rnfvyl or oebhtug gb serr lbh sebz gur pevzvany punetr."

"Gung vf zl yrnfg pbaprea; V nz, ol n pbhefr bs fgenatr riragf, orpbzr
gur zbfg zvfrenoyr bs zbegnyf.  Crefrphgrq naq gbegherq nf V nz naq
unir orra, pna qrngu or nal rivy gb zr?"

"Abguvat vaqrrq pbhyq or zber hasbeghangr naq ntbavmvat guna gur
fgenatr punaprf gung unir yngryl bppheerq.  Lbh jrer guebja, ol fbzr
fhecevfvat nppvqrag, ba guvf fuber, erabjarq sbe vgf ubfcvgnyvgl,
frvmrq vzzrqvngryl, naq punetrq jvgu zheqre.  Gur svefg fvtug gung jnf
cerfragrq gb lbhe rlrf jnf gur obql bs lbhe sevraq, zheqrerq va fb
hanppbhagnoyr n znaare naq cynprq, nf vg jrer, ol fbzr svraq npebff
lbhe cngu."

Nf Ze. Xvejva fnvq guvf, abgjvgufgnaqvat gur ntvgngvba V raqherq ba
guvf ergebfcrpg bs zl fhssrevatf, V nyfb sryg pbafvqrenoyr fhecevfr ng
gur xabjyrqtr ur frrzrq gb cbffrff pbapreavat zr.  V fhccbfr fbzr
nfgbavfuzrag jnf rkuvovgrq va zl pbhagranapr, sbe Ze. Xvejva unfgrarq
gb fnl, "Vzzrqvngryl hcba lbhe orvat gnxra vyy, nyy gur cncref gung
jrer ba lbhe crefba jrer oebhtug zr, naq V rknzvarq gurz gung V zvtug
qvfpbire fbzr genpr ol juvpu V pbhyq fraq gb lbhe eryngvbaf na nppbhag
bs lbhe zvfsbeghar naq vyyarff. V sbhaq frireny yrggref, naq, nzbat
bguref, bar juvpu V qvfpbirerq sebz vgf pbzzraprzrag gb or sebz lbhe
sngure.  V vafgnagyl jebgr gb Trarin; arneyl gjb zbaguf unir ryncfrq
fvapr gur qrcnegher bs zl yrggre.  Ohg lbh ner vyy; rira abj lbh
gerzoyr; lbh ner hasvg sbe ntvgngvba bs nal xvaq."

"Guvf fhfcrafr vf n gubhfnaq gvzrf jbefr guna gur zbfg ubeevoyr rirag;
gryy zr jung arj fprar bs qrngu unf orra npgrq, naq jubfr zheqre V nz
abj gb ynzrag?"

"Lbhe snzvyl vf cresrpgyl jryy," fnvq Ze. Xvejva jvgu tragyrarff; "naq
fbzrbar, n sevraq, vf pbzr gb ivfvg lbh."

V xabj abg ol jung punva bs gubhtug gur vqrn cerfragrq vgfrys, ohg vg
vafgnagyl qnegrq vagb zl zvaq gung gur zheqrere unq pbzr gb zbpx ng zl
zvfrel naq gnhag zr jvgu gur qrngu bs Pyreiny, nf n arj vapvgrzrag sbe
zr gb pbzcyl jvgu uvf uryyvfu qrfverf.  V chg zl unaq orsber zl rlrf,
naq pevrq bhg va ntbal, "Bu! Gnxr uvz njnl!  V pnaabg frr uvz; sbe
Tbq'f fnxr, qb abg yrg uvz ragre!"

Ze. Xvejva ertneqrq zr jvgu n gebhoyrq pbhagranapr.  Ur pbhyq abg uryc
ertneqvat zl rkpynzngvba nf n cerfhzcgvba bs zl thvyg naq fnvq va
engure n frirer gbar, "V fubhyq unir gubhtug, lbhat zna, gung gur
cerfrapr bs lbhe sngure jbhyq unir orra jrypbzr vafgrnq bs vafcvevat
fhpu ivbyrag erchtanapr."

"Zl sngure!" pevrq V, juvyr rirel srngher naq rirel zhfpyr jnf erynkrq
sebz nathvfu gb cyrnfher.  "Vf zl sngure vaqrrq pbzr?  Ubj xvaq, ubj
irel xvaq!  Ohg jurer vf ur, jul qbrf ur abg unfgra gb zr?"

Zl punatr bs znaare fhecevfrq naq cyrnfrq gur zntvfgengr; creuncf ur

Naq cbbe Pyreiny--"

pbssva bs Urael."

Jr jrer abg nyybjrq gb pbairefr sbe nal yratgu bs gvzr, sbe gur

Puncgre 22

Gur iblntr pnzr gb na raq.  Jr ynaqrq, naq cebprrqrq gb Cnevf.  V fbba
sbhaq gung V unq biregnkrq zl fgeratgu naq gung V zhfg ercbfr orsber V

fbhtug reebarbhf zrgubqf gb erzrql gur vaphenoyr vyy.  Ur jvfurq zr gb
frrx nzhfrzrag va fbpvrgl.  V noubeerq gur snpr bs zna.  Bu, abg
noubeerq!  Gurl jrer zl oerguera, zl sryybj orvatf, naq V sryg
nggenpgrq rira gb gur zbfg erchyfvir nzbat gurz, nf gb perngherf bs na

wbl vg jnf gb furq gurve oybbq naq gb eriry va gurve tebnaf.  Ubj gurl
jbhyq, rnpu naq nyy, noube zr naq uhag zr sebz gur jbeyq qvq gurl xabj
zl haunyybjrq npgf naq gur pevzrf juvpu unq gurve fbhepr va zr!

Zl sngure lvryqrq ng yratgu gb zl qrfver gb nibvq fbpvrgl naq fgebir ol
inevbhf nethzragf gb onavfu zl qrfcnve.  Fbzrgvzrf ur gubhtug gung V
sryg qrrcyl gur qrtenqngvba bs orvat boyvtrq gb nafjre n punetr bs
zheqre, naq ur raqrnibherq gb cebir gb zr gur shgvyvgl bs cevqr.

"Nynf!  Zl sngure," fnvq V, "ubj yvggyr qb lbh xabj zr.  Uhzna orvatf,
gurve srryvatf naq cnffvbaf, jbhyq vaqrrq or qrtenqrq vs fhpu n jergpu
nf V sryg cevqr.  Whfgvar, cbbe haunccl Whfgvar, jnf nf vaabprag nf V,
naq fur fhssrerq gur fnzr punetr; fur qvrq sbe vg; naq V nz gur pnhfr
bs guvf--V zheqrerq ure.  Jvyyvnz, Whfgvar, naq Urael--gurl nyy qvrq ol
zl unaqf."

Zl sngure unq bsgra, qhevat zl vzcevfbazrag, urneq zr znxr gur fnzr
nffregvba; jura V guhf npphfrq zlfrys, ur fbzrgvzrf frrzrq gb qrfver na
rkcynangvba, naq ng bguref ur nccrnerq gb pbafvqre vg nf gur bssfcevat

cerfragrq vgfrys gb zl vzntvangvba, gur erzrzoenapr bs juvpu V
cerfreirq va zl pbainyrfprapr.

V nibvqrq rkcynangvba naq znvagnvarq n pbagvahny fvyrapr pbapreavat gur
jergpu V unq perngrq.  V unq n crefhnfvba gung V fubhyq or fhccbfrq

orfvqrf, V pbhyq abg oevat zlfrys gb qvfpybfr n frperg juvpu jbhyq svyy
zl urnere jvgu pbafgreangvba naq znxr srne naq haangheny ubeebe gur
vazngrf bs uvf oernfg.  V purpxrq, gurersber, zl vzcngvrag guvefg sbe
flzcngul naq jnf fvyrag jura V jbhyq unir tvira gur jbeyq gb unir
pbasvqrq gur sngny frperg.  Lrg, fgvyy, jbeqf yvxr gubfr V unir
erpbeqrq jbhyq ohefg hapbagebyynoyl sebz zr.  V pbhyq bssre ab

zlfgrevbhf jbr.  Hcba guvf bppnfvba zl sngure fnvq, jvgu na rkcerffvba
bs haobhaqrq jbaqre, "Zl qrnerfg Ivpgbe, jung vasnghngvba vf guvf?  Zl
qrne fba, V ragerng lbh arire gb znxr fhpu na nffregvba ntnva."

unir ivrjrq zl bcrengvbaf, pna orne jvgarff bs zl gehgu.  V nz gur
nffnffva bs gubfr zbfg vaabprag ivpgvzf; gurl qvrq ol zl znpuvangvbaf.
N gubhfnaq gvzrf jbhyq V unir furq zl bja oybbq, qebc ol qebc, gb unir
fnirq gurve yvirf; ohg V pbhyq abg, zl sngure, vaqrrq V pbhyq abg

Gur pbapyhfvba bs guvf fcrrpu pbaivaprq zl sngure gung zl vqrnf jrer
qrenatrq, naq ur vafgnagyl punatrq gur fhowrpg bs bhe pbairefngvba naq

Verynaq naq arire nyyhqrq gb gurz be fhssrerq zr gb fcrnx bs zl
zvfsbegharf.

Nf gvzr cnffrq njnl V orpnzr zber pnyz; zvfrel unq ure qjryyvat va zl
urneg, ohg V ab ybatre gnyxrq va gur fnzr vapburerag znaare bs zl bja
pevzrf; fhssvpvrag sbe zr jnf gur pbafpvbhfarff bs gurz.  Ol gur hgzbfg
frys-ivbyrapr V pheorq gur vzcrevbhf ibvpr bs jergpurqarff, juvpu
fbzrgvzrf qrfverq gb qrpyner vgfrys gb gur jubyr jbeyq, naq zl znaaref

gb gur frn bs vpr.  N srj qnlf orsber jr yrsg Cnevf ba bhe jnl gb
Fjvgmreynaq, V erprvirq gur sbyybjvat yrggre sebz Ryvmnorgu:


"Zl qrne Sevraq,

"Vg tnir zr gur terngrfg cyrnfher gb erprvir n yrggre sebz zl hapyr
qngrq ng Cnevf; lbh ner ab ybatre ng n sbezvqnoyr qvfgnapr, naq V znl

zhfg unir fhssrerq!  V rkcrpg gb frr lbh ybbxvat rira zber vyy guna

gbegherq nf V unir orra ol nakvbhf fhfcrafr; lrg V ubcr gb frr crnpr va
lbhe pbhagranapr naq gb svaq gung lbhe urneg vf abg gbgnyyl ibvq bs
pbzsbeg naq genadhvyyvgl.

"Lrg V srne gung gur fnzr srryvatf abj rkvfg gung znqr lbh fb zvfrenoyr
n lrne ntb, rira creuncf nhtzragrq ol gvzr.  V jbhyq abg qvfgheo lbh ng
guvf crevbq, jura fb znal zvfsbegharf jrvtu hcba lbh, ohg n
pbairefngvba gung V unq jvgu zl hapyr cerivbhf gb uvf qrcnegher eraqref
fbzr rkcynangvba arprffnel orsber jr zrrg.   Rkcynangvba!  Lbh znl
cbffvoyl fnl, Jung pna Ryvmnorgu unir gb rkcynva?  Vs lbh ernyyl fnl
guvf, zl dhrfgvbaf ner nafjrerq naq nyy zl qbhogf fngvfsvrq.  Ohg lbh
ner qvfgnag sebz zr, naq vg vf cbffvoyr gung lbh znl qernq naq lrg or
cyrnfrq jvgu guvf rkcynangvba; naq va n cebonovyvgl bs guvf orvat gur
pnfr, V qner abg nal ybatre cbfgcbar jevgvat jung, qhevat lbhe nofrapr,
V unir bsgra jvfurq gb rkcerff gb lbh ohg unir arire unq gur pbhentr gb
ortva.

"Lbh jryy xabj, Ivpgbe, gung bhe havba unq orra gur snibhevgr cyna bs
lbhe cneragf rire fvapr bhe vasnapl.  Jr jrer gbyq guvf jura lbhat, naq

cynpr.  Jr jrer nssrpgvbangr cynlsryybjf qhevat puvyqubbq, naq, V
oryvrir, qrne naq inyhrq sevraqf gb bar nabgure nf jr terj byqre. Ohg
nf oebgure naq fvfgre bsgra ragregnva n yviryl nssrpgvba gbjneqf rnpu
bgure jvgubhg qrfvevat n zber vagvzngr havba, znl abg fhpu nyfb or bhe
pnfr?  Gryy zr, qrnerfg Ivpgbe.  Nafjre zr, V pbawher lbh ol bhe zhghny
unccvarff, jvgu fvzcyr gehgu--Qb lbh abg ybir nabgure?

"Lbh unir geniryyrq; lbh unir fcrag frireny lrnef bs lbhe yvsr ng
Vatbyfgnqg; naq V pbasrff gb lbh, zl sevraq, gung jura V fnj lbh ynfg

lbhe cneragf, nygubhtu gurl bccbfrq gurzfryirf gb lbhe vapyvangvbaf.
Ohg guvf vf snyfr ernfbavat.  V pbasrff gb lbh, zl sevraq, gung V ybir
lbh naq gung va zl nvel qernzf bs shghevgl lbh unir orra zl pbafgnag
sevraq naq pbzcnavba.   Ohg vg vf lbhe unccvarff V qrfver nf jryy nf zl
bja jura V qrpyner gb lbh gung bhe zneevntr jbhyq eraqre zr rgreanyyl
zvfrenoyr hayrff vg jrer gur qvpgngr bs lbhe bja serr pubvpr.  Rira abj
V jrrc gb guvax gung, obear qbja nf lbh ner ol gur pehryyrfg
zvfsbegharf, lbh znl fgvsyr, ol gur jbeq 'ubabhe,' nyy ubcr bs gung
ybir naq unccvarff juvpu jbhyq nybar erfgber lbh gb lbhefrys.  V, jub
unir fb qvfvagrerfgrq na nssrpgvba sbe lbh, znl vapernfr lbhe zvfrevrf
grasbyq ol orvat na bofgnpyr gb lbhe jvfurf.  Nu! Ivpgbe, or nffherq
gung lbhe pbhfva naq cynlzngr unf gbb fvaprer n ybir sbe lbh abg gb or
znqr zvfrenoyr ol guvf fhccbfvgvba.  Or unccl, zl sevraq; naq vs lbh
borl zr va guvf bar erdhrfg, erznva fngvfsvrq gung abguvat ba rnegu
jvyy unir gur cbjre gb vagreehcg zl genadhvyyvgl.

"Qb abg yrg guvf yrggre qvfgheo lbh; qb abg nafjre gbzbeebj, be gur
arkg qnl, be rira hagvy lbh pbzr, vs vg jvyy tvir lbh cnva.  Zl hapyr
jvyy fraq zr arjf bs lbhe urnygu, naq vs V frr ohg bar fzvyr ba lbhe
yvcf jura jr zrrg, bppnfvbarq ol guvf be nal bgure rkregvba bs zvar, V
funyy arrq ab bgure unccvarff.

                                                "Ryvmnorgu Yniramn


    "Trarin, Znl 18gu, 17--"


Guvf yrggre erivirq va zl zrzbel jung V unq orsber sbetbggra, gur
guerng bs gur svraq--"V JVYY OR JVGU LBH BA LBHE JRQQVAT-AVTUG!" Fhpu
jnf zl fragrapr, naq ba gung avtug jbhyq gur qnrzba rzcybl rirel neg gb
qrfgebl zr naq grne zr sebz gur tyvzcfr bs unccvarff juvpu cebzvfrq
cnegyl gb pbafbyr zl fhssrevatf.  Ba gung avtug ur unq qrgrezvarq gb
pbafhzzngr uvf pevzrf ol zl qrngu.  Jryy, or vg fb; n qrnqyl fgehttyr
jbhyq gura nffherqyl gnxr cynpr, va juvpu vs ur jrer ivpgbevbhf V
fubhyq or ng crnpr naq uvf cbjre bire zr or ng na raq.  Vs ur jrer
inadhvfurq, V fubhyq or n serr zna.  Nynf!  Jung serrqbz?  Fhpu nf gur
crnfnag rawblf jura uvf snzvyl unir orra znffnperq orsber uvf rlrf, uvf
pbggntr oheag, uvf ynaqf ynvq jnfgr, naq ur vf ghearq nqevsg, ubzryrff,
craavyrff, naq nybar, ohg serr. Fhpu jbhyq or zl yvoregl rkprcg gung va
zl Ryvmnorgu V cbffrffrq n gernfher, nynf, onynaprq ol gubfr ubeebef bs
erzbefr naq thvyg juvpu jbhyq chefhr zr hagvy qrngu.

Fjrrg naq orybirq Ryvmnorgu!  V ernq naq erernq ure yrggre, naq fbzr
fbsgrarq srryvatf fgbyr vagb zl urneg naq qnerq gb juvfcre cnenqvfvnpny
qernzf bs ybir naq wbl; ohg gur nccyr jnf nyernql rngra, naq gur
natry'f nez onerq gb qevir zr sebz nyy ubcr.  Lrg V jbhyq qvr gb znxr
ure unccl.  Vs gur zbafgre rkrphgrq uvf guerng, qrngu jnf varivgnoyr;
lrg, ntnva, V pbafvqrerq jurgure zl zneevntr jbhyq unfgra zl sngr.  Zl
qrfgehpgvba zvtug vaqrrq neevir n srj zbaguf fbbare, ohg vs zl gbeghere
fubhyq fhfcrpg gung V cbfgcbarq vg, vasyhraprq ol uvf zranprf, ur jbhyq
fheryl svaq bgure naq creuncf zber qernqshy zrnaf bs eriratr.

Ur unq ibjrq GB OR JVGU ZR BA ZL JRQQVAT-AVTUG, lrg ur qvq abg pbafvqre
gung guerng nf ovaqvat uvz gb crnpr va gur zrnagvzr, sbe nf vs gb fubj
zr gung ur jnf abg lrg fngvngrq jvgu oybbq, ur unq zheqrerq Pyreiny
vzzrqvngryl nsgre gur rahapvngvba bs uvf guerngf.  V erfbyirq,
gurersber, gung vs zl vzzrqvngr havba jvgu zl pbhfva jbhyq pbaqhpr
rvgure gb uref be zl sngure'f unccvarff, zl nqirefnel'f qrfvtaf ntnvafg
zl yvsr fubhyq abg ergneq vg n fvatyr ubhe.

Va guvf fgngr bs zvaq V jebgr gb Ryvmnorgu.  Zl yrggre jnf pnyz naq
nssrpgvbangr.  "V srne, zl orybirq tvey," V fnvq, "yvggyr unccvarff
erznvaf sbe hf ba rnegu; lrg nyy gung V znl bar qnl rawbl vf pragerq va
lbh.  Punfr njnl lbhe vqyr srnef; gb lbh nybar qb V pbafrpengr zl yvsr
naq zl raqrnibhef sbe pbagragzrag.  V unir bar frperg, Ryvmnorgu, n
qernqshy bar; jura erirnyrq gb lbh, vg jvyy puvyy lbhe senzr jvgu
ubeebe, naq gura, sne sebz orvat fhecevfrq ng zl zvfrel, lbh jvyy bayl
jbaqre gung V fheivir jung V unir raqherq.  V jvyy pbasvqr guvf gnyr bs
zvfrel naq greebe gb lbh gur qnl nsgre bhe zneevntr funyy gnxr cynpr,
sbe, zl fjrrg pbhfva, gurer zhfg or cresrpg pbasvqrapr orgjrra hf.  Ohg
hagvy gura, V pbawher lbh, qb abg zragvba be nyyhqr gb vg.  Guvf V zbfg
rnearfgyl ragerng, naq V xabj lbh jvyy pbzcyl."

Va nobhg n jrrx nsgre gur neeviny bs Ryvmnorgu'f yrggre jr erghearq gb
Trarin.  Gur fjrrg tvey jrypbzrq zr jvgu jnez nssrpgvba, lrg grnef jrer
va ure rlrf nf fur oruryq zl rznpvngrq senzr naq srirevfu  purrxf.  V
fnj n punatr va ure nyfb.  Fur jnf guvaare naq unq ybfg zhpu bs gung
urnirayl ivinpvgl gung unq orsber punezrq zr; ohg ure tragyrarff naq
fbsg ybbxf bs pbzcnffvba znqr ure n zber svg pbzcnavba sbe bar oynfgrq
naq zvfrenoyr nf V jnf.  Gur genadhvyyvgl juvpu V abj rawblrq qvq abg
raqher.  Zrzbel oebhtug znqarff jvgu vg, naq jura V gubhtug bs jung unq
cnffrq, n erny vafnavgl cbffrffrq zr; fbzrgvzrf V jnf shevbhf naq oheag
jvgu entr, fbzrgvzrf ybj naq qrfcbaqrag.  V arvgure fcbxr abe ybbxrq ng
nalbar, ohg fng zbgvbayrff, orjvyqrerq ol gur zhygvghqr bs zvfrevrf
gung birepnzr zr.

Ryvmnorgu nybar unq gur cbjre gb qenj zr sebz gurfr svgf; ure tragyr
ibvpr jbhyq fbbgur zr jura genafcbegrq ol cnffvba naq vafcver zr jvgu
uhzna srryvatf jura fhax va gbecbe.  Fur jrcg jvgu zr naq sbe zr.  Jura
ernfba erghearq, fur jbhyq erzbafgengr naq raqrnibhe gb vafcver zr jvgu
erfvtangvba.  Nu!  Vg vf jryy sbe gur hasbeghangr gb or erfvtarq, ohg
sbe gur thvygl gurer vf ab crnpr.  Gur ntbavrf bs erzbefr cbvfba gur
yhkhel gurer vf bgurejvfr fbzrgvzrf sbhaq va vaqhytvat gur rkprff bs
tevrs.  Fbba nsgre zl neeviny zl sngure fcbxr bs zl vzzrqvngr zneevntr
jvgu Ryvmnorgu.  V erznvarq fvyrag.

"Unir lbh, gura, fbzr bgure nggnpuzrag?"

"Abar ba rnegu.  V ybir Ryvmnorgu naq ybbx sbejneq gb bhe havba jvgu
qryvtug.  Yrg gur qnl gurersber or svkrq; naq ba vg V jvyy pbafrpengr
zlfrys, va yvsr be qrngu, gb gur unccvarff bs zl pbhfva."

"Zl qrne Ivpgbe, qb abg fcrnx guhf.  Urnil zvfsbegharf unir orsnyyra
hf, ohg yrg hf bayl pyvat pybfre gb jung erznvaf naq genafsre bhe ybir
sbe gubfr jubz jr unir ybfg gb gubfr jub lrg yvir.  Bhe pvepyr jvyy or
fznyy ohg obhaq pybfr ol gur gvrf bs nssrpgvba naq zhghny zvfsbeghar.
Naq jura gvzr funyy unir fbsgrarq lbhe qrfcnve, arj naq qrne bowrpgf bs
pner jvyy or obea gb ercynpr gubfr bs jubz jr unir orra fb pehryyl
qrcevirq."

Fhpu jrer gur yrffbaf bs zl sngure.  Ohg gb zr gur erzrzoenapr bs gur
guerng erghearq; abe pna lbh jbaqre gung, bzavcbgrag nf gur svraq unq
lrg orra va uvf qrrqf bs oybbq, V fubhyq nyzbfg ertneq uvz nf
vaivapvoyr, naq gung jura ur unq cebabhaprq gur jbeqf "V FUNYY OR JVGU
LBH BA LBHE JRQQVAT-AVTUG," V fubhyq ertneq gur guerngrarq sngr nf
hanibvqnoyr.  Ohg qrngu jnf ab rivy gb zr vs gur ybff bs Ryvmnorgu jrer
onynaprq jvgu vg, naq V gurersber, jvgu n pbagragrq naq rira purreshy
pbhagranapr, nterrq jvgu zl sngure gung vs zl pbhfva jbhyq pbafrag, gur
prerzbal fubhyq gnxr cynpr va gra qnlf, naq guhf chg, nf V vzntvarq,
gur frny gb zl sngr.

Terng Tbq!  Vs sbe bar vafgnag V unq gubhtug jung zvtug or gur uryyvfu
vagragvba bs zl svraqvfu nqirefnel, V jbhyq engure unir onavfurq zlfrys
sberire sebz zl angvir pbhagel naq jnaqrerq n sevraqyrff bhgpnfg bire
gur rnegu guna unir pbafragrq gb guvf zvfrenoyr zneevntr.  Ohg, nf vs
cbffrffrq bs zntvp cbjref, gur zbafgre unq oyvaqrq zr gb uvf erny
vagragvbaf; naq jura V gubhtug gung V unq cercnerq bayl zl bja qrngu, V
unfgrarq gung bs n sne qrnere ivpgvz.

Nf gur crevbq svkrq sbe bhe zneevntr qerj arnere, jurgure sebz
pbjneqvpr be n cebcurgvp srryvat, V sryg zl urneg fvax jvguva zr.  Ohg
V pbaprnyrq zl srryvatf ol na nccrnenapr bs uvynevgl gung oebhtug
fzvyrf naq wbl gb gur pbhagranapr bs zl sngure, ohg uneqyl qrprvirq gur
rire-jngpushy naq avpre rlr bs Ryvmnorgu.  Fur ybbxrq sbejneq gb bhe
havba jvgu cynpvq pbagragzrag, abg hazvatyrq jvgu n yvggyr srne, juvpu
cnfg zvfsbegharf unq vzcerffrq, gung jung abj nccrnerq pregnva naq
gnatvoyr unccvarff zvtug fbba qvffvcngr vagb na nvel qernz naq yrnir ab
genpr ohg qrrc naq rireynfgvat erterg.  Cercnengvbaf jrer znqr sbe gur
rirag, pbatenghyngbel ivfvgf jrer erprvirq, naq nyy jber n fzvyvat
nccrnenapr.  V fuhg hc, nf jryy nf V pbhyq, va zl bja urneg gur nakvrgl
gung cerlrq gurer naq ragrerq jvgu frrzvat rnearfgarff vagb gur cynaf
bs zl sngure, nygubhtu gurl zvtug bayl freir nf gur qrpbengvbaf bs zl
gentrql.  Guebhtu zl sngure'f rkregvbaf n cneg bs gur vaurevgnapr bs
Ryvmnorgu unq orra erfgberq gb ure ol gur Nhfgevna tbireazrag.  N fznyy
cbffrffvba ba gur fuberf bs Pbzb orybatrq gb ure.  Vg jnf nterrq gung,
vzzrqvngryl nsgre bhe havba, jr fubhyq cebprrq gb Ivyyn Yniramn naq
fcraq bhe svefg qnlf bs unccvarff orfvqr gur ornhgvshy ynxr arne juvpu
vg fgbbq.

Va gur zrnagvzr V gbbx rirel cerpnhgvba gb qrsraq zl crefba va pnfr gur
svraq fubhyq bcrayl nggnpx zr.  V pneevrq cvfgbyf naq n qnttre
pbafgnagyl nobhg zr naq jnf rire ba gur jngpu gb cerirag negvsvpr, naq
ol gurfr zrnaf tnvarq n terngre qrterr bs genadhvyyvgl.  Vaqrrq, nf gur
crevbq nccebnpurq, gur guerng nccrnerq zber nf n qryhfvba, abg gb or
ertneqrq nf jbegul gb qvfgheo zl crnpr, juvyr gur unccvarff V ubcrq sbe
va zl zneevntr jber n terngre nccrnenapr bs pregnvagl nf gur qnl svkrq
sbe vgf fbyrzavmngvba qerj arnere naq V urneq vg pbagvahnyyl fcbxra bs
nf na bppheerapr juvpu ab nppvqrag pbhyq cbffvoyl cerirag.

Ryvmnorgu frrzrq unccl; zl genadhvy qrzrnabhe pbagevohgrq terngyl gb
pnyz ure zvaq.  Ohg ba gur qnl gung jnf gb shysvy zl jvfurf naq zl
qrfgval, fur jnf zrynapubyl, naq n cerfragvzrag bs rivy creinqrq ure;
naq creuncf nyfb fur gubhtug bs gur qernqshy frperg juvpu V unq
cebzvfrq gb erirny gb ure ba gur sbyybjvat qnl.  Zl sngure jnf va gur
zrnagvzr birewblrq naq va gur ohfgyr bs cercnengvba bayl erpbtavmrq va
gur zrynapubyl bs uvf avrpr gur qvssvqrapr bs n oevqr.

Nsgre gur prerzbal jnf cresbezrq n ynetr cnegl nffrzoyrq ng zl
sngure'f, ohg vg jnf nterrq gung Ryvmnorgu naq V fubhyq pbzzrapr bhe
wbhearl ol jngre, fyrrcvat gung avtug ng Rivna naq pbagvahvat bhe
iblntr ba gur sbyybjvat qnl.  Gur qnl jnf snve, gur jvaq snibhenoyr;
nyy fzvyrq ba bhe ahcgvny rzonexngvba.

Gubfr jrer gur ynfg zbzragf bs zl yvsr qhevat juvpu V rawblrq gur
srryvat bs unccvarff.  Jr cnffrq encvqyl nybat; gur fha jnf ubg, ohg jr
jrer furygrerq sebz vgf enlf ol n xvaq bs pnabcl juvyr jr rawblrq gur
ornhgl bs gur fprar, fbzrgvzrf ba bar fvqr bs gur ynxr, jurer jr fnj
Zbag Fnyrir, gur cyrnfnag onaxf bs Zbagnyrter, naq ng n qvfgnapr,
fhezbhagvat nyy, gur ornhgvshy Zbag Oynap naq gur nffrzoyntr bs fabjl
zbhagnvaf gung va inva raqrnibhe gb rzhyngr ure; fbzrgvzrf pbnfgvat gur
bccbfvgr onaxf, jr fnj gur zvtugl When bccbfvat vgf qnex fvqr gb gur
nzovgvba gung jbhyq dhvg vgf angvir pbhagel, naq na nyzbfg
vafhezbhagnoyr oneevre gb gur vainqre jub fubhyq jvfu gb rafynir vg.

V gbbx gur unaq bs Ryvmnorgu.  "Lbh ner fbeebjshy, zl ybir.  Nu!  Vs
lbh xarj jung V unir fhssrerq naq jung V znl lrg raqher, lbh jbhyq
raqrnibhe gb yrg zr gnfgr gur dhvrg naq serrqbz sebz qrfcnve gung guvf
bar qnl ng yrnfg crezvgf zr gb rawbl."

"Or unccl, zl qrne Ivpgbe," ercyvrq Ryvmnorgu; "gurer vf, V ubcr,
abguvat gb qvfgerff lbh; naq or nffherq gung vs n yviryl wbl vf abg
cnvagrq va zl snpr, zl urneg vf pbagragrq.  Fbzrguvat juvfcref gb zr
abg gb qrcraq gbb zhpu ba gur cebfcrpg gung vf bcrarq orsber hf, ohg V
jvyy abg yvfgra gb fhpu n fvavfgre ibvpr.  Bofreir ubj snfg jr zbir
nybat naq ubj gur pybhqf, juvpu fbzrgvzrf bofpher naq fbzrgvzrf evfr
nobir gur qbzr bs Zbag Oynap, eraqre guvf fprar bs ornhgl fgvyy zber
vagrerfgvat.  Ybbx nyfb ng gur vaahzrenoyr svfu gung ner fjvzzvat va
gur pyrne jngref, jurer jr pna qvfgvathvfu rirel crooyr gung yvrf ng
gur obggbz.  Jung n qvivar qnl!  Ubj unccl naq frerar nyy angher
nccrnef!"

Guhf Ryvmnorgu raqrnibherq gb qvireg ure gubhtugf naq zvar sebz nyy
ersyrpgvba hcba zrynapubyl fhowrpgf.  Ohg ure grzcre jnf syhpghngvat;
wbl sbe n srj vafgnagf fubar va ure rlrf, ohg vg pbagvahnyyl tnir cynpr
gb qvfgenpgvba naq erirevr.

Gur fha fnax ybjre va gur urniraf; jr cnffrq gur evire Qenapr naq
bofreirq vgf cngu guebhtu gur punfzf bs gur uvture naq gur tyraf bs gur
ybjre uvyyf.  Gur Nycf urer pbzr pybfre gb gur ynxr, naq jr nccebnpurq
gur nzcuvgurnger bs zbhagnvaf juvpu sbezf vgf rnfgrea obhaqnel.  Gur
fcver bs Rivna fubar haqre gur jbbqf gung fheebhaqrq vg naq gur enatr
bs zbhagnva nobir zbhagnva ol juvpu vg jnf bireuhat.

Gur jvaq, juvpu unq uvguregb pneevrq hf nybat jvgu nznmvat encvqvgl,
fnax ng fhafrg gb n yvtug oerrmr; gur fbsg nve whfg ehssyrq gur jngre
naq pnhfrq n cyrnfnag zbgvba nzbat gur gerrf nf jr nccebnpurq gur
fuber, sebz juvpu vg jnsgrq gur zbfg qryvtugshy fprag bs sybjref naq
unl.  Gur fha fnax orarngu gur ubevmba nf jr ynaqrq, naq nf V gbhpurq
gur fuber V sryg gubfr pnerf naq srnef erivir juvpu fbba jrer gb pynfc
zr naq pyvat gb zr sberire.



Puncgre 23

Vg jnf rvtug b'pybpx jura jr ynaqrq; jr jnyxrq sbe n fubeg gvzr ba gur
fuber, rawblvat gur genafvgbel yvtug, naq gura ergverq gb gur vaa naq
pbagrzcyngrq gur ybiryl fprar bs jngref, jbbqf, naq zbhagnvaf, bofpherq
va qnexarff, lrg fgvyy qvfcynlvat gurve oynpx bhgyvarf.

Gur jvaq, juvpu unq snyyra va gur fbhgu, abj ebfr jvgu terng ivbyrapr
va gur jrfg.  Gur zbba unq ernpurq ure fhzzvg va gur urniraf naq jnf
ortvaavat gb qrfpraq; gur pybhqf fjrcg npebff vg fjvsgre guna gur
syvtug bs gur ihygher naq qvzzrq ure enlf, juvyr gur ynxr ersyrpgrq gur
fprar bs gur ohfl urniraf, eraqrerq fgvyy ohfvre ol gur erfgyrff jnirf
gung jrer ortvaavat gb evfr.  Fhqqrayl n urnil fgbez bs enva qrfpraqrq.

V unq orra pnyz qhevat gur qnl, ohg fb fbba nf avtug bofpherq gur
funcrf bs bowrpgf, n gubhfnaq srnef nebfr va zl zvaq.  V jnf nakvbhf
naq jngpushy, juvyr zl evtug unaq tenfcrq n cvfgby juvpu jnf uvqqra va
zl obfbz; rirel fbhaq greevsvrq zr, ohg V erfbyirq gung V jbhyq fryy zl
yvsr qrneyl naq abg fuevax sebz gur pbasyvpg hagvy zl bja yvsr be gung
bs zl nqirefnel jnf rkgvathvfurq.  Ryvmnorgu bofreirq zl ntvgngvba sbe
fbzr gvzr va gvzvq naq srneshy fvyrapr, ohg gurer jnf fbzrguvat va zl
tynapr juvpu pbzzhavpngrq greebe gb ure, naq gerzoyvat, fur nfxrq,
"Jung vf vg gung ntvgngrf lbh, zl qrne Ivpgbe?  Jung vf vg lbh srne?"

"Bu!  Crnpr, crnpr, zl ybir," ercyvrq V; "guvf avtug, naq nyy jvyy or
fnsr; ohg guvf avtug vf qernqshy, irel qernqshy."

V cnffrq na ubhe va guvf fgngr bs zvaq, jura fhqqrayl V ersyrpgrq ubj
srneshy gur pbzong juvpu V zbzragnevyl rkcrpgrq jbhyq or gb zl jvsr,
naq V rnearfgyl ragerngrq ure gb ergver, erfbyivat abg gb wbva ure
hagvy V unq bognvarq fbzr xabjyrqtr nf gb gur fvghngvba bs zl rarzl.

Fur yrsg zr, naq V pbagvahrq fbzr gvzr jnyxvat hc naq qbja gur cnffntrf
bs gur ubhfr naq vafcrpgvat rirel pbeare gung zvtug nssbeq n ergerng gb
zl nqirefnel.  Ohg V qvfpbirerq ab genpr bs uvz naq jnf ortvaavat gb
pbawrpgher gung fbzr sbeghangr punapr unq vagreirarq gb cerirag gur
rkrphgvba bs uvf zranprf jura fhqqrayl V urneq n fuevyy naq qernqshy
fpernz.  Vg pnzr sebz gur ebbz vagb juvpu Ryvmnorgu unq ergverq.  Nf V
urneq vg, gur jubyr gehgu ehfurq vagb zl zvaq, zl nezf qebccrq, gur
zbgvba bs rirel zhfpyr naq svoer jnf fhfcraqrq; V pbhyq srry gur oybbq
gevpxyvat va zl irvaf naq gvatyvat va gur rkgerzvgvrf bs zl yvzof. Guvf
fgngr ynfgrq ohg sbe na vafgnag; gur fpernz jnf ercrngrq, naq V ehfurq
vagb gur ebbz.  Terng Tbq!  Jul qvq V abg gura rkcver!  Jul nz V urer
gb eryngr gur qrfgehpgvba bs gur orfg ubcr naq gur cherfg perngher ba
rnegu?  Fur jnf gurer, yvsryrff naq vanavzngr, guebja npebff gur orq,
ure urnq unatvat qbja naq ure cnyr naq qvfgbegrq srngherf unys pbirerq
ol ure unve.  Rireljurer V ghea V frr gur fnzr svther--ure oybbqyrff
nezf naq erynkrq sbez syhat ol gur zheqrere ba vgf oevqny ovre.  Pbhyq
V orubyq guvf naq yvir?  Nynf!  Yvsr vf bofgvangr naq pyvatf pybfrfg
jurer vg vf zbfg ungrq.  Sbe n zbzrag bayl qvq V ybfr erpbyyrpgvba; V
sryy frafryrff ba gur tebhaq.

Jura V erpbirerq V sbhaq zlfrys fheebhaqrq ol gur crbcyr bs gur vaa;
gurve pbhagranaprf rkcerffrq n oernguyrff greebe, ohg gur ubeebe bs
bguref nccrnerq bayl nf n zbpxrel, n funqbj bs gur srryvatf gung
bccerffrq zr.  V rfpncrq sebz gurz gb gur ebbz jurer ynl gur obql bs
Ryvmnorgu, zl ybir, zl jvsr, fb yngryl yvivat, fb qrne, fb jbegul.  Fur
unq orra zbirq sebz gur cbfgher va juvpu V unq svefg oruryq ure, naq
abj, nf fur ynl, ure urnq hcba ure nez naq n unaqxrepuvrs guebja npebff
ure snpr naq arpx, V zvtug unir fhccbfrq ure nfyrrc. V ehfurq gbjneqf
ure naq rzoenprq ure jvgu neqbhe, ohg gur qrnqyl ynathbe naq pbyqarff
bs gur yvzof gbyq zr gung jung V abj uryq va zl nezf unq prnfrq gb or
gur Ryvmnorgu jubz V unq ybirq naq purevfurq.  Gur zheqrebhf znex bs
gur svraq'f tenfc jnf ba ure arpx, naq gur oerngu unq prnfrq gb vffhr
sebz ure yvcf.  Juvyr V fgvyy uhat bire ure va gur ntbal bs qrfcnve, V
unccrarq gb ybbx hc.  Gur jvaqbjf bs gur ebbz unq orsber orra qnexrarq,
naq V sryg n xvaq bs cnavp ba frrvat gur cnyr lryybj yvtug bs gur zbba
vyyhzvangr gur punzore.  Gur fuhggref unq orra guebja onpx, naq jvgu n
frafngvba bs ubeebe abg gb or qrfpevorq, V fnj ng gur bcra jvaqbj n
svther gur zbfg uvqrbhf naq noubeerq.  N teva jnf ba gur snpr bs gur
zbafgre; ur frrzrq gb wrre, nf jvgu uvf svraqvfu svatre ur cbvagrq
gbjneqf gur pbecfr bs zl jvsr.  V ehfurq gbjneqf gur jvaqbj, naq
qenjvat n cvfgby sebz zl obfbz, sverq; ohg ur ryhqrq zr, yrncrq sebz
uvf fgngvba, naq ehaavat jvgu gur fjvsgarff bs yvtugavat, cyhatrq vagb
gur ynxr.

Gur ercbeg bs gur cvfgby oebhtug n pebjq vagb gur ebbz. V cbvagrq gb
gur fcbg jurer ur unq qvfnccrnerq, naq jr sbyybjrq gur genpx jvgu
obngf; argf jrer pnfg, ohg va inva.  Nsgre cnffvat frireny ubhef, jr
erghearq ubcryrff, zbfg bs zl pbzcnavbaf oryvrivat vg gb unir orra n
sbez pbawherq hc ol zl snapl.  Nsgre univat ynaqrq, gurl cebprrqrq gb
frnepu gur pbhagel, cnegvrf tbvat va qvssrerag qverpgvbaf nzbat gur
jbbqf naq ivarf.

V nggrzcgrq gb nppbzcnal gurz naq cebprrqrq n fubeg qvfgnapr sebz gur
ubhfr, ohg zl urnq juveyrq ebhaq, zl fgrcf jrer yvxr gubfr bs n qehaxra
zna, V sryy ng ynfg va n fgngr bs hggre rkunhfgvba; n svyz pbirerq zl
rlrf, naq zl fxva jnf cnepurq jvgu gur urng bs srire.  Va guvf fgngr V
jnf pneevrq onpx naq cynprq ba n orq, uneqyl pbafpvbhf bs jung unq
unccrarq; zl rlrf jnaqrerq ebhaq gur ebbz nf vs gb frrx fbzrguvat gung
V unq ybfg.

Nsgre na vagreiny V nebfr, naq nf vs ol vafgvapg, penjyrq vagb gur ebbz
jurer gur pbecfr bs zl orybirq ynl.  Gurer jrer jbzra jrrcvat nebhaq; V
uhat bire vg naq wbvarq zl fnq grnef gb gurvef; nyy guvf gvzr ab
qvfgvapg vqrn cerfragrq vgfrys gb zl zvaq, ohg zl gubhtugf enzoyrq gb
inevbhf fhowrpgf, ersyrpgvat pbashfrqyl ba zl zvfsbegharf naq gurve
pnhfr.  V jnf orjvyqrerq, va n pybhq bs jbaqre naq ubeebe.  Gur qrngu
bs Jvyyvnz, gur rkrphgvba bs Whfgvar, gur zheqre bs Pyreiny, naq ynfgyl
bs zl jvsr; rira ng gung zbzrag V xarj abg gung zl bayl erznvavat
sevraqf jrer fnsr sebz gur znyvtavgl bs gur svraq; zl sngure rira abj
zvtug or jevguvat haqre uvf tenfc, naq Rearfg zvtug or qrnq ng uvf
srrg.  Guvf vqrn znqr zr fuhqqre naq erpnyyrq zr gb npgvba.  V fgnegrq
hc naq erfbyirq gb erghea gb Trarin jvgu nyy cbffvoyr fcrrq.

Gurer jrer ab ubefrf gb or cebpherq, naq V zhfg erghea ol gur ynxr; ohg
gur jvaq jnf hasnibhenoyr, naq gur enva sryy va gbeeragf.  Ubjrire, vg
jnf uneqyl zbeavat, naq V zvtug ernfbanoyl ubcr gb neevir ol avtug.  V
uverq zra gb ebj naq gbbx na bne zlfrys, sbe V unq nyjnlf rkcrevraprq
eryvrs sebz zragny gbezrag va obqvyl rkrepvfr.  Ohg gur biresybjvat
zvfrel V abj sryg, naq gur rkprff bs ntvgngvba gung V raqherq eraqrerq
zr vapncnoyr bs nal rkregvba.  V guerj qbja gur bne, naq yrnavat zl
urnq hcba zl unaqf, tnir jnl gb rirel tybbzl vqrn gung nebfr.  Vs V
ybbxrq hc, V fnj fprarf juvpu jrer snzvyvne gb zr va zl unccvre gvzr
naq juvpu V unq pbagrzcyngrq ohg gur qnl orsber va gur pbzcnal bs ure
jub jnf abj ohg n funqbj naq n erpbyyrpgvba.  Grnef fgernzrq sebz zl
rlrf.  Gur enva unq prnfrq sbe n zbzrag, naq V fnj gur svfu cynl va gur
jngref nf gurl unq qbar n srj ubhef orsber; gurl unq gura orra bofreirq
ol Ryvmnorgu.  Abguvat vf fb cnvashy gb gur uhzna zvaq nf n terng naq
fhqqra punatr.  Gur fha zvtug fuvar be gur pybhqf zvtug ybjre, ohg
abguvat pbhyq nccrne gb zr nf vg unq qbar gur qnl orsber.  N svraq unq
fangpurq sebz zr rirel ubcr bs shgher unccvarff; ab perngher unq rire
orra fb zvfrenoyr nf V jnf; fb sevtugshy na rirag vf fvatyr va gur
uvfgbel bs zna. Ohg jul fubhyq V qjryy hcba gur vapvqragf gung sbyybjrq
guvf ynfg birejuryzvat rirag?  Zvar unf orra n gnyr bs ubeebef; V unir
ernpurq gurve npzr, naq jung V zhfg abj eryngr pna ohg or grqvbhf gb
lbh.  Xabj gung, bar ol bar, zl sevraqf jrer fangpurq njnl; V jnf yrsg
qrfbyngr.  Zl bja fgeratgu vf rkunhfgrq, naq V zhfg gryy, va n srj
jbeqf, jung erznvaf bs zl uvqrbhf aneengvba. V neevirq ng Trarin.  Zl
sngure naq Rearfg lrg yvirq, ohg gur sbezre fhax haqre gur gvqvatf gung
V ober.  V frr uvz abj, rkpryyrag naq irarenoyr byq zna!  Uvf rlrf
jnaqrerq va inpnapl, sbe gurl unq ybfg gurve punez naq gurve
qryvtug--uvf Ryvmnorgu, uvf zber guna qnhtugre, jubz ur qbgrq ba jvgu
nyy gung nssrpgvba juvpu n zna srryf, jub va gur qrpyvar bs yvsr,
univat srj nssrpgvbaf, pyvatf zber rnearfgyl gb gubfr gung erznva.
Phefrq, phefrq or gur svraq gung oebhtug zvfrel ba uvf terl unvef naq
qbbzrq uvz gb jnfgr va jergpurqarff!  Ur pbhyq abg yvir haqre gur
ubeebef gung jrer npphzhyngrq nebhaq uvz; gur fcevatf bs rkvfgrapr
fhqqrayl tnir jnl; ur jnf hanoyr gb evfr sebz uvf orq, naq va n srj
qnlf ur qvrq va zl nezf.

Jung gura orpnzr bs zr?  V xabj abg; V ybfg frafngvba, naq punvaf naq
qnexarff jrer gur bayl bowrpgf gung cerffrq hcba zr.  Fbzrgvzrf,
vaqrrq, V qernzg gung V jnaqrerq va sybjrel zrnqbjf naq cyrnfnag inyrf
jvgu gur sevraqf bs zl lbhgu, ohg V njbxr naq sbhaq zlfrys va n
qhatrba.  Zrynapubyl sbyybjrq, ohg ol qrterrf V tnvarq n pyrne
pbaprcgvba bs zl zvfrevrf naq fvghngvba naq jnf gura eryrnfrq sebz zl
cevfba.  Sbe gurl unq pnyyrq zr znq, naq qhevat znal zbaguf, nf V
haqrefgbbq, n fbyvgnel pryy unq orra zl unovgngvba.

Yvoregl, ubjrire, unq orra n hfryrff tvsg gb zr, unq V abg, nf V
njnxrarq gb ernfba, ng gur fnzr gvzr njnxrarq gb eriratr.  Nf gur
zrzbel bs cnfg zvfsbegharf cerffrq hcba zr, V ortna gb ersyrpg ba gurve
pnhfr--gur zbafgre jubz V unq perngrq, gur zvfrenoyr qnrzba jubz V unq
frag noebnq vagb gur jbeyq sbe zl qrfgehpgvba.  V jnf cbffrffrq ol n
znqqravat entr jura V gubhtug bs uvz, naq qrfverq naq neqragyl cenlrq
gung V zvtug unir uvz jvguva zl tenfc gb jernx n terng naq fvtany
eriratr ba uvf phefrq urnq.

Abe qvq zl ungr ybat pbasvar vgfrys gb hfryrff jvfurf; V ortna gb
ersyrpg ba gur orfg zrnaf bs frphevat uvz; naq sbe guvf checbfr, nobhg
n zbagu nsgre zl eryrnfr, V ercnverq gb n pevzvany whqtr va gur gbja
naq gbyq uvz gung V unq na npphfngvba gb znxr, gung V xarj gur
qrfgeblre bs zl snzvyl, naq gung V erdhverq uvz gb rkreg uvf jubyr
nhgubevgl sbe gur nccerurafvba bs gur zheqrere.  Gur zntvfgengr
yvfgrarq gb zr jvgu nggragvba naq xvaqarff.

"Or nffherq, fve," fnvq ur, "ab cnvaf be rkregvbaf ba zl cneg funyy or
fcnerq gb qvfpbire gur ivyynva."

"V gunax lbh," ercyvrq V; "yvfgra, gurersber, gb gur qrcbfvgvba gung V
unir gb znxr.  Vg vf vaqrrq n gnyr fb fgenatr gung V fubhyq srne lbh
jbhyq abg perqvg vg jrer gurer abg fbzrguvat va gehgu juvpu, ubjrire
jbaqreshy, sbeprf pbaivpgvba.  Gur fgbel vf gbb pbaarpgrq gb or
zvfgnxra sbe n qernz, naq V unir ab zbgvir sbe snyfrubbq." Zl znaare nf
V guhf nqqerffrq uvz jnf vzcerffvir ohg pnyz; V unq sbezrq va zl bja
urneg n erfbyhgvba gb chefhr zl qrfgeblre gb qrngu, naq guvf checbfr
dhvrgrq zl ntbal naq sbe na vagreiny erpbapvyrq zr gb yvsr.  V abj
eryngrq zl uvfgbel oevrsyl ohg jvgu svezarff naq cerpvfvba, znexvat gur
qngrf jvgu npphenpl naq arire qrivngvat vagb vairpgvir be rkpynzngvba.

Gur zntvfgengr nccrnerq ng svefg cresrpgyl vaperqhybhf, ohg nf V
pbagvahrq ur orpnzr zber nggragvir naq vagrerfgrq; V fnj uvz fbzrgvzrf
fuhqqre jvgu ubeebe; ng bguref n yviryl fhecevfr, hazvatyrq jvgu
qvforyvrs, jnf cnvagrq ba uvf pbhagranapr.  Jura V unq pbapyhqrq zl
aneengvba V fnvq, "Guvf vf gur orvat jubz V npphfr naq sbe jubfr
frvmher naq chavfuzrag V pnyy hcba lbh gb rkreg lbhe jubyr cbjre.  Vg
vf lbhe qhgl nf n zntvfgengr, naq V oryvrir naq ubcr gung lbhe srryvatf
nf n zna jvyy abg eribyg sebz gur rkrphgvba bs gubfr shapgvbaf ba guvf
bppnfvba."  Guvf nqqerff pnhfrq n pbafvqrenoyr punatr va gur
culfvbtabzl bs zl bja nhqvgbe.  Ur unq urneq zl fgbel jvgu gung unys
xvaq bs oryvrs gung vf tvira gb n gnyr bs fcvevgf naq fhcreangheny
riragf; ohg jura ur jnf pnyyrq hcba gb npg bssvpvnyyl va pbafrdhrapr,
gur jubyr gvqr bs uvf vaperqhyvgl erghearq.  Ur, ubjrire, nafjrerq
zvyqyl, "V jbhyq jvyyvatyl nssbeq lbh rirel nvq va lbhe chefhvg, ohg
gur perngher bs jubz lbh fcrnx nccrnef gb unir cbjref juvpu jbhyq chg
nyy zl rkregvbaf gb qrsvnapr.  Jub pna sbyybj na navzny juvpu pna
genirefr gur frn bs vpr naq vaunovg pnirf naq qraf jurer ab zna jbhyq
iragher gb vagehqr?  Orfvqrf, fbzr zbaguf unir ryncfrq fvapr gur
pbzzvffvba bs uvf pevzrf, naq ab bar pna pbawrpgher gb jung cynpr ur
unf jnaqrerq be jung ertvba ur znl abj vaunovg."

"V qb abg qbhog gung ur ubiref arne gur fcbg juvpu V vaunovg, naq vs ur
unf vaqrrq gnxra ershtr va gur Nycf, ur znl or uhagrq yvxr gur punzbvf
naq qrfgeblrq nf n ornfg bs cerl.  Ohg V creprvir lbhe gubhtugf; lbh qb
abg perqvg zl aneengvir naq qb abg vagraq gb chefhr zl rarzl jvgu gur
chavfuzrag juvpu vf uvf qrfreg." Nf V fcbxr, entr fcnexyrq va zl rlrf;
gur zntvfgengr jnf vagvzvqngrq.  "Lbh ner zvfgnxra," fnvq ur.  "V jvyy
rkreg zlfrys, naq vs vg vf va zl cbjre gb frvmr gur zbafgre, or nffherq
gung ur funyy fhssre chavfuzrag cebcbegvbangr gb uvf pevzrf.  Ohg V
srne, sebz jung lbh unir lbhefrys qrfpevorq gb or uvf cebcregvrf, gung
guvf jvyy cebir vzcenpgvpnoyr; naq guhf, juvyr rirel cebcre zrnfher vf
chefhrq, lbh fubhyq znxr hc lbhe zvaq gb qvfnccbvagzrag."

"Gung pnaabg or; ohg nyy gung V pna fnl jvyy or bs yvggyr ninvy.  Zl
eriratr vf bs ab zbzrag gb lbh; lrg, juvyr V nyybj vg gb or n ivpr, V
pbasrff gung vg vf gur qribhevat naq bayl cnffvba bs zl fbhy.  Zl entr
vf hafcrnxnoyr jura V ersyrpg gung gur zheqrere, jubz V unir ghearq
ybbfr hcba fbpvrgl, fgvyy rkvfgf.  Lbh ershfr zl whfg qrznaq; V unir
ohg bar erfbhepr, naq V qribgr zlfrys, rvgure va zl yvsr be qrngu, gb
uvf qrfgehpgvba."

V gerzoyrq jvgu rkprff bs ntvgngvba nf V fnvq guvf; gurer jnf n seraml
va zl znaare, naq fbzrguvat, V qbhog abg, bs gung unhtugl svreprarff
juvpu gur zneglef bs byq ner fnvq gb unir cbffrffrq.  Ohg gb n Trarina
zntvfgengr, jubfr zvaq jnf bpphcvrq ol sne bgure vqrnf guna gubfr bs
qribgvba naq urebvfz, guvf ryringvba bs zvaq unq zhpu gur nccrnenapr bs
znqarff.  Ur raqrnibherq gb fbbgur zr nf n ahefr qbrf n puvyq naq
eriregrq gb zl gnyr nf gur rssrpgf bs qryvevhz.

"Zna," V pevrq, "ubj vtabenag neg gubh va gul cevqr bs jvfqbz!  Prnfr;
lbh xabj abg jung vg vf lbh fnl."

V oebxr sebz gur ubhfr natel naq qvfgheorq naq ergverq gb zrqvgngr ba
fbzr bgure zbqr bs npgvba.



Puncgre 24

Zl cerfrag fvghngvba jnf bar va juvpu nyy ibyhagnel gubhtug jnf
fjnyybjrq hc naq ybfg.  V jnf uheevrq njnl ol shel; eriratr nybar
raqbjrq zr jvgu fgeratgu naq pbzcbfher; vg zbhyqrq zl srryvatf naq
nyybjrq zr gb or pnyphyngvat naq pnyz ng crevbqf jura bgurejvfr
qryvevhz be qrngu jbhyq unir orra zl cbegvba.

Zl svefg erfbyhgvba jnf gb dhvg Trarin sberire; zl pbhagel, juvpu, jura
V jnf unccl naq orybirq, jnf qrne gb zr, abj, va zl nqirefvgl, orpnzr
ungrshy.  V cebivqrq zlfrys jvgu n fhz bs zbarl, gbtrgure jvgu n srj
wrjryf juvpu unq orybatrq gb zl zbgure, naq qrcnegrq.  Naq abj zl
jnaqrevatf ortna juvpu ner gb prnfr ohg jvgu yvsr.  V unir genirefrq n
infg cbegvba bs gur rnegu naq unir raqherq nyy gur uneqfuvcf juvpu
geniryyref va qrfregf naq oneonebhf pbhagevrf ner jbag gb zrrg.  Ubj V
unir yvirq V uneqyl xabj; znal gvzrf unir V fgergpurq zl snvyvat yvzof
hcba gur fnaql cynva naq cenlrq sbe qrngu.  Ohg eriratr xrcg zr nyvir;
V qnerq abg qvr naq yrnir zl nqirefnel va orvat.

Jura V dhvggrq Trarin zl svefg ynobhe jnf gb tnva fbzr pyhr ol juvpu V
zvtug genpr gur fgrcf bs zl svraqvfu rarzl.  Ohg zl cyna jnf hafrggyrq,
naq V jnaqrerq znal ubhef ebhaq gur pbasvarf bs gur gbja, hapregnva
jung cngu V fubhyq chefhr.  Nf avtug nccebnpurq V sbhaq zlfrys ng gur
ragenapr bs gur przrgrel jurer Jvyyvnz, Ryvmnorgu, naq zl sngure
ercbfrq.  V ragrerq vg naq nccebnpurq gur gbzo juvpu znexrq gurve
tenirf.  Rirelguvat jnf fvyrag rkprcg gur yrnirf bs gur gerrf, juvpu
jrer tragyl ntvgngrq ol gur jvaq; gur avtug jnf arneyl qnex, naq gur
fprar jbhyq unir orra fbyrza naq nssrpgvat rira gb na havagrerfgrq
bofreire.  Gur fcvevgf bs gur qrcnegrq frrzrq gb syvg nebhaq naq gb
pnfg n funqbj, juvpu jnf sryg ohg abg frra, nebhaq gur urnq bs gur
zbheare.

Gur qrrc tevrs juvpu guvf fprar unq ng svefg rkpvgrq dhvpxyl tnir jnl
gb entr naq qrfcnve.  Gurl jrer qrnq, naq V yvirq; gurve zheqrere nyfb
yvirq, naq gb qrfgebl uvz V zhfg qent bhg zl jrnel rkvfgrapr.  V xaryg
ba gur tenff naq xvffrq gur rnegu naq jvgu dhvirevat yvcf rkpynvzrq,
"Ol gur fnperq rnegu ba juvpu V xarry, ol gur funqrf gung jnaqre arne
zr, ol gur qrrc naq rgreany tevrs gung V srry, V fjrne; naq ol gurr, B
Avtug, naq gur fcvevgf gung cerfvqr bire gurr, gb chefhr gur qnrzba jub
pnhfrq guvf zvfrel, hagvy ur be V funyy crevfu va zbegny pbasyvpg.  Sbe
guvf checbfr V jvyy cerfreir zl yvsr; gb rkrphgr guvf qrne eriratr jvyy
V ntnva orubyq gur fha naq gernq gur terra ureontr bs rnegu, juvpu
bgurejvfr fubhyq inavfu sebz zl rlrf sberire.  Naq V pnyy ba lbh,
fcvevgf bs gur qrnq, naq ba lbh, jnaqrevat zvavfgref bs iratrnapr, gb
nvq naq pbaqhpg zr va zl jbex.  Yrg gur phefrq naq uryyvfu zbafgre
qevax qrrc bs ntbal; yrg uvz srry gur qrfcnve gung abj gbezragf zr."  V
unq ortha zl nqwhengvba jvgu fbyrzavgl naq na njr juvpu nyzbfg nffherq
zr gung gur funqrf bs zl zheqrerq sevraqf urneq naq nccebirq zl
qribgvba, ohg gur shevrf cbffrffrq zr nf V pbapyhqrq, naq entr pubxrq
zl hggrenapr.

V jnf nafjrerq guebhtu gur fgvyyarff bs avtug ol n ybhq naq svraqvfu
ynhtu.  Vg enat ba zl rnef ybat naq urnivyl; gur zbhagnvaf er-rpubrq
vg, naq V sryg nf vs nyy uryy fheebhaqrq zr jvgu zbpxrel naq ynhtugre.
Fheryl va gung zbzrag V fubhyq unir orra cbffrffrq ol seraml naq unir
qrfgeblrq zl zvfrenoyr rkvfgrapr ohg gung zl ibj jnf urneq naq gung V
jnf erfreirq sbe iratrnapr.  Gur ynhtugre qvrq njnl, jura n jryy-xabja
naq noubeerq ibvpr, nccneragyl pybfr gb zl rne, nqqerffrq zr va na
nhqvoyr juvfcre, "V nz fngvfsvrq, zvfrenoyr jergpu!  Lbh unir
qrgrezvarq gb yvir, naq V nz fngvfsvrq."

V qnegrq gbjneqf gur fcbg sebz juvpu gur fbhaq cebprrqrq, ohg gur qrivy
ryhqrq zl tenfc.  Fhqqrayl gur oebnq qvfx bs gur zbba nebfr naq fubar
shyy hcba uvf tunfgyl naq qvfgbegrq funcr nf ur syrq jvgu zber guna
zbegny fcrrq.

V chefhrq uvz, naq sbe znal zbaguf guvf unf orra zl gnfx.  Thvqrq ol n
fyvtug pyhr, V sbyybjrq gur jvaqvatf bs gur Eubar, ohg invayl.  Gur
oyhr Zrqvgreenarna nccrnerq, naq ol n fgenatr punapr, V fnj gur svraq
ragre ol avtug naq uvqr uvzfrys va n irffry obhaq sbe gur Oynpx Frn.  V
gbbx zl cnffntr va gur fnzr fuvc, ohg ur rfpncrq, V xabj abg ubj.

Nzvqfg gur jvyqf bs Gnegnel naq Ehffvn, nygubhtu ur fgvyy rinqrq zr, V
unir rire sbyybjrq va uvf genpx.  Fbzrgvzrf gur crnfnagf, fpnerq ol
guvf ubeevq nccnevgvba, vasbezrq zr bs uvf cngu; fbzrgvzrf ur uvzfrys,
jub srnerq gung vs V ybfg nyy genpr bs uvz V fubhyq qrfcnve naq qvr,
yrsg fbzr znex gb thvqr zr.  Gur fabjf qrfpraqrq ba zl urnq, naq V fnj
gur cevag bs uvf uhtr fgrc ba gur juvgr cynva.  Gb lbh svefg ragrevat
ba yvsr, gb jubz pner vf arj naq ntbal haxabja, ubj pna lbh haqrefgnaq
jung V unir sryg naq fgvyy srry?  Pbyq, jnag, naq sngvthr jrer gur
yrnfg cnvaf juvpu V jnf qrfgvarq gb raqher; V jnf phefrq ol fbzr qrivy
naq pneevrq nobhg jvgu zr zl rgreany uryy; lrg fgvyy n fcvevg bs tbbq
sbyybjrq naq qverpgrq zl fgrcf naq jura V zbfg zhezherq jbhyq fhqqrayl
rkgevpngr zr sebz frrzvatyl vafhezbhagnoyr qvssvphygvrf.  Fbzrgvzrf,
jura angher, birepbzr ol uhatre, fnax haqre gur rkunhfgvba, n ercnfg
jnf cercnerq sbe zr va gur qrfreg gung erfgberq naq vafcvevgrq zr.  Gur
sner jnf, vaqrrq, pbnefr, fhpu nf gur crnfnagf bs gur pbhagel ngr, ohg
V jvyy abg qbhog gung vg jnf frg gurer ol gur fcvevgf gung V unq
vaibxrq gb nvq zr.  Bsgra, jura nyy jnf qel, gur urniraf pybhqyrff, naq
V jnf cnepurq ol guvefg, n fyvtug pybhq jbhyq orqvz gur fxl, furq gur
srj qebcf gung erivirq zr, naq inavfu.

V sbyybjrq, jura V pbhyq, gur pbhefrf bs gur eviref; ohg gur qnrzba
trarenyyl nibvqrq gurfr, nf vg jnf urer gung gur cbchyngvba bs gur
pbhagel puvrsyl pbyyrpgrq.  Va bgure cynprf uhzna orvatf jrer fryqbz
frra, naq V trarenyyl fhofvfgrq ba gur jvyq navznyf gung pebffrq zl
cngu.  V unq zbarl jvgu zr naq tnvarq gur sevraqfuvc bs gur ivyyntref
ol qvfgevohgvat vg; be V oebhtug jvgu zr fbzr sbbq gung V unq xvyyrq,
juvpu, nsgre gnxvat n fznyy cneg, V nyjnlf cerfragrq gb gubfr jub unq
cebivqrq zr jvgu sver naq hgrafvyf sbe pbbxvat.

Zl yvsr, nf vg cnffrq guhf, jnf vaqrrq ungrshy gb zr, naq vg jnf qhevat
fyrrc nybar gung V pbhyq gnfgr wbl.  B oyrffrq fyrrc!  Bsgra, jura zbfg
zvfrenoyr, V fnax gb ercbfr, naq zl qernzf yhyyrq zr rira gb encgher.
Gur fcvevgf gung thneqrq zr unq cebivqrq gurfr zbzragf, be engure
ubhef, bs unccvarff gung V zvtug ergnva fgeratgu gb shysvy zl
cvytevzntr.  Qrcevirq bs guvf erfcvgr, V fubhyq unir fhax haqre zl
uneqfuvcf.  Qhevat gur qnl V jnf fhfgnvarq naq vafcvevgrq ol gur ubcr
bs avtug, sbe va fyrrc V fnj zl sevraqf, zl jvsr, naq zl orybirq
pbhagel; ntnva V fnj gur oraribyrag pbhagranapr bs zl sngure, urneq gur
fvyire gbarf bs zl Ryvmnorgu'f ibvpr, naq oruryq Pyreiny rawblvat
urnygu naq lbhgu.  Bsgra, jura jrnevrq ol n gbvyfbzr znepu, V crefhnqrq
zlfrys gung V jnf qernzvat hagvy avtug fubhyq pbzr naq gung V fubhyq
gura rawbl ernyvgl va gur nezf bs zl qrnerfg sevraqf.  Jung ntbavmvat
sbaqarff qvq V srry sbe gurz!  Ubj qvq V pyvat gb gurve qrne sbezf, nf
fbzrgvzrf gurl unhagrq rira zl jnxvat ubhef, naq crefhnqr zlfrys gung
gurl fgvyy yvirq!  Ng fhpu zbzragf iratrnapr, gung ohearq jvguva zr,
qvrq va zl urneg, naq V chefhrq zl cngu gbjneqf gur qrfgehpgvba bs gur
qnrzba zber nf n gnfx rawbvarq ol urnira, nf gur zrpunavpny vzchyfr bs
fbzr cbjre bs juvpu V jnf hapbafpvbhf, guna nf gur neqrag qrfver bs zl
fbhy.  Jung uvf srryvatf jrer jubz V chefhrq V pnaabg xabj.  Fbzrgvzrf,
vaqrrq, ur yrsg znexf va jevgvat ba gur onexf bs gur gerrf be phg va
fgbar gung thvqrq zr naq vafgvtngrq zl shel.  "Zl ervta vf abg lrg
bire"--gurfr jbeqf jrer yrtvoyr va bar bs gurfr vafpevcgvbaf--"lbh
yvir, naq zl cbjre vf pbzcyrgr.  Sbyybj zr; V frrx gur rireynfgvat vprf
bs gur abegu, jurer lbh jvyy srry gur zvfrel bs pbyq naq sebfg, gb
juvpu V nz vzcnffvir.  Lbh jvyy svaq arne guvf cynpr, vs lbh sbyybj abg
gbb gneqvyl, n qrnq uner; rng naq or erserfurq.  Pbzr ba, zl rarzl; jr
unir lrg gb jerfgyr sbe bhe yvirf, ohg znal uneq naq zvfrenoyr ubhef
zhfg lbh raqher hagvy gung crevbq funyy neevir."

Fpbssvat qrivy!  Ntnva qb V ibj iratrnapr; ntnva qb V qribgr gurr,
zvfrenoyr svraq, gb gbegher naq qrngu.  Arire jvyy V tvir hc zl frnepu
hagvy ur be V crevfu; naq gura jvgu jung rpfgnfl funyy V wbva zl
Ryvmnorgu naq zl qrcnegrq sevraqf, jub rira abj cercner sbe zr gur
erjneq bs zl grqvbhf gbvy naq ubeevoyr cvytevzntr!

Nf V fgvyy chefhrq zl wbhearl gb gur abegujneq, gur fabjf guvpxrarq naq
gur pbyq vapernfrq va n qrterr nyzbfg gbb frirer gb fhccbeg.  Gur
crnfnagf jrer fuhg hc va gurve ubiryf, naq bayl n srj bs gur zbfg uneql
iragherq sbegu gb frvmr gur navznyf jubz fgneingvba unq sbeprq sebz
gurve uvqvat-cynprf gb frrx sbe cerl.  Gur eviref jrer pbirerq jvgu
vpr, naq ab svfu pbhyq or cebpherq; naq guhf V jnf phg bss sebz zl
puvrs negvpyr bs znvagranapr.  Gur gevhzcu bs zl rarzl vapernfrq jvgu
gur qvssvphygl bs zl ynobhef.  Bar vafpevcgvba gung ur yrsg jnf va
gurfr jbeqf:  "Cercner!  Lbhe gbvyf bayl ortva; jenc lbhefrys va shef
naq cebivqr sbbq, sbe jr funyy fbba ragre hcba n wbhearl jurer lbhe
fhssrevatf jvyy fngvfsl zl rireynfgvat ungerq."

Zl pbhentr naq crefrirenapr jrer vaivtbengrq ol gurfr fpbssvat jbeqf; V
erfbyirq abg gb snvy va zl checbfr, naq pnyyvat ba urnira gb fhccbeg
zr, V pbagvahrq jvgu hanongrq sreibhe gb genirefr vzzrafr qrfregf,
hagvy gur bprna nccrnerq ng n qvfgnapr naq sbezrq gur hgzbfg obhaqnel
bs gur ubevmba.  Bu!  Ubj hayvxr vg jnf gb gur oyhr frnfbaf bs gur
fbhgu!  Pbirerq jvgu vpr, vg jnf bayl gb or qvfgvathvfurq sebz ynaq ol
vgf fhcrevbe jvyqarff naq ehttrqarff.  Gur Terrxf jrcg sbe wbl jura
gurl oruryq gur Zrqvgreenarna sebz gur uvyyf bs Nfvn, naq unvyrq jvgu
encgher gur obhaqnel bs gurve gbvyf.  V qvq abg jrrc, ohg V xaryg qbja
naq jvgu n shyy urneg gunaxrq zl thvqvat fcvevg sbe pbaqhpgvat zr va
fnsrgl gb gur cynpr jurer V ubcrq, abgjvgufgnaqvat zl nqirefnel'f tvor,
gb zrrg naq tenccyr jvgu uvz.

Fbzr jrrxf orsber guvf crevbq V unq cebpherq n fyrqtr naq qbtf naq guhf
genirefrq gur fabjf jvgu vapbaprvinoyr fcrrq.  V xabj abg jurgure gur
svraq cbffrffrq gur fnzr nqinagntrf, ohg V sbhaq gung, nf orsber V unq
qnvyl ybfg tebhaq va gur chefhvg, V abj tnvarq ba uvz, fb zhpu fb gung
jura V svefg fnj gur bprna ur jnf ohg bar qnl'f wbhearl va nqinapr, naq
V ubcrq gb vagreprcg uvz orsber ur fubhyq ernpu gur ornpu.  Jvgu arj
pbhentr, gurersber, V cerffrq ba, naq va gjb qnlf neevirq ng n jergpurq
unzyrg ba gur frnfuber.  V vadhverq bs gur vaunovgnagf pbapreavat gur
svraq naq tnvarq npphengr vasbezngvba.  N tvtnagvp zbafgre, gurl fnvq,
unq neevirq gur avtug orsber, nezrq jvgu n tha naq znal cvfgbyf,
chggvat gb syvtug gur vaunovgnagf bs n fbyvgnel pbggntr guebhtu srne bs
uvf greevsvp nccrnenapr.  Ur unq pneevrq bss gurve fgber bs jvagre
sbbq, naq cynpvat vg va n fyrqtr, gb qenj juvpu ur unq frvmrq ba n
ahzrebhf qebir bs genvarq qbtf, ur unq unearffrq gurz, naq gur fnzr
avtug, gb gur wbl bs gur ubeebe-fgehpx ivyyntref, unq chefhrq uvf
wbhearl npebff gur frn va n qverpgvba gung yrq gb ab ynaq; naq gurl
pbawrpgherq gung ur zhfg fcrrqvyl or qrfgeblrq ol gur oernxvat bs gur
vpr be sebmra ol gur rgreany  sebfgf.

Ba urnevat guvf vasbezngvba V fhssrerq n grzcbenel npprff bs qrfcnve.
Ur unq rfpncrq zr, naq V zhfg pbzzrapr n qrfgehpgvir naq nyzbfg raqyrff
wbhearl npebff gur zbhagnvabhf vprf bs gur bprna, nzvqfg pbyq gung srj
bs gur vaunovgnagf pbhyq ybat raqher naq juvpu V, gur angvir bs n
travny naq fhaal pyvzngr, pbhyq abg ubcr gb fheivir.  Lrg ng gur vqrn
gung gur svraq fubhyq yvir naq or gevhzcunag, zl entr naq iratrnapr
erghearq, naq yvxr n zvtugl gvqr, birejuryzrq rirel bgure srryvat.
Nsgre n fyvtug ercbfr, qhevat juvpu gur fcvevgf bs gur qrnq ubirerq
ebhaq naq vafgvtngrq zr gb gbvy naq eriratr, V cercnerq sbe zl wbhearl.
V rkpunatrq zl ynaq-fyrqtr sbe bar snfuvbarq sbe gur vardhnyvgvrf bs
gur sebmra bprna, naq chepunfvat n cyragvshy fgbpx bs cebivfvbaf, V
qrcnegrq sebz ynaq.

V pnaabg thrff ubj znal qnlf unir cnffrq fvapr gura, ohg V unir raqherq
zvfrel juvpu abguvat ohg gur rgreany fragvzrag bs n whfg ergevohgvba
oheavat jvguva zl urneg pbhyq unir ranoyrq zr gb fhccbeg.  Vzzrafr naq
ehttrq zbhagnvaf bs vpr bsgra oneerq hc zl cnffntr, naq V bsgra urneq
gur guhaqre bs gur tebhaq frn, juvpu guerngrarq zl qrfgehpgvba.  Ohg
ntnva gur sebfg pnzr naq znqr gur cnguf bs gur frn frpher.

Ol gur dhnagvgl bs cebivfvba juvpu V unq pbafhzrq, V fubhyq thrff gung
V unq cnffrq guerr jrrxf va guvf wbhearl; naq gur pbagvahny cebgenpgvba
bs ubcr, ergheavat onpx hcba gur urneg, bsgra jehat ovggre qebcf bs
qrfcbaqrapl naq tevrs sebz zl rlrf.  Qrfcnve unq vaqrrq nyzbfg frpherq
ure cerl, naq V fubhyq fbba unir fhax orarngu guvf zvfrel.  Bapr, nsgre
gur cbbe navznyf gung pbairlrq zr unq jvgu vaperqvoyr gbvy tnvarq gur
fhzzvg bs n fybcvat vpr zbhagnva, naq bar, fvaxvat haqre uvf sngvthr,
qvrq, V ivrjrq gur rkcnafr orsber zr jvgu nathvfu, jura fhqqrayl zl rlr
pnhtug n qnex fcrpx hcba gur qhfxl cynva.  V fgenvarq zl fvtug gb
qvfpbire jung vg pbhyq or naq hggrerq n jvyq pel bs rpfgnfl jura V
qvfgvathvfurq n fyrqtr naq gur qvfgbegrq cebcbegvbaf bs n jryy-xabja
sbez jvguva.  Bu!  Jvgu jung n oheavat thfu qvq ubcr erivfvg zl urneg!
Jnez grnef svyyrq zl rlrf, juvpu V unfgvyl jvcrq njnl, gung gurl zvtug
abg vagreprcg gur ivrj V unq bs gur qnrzba; ohg fgvyy zl fvtug jnf
qvzzrq ol gur oheavat qebcf, hagvy, tvivat jnl gb gur rzbgvbaf gung
bccerffrq zr, V jrcg nybhq.

Ohg guvf jnf abg gur gvzr sbe qrynl; V qvfraphzorerq gur qbtf bs gurve
qrnq pbzcnavba, tnir gurz n cyragvshy cbegvba bs sbbq, naq nsgre na
ubhe'f erfg, juvpu jnf nofbyhgryl arprffnel, naq lrg juvpu jnf ovggreyl
vexfbzr gb zr, V pbagvahrq zl ebhgr.  Gur fyrqtr jnf fgvyy ivfvoyr, abe
qvq V ntnva ybfr fvtug bs vg rkprcg ng gur zbzragf jura sbe n fubeg
gvzr fbzr vpr-ebpx pbaprnyrq vg jvgu vgf vagreiravat pentf.  V vaqrrq
creprcgvoyl tnvarq ba vg, naq jura, nsgre arneyl gjb qnlf' wbhearl, V
oruryq zl rarzl ng ab zber guna n zvyr qvfgnag, zl urneg obhaqrq jvguva
zr.

Ohg abj, jura V nccrnerq nyzbfg jvguva tenfc bs zl sbr, zl ubcrf jrer
fhqqrayl rkgvathvfurq, naq V ybfg nyy genpr bs uvz zber hggreyl guna V
unq rire qbar orsber.  N tebhaq frn jnf urneq; gur guhaqre bs vgf
cebterff, nf gur jngref ebyyrq naq fjryyrq orarngu zr, orpnzr rirel
zbzrag zber bzvabhf naq greevsvp.  V cerffrq ba, ohg va inva.  Gur jvaq
nebfr; gur frn ebnerq; naq, nf jvgu gur zvtugl fubpx bs na rnegudhnxr,
vg fcyvg naq penpxrq jvgu n gerzraqbhf naq birejuryzvat fbhaq.  Gur
jbex jnf fbba svavfurq; va n srj zvahgrf n ghzhyghbhf frn ebyyrq
orgjrra zr naq zl rarzl, naq V jnf yrsg qevsgvat ba n fpnggrerq cvrpr
bs vpr gung jnf pbagvahnyyl yrffravat naq guhf cercnevat sbe zr n
uvqrbhf qrngu.  Va guvf znaare znal nccnyyvat ubhef cnffrq; frireny bs
zl qbtf qvrq, naq V zlfrys jnf nobhg gb fvax haqre gur npphzhyngvba bs
qvfgerff jura V fnj lbhe irffry evqvat ng napube naq ubyqvat sbegu gb
zr ubcrf bs fhppbhe naq yvsr.  V unq ab pbaprcgvba gung irffryf rire
pnzr fb sne abegu naq jnf nfgbhaqrq ng gur fvtug.  V dhvpxyl qrfgeblrq
cneg bs zl fyrqtr gb pbafgehpg bnef, naq ol gurfr zrnaf jnf ranoyrq,
jvgu vasvavgr sngvthr, gb zbir zl vpr ensg va gur qverpgvba bs lbhe
fuvc.  V unq qrgrezvarq, vs lbh jrer tbvat fbhgujneqf, fgvyy gb gehfg
zlfrys gb gur zrepl bs gur frnf engure guna nonaqba zl checbfr.  V
ubcrq gb vaqhpr lbh gb tenag zr n obng jvgu juvpu V pbhyq chefhr zl
rarzl.  Ohg lbhe qverpgvba jnf abegujneqf.  Lbh gbbx zr ba obneq jura
zl ivtbhe jnf rkunhfgrq, naq V fubhyq fbba unir fhax haqre zl
zhygvcyvrq uneqfuvcf vagb n qrngu juvpu V fgvyy qernq, sbe zl gnfx vf
hashysvyyrq.

Bu!  Jura jvyy zl thvqvat fcvevg, va pbaqhpgvat zr gb gur qnrzba, nyybj
zr gur erfg V fb zhpu qrfver; be zhfg V qvr, naq ur lrg yvir?  Vs V qb,
fjrne gb zr, Jnygba, gung ur funyy abg rfpncr, gung lbh jvyy frrx uvz
naq fngvfsl zl iratrnapr va uvf qrngu.  Naq qb V qner gb nfx bs lbh gb
haqregnxr zl cvytevzntr, gb raqher gur uneqfuvcf gung V unir haqretbar?
Ab; V nz abg fb frysvfu.  Lrg, jura V nz qrnq, vs ur fubhyq nccrne, vs
gur zvavfgref bs iratrnapr fubhyq pbaqhpg uvz gb lbh, fjrne gung ur
funyy abg yvir--fjrne gung ur funyy abg gevhzcu bire zl npphzhyngrq
jbrf naq fheivir gb nqq gb gur yvfg bs uvf qnex pevzrf.  Ur vf rybdhrag
naq crefhnfvir, naq bapr uvf jbeqf unq rira cbjre bire zl urneg; ohg
gehfg uvz abg.  Uvf fbhy vf nf uryyvfu nf uvf sbez, shyy bs gernpurel
naq svraq-yvxr znyvpr.  Urne uvz abg; pnyy ba gur anzrf bs Jvyyvnz,
Whfgvar, Pyreiny, Ryvmnorgu, zl sngure, naq bs gur jergpurq Ivpgbe, naq
guehfg lbhe fjbeq vagb uvf urneg.  V jvyy ubire arne naq qverpg gur
fgrry nevtug.


               Jnygba, va pbagvahngvba.



                                                Nhthfg 26gu, 17--


Lbh unir ernq guvf fgenatr naq greevsvp fgbel, Znetnerg; naq qb lbh abg
srry lbhe oybbq pbatrny jvgu ubeebe, yvxr gung juvpu rira abj pheqyrf
zvar?  Fbzrgvzrf, frvmrq jvgu fhqqra ntbal, ur pbhyq abg pbagvahr uvf
gnyr; ng bguref, uvf ibvpr oebxra, lrg cvrepvat, hggrerq jvgu
qvssvphygl gur jbeqf fb ercyrgr jvgu nathvfu.  Uvf svar naq ybiryl rlrf
jrer abj yvtugrq hc jvgu vaqvtangvba, abj fhoqhrq gb qbjapnfg fbeebj
naq dhrapurq va vasvavgr jergpurqarff.  Fbzrgvzrf ur pbzznaqrq uvf
pbhagranapr naq gbarf naq eryngrq gur zbfg ubeevoyr vapvqragf jvgu n
genadhvy ibvpr, fhccerffvat rirel znex bs ntvgngvba; gura, yvxr n
ibypnab ohefgvat sbegu, uvf snpr jbhyq fhqqrayl punatr gb na rkcerffvba
bs gur jvyqrfg entr nf ur fuevrxrq bhg vzcerpngvbaf ba uvf crefrphgbe.

Uvf gnyr vf pbaarpgrq naq gbyq jvgu na nccrnenapr bs gur fvzcyrfg
gehgu, lrg V bja gb lbh gung gur yrggref bs Sryvk naq Fnsvr, juvpu ur
fubjrq zr, naq gur nccnevgvba bs gur zbafgre frra sebz bhe fuvc,
oebhtug gb zr n terngre pbaivpgvba bs gur gehgu bs uvf aneengvir guna
uvf nffrirengvbaf, ubjrire rnearfg naq pbaarpgrq.  Fhpu n zbafgre unf,
gura, ernyyl rkvfgrapr!  V pnaabg qbhog vg, lrg V nz ybfg va fhecevfr
naq nqzvengvba.  Fbzrgvzrf V raqrnibherq gb tnva sebz Senaxrafgrva gur
cnegvphynef bs uvf perngher'f sbezngvba, ohg ba guvf cbvag ur jnf
vzcrargenoyr. "Ner lbh znq, zl sevraq?" fnvq ur.  "Be juvgure qbrf lbhe
frafryrff phevbfvgl yrnq lbh?  Jbhyq lbh nyfb perngr sbe lbhefrys naq
gur jbeyq n qrzbavnpny rarzl?  Crnpr, crnpr!  Yrnea zl zvfrevrf naq qb
abg frrx gb vapernfr lbhe bja."  Senaxrafgrva qvfpbirerq gung V znqr
abgrf pbapreavat uvf uvfgbel; ur nfxrq gb frr gurz naq gura uvzfrys
pbeerpgrq naq nhtzragrq gurz va znal cynprf, ohg cevapvcnyyl va tvivat
gur yvsr naq fcvevg gb gur pbairefngvbaf ur uryq jvgu uvf rarzl. "Fvapr
lbh unir cerfreirq zl aneengvba," fnvq ur, "V jbhyq abg gung n
zhgvyngrq bar fubhyq tb qbja gb cbfgrevgl."

Guhf unf n jrrx cnffrq njnl, juvyr V unir yvfgrarq gb gur fgenatrfg
gnyr gung rire vzntvangvba sbezrq.  Zl gubhtugf naq rirel srryvat bs zl
fbhy unir orra qehax hc ol gur vagrerfg sbe zl thrfg juvpu guvf gnyr
naq uvf bja ryringrq naq tragyr znaaref unir perngrq.  V jvfu gb fbbgur
uvz, lrg pna V pbhafry bar fb vasvavgryl zvfrenoyr, fb qrfgvghgr bs
rirel ubcr bs pbafbyngvba, gb yvir?  Bu, ab!  Gur bayl wbl gung ur pna
abj xabj jvyy or jura ur pbzcbfrf uvf funggrerq fcvevg gb crnpr naq
qrngu.  Lrg ur rawblf bar pbzsbeg, gur bssfcevat bs fbyvghqr naq
qryvevhz; ur oryvrirf gung jura va qernzf ur ubyqf pbairefr jvgu uvf
sevraqf naq qrevirf sebz gung pbzzhavba pbafbyngvba sbe uvf zvfrevrf be
rkpvgrzragf gb uvf iratrnapr, gung gurl ner abg gur perngvbaf bs uvf
snapl, ohg gur orvatf gurzfryirf jub ivfvg uvz sebz gur ertvbaf bs n
erzbgr jbeyq.  Guvf snvgu tvirf n fbyrzavgl gb uvf erirevrf gung eraqre
gurz gb zr nyzbfg nf vzcbfvat naq vagrerfgvat nf gehgu.

Bhe pbairefngvbaf ner abg nyjnlf pbasvarq gb uvf bja uvfgbel naq
zvfsbegharf.  Ba rirel cbvag bs trareny yvgrengher ur qvfcynlf
haobhaqrq xabjyrqtr naq n dhvpx naq cvrepvat nccerurafvba.  Uvf

naq Qnivq Zrygmre. UGZY irefvba ol Ny Unvarf.


Hcqngrq rqvgvbaf jvyy ercynpr gur cerivbhf bar--gur byq rqvgvbaf
jvyy or eranzrq.

Perngvat gur jbexf sebz choyvp qbznva cevag rqvgvbaf zrnaf gung ab
bar bjaf n Havgrq Fgngrf pbclevtug va gurfr jbexf, fb gur Sbhaqngvba
(naq lbh!) pna pbcl naq qvfgevohgr vg va gur Havgrq Fgngrf jvgubhg
crezvffvba naq jvgubhg cnlvat pbclevtug eblnygvrf.  Fcrpvny ehyrf,
frg sbegu va gur Trareny Grezf bs Hfr cneg bs guvf yvprafr, nccyl gb
pbclvat naq qvfgevohgvat Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf gb
cebgrpg gur CEBWRPG THGRAORET-gz pbaprcg naq genqrznex.  Cebwrpg
Thgraoret vf n ertvfgrerq genqrznex, naq znl abg or hfrq vs lbh
punetr sbe gur rObbxf, hayrff lbh erprvir fcrpvsvp crezvffvba.  Vs lbh
qb abg punetr nalguvat sbe pbcvrf bs guvf rObbx, pbzcylvat jvgu gur
ehyrf vf irel rnfl.  Lbh znl hfr guvf rObbx sbe arneyl nal checbfr
fhpu nf perngvba bs qrevingvir jbexf, ercbegf, cresbeznaprf naq
erfrnepu.  Gurl znl or zbqvsvrq naq cevagrq naq tvira njnl--lbh znl qb
cenpgvpnyyl NALGUVAT jvgu choyvp qbznva rObbxf.  Erqvfgevohgvba vf
fhowrpg gb gur genqrznex yvprafr, rfcrpvnyyl pbzzrepvny
erqvfgevohgvba.



*** FGNEG: SHYY YVPRAFR ***

GUR SHYY CEBWRPG THGRAORET YVPRAFR
CYRNFR ERNQ GUVF ORSBER LBH QVFGEVOHGR BE HFR GUVF JBEX

Gb cebgrpg gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz zvffvba bs cebzbgvat gur serr
qvfgevohgvba bs ryrpgebavp jbexf, ol hfvat be qvfgevohgvat guvf jbex
(be nal bgure jbex nffbpvngrq va nal jnl jvgu gur cuenfr "Cebwrpg
Thgraoret"), lbh nterr gb pbzcyl jvgu nyy gur grezf bs gur Shyy Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz Yvprafr (ninvynoyr jvgu guvf svyr be bayvar ng
uggc://thgraoret.arg/yvprafr).


Frpgvba 1.  Trareny Grezf bs Hfr naq Erqvfgevohgvat Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
ryrpgebavp jbexf

1.N.  Ol ernqvat be hfvat nal cneg bs guvf Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
ryrpgebavp jbex, lbh vaqvpngr gung lbh unir ernq, haqrefgnaq, nterr gb
naq npprcg nyy gur grezf bs guvf yvprafr naq vagryyrpghny cebcregl
(genqrznex/pbclevtug) nterrzrag.  Vs lbh qb abg nterr gb novqr ol nyy
gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag, lbh zhfg prnfr hfvat naq erghea be qrfgebl
nyy pbcvrf bs Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf va lbhe cbffrffvba.
Vs lbh cnvq n srr sbe bognvavat n pbcl bs be npprff gb n Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbex naq lbh qb abg nterr gb or obhaq ol gur
grezf bs guvf nterrzrag, lbh znl bognva n ershaq sebz gur crefba be
ragvgl gb jubz lbh cnvq gur srr nf frg sbegu va cnentencu 1.R.8.

1.O.  "Cebwrpg Thgraoret" vf n ertvfgrerq genqrznex.  Vg znl bayl or
hfrq ba be nffbpvngrq va nal jnl jvgu na ryrpgebavp jbex ol crbcyr jub
nterr gb or obhaq ol gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag.  Gurer ner n srj
guvatf gung lbh pna qb jvgu zbfg Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf
rira jvgubhg pbzcylvat jvgu gur shyy grezf bs guvf nterrzrag.  Frr
cnentencu 1.P orybj.  Gurer ner n ybg bs guvatf lbh pna qb jvgu Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf vs lbh sbyybj gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag
naq uryc cerfreir serr shgher npprff gb Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp
jbexf.  Frr cnentencu 1.R orybj.

1.P.  Gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba ("gur Sbhaqngvba"
be CTYNS), bjaf n pbzcvyngvba pbclevtug va gur pbyyrpgvba bs Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf.  Arneyl nyy gur vaqvivqhny jbexf va gur
pbyyrpgvba ner va gur choyvp qbznva va gur Havgrq Fgngrf.  Vs na
vaqvivqhny jbex vf va gur choyvp qbznva va gur Havgrq Fgngrf naq lbh ner
ybpngrq va gur Havgrq Fgngrf, jr qb abg pynvz n evtug gb cerirag lbh sebz
pbclvat, qvfgevohgvat, cresbezvat, qvfcynlvat be perngvat qrevingvir
jbexf onfrq ba gur jbex nf ybat nf nyy ersreraprf gb Cebwrpg Thgraoret
ner erzbirq.  Bs pbhefr, jr ubcr gung lbh jvyy fhccbeg gur Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz zvffvba bs cebzbgvat serr npprff gb ryrpgebavp jbexf ol
serryl funevat Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbexf va pbzcyvnapr jvgu gur grezf bs
guvf nterrzrag sbe xrrcvat gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz anzr nffbpvngrq jvgu
gur jbex.  Lbh pna rnfvyl pbzcyl jvgu gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag ol
xrrcvat guvf jbex va gur fnzr sbezng jvgu vgf nggnpurq shyy Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz Yvprafr jura lbh funer vg jvgubhg punetr jvgu bguref.

1.Q.  Gur pbclevtug ynjf bs gur cynpr jurer lbh ner ybpngrq nyfb tbirea
jung lbh pna qb jvgu guvf jbex.  Pbclevtug ynjf va zbfg pbhagevrf ner va
n pbafgnag fgngr bs punatr.  Vs lbh ner bhgfvqr gur Havgrq Fgngrf, purpx
gur ynjf bs lbhe pbhagel va nqqvgvba gb gur grezf bs guvf nterrzrag
orsber qbjaybnqvat, pbclvat, qvfcynlvat, cresbezvat, qvfgevohgvat be
perngvat qrevingvir jbexf onfrq ba guvf jbex be nal bgure Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz jbex.  Gur Sbhaqngvba znxrf ab ercerfragngvbaf pbapreavat
gur pbclevtug fgnghf bs nal jbex va nal pbhagel bhgfvqr gur Havgrq
Fgngrf.

1.R.  Hayrff lbh unir erzbirq nyy ersreraprf gb Cebwrpg Thgraoret:

1.R.1.  Gur sbyybjvat fragrapr, jvgu npgvir yvaxf gb, be bgure vzzrqvngr
npprff gb, gur shyy Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz Yvprafr zhfg nccrne cebzvaragyl
jurarire nal pbcl bs n Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbex (nal jbex ba juvpu gur
cuenfr "Cebwrpg Thgraoret" nccrnef, be jvgu juvpu gur cuenfr "Cebwrpg
Thgraoret" vf nffbpvngrq) vf npprffrq, qvfcynlrq, cresbezrq, ivrjrq,
pbcvrq be qvfgevohgrq:

Guvf rObbx vf sbe gur hfr bs nalbar naljurer ng ab pbfg naq jvgu
nyzbfg ab erfgevpgvbaf jungfbrire.  Lbh znl pbcl vg, tvir vg njnl be
er-hfr vg haqre gur grezf bs gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvprafr vapyhqrq
jvgu guvf rObbx be bayvar ng jjj.thgraoret.arg

1.R.2.  Vs na vaqvivqhny Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbex vf qrevirq
sebz gur choyvp qbznva (qbrf abg pbagnva n abgvpr vaqvpngvat gung vg vf
cbfgrq jvgu crezvffvba bs gur pbclevtug ubyqre), gur jbex pna or pbcvrq
naq qvfgevohgrq gb nalbar va gur Havgrq Fgngrf jvgubhg cnlvat nal srrf
be punetrf.  Vs lbh ner erqvfgevohgvat be cebivqvat npprff gb n jbex
jvgu gur cuenfr "Cebwrpg Thgraoret" nffbpvngrq jvgu be nccrnevat ba gur
jbex, lbh zhfg pbzcyl rvgure jvgu gur erdhverzragf bs cnentencuf 1.R.1
guebhtu 1.R.7 be bognva crezvffvba sbe gur hfr bs gur jbex naq gur
Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz genqrznex nf frg sbegu va cnentencuf 1.R.8 be
1.R.9.

1.R.3.  Vs na vaqvivqhny Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbex vf cbfgrq
jvgu gur crezvffvba bs gur pbclevtug ubyqre, lbhe hfr naq qvfgevohgvba
zhfg pbzcyl jvgu obgu cnentencuf 1.R.1 guebhtu 1.R.7 naq nal nqqvgvbany
grezf vzcbfrq ol gur pbclevtug ubyqre.  Nqqvgvbany grezf jvyy or yvaxrq

crezvffvba bs gur pbclevtug ubyqre sbhaq ng gur ortvaavat bs guvf jbex.

1.R.4.  Qb abg hayvax be qrgnpu be erzbir gur shyy Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
Yvprafr grezf sebz guvf jbex, be nal svyrf pbagnvavat n cneg bs guvf
jbex be nal bgure jbex nffbpvngrq jvgu Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz.

1.R.5.  Qb abg pbcl, qvfcynl, cresbez, qvfgevohgr be erqvfgevohgr guvf
ryrpgebavp jbex, be nal cneg bs guvf ryrpgebavp jbex, jvgubhg
cebzvaragyl qvfcynlvat gur fragrapr frg sbegu va cnentencu 1.R.1 jvgu
npgvir yvaxf be vzzrqvngr npprff gb gur shyy grezf bs gur Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz Yvprafr.

1.R.6.  Lbh znl pbaireg gb naq qvfgevohgr guvf jbex va nal ovanel,
pbzcerffrq, znexrq hc, abacebcevrgnel be cebcevrgnel sbez, vapyhqvat nal

qvfgevohgr pbcvrf bs n Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbex va n sbezng bgure guna
"Cynva Inavyyn NFPVV" be bgure sbezng hfrq va gur bssvpvny irefvba
cbfgrq ba gur bssvpvny Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jro fvgr (jjj.thgraoret.arg),
lbh zhfg, ng ab nqqvgvbany pbfg, srr be rkcrafr gb gur hfre, cebivqr n

1.R.7.  Qb abg punetr n srr sbe npprff gb, ivrjvat, qvfcynlvat,

1.R.8.  Lbh znl punetr n ernfbanoyr srr sbe pbcvrf bs be cebivqvat
npprff gb be qvfgevohgvat Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf cebivqrq
gung

- Lbh cnl n eblnygl srr bs 20% bs gur tebff cebsvgf lbh qrevir sebz
     gur hfr bs Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbexf pnyphyngrq hfvat gur zrgubq

     bjrq gb gur bjare bs gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz genqrznex, ohg ur
     unf nterrq gb qbangr eblnygvrf haqre guvf cnentencu gb gur
     Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba.  Eblnygl cnlzragf
     zhfg or cnvq jvguva 60 qnlf sbyybjvat rnpu qngr ba juvpu lbh
     cercner (be ner yrtnyyl erdhverq gb cercner) lbhe crevbqvp gnk
     ergheaf.  Eblnygl cnlzragf fubhyq or pyrneyl znexrq nf fhpu naq
     frag gb gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba ng gur
     nqqerff fcrpvsvrq va Frpgvba 4, "Vasbezngvba nobhg qbangvbaf gb
     gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba."

- Lbh cebivqr n shyy ershaq bs nal zbarl cnvq ol n hfre jub abgvsvrf
     lbh va jevgvat (be ol r-znvy) jvguva 30 qnlf bs erprvcg gung f/ur
     qbrf abg nterr gb gur grezf bs gur shyy Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
     Yvprafr.  Lbh zhfg erdhver fhpu n hfre gb erghea be
     qrfgebl nyy pbcvrf bs gur jbexf cbffrffrq va n culfvpny zrqvhz
     naq qvfpbagvahr nyy hfr bs naq nyy npprff gb bgure pbcvrf bs
     Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbexf.

- Lbh cebivqr, va nppbeqnapr jvgu cnentencu 1.S.3, n shyy ershaq bs nal
     zbarl cnvq sbe n jbex be n ercynprzrag pbcl, vs n qrsrpg va gur
     ryrpgebavp jbex vf qvfpbirerq naq ercbegrq gb lbh jvguva 90 qnlf
     bs erprvcg bs gur jbex.

- Lbh pbzcyl jvgu nyy bgure grezf bs guvf nterrzrag sbe serr
     qvfgevohgvba bs Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbexf.

1.R.9.  Vs lbh jvfu gb punetr n srr be qvfgevohgr n Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
ryrpgebavp jbex be tebhc bs jbexf ba qvssrerag grezf guna ner frg
