Sbhaqngvba nf frg sbegu va Frpgvba 3 orybj.

1.S.

1.S.1.  Cebwrpg Thgraoret ibyhagrref naq rzcyblrrf rkcraq pbafvqrenoyr
rssbeg gb vqragvsl, qb pbclevtug erfrnepu ba, genafpevor naq cebbsernq
choyvp qbznva jbexf va perngvat gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
pbyyrpgvba.  Qrfcvgr gurfr rssbegf, Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp
jbexf, naq gur zrqvhz ba juvpu gurl znl or fgberq, znl pbagnva
"Qrsrpgf," fhpu nf, ohg abg yvzvgrq gb, vapbzcyrgr, vanpphengr be
pbeehcg qngn, genafpevcgvba reebef, n pbclevtug be bgure vagryyrpghny
cebcregl vasevatrzrag, n qrsrpgvir be qnzntrq qvfx be bgure zrqvhz, n
pbzchgre ivehf, be pbzchgre pbqrf gung qnzntr be pnaabg or ernq ol
lbhe rdhvczrag.

1.S.2.  YVZVGRQ JNEENAGL, QVFPYNVZRE BS QNZNTRF - Rkprcg sbe gur "Evtug
bs Ercynprzrag be Ershaq" qrfpevorq va cnentencu 1.S.3, gur Cebwrpg
Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba, gur bjare bs gur Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz genqrznex, naq nal bgure cnegl qvfgevohgvat n Cebwrpg
Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbex haqre guvf nterrzrag, qvfpynvz nyy
yvnovyvgl gb lbh sbe qnzntrf, pbfgf naq rkcrafrf, vapyhqvat yrtny
srrf.  LBH NTERR GUNG LBH UNIR AB ERZRQVRF SBE ARTYVTRAPR, FGEVPG
YVNOVYVGL, OERNPU BS JNEENAGL BE OERNPU BS PBAGENPG RKPRCG GUBFR
CEBIVQRQ VA CNENTENCU S3.  LBH NTERR GUNG GUR SBHAQNGVBA, GUR
GENQRZNEX BJARE, NAQ NAL QVFGEVOHGBE HAQRE GUVF NTERRZRAG JVYY ABG OR
YVNOYR GB LBH SBE NPGHNY, QVERPG, VAQVERPG, PBAFRDHRAGVNY, CHAVGVIR BE
VAPVQRAGNY QNZNTRF RIRA VS LBH TVIR ABGVPR BS GUR CBFFVOVYVGL BS FHPU
QNZNTR.

1.S.3.  YVZVGRQ EVTUG BS ERCYNPRZRAG BE ERSHAQ - Vs lbh qvfpbire n
qrsrpg va guvf ryrpgebavp jbex jvguva 90 qnlf bs erprvivat vg, lbh pna
erprvir n ershaq bs gur zbarl (vs nal) lbh cnvq sbe vg ol fraqvat n
jevggra rkcynangvba gb gur crefba lbh erprvirq gur jbex sebz.  Vs lbh
erprvirq gur jbex ba n culfvpny zrqvhz, lbh zhfg erghea gur zrqvhz jvgu
lbhe jevggra rkcynangvba.  Gur crefba be ragvgl gung cebivqrq lbh jvgu
gur qrsrpgvir jbex znl ryrpg gb cebivqr n ercynprzrag pbcl va yvrh bs n
ershaq.  Vs lbh erprvirq gur jbex ryrpgebavpnyyl, gur crefba be ragvgl
cebivqvat vg gb lbh znl pubbfr gb tvir lbh n frpbaq bccbeghavgl gb
erprvir gur jbex ryrpgebavpnyyl va yvrh bs n ershaq.  Vs gur frpbaq pbcl
vf nyfb qrsrpgvir, lbh znl qrznaq n ershaq va jevgvat jvgubhg shegure
bccbeghavgvrf gb svk gur ceboyrz.

1.S.4.  Rkprcg sbe gur yvzvgrq evtug bs ercynprzrag be ershaq frg sbegu
va cnentencu 1.S.3, guvf jbex vf cebivqrq gb lbh 'NF-VF' JVGU AB BGURE
JNEENAGVRF BS NAL XVAQ, RKCERFF BE VZCYVRQ, VAPYHQVAT OHG ABG YVZVGRQ GB
JNEENAGVRF BS ZREPUNAGVOVYVGL BE SVGARFF SBE NAL CHECBFR.

1.S.5.  Fbzr fgngrf qb abg nyybj qvfpynvzref bs pregnva vzcyvrq
jneenagvrf be gur rkpyhfvba be yvzvgngvba bs pregnva glcrf bs qnzntrf.
Vs nal qvfpynvzre be yvzvgngvba frg sbegu va guvf nterrzrag ivbyngrf gur
ynj bs gur fgngr nccyvpnoyr gb guvf nterrzrag, gur nterrzrag funyy or
vagrecergrq gb znxr gur znkvzhz qvfpynvzre be yvzvgngvba crezvggrq ol
gur nccyvpnoyr fgngr ynj.  Gur vainyvqvgl be harasbeprnovyvgl bs nal
cebivfvba bs guvf nterrzrag funyy abg ibvq gur erznvavat cebivfvbaf.

1.S.6.  VAQRZAVGL - Lbh nterr gb vaqrzavsl naq ubyq gur Sbhaqngvba, gur
genqrznex bjare, nal ntrag be rzcyblrr bs gur Sbhaqngvba, nalbar
cebivqvat pbcvrf bs Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf va nppbeqnapr
jvgu guvf nterrzrag, naq nal ibyhagrref nffbpvngrq jvgu gur cebqhpgvba,
cebzbgvba naq qvfgevohgvba bs Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz ryrpgebavp jbexf,
unezyrff sebz nyy yvnovyvgl, pbfgf naq rkcrafrf, vapyhqvat yrtny srrf,
gung nevfr qverpgyl be vaqverpgyl sebz nal bs gur sbyybjvat juvpu lbh qb
be pnhfr gb bpphe: (n) qvfgevohgvba bs guvf be nal Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz
jbex, (o) nygrengvba, zbqvsvpngvba, be nqqvgvbaf be qryrgvbaf gb nal
Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz jbex, naq (p) nal Qrsrpg lbh pnhfr.


Frpgvba  2.  Vasbezngvba nobhg gur Zvffvba bs Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz

Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz vf flabalzbhf jvgu gur serr qvfgevohgvba bs
ryrpgebavp jbexf va sbezngf ernqnoyr ol gur jvqrfg inevrgl bs pbzchgref
vapyhqvat bofbyrgr, byq, zvqqyr-ntrq naq arj pbzchgref.  Vg rkvfgf
orpnhfr bs gur rssbegf bs uhaqerqf bs ibyhagrref naq qbangvbaf sebz
crbcyr va nyy jnyxf bs yvsr.

Ibyhagrref naq svanapvny fhccbeg gb cebivqr ibyhagrref jvgu gur
nffvfgnapr gurl arrq, vf pevgvpny gb ernpuvat Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz'f
tbnyf naq rafhevat gung gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz pbyyrpgvba jvyy
erznva serryl ninvynoyr sbe trarengvbaf gb pbzr.  Va 2001, gur Cebwrpg
Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba jnf perngrq gb cebivqr n frpher
naq creznarag shgher sbe Cebwrpg Thgraoret-gz naq shgher trarengvbaf.
Gb yrnea zber nobhg gur Cebwrpg Thgraoret Yvgrenel Nepuvir Sbhaqngvba
naq ubj lbhe rssbegf naq qbangvbaf pna uryc, frr Frpgvbaf 3 naq 4
naq gur Sbhaqngvba jro cntr ng uggc://jjj.ctyns.bet.
